Recovery-only authority cannot serve or perform ordinary work; unavailable/stale continuity authority makes same-identity recovery read-only or forces `CloneNewIdentity`.

   The archive is crossed only through `BackupArchiveRef<T> -> PriorIncarnationObjectRef<T> -> RestoreArchiveRef<T>` under the live restore-source lease. `RecoveryIncarnationTransformPlan` is pre-order; leaves-first execution produces `RecoveryIncarnationProjectionResult` before any bridge. For every changed canonical body it verifies/decrypts the source, rewrites only already-produced target references, recomputes ObjectId, performs new AEAD because AAD includes that ObjectId, builds new CiphertextId/EncodingId/Placement/openers/wraps, and proves target availability. Registry-proved incarnation-neutral values alone may reuse a realization. Externally signed historical evidence remains byte-identical as `CarryPriorIncarnationEvidence`; it is not rewritten or fraudulently re-signed. Current configurations/certificates/keys/trust are recreated, and old sessions/capabilities are invalidated with tombstones—new capabilities require fresh authentication/authorization.

   `PendingRestoreCreationGuard` is the only filesystem path that can publish the first non-Genesis `RecoveryReconciling` root. It is limited to the exact projection result, recreated current authority, role-tagged `RestoreState`, bridge, bootstrap closure, manifest, and RootSlot; it cannot encode user work, ordinary receipts/Raft, `Operational`, or service advertisement. It follows the same exclusive staging-inode, sync, no-replace rename, directory-sync, inode-reread, and loser isolation as creation, then yields only `RecoveryWriterLeaseGuard`. The bridge uses typed nonretaining prior-incarnation identities and never validates an old root as current.

   Before activation, recovery CAS-reserves an allocation epoch above the external identity floor; burns every possibly issued post-backup range; reconciles latest privacy/audit continuity and pending DP/audit transitions; resolves or explicitly retains prepared/decision, remote retention/trust, key, backup/replay, cursor/delivery, resource, and derived obligations; and rotates current channel/signing/wrap/verifier authority. `RestoreReconciliationRoot` has one generated slot per obligation class, each `Pending|Resolved|ExplicitlyRetained|DisabledFailClosed`; readiness forbids `Pending`. Unavailable privacy authority disables DP, unavailable audit evidence disables completeness-gated work, and a permanent gap requires the exact external CAS plus local mirror. Incarnation change hides no obligation.

   Canonical Local state is `Reconciling -> VisibilityCommitted -> ServicePreparedHidden -> Operational`; Sharded Meta is `Reconciling -> ActivationOrdered -> VisibilityCommitted -> ServicePreparedHidden -> Operational`; each shard is `Reconciling -> ActivationAppliedHidden -> VisibilityApplied -> ServicePreparedHidden -> Operational`. “Ready” is not an unsequenced canonical-state mutation: it is a same-group certificate over a current hidden `Reconciling` root whose exhaustive reconciliation status is `Complete`. Activation, visibility, service-ready, and operational certificates/acknowledgements are likewise created only after their source root exists, are owned by the certificate ledger, and are consumed by a later command; the source `RestoreState` never points forward to one. Every such artifact strongly owns its exact local closure and binds one restore/service-visibility epoch. Visibility is never endpoint publication. After every shard is visibility-applied, Meta orders `GlobalRestoreServicePrepareSpec`, shards order their prepare and export ready acks, and only then can a portable manifest CAS the continuity head and external catalog and yield `RestoreServicePromotionReceipt`. `GlobalRestoreServiceFinalizeSpec` and each `ShardRestoreServiceOpenSpec` must consume that existing receipt before clearing restore state. Fabric/direct endpoints require the current receipt plus the role-valid local open state; Meta routing also requires the destination shard operational ack. Every handshake, request, session, forwarded shard request, query/transaction child, delivery cursor, and cross-session capability binds `{cluster_incarnation,service_visibility_epoch}`; missing or stale values fail before observation. The `RestoreSourceLease` remains live through independent target reopen and the post-open completion record, then releases.

   `CloneNewIdentity` uses the same archive lease, exhaustive transform, staging guard, reconciliation, and service gate, but assigns a new database/security namespace, `K_oid`, continuity domain, group IDs, and current authority. It preserves source posture—Local stays Local, Sharded stays Sharded; Local→W12 is a later separate audited activation. Historical signed evidence remains behind an explicit clone boundary; only current target authority is newly signed. Old capabilities are invalid. The privacy domain remains shared unless an externally authorized disjoint-population record permits a new one; a new `AuditDomainId` plus signed `AuditCloneBoundary` links source evidence without claiming old tickets were target-issued. RPO/RTO, incremental-base retention, offsite failure domains, key recovery, continuity split-brain, rollback/ID/privacy/audit detection, Local/Sharded restore drills, and every backup/restore/service-gate crash point are deployment gates.

---

## 17. Performance Doctrine & Targets

Reference machine: 32-core/64-thread, 256 GB RAM, PCIe-4 NVMe, single node. Every number below is a provisional `EmpiricalGate`, activated only when its benchmark manifest pins CPU/microcode, kernel/filesystem/mount options, NVMe model/firmware and measured fsync distribution, toolchain/build, database configuration, graph/schema, transaction size and concurrency, retention/FEC/encryption/index policy, cold/warm state, result consumption, and statistical comparison rule. External “best” comparisons pin a publication, version, dataset, and configuration; moving or unavailable comparators cannot be CI gates.

| Domain | Gate |
|---|---|
| Cold bulk load (CSV/Parquet-lite → sealed runs) | ≥ 40M edges/s sustained (I/O-bound: ≥ 60% of NVMe seq-write ceiling) |
| Transactional ingest | Provisional ≥ 2M edge inserts/s for the pinned batch/txn mix; latency includes final rebase/constraint work, payload D1, root D2, configured encryption/FEC, and in replicated mode payload quorum + Raft. No marker-only benchmark is reported as commit latency. |
| Tier-migration churn | report promote↔demote reversals per descriptor, minimum-dwell violations (must be zero), conversion-cost regret, and soak-test limit cycles. SPRT type-I/type-II bounds apply only to its declared decision hypotheses; they are not reversal-rate bounds. |
| Point reads (vertex by key, 1-hop existence) | ≥ 8M lookups/s across cores; p99 < 15 µs warm |
| Neighbor scans, sealed runs (decoded-cache path) | ≥ 500M edges/s per core; ≥ 10B edges/s node aggregate (memory-bandwidth-bound: EF+varint decode ≥ 4 B/edge effective) |
| 2-hop factorized count (10⁸-flat-row equivalent) | < 50 ms (factorization gate: must not materialize) |
| Triangle count (WCOJ over compressed runs), e.g. com-Orkut-class | within 2× of best published static-CSR WCOJ systems; ≥ 20× any pointer-chasing GDBMS |
| LDBC SNB Interactive SF-100 | full compliance run; throughput ≥ 3× Neo4j, ≥ 1.5× best published embedded engine on reference class |
| LDBC Graphalytics (BFS/PR/WCC/CDLP/LCC/SSSP) | within 1.5× of dedicated static analytics engines *on transactional storage* (the Sortledton bar, beaten) |
| LDBC FinBench (write-heavy, temporal-flavored) | publishable leadership run |
| Time-travel query overhead | Measure current OLTP cost by retention policy plus historical latency by checkpoint distance and suffix bytes; provisional targets are <8% current-path overhead and <2.5× for the declared recent-history fixture, not universal guarantees. |
| Vector: 10M × 768-d f32, HNSW | Provisional ≥20k QPS at measured recall ≥0.95 on a pinned authorized-snapshot corpus; publish exact-baseline sampling and confidence interval. Separately report logical commit→delta-tail searchable and commit→merged-generation latency. No sample can “certify” each insert. |
| Ripple view maintenance | delta application ≥ 1M input-changes/s per circuit worker; subscription end-to-end p99 < 10 ms |
| Branch create / snapshot open | Snapshot open is O(1) metadata and provisional <100 µs warm. Durable branch creation is O(1) data-copy complexity but includes root publication/fsync or Raft and has a separate latency distribution. |
| Recovery (clean shutdown / crash @ 1 TB) | < 1 s / < 30 s to first query (anchor-mapped, capsule tail replay) |
| Temporal connectivity (`CONNECTED … AS OF`, sealed history) | Provisional <100 µs per probe over every sequence sampled by the pinned sealed-history fixture. The result is exact only for a matching `sealed-exact` projection/root; branch overlays or uncovered tails must be compensated or fall back (§10.7). |
| Cardinality-interval evidence | Report realized marginal coverage, stratum counts, selection/window policy, drift alarms, and any nonexchangeability penalty; failure reverts to conservative costing. This is `FG-CAL-02`, not a correctness gate. |
| Tail evidence | p99.9 is empirical when sufficiently observed; any POT/GPD extrapolation separately reports threshold, exceedance count, dependence/stability diagnostics, fit uncertainty, and sensitivity. A model failure blocks the extrapolated claim rather than “certifying” the tail. |
| Durability model | Modeled MTTDL ≥ declared target with sensitivity bounds for every shipped profile (`FG-CFG-01`); crash/restore tests remain separate empirical evidence. |
| Controller stability | Defaults outside the named model's predicted instability region with sensitivity margin (`FG-CFG-02`) plus no limit cycle in pinned soak fixtures. |
| Adaptive-policy audit | Promotion requires the registered `FG-CAL-01` evidence rule, overlap/effective-sample checks, and deterministic fallback; reports never claim arbitrary-policy OPE. |

Method: every gate has a bench binary, a committed baseline, a variance budget, and a flamegraph artifact on regression; the harness itself is deterministic (seeded workloads, pinned schedules) so regressions replay. Performance work follows the asupersync "How We Made It Fast" discipline: profile → remove one contention/allocation → re-verify determinism and cancel-correctness → commit with evidence — one lever per change, never a bundle. Five standing laws bind every published number: (1) *no benchmark-only semantics* — durability, isolation, and result consumption match the declared production mode; (2) *distributions, not averages* — p50/p95/p99/p99.9 and worst hot-key behavior are always reported, with extreme quantiles carrying their fitted-tail confidence intervals rather than raw sample maxima; (3) *never hide compaction* — foreground latency during compaction, checkpoint, GC, and index build is part of the result; (4) *memory is a first-class metric* — bytes per live edge include versions, indexes, witnesses, and allocator slack, not just payload; (5) *adaptive numbers disclose their policy epoch* — any result produced under a non-fallback policy names it, and the fallback's number is published beside it.

---

## 18. Workspace Layout & the Build-It-Ourselves Inventory

### 18.1 Crates (`fgdb-*` workspace, layered; Cargo-enforced boundaries per frankensqlite)

| Layer | Crates |
|---|---|
| Foundation | `fgdb-types`, `fgdb-bigint` (canonical exact integers), `fgdb-delta-types` (G0/W2 delta schema only), `fgdb-claim`, `fgdb-authz-types`, `fgdb-policy` (restricted verifier IR), `fgdb-resource`, `fgdb-codec`, `fgdb-sketch`, `fgdb-collections`, `fgdb-crypto`, `fgdb-calibrate`, `fgdb-evidence` |
| Unsafe islands | `fgdb-unsafe-simd`, `fgdb-unsafe-arena`, `fgdb-unsafe-vfs` — the only crate roots not using `forbid(unsafe_code)`; every site is ledgered and exposed only through safe APIs |
| Chronicle | `fgdb-ecs` (identity/encoding/bootstrap/object locator), `fgdb-order` (durable Raft log/state core and quorum-one driver), `fgdb-chronicle` (capsule/marker/logical-local roots, allocator, outcomes, checkpoints/retention, recovery/GC/scrub), `fgdb-branch`, `fgdb-keymgr`, `fgdb-audit`, `fgdb-backup` |
| Strata | `fgdb-strata` (label-independent tiers, seal/compact, stable-ID directory), `fgdb-props`, `fgdb-buffer`, `fgdb-scratch` |
| Txn + secure access | `fgdb-txn` (MVCC, Graph-SSI/witness lifecycle, coordinator, final-effect merge ladder), `fgdb-constraints` (branch-scoped canonical enforcement), `fgdb-secure-view` (sole authorized storage/permit facade); depends on Chronicle + Strata + foundation policy verifier |
| Loom | `fgdb-gql` + `fgdb-cypher` (syntax only), `fgdb-bind`, `fgdb-algebra`, `fgdb-planner`, `fgdb-exec`, `fgdb-linalg`, `fgdb-datalog`; all reads flow through `fgdb-secure-view` |
| Ripple | `fgdb-ripple` (Z-sets, circuits, incrementalizer), `fgdb-views`, `fgdb-subs` |
| Beacon | `fgdb-index-core`, `fgdb-btree`, `fgdb-fts`, `fgdb-vector`, `fgdb-pathidx` (2-hop/landmark + the persistent-union-find temporal-connectivity index, §10.7) |
| Prism | `fgdb-prism` (authorized projection bridge, fnx cursor/cache/materialization paths, native kernels) |
| Warden | `fgdb-warden` (issuance/revocation/discharges/policy admin), `fgdb-privacy`, `fgdb-redaction` |
| Surface/operations | `fgdb-protocol` (FGP state machine), `fgdb-bolt`, `fgdb-formats`, `fgdb-udf-vm`, `fgdb-observatory`, `fgdb-system-graph` |
| Aegis | `fgdb-raft` (multi-member protocol over `fgdb-order`), `fgdb-repl` (payload availability, anti-entropy, reconfiguration, fenced GC); future `fgdb-shard` belongs only to W12 |
| Composition | `fgdb` (embedded API), `fgdb-server` (top-level Fabric+Warden+Aegis composition), `fgdb-cli`, `fgdb-python` (allowed fnx-python packaging boundary only) |
| Verification | `fgdb-sim`, `fgdb-reference` (executable semantics oracle), `fgdb-oracles`, `fgdb-bench`, `fgdb-conformance`, `fgdb-fuzz` |

G0 materializes `invariants.toml`, `evidence.toml`, `slo.toml`, the unsafe-boundary ledger, feature/conformance matrices, threat model, format registries, proof-lane manifests, and exit-criteria contracts before Genesis implementation.

### 18.2 Built in-house (because the universe is closed)

Compression codecs (EF, delta-varint, bitpacking, snappy, roaring-like), canonical signed-limb exact integers, sketches, ART/radix structures, succinct rank/select, vectorized hash tables, B-tree, HNSW + quantizers + IVF-PQ cold tier, persistent union-find, masked-semiring SpMV/SpMSpV kernels, inverted index + BM25 + Levenshtein automata, tokenizers, CSV/JSONL/Parquet-lite readers, GQL/Cypher parsers (hand-written recursive descent + Pratt — the frankensqlite parser school), the DBSP-style circuit runtime, Raft, FGP, Bolt subset, crypto profiles/primitives not already supplied by an audited foundation, the MMR accumulator + transparency checkpoints, the Sextant calibration scores/ledgers (over asupersync's e-process core), the deterministic UDF bytecode VM (§13.8), bench harness. **Explicitly not built**: async runtime, scheduler, channels, TLS/QUIC/HTTP/gRPC stacks, RaptorQ, macaroons, metrics/OTel, deterministic lab, supervision, cluster membership (SWIM+Lifeguard), Merkle-range anti-entropy, coded symbol distribution, CRDT obligation ledgers, HLC, choreographic projection, LDFI/delta-debug/dual-run/trace-export tooling, Kafka/JetStream clients — all asupersync; graph algorithms & legacy formats — all fnx. The closed-universe constraint, which sounds like an albatross, is the moat: the entire dependency surface is auditable, deterministic under lab, and owned.


---

## 19. Workstreams & Convergence Gates

No MVP and no substitute architectures. Work is sequenced by dependency and converges through constitutional gate G0 plus four integration gates. Sharding is W12 after 1.0 and cannot weaken the single-node/replicated contracts.

**Gate G0 — Constitutional Contracts:** before Genesis code, land the threat/trust model; six-bet vocabulary; exact twenty-invariant spine; `invariants.toml`, `evidence.toml`, and `slo.toml`; the four disjoint generated registries `logical_object_kinds.toml`, `physical_record_kinds.toml`, `bootstrap_frames.toml`, and `wire_types.toml`, plus exhaustive `durable_fields.toml`, registered BodyDigest/transcript recipes, acyclic construction/reference checks, and every reserved W12 kind and role-tagged Raft/root/checkpoint variant; full logical/ciphertext/complete-encoding/non-self-referential-placement identity and self-sufficient root bootstrap; dual-slot/local root plus versioned filesystem profile and exact lease→recover→fence-root→enable takeover protocol; layered `LogicalStatePayload`/command/root, the exact fresh-creation three-phase bootstrap plus the sole guarded restore-only RecoveryReconciling bridge and receipt-first hidden service/reopen/completion machine, stable prepared ownership, normative pre-order command/applied-result split, logical-command sequence/HLC, projected-basis `CheckpointStateVector` plus mandatory genesis or paired operational checkpoint/floor install, exact `ConfigurationState`/cuttable weak-checkpoint-observing floor, exact-cut Raft snapshots, and quorum-one state machines; externally fenced stable ID allocator plus privacy and audit continuity; branch-scoped constraints, constructive key-envelope DAG/fork double rotation/recipient grant, pre-minted merge-token/imported-range idempotency ledger, and disclosure contracts; policy IR/permit types; Local two-stage key lifecycle/destruction proof and separately registered W12 Staged-to-Active distributed key/physical-destruction lifecycle; resource/DP/submission+abort outcome/audit admission plus authorization/terminal gates, transaction/control event, resolution/mirror/gap states; distinct answer-requirement/approximation-profile/result-contract plus replay evidence-slot/registry/archive contracts; conditional delta-template and self-contained retained-batch schemas; publicly digested delivered baseline/delta payloads, keyed envelope ID, durable resume cursor, and tagged baseline/delta lease registry; all four cross-session capabilities and their exact FGP issue/present fields; GLA operator and answer-transfer schema; frozen tagged `LanguageContract`s for every advertised surface, including the GQL 1.0 contract's ISO minimum closure, `GG01` or `GG02` plus one of `GG20`–`GG23` as applicable, all prerequisites, synchronous Unicode/UTS #10/UAX #15/UAX #31 bundle, and optional IDs plus exact openCypher/FQL/Datalog profiles; proof-lane manifests; and the clause-granular twenty-ID activation contract whose reachable clauses all have resolvable checker/negative-test entrypoints and `waiver=forbidden`. G0 also synchronizes README/AGENTS summaries and validates their normative examples against these registries. It runs self-containment, dependency-DAG, justification, and fresh-review checks. No workstream may invent a missing semantic choice locally.

| WS | Name | Contents | Depends on |
|---|---|---|---|
| W1 | Bedrock + security foundations | scalar/bigint/delta/claim/authz/policy/resource/codec/crypto/evidence types; unsafe islands/ledgers; lab VFS/sim; reference semantics; generated format parsers and policy verifier | G0 |
| W2 | Chronicle contracts + durability core | self-sufficient bootstrap and metadata-key AAD; dual-slot root under the versioned filesystem profile and exact writer-takeover fence state machine; fresh-Local three-phase logical payload/command/root plus guarded restore bridge plus local/prepared roots; stable prepared ownership; complete encoding versus descriptor-derived placement identity; allocator/privacy/audit continuity; pre-order specs versus applied records; capsule, normative command, logical-command record, marker, and two-sequence state machines; quorum-one Raft ordering and exact-cut snapshots; projected-basis checkpoint plus mandatory Genesis/paired-operational install, operational install of a Provisional cut, inherited-absence/no-new-reclaim enforcement, and separate cut activation; exact configuration schema and weak-checkpoint-observing floor; canonical final-effect→conditional-coordinate `LogicalDeltaTemplate`→self-contained marker-identified `LogicalDeltaBatch` differential; branch-scoped constraint/resource/submission-abort outcome/key-envelope+fork/pre-minted merge/privacy/DP/replay/delivered-baseline+delta cursor/audit admission+terminal+mirror+gap records; retention, Local two-stage key destruction, storage/pin-only backup interfaces, and payload interfaces | W1 |
| W3 | Strata | label-independent tiers, stable-ID directories/ordinal maps, property storage, buffer/scratch, checkpoints, bulk/seal/compaction and physical equivalence | W1, W2 object/snapshot interfaces |
| W4 | Transactions + Secure View | MVCC/SSI/witness lifetime, branch-scoped constraint enforcement, canonical locking, coordinator/rebase/final effects, authorization permit verification, authorized cursor/view/mutation facade | W1 policy verifier, W2, W3 |
| W5 | Loom | syntax → binder → complete GLA → planner/stats → factorized/spillable executor/path semantics; compositional `AnswerContract`; authorization-, witness-, and exactness-preserving rewrites | W2 snapshots, W3 storage, W4 txn/secure view |
| W6 | Ripple | consume W2's canonical delta contract; exact Z-sets, derivative=batch laws, validated recursion, policy-labeled table/graph views, subscriptions/resets | W2 committed effects/delta schema, W5 algebra |
| W7 | Beacon | watermark/tail-correct rebuildable property/adjacency/FTS/vector/path indexes; authority domains; optimized adapters for W4 canonical constraints, never duplicate ownership | W3, W4 constraints/secure view, W5 planner, W6 feeds |
| W8 | Prism + fnx upstream | authorized projection spec, cursor/GAT upstream work, spillable materialization/external algorithms, native kernels | W1 authority, W3, W4 secure view, W5 semantics |
| W9 | Warden | issuance/revocation/discharges, policy administration, constraint declassification/noninterference, irreversible-before-access DP state, Local two-stage reachability-fenced key lifecycle, externally monotonic ticket-gated audit/redaction and rollback reconciliation, replay-resolver and observability authority | W1 verifier/crypto, W2 roots, W4 secure view, W6–W8 derived domains |
| W10 | Fabric + operations | bounded FGP connection, explicit multi-statement transaction, statement/result-delivery, and subscription machines; HTTP/gRPC/WebSocket/Bolt adapters with exact epoch/status parity; admission/QoS; exact Local backup and receipt-first restore/service/reopen gates; CDC; CLI/server/Python/system graph | W2–W9 |
| W11 | Aegis replication + HA | extend W2's quorum-one Raft to multi-member consensus; stable prepared-owner payload availability; joint/final/final-retirement-floor reconfiguration; current-root-recomputed, all-typed-root consensus GC with quarantine and physical-completion evidence; anti-entropy/seeding; follower security/data fences; witnessed transparency | W2 commit/payload/Raft interfaces, W9 authority, W10 protocol/status contracts |
| W12 | Post-1.0 sharding | fresh Sharded Genesis and audited Local activation/authority transfer/RetiredLocal finalization and reclamation; Meta-only semantic time; durable begin-key/outcome reservation, attempt-family generation CAS, operation-ticket claim, TerminalPending/Ready status and detailed/compacted equivalence; explicit statement registration, certified workspace generations, read-your-own-writes, publication/generalized delivery/read-close/cancellation discharge; fixed-point read/effect routing, global authorization, shard D1 prepares, serialization/constraint certificates, signer-locked terminal audit, decision publication, shard audit projection/post-mirror acks and complete GlobalLogicalDeltaBatch publication; cumulative conflict/statement/outcome compaction; remote configuration trust and six-stage retention release; provisional cuts; staged key activation and physical destruction; staged GC quarantine and physical completion; reconfiguration/topology; exact sharded backup/release and hidden receipt-first restore/service/reopen completion | 1.0/G4 and W11; dedicated W12 gate below |

**The Genesis slice.** The first W1–W5 integration begins by proving `Genesis -> CheckpointInstalled -> Operational`, including crashes before/after each checkpoint/floor command, and admits no user operation earlier. It then replaces an operational checkpoint with bytes already absent under the inherited activated cut: recovery must succeed, the replacement Provisional cut must dominate that inherited absence, and no new reclaim may occur until its distinct activation command. It then exercises final abstractions end to end: authenticated authority → pinned GQL `LanguageContract`/Unicode bundle/binder/role-bearing graph references → typed GLA subset → planner → authorized Strata cursor → positive/absence/path witness → SSI/constraint validation → forced base drift and new post-rebase capsule under `IntentSemanticsOid` → D1/D2 logical/local-root publication → crash recovery from both slots and the installed checkpoint → canonical result + executable `ReplayManifest`. It includes stable IDs under label mutation, factorized/flat equivalence, spill, one safe replan class, and a correctly typed decision card. The lab explores declared bounded interleavings and differentials against independent semantics/oracles. No stub transaction, post-filter security, pre-rebase capsule, or parser-interpreted execution qualifies.

**Gate G1 — "The Engine Lives":** fresh-creation three-phase bootstrap and embedded authorized path; bounded resources; declared GQL/Cypher feature subset, synchronous Unicode bundle, and matrix; acyclic durable-object construction; final-capsule/command/pre-minted-merge coherence; stable D1 prepared-root ownership and quorum-one ordered-command crash recovery; generated complete projected checkpoint-vector + mandatory genesis/paired-operational checkpoint-floor install + logical-command/transaction-marker suffix recovery with no historical-floor retention chain, including inherited absent bytes under a dominating replacement Provisional cut and proof that it authorizes no new reclamation before separate activation; exact Raft snapshot cut binding; serializable witness families formally and independently validated; accepted-filesystem conformance plus lease-owner-death/fence-root-before-enable/torn-root/marker-tail/stale-writer/bootstrap/recovery matrices green; constraint state authoritative; compaction/label changes preserve logical digests; strict canonical replay closure works; every clause reachable by the compiled/negotiated G1 capability manifest is live, otherwise that capability is absent. Full language breadth is not claimed until its binder/operator rows exist.

**Gate G2 — "One Version Universe":** verified generated-complete checkpoint-install+logical-command suffix recovery and per-graph retention over mixed transaction/control commands; branch fork double rotation, exact envelope DAG/AAD and `StrongCiphertextRef` realization retention, snapshot/advancing handoff, re-encryption/movement under live grants, sibling/post-fork-parent non-decryption, and pre-minted merge-token/imported-range-idempotent explicit-base merges across history cuts; conditional source templates plus self-contained retained Ripple batches; publicly authenticated baseline results and atomic/coalesced delta provenance/output; durable cursor-generation plus tagged baseline/delta lease, baseline-ACK/delta-ACK/resume/lost-response/expiry recovery with no delta-before-baseline or silent gap; table/graph views with explicit read policies; watermark/tail-correct indexes; historical/capability-safe ANN roots with exact fallback; authorized Prism projections; exact Local backup barrier/pin -> copy and independent archive reopen -> closure certificate -> seal -> publication receipt/archive grant -> ordered pin release; RestoreSourceLease -> exhaustive leaves-first incarnation transform/re-encryption -> guarded RecoveryReconciling bridge -> identity/privacy/audit/cluster-incarnation reconciliation -> hidden activation and service preparation -> continuity-then-catalog CAS receipt -> Local service promotion -> independent target reopen -> completion/audit mirror -> lease release, with stale incarnation/service epochs and old capabilities rejected; Sharded round-trip remains reserved for W12; empirical/statistical gates reported with assumptions.

**Gate G3 — "Verified & Networked":** bounded FGP connection, explicit multi-statement transaction, query/result-delivery/subscription/FEC machines and adapter parity, including durable BeginStaging reservation and lost-BEGIN recovery; statement sequence/key/class and workspace generations; exact SymbolRecord; RESULT_BEGIN/CHUNK/END plus terminal-or-statement ACK/typed release; read-close/write-commit outcomes; `TxnCompletionState::InProgress|TerminalPending(bitmap)|TerminalReady(public outcome)`; NeverRegistered detailed/compacted and terminal detailed/compacted status; canonical baseline/delta transport and ACK/resume; and cluster-incarnation/service-visibility binding in every authenticated frame, handle, cursor, capability, and adapter. Uniform NotVisibleOrUnknown is limited to invalid/unauthorized/wrong-epoch lookup. End-to-end Warden gates noninterference, declared constraint declassifications, revocation, externally monotonic irreversible-before-access DP debit/rollback reconciliation, Local two-stage current-root-recomputed key destruction, and exact audit `PendingUnclaimed -> Claimed(owner) -> Resolved` plus signer-lock/candidate/external-CAS/mirror recovery; lifecycle gates are nonrecursive and permanent gaps are durable. Local receipt-first restore requires continuity/catalog fencing, hidden direct-endpoint negatives, independent archive and target reopen, completion, and source-lease release. Multi-member Raft proves prepared-root payload ownership/availability before ordering, exact stable/joint/final-retirement-floor semantics, paired checkpoint/floor replacement, exact-cut snapshots, leader loss at every phase, two-prefix fenced reads, Local/multi-member all-typed-root GC with exact current-root recomputation and physical-retirement evidence, and idempotent unknown/abort outcomes; W12 quarantine/aggregate GC remains W12-only. Rollback, witnessed-detection, and witnessed-non-equivocation claims remain distinct, with quorum intersection, durable witnesses, consistency, freshness, cross-log, and joint-rotation matrices green wherever prevention is claimed. Raw versus filtered proof scopes, formal/model bounds, and implementation bridges land before their advertised guarantees.

**Gate G4 — "Leapfrog, Published":** all activated §17 benchmark manifests green/public; 100% of G0's 1.0 `LanguageContract`—ISO minimum closure, `GG01` or `GG02` plus one of `GG20`–`GG23` as applicable, all prerequisites, required scalar profile, validated synchronous Unicode/UTS #10/UAX #15/UAX #31 bundle and UCS_BASIC behavior, and named optional IDs—passes its ISO-ID/TCK corpus, while every out-of-contract feature is rejected/documented; canonical replay/archive/answer requirement/profile/result-contract and security matrices; production-format recovery plus Local receipt-first restore, continuity split-brain, stale service epoch, independent archive/target reopen, and source-lease-release drills; crash-fault multi-writer preparation and globally ordered commitment; evidence reports correctly qualified; papers match proven scope; 1.0. W12 sharding is excluded and cannot reuse G4 evidence as its gate.

**Gate W12 — "One Universe, Many Shards" (post-1.0):** every reserved kind/tag/field has an exact registry row; role-tagged Local/Meta/Shard logs, roots, floors, and exact-cut snapshots reject cross-role commands; fresh Sharded Genesis and audited Local freeze/seal/activation/authority transfer/RetiredLocal finalization/reclamation pass every crash point; and every semantic mutation, including single-shard work, enters Meta Raft for one global logical/transaction/HLC order. BEGIN durably reserves its key/outcome capability before response; registration atomically claims the operation ticket and roots workspace zero before every serializable read. Every explicit statement is Meta-registered against one sequence/key/class/error policy and workspace generation; every routed shard reads registered snapshot plus the exact certified overlay for every previously touched shard; Meta publication atomically advances statement/delivery/workspace/witness/effect state and constructs the successor Registered outcome. No result streams before its distinct statement/read-close audit mirror and typed delivery lease; terminal/autocommit and statement results share exact ACK/typed-release transitions. Cancellation proves open-statement, result, overlay, and remote-grant discharge. Read close is a Global control. ReadWrite admission names complete statement/delivery/workspace frontiers; effect-only bases then feed one union-wide authorization decision, while terminal audit remains a separately signer-locked event/resolution. Fence-free prepares, constraint/serialization certificates, pre-command availability, Meta candidate/external CAS/mirror, decision-certificate publication, shard decision, audit projection, post-mirror acknowledgements, complete GlobalLogicalDeltaBatch publication, and TerminalReady status pass exact DAG/crash proofs. Detailed/compacted NeverRegistered and terminal outcomes are byte-identical; attempt compaction's build/attest/publish protocol proves every result/workspace/remote-grant/public-status obligation before release.

Every cross-group edge passes two-sided CertifiedRemoteStrongRef trust/retention/GC tests; every participant prepare has durable availability and one terminal decision; no timeout fractures atomicity under crash/partition/leader loss/reconfiguration. The independent global SCC/history oracle finds no committed cycle across local, cross-shard, negative/gap/path, read-only, workspace, and batch interleavings; deterministic constraint owners/reservations agree with the single-threaded reference. Branch/key/ID/security/resource/privacy/audit authority and activation state is Meta-atomic; shard-local key material changes only through certified Staged-to-Active or destruction protocols. Cross-shard reads use one retained registered snapshot plus exact workspace generation and overlays. Remote configuration trust and the six-stage grant release, replacement Provisional cuts with no-new-reclaim before activation, current-root staged key zero/destroy/member-KMS completion, and GC preflight/quarantine/no-resurrection/member/aggregate completion pass models and physical evidence gates. Exact backup at barrier P proves per-shard copy/reopen/closure, portable Global manifest publication, archive grants, ordered shard release acks, and Meta finalize. Restore proves continuity reservation, exhaustive leaves-first readdress/re-encryption, hidden activation/visibility/service preparation, receipt-first continuity/catalog publication, Meta finalize, shard open, independent reopen, operational acknowledgements, completion, and source-lease release. Three-phase topology copy/cutover/retire proves no ambient evidence, straddled epoch, or premature byte/key retirement. Every failure artifact carries §15's structured replay fields. Meta and every shard pass payload/certificate loss, checkpoint+suffix, donor loss, rolling upgrade, and exact status/backup/restore matrices; every compiled-and-negotiated subordinate clause of FG-INV-01–20 is live and published benchmarks disclose the global sequencer ceiling. Otherwise `sharding=true` is absent.

---

## 20. Risks & Mitigations

| Risk | Reality check | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Scope: this is a multi-hundred-KLOC system | True — and smaller than frankensqlite, on stronger foundations | Agent-swarm methodology with ledger-driven exit criteria (proven twice in-family at this scale); sim-first testing collapses the debugging tail that normally dominates DB schedules; crate boundaries sized for parallel agents |
| Free-Join + factorization + adaptivity interplay is the hardest novel engineering | Correct — this is the crown-jewel risk | Build order inside W5: binary FreeJoin → run-trie WCOJ → factorized columns → adaptivity; each stage gets independent semantic and benchmark evidence; published artifacts are behavioral references, not inherited certificates. |
| Graph-SSI phantom/path witness design could be unsound | Central correctness risk | SERIALIZABLE rejects unverified witness families; formal concretization/may-affect proofs, optimizer-preservation laws, independent small-model histories, and gap/negative/path mutation tests gate each family. SNAPSHOT is an explicit weaker contract, not containment for a false serializable claim. |
| HNSW under MVCC/capabilities/compaction | Known-hard industry-wide | Pin historical authorized topology roots, compensate complete delta tails, retain exact fallback, and label recall evidence by population. Output filtering and exact rerank cannot repair missed candidates. |
| Adaptive tiering thrashes (representation churn eats its own benefit) | The classic failure mode of every adaptive store | SPRT migration cards with indifference-region hysteresis and model-conditional type-I/type-II evidence (§6.6); benefit must exceed conversion cost + uncertainty; pinned deterministic fallback policy under lab; observed migration churn is a separate gated §17 metric |
| Witness refinement becomes a second query (cost eats the abort savings) | Possible on pathological predicates | Refinement is budgeted with conservative-abort fallback; `WitnessTrace` is a byproduct of normal execution (no re-execution); refined-vs-saved accounting on every decision card; the knob defaults conservative |
| Nightly Rust | Both foundations already pin nightly; MSRV churn is real | Pinned toolchain per repo (house pattern), portable-SIMD isolated behind `fgdb-codec`/kernel traits with scalar fallbacks |
| fnx algorithms not yet trait-generic or external-memory where required | Verified: `GraphView` exists with integer rows; compatible larger-than-memory coverage is partial | W8 upstream/cursor work plus spillable materialization and family-specific external algorithms. Unsupported functions remain unregistered—there is no “always-correct fallback” that secretly requires the whole graph in RAM. |
| Final-capsule encoding and quorum distribution limit commit throughput | Correctness requires them before publication | Pipeline/group finalization after coordinator-approved effects, benchmark the complete D1/D2/Raft path, and optimize only after effect-digest and availability invariants remain green. |
| Root/checkpoint/retention protocol loses recovery closure | Catastrophic | Dual root slots, full closure validation, checkpoint authority transfer, stale-writer fencing, two-root GC accounting, and crash matrices at every file/directory barrier. |
| Kùzu's fate as a cautionary tale (great engine, no oxygen) | The sharpest non-technical risk | FrankenGraphDB is an open-source ecosystem asset; B1/B4/B5/B6 target agent memory, auditability, and governance without making ungrounded market guarantees. |
| The calibration plane becomes ornamental math (monitors nobody gates on) | The classic fate of statistical infrastructure | Every Sextant artifact binds to a named decision card, `evidence.toml` row, or `slo.toml` row—or is removed as dead instrumentation. It can gate an adaptive promotion or empirical claim but never masquerades as an invariant checker. |
| Adaptive policies diverge logical results | Fatal | FG-INV-19 separately pins answer-affecting choices in the bound/replay closure and logical-command-sequences canonical-state-affecting policy epochs; answer-preserving physical classification has equivalence tests and replica logical-digest oracles. Physical encodings need not be identical. |
| Statistical guarantees rest on modeling assumptions | Unavoidable | Every claim names assumptions and scope; monitoring can trigger fallback but does not retroactively restore invalid coverage. Safety remains independent of statistical success. |
| In-house cryptography fails despite vectors | High-impact specialized risk | Prefer audited foundation primitives; constant-time/misuse verification, algorithm agility, independent review, and external release audit are mandatory. |
| Planner-only authorization leaks through another path | Unacceptable | `fgdb-secure-view` is the unforgeable access boundary for storage, indexes, Prism, Ripple, UDFs, backup, errors, and observability; cross-capability differential matrices gate releases. |
| Global meta sequencing preserves semantics but may bottleneck post-1.0 sharding | Deliberate correctness/performance tradeoff | The protocol is fixed in §14.6: no shard-local semantic bypass, exact global certification and one-prefix visibility. Batch/pipeline the meta order and publish the ceiling honestly; reopen scalar time only as a new architecture with new Chronicle/branch/Ripple/replay proofs, never as an optimization. |
| Newer runtime surfaces adopted for Aegis (choreographic codegen, coded fan-out) prove less mature than core asupersync | Adoption risk, inherited not created | Each adoption sits behind a protocol trait with the hand-built degenerate mode preserved (static membership, unicast fan-out, hand-written state machines); the lab's dual-run harness compares adopted vs. degenerate paths before any promotion |

---

## Appendix A — On-Disk Object Formats (normative contract)

`RoleTransitionActivationState` is the closed role union `Meta{migration_nonce,transition_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRoleTransitionRef>,continuity_reservation_receipt_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionContinuityReservationReceipt>,target_service_visibility_epoch,phase:ProjectionPreparedHidden{activation_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef}|ServicePrepareApplied{prepare_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef}|FinalizedPendingIndependentReopen{finalize_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef,seal_state:Unsealed|Sealed{seal_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionPromotionRootSeal<Meta>>}}|MetaReopenedAwaitingShardAcks{reopen_confirm_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef,seal_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionPromotionRootSeal<Meta>>,independent_reopen_proof_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionIndependentReopenProof<Meta>>}|Complete{completion_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef,completion_audit_mirror_identity,seal_release_state}}|Shard{migration_nonce,transition_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRoleTransitionRef>,shard_id,continuity_reservation_receipt_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionContinuityReservationReceipt>,target_service_visibility_epoch,phase:ProjectionPreparedHidden{install_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef}|OpenedPendingIndependentReopen{open_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef,seal_state:Unsealed|Sealed{seal_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionPromotionRootSeal<Shard>>}}|ShardOperationalAwaitingMetaCompletion{reopen_confirm_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef,seal_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionPromotionRootSeal<Shard>>,independent_reopen_proof_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionIndependentReopenProof<Shard>>}|Complete{completion_apply_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef,seal_release_state}}`. This exact schema supersedes any earlier compact navigation rendering. The state object, reached by the payload's existing strong field, is the canonical owner of role-transition seals/proofs; `None` is legal only outside a role transition. Generated phase/bootstrap/admission rows require `RoleTransitionPreparedHidden` through prepare, `OperationalPendingIndependentReopen` through Unsealed/Sealed, `Operational` plus an awaiting phase after reopen, and ordinary service only in `Complete`.

All durable encodings use a declared format major/minor, little-endian fixed integers, canonical unsigned LEB128 only where the field says varint, length-before-allocation, checked arithmetic, and per-kind maximum sizes. Unknown additive-minor fields are length-delimited and skipped; unknown required flags fail closed. `CanonicalScalarProfile` defines float/decimal/string/time bytes. Readers authenticate/validate headers and resource bounds before allocating or decompressing.

**Reference semantics.** Every ObjectId-bearing edge declares a wire tag: `StrongRef{oid}` (always followed); `StrongMarkerRef{marker_ref}` and `StrongCommandRef{command_ref}` (retain the named history object); `ConditionalCoordinateRef{oid,graph,branch}` (sequence-neutral payload whose retention sequence comes from its enclosing committed marker); `ConditionalMarkerRef{marker_ref,axis:Global|Branch(graph,branch)}` and `ConditionalCommandRef{command_ref,axis:Logical}` (followed until an authenticated matching checkpoint/cut); `WeakMarkerIdentity{marker_oid,commit_seq}` (provenance/identity only); `WeakLocator`/`PhysicalRealizationRef` (nonretaining local lookup metadata); or `WeakDigest{digest}` (comparison only). Bare `MarkerRef{marker_oid:[u8;32],commit_seq:u64}` and `CommandRef{command_record_oid:[u8;32],logical_command_seq:u64}` are identities, **not reachability by themselves**; an enclosing tag supplies that. `StrongCommandRef` always means a previously constructed `LogicalCommandRecord`; an applied result cites its already identified input and assigned order only through the exact closed `AppliedControlRef`, `AppliedAbortRef`, or `AuthorityAppliedRef` tags below, never an ambient/local-only assumption.

`ConsensusDomain {database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,group_role:Local|Meta|Shard{shard_id},group_id}` is the indivisible authority/consumer identity in every signed, MACed, indexed, or retained cross-group transcript. `group_id` is also a random 256-bit database-global unique identifier, but no validator relies on uniqueness without matching the complete domain. Later shorthand `authority_group_id`, `consumer_group_id`, or `group_id` in a cross-group schema means the corresponding full `ConsensusDomain`; wire encoders never serialize the scalar alone. `RemoteObjectIdentity {authority_domain:ConsensusDomain,object_oid,object_kind,canonical_digest}` is comparison-only and never a local reachability edge.

`RootAuthorityTrustBody` is the signature-free immutable `{authority_domain:ConsensusDomain,artifact_kind:FreshShardedGenesis|CertifiedLocalRoleTransition,canonical_genesis_or_transition_bytes,target_configuration_oid,target_configuration_canonical_digest,externally_pinned_root_policy_id,expected_root_verification_key_set_digest,threshold,source_identity_or_transition_continuity_commitment,body_digest:BodyDigest<RootAuthorityTrustBody>}`; its registered body transcript includes every preceding field and excludes exactly `body_digest`. `RootAuthorityTrustArtifact` is `{body_ref:StrongRef<RootAuthorityTrustBody>,body_digest:BodyDigest<RootAuthorityTrustBody>,canonical_root_authority_signature_set,signed_transcript_digest:TranscriptDigest<RootAuthorityTrustArtifact>}`. Each root signature signs the domain-separated tuple `{schema/tag,authority_domain,artifact_kind,body_digest,externally_pinned_root_policy_id}`; the artifact transcript includes the body digest and canonically sorted signatures and excludes exactly `signed_transcript_digest`. Validation first resolves the deployment's externally pinned policy, key set, and threshold and byte-matches their IDs/digest to the body, then verifies signatures and transcript; keys merely embedded in the object can never select their own trust root. The canonical genesis/transition bytes and policy evidence remain strongly retained and independently reverified. `RemoteAuthorityConfigurationEvidence` is the nonrecursive imported leaf `{authority_domain:ConsensusDomain,configuration_oid,configuration_canonical_digest,canonical_configuration_bytes,configuration_adoption_raft_index,adoption_log_prefix_digest,member_verification_key_set,payload_predicate_digest,trust_transition:Genesis{root_authority_trust_artifact_ref:StrongRef<RootAuthorityTrustArtifact>}|Successor{predecessor_evidence_ref:StrongRef<RemoteAuthorityConfigurationEvidence>,joint_transition_transcript,old_configuration_quorum_signatures,new_configuration_quorum_signatures,final_retirement_floor_digest}|ValidatedCheckpointSuccessor{predecessor_anchor_ref:StrongRef<ValidatedRemoteConfigurationAnchor>,joint_transition_transcript,old_configuration_quorum_signatures,new_configuration_quorum_signatures,final_retirement_floor_digest},minimum_configuration_retention_floor,signer_epoch,configuration_quorum_signatures}`. Current-member signatures alone are never a trust root. Embedded canonical configuration bytes recompute the OID/digest and self-bind the complete domain; the transition proves adoption from an already trusted root artifact, predecessor, or anchor. `RemoteConfigurationRef` means a consumer-local `StrongRef<RemoteAuthorityConfigurationEvidence>`.

Authority-local certificate object `T` and its imported representation are deliberately different schemas. `ExportLeaf<T> {domain:ImportedCertificateDomain,target_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,export_projection_version,object_specific_scalar_projection,local_strong_ref_projection[RemoteObjectIdentity],target_closure_inventory_digest,authority_ledger_floor,quorum_signatures}` replaces every authority-local strong reference with a typed remote identity/closure commitment while preserving every verifier-relevant scalar. Its generated projector is injectively bound to the canonical digest of `T`; a consumer never decodes an authority-local `StrongRef` as local. `RemotePayloadAvailabilityEvidence` is the consumer-local leaf `{authority_configuration_evidence_ref:RemoteConfigurationRef,certificate_export_leaf_ref:StrongRef<ExportLeaf<PayloadAvailabilityCertificate>>,target_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,target_closure_inventory_digest,payload_predicate_digest,receipt_set_commitment,encoding_placement_coverage,failure_domains,authority_retention_floor,signer_epoch,authority_quorum_signatures}`; the authority ledger separately roots the real certificate/receipts.

W12's one cross-consensus edge is `CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<T> {authority_domain:ConsensusDomain,authority_configuration_evidence_ref:RemoteConfigurationRef,consumer_domain:ConsensusDomain,target_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,export_leaf_ref:StrongRef<ExportLeaf<T>>,target_closure_inventory_digest,payload_availability_evidence_ref:StrongRef<RemotePayloadAvailabilityEvidence>,retention_grant_evidence_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantEvidence>}`. Every `StrongRef` inside it targets a complete consumer-local leaf; none targets `T` in the authority group. The generated `T -> ExportLeaf<T>` verifier and field-level schema registry define exactly which refs become remote identities. `grant_id = H("fgdb:remote-grant:v1", authority_domain, consumer_domain, target_identity, grant_nonce)`; consumer and authority maps are keyed by `(authority_domain,grant_id)`, and any collision with nonidentical bytes fails closed. `RemoteRetentionGrantSpec` is authority-group input `{grant_id,authority_domain:ConsensusDomain,authority_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,consumer_domain:ConsensusDomain,target_ref:StrongRef,target_kind,target_canonical_digest,target_closure_inventory_digest,payload_availability_certificate_ref:StrongRef<PayloadAvailabilityCertificate>,minimum_authority_checkpoint_floor,grant_nonce}`. Authority apply creates `RemoteRetentionGrantRecord {spec_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantSpec>,authority_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef,state:Active}` in `RemoteRetentionObligationRoot`, which roots the exact target closure. Its quorum exports `RemoteRetentionGrantEvidence {authority_configuration_evidence_ref:RemoteConfigurationRef,grant_record_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,grant_id,consumer_domain:ConsensusDomain,target_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,target_closure_inventory_digest,payload_availability_evidence_ref:StrongRef<RemotePayloadAvailabilityEvidence>,authority_order_index,minimum_authority_checkpoint_floor,grant_nonce,signer_epoch,authority_quorum_signatures}`. The consumer may publish the wrapper only after authenticating all leaves and byte-matching both complete domains; the authority ledger, not the evidence, owns the remote target.

Release is an explicit six-transition handshake, never inferred from time or a missing client. (1) After canonically removing/replacing every reference while retaining the grant leaf, the consumer orders `RemoteRetentionReleaseRequestSpec {grant_evidence_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantEvidence>,consumer_release_state_identity:WeakDigest,complete_consumer_root_digest,consumer_checkpoint_floor,successor_grant_evidence_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantEvidence>?,release_nonce}`; apply rechecks the complete consumer root, constructs `RemoteRetentionReleaseRequestRecord {spec_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionReleaseRequestSpec>,consumer_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef,consumer_no_reference_floor_digest}`, and installs `ReleaseRequested`. That type state cannot acquire or create another local ref under the old grant; any concurrent/new use must first acquire and publish a distinct successor grant. (2) Only afterward does the consumer quorum create authority-local `RemoteRetentionReleaseRequestCertificate {SameGroupCertificateHeader,request_record_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionReleaseRequestRecord>,complete_consumer_root_digest,consumer_no_reference_floor_digest,successor_grant_identity?,release_nonce,one_digest_signer_lock_ref,quorum_signatures}` after rechecking the root. A generated specialized `ExportLeaf<RemoteRetentionReleaseRequestCertificate>` replaces its local refs with remote identities; the later consumer publish control installs this portable leaf as `ReleaseCertified`. (3) The authority imports that leaf and orders `RemoteRetentionReleaseApplySpec {active_grant_record_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantRecord>,release_request_leaf_ref:StrongRef<ExportLeaf<RemoteRetentionReleaseRequestCertificate>>,expected_active_grant_digest,verified_consumer_no_reference_floor,successor_transfer_proof?}`. Apply rechecks every stronger authority root, removes the active grant, and creates `RemoteRetentionReleaseTombstone {grant_record_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,grant_spec_digest:WeakDigest,target_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,request_certificate_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,release_nonce,authority_command_input_digest:WeakDigest,authority_order_index}` with no strong edge to the active record, spec, target, or apply command. The release command/log retains those inputs only until its verified cut. (4) Only after that applied root does the authority quorum create local `RemoteRetentionReleaseAckCertificate {SameGroupCertificateHeader,tombstone_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionReleaseTombstone>,grant_id,consumer_domain:ConsensusDomain,target_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,release_nonce,authority_order_index,authority_state_root_digest,one_digest_signer_lock_ref,quorum_signatures}` and its specialized portable ExportLeaf. (5) A later authority publish control atomically creates `RemoteRetentionAckPublishRecord {ack_certificate_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionReleaseAckCertificate>,ack_leaf_ref:StrongRef<ExportLeaf<RemoteRetentionReleaseAckCertificate>>,authority_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef,summary_key}` and installs `RemoteReleaseSummaryEntry {authority_domain,consumer_domain,grant_id,target_identity,release_nonce,ack_leaf_identity,ack_digest,authority_order_index,published_at_order_index,permanent_release_proof_floor}` in `RemoteReleaseSummaryRoot`. The summary and nonrecursive archive-backed ack leaf remain available through the database's capability-safe permanent release-proof floor and require no new releasable grant merely to prove the old grant released. (6) The consumer imports the portable leaf without a CRSR, rechecks that its current complete root still contains no old-grant ref, orders `ConsumeReleaseAck`, and creates `RemoteRetentionConsumeAckRecord {ack_leaf_ref:StrongRef<ExportLeaf<RemoteRetentionReleaseAckCertificate>>,consumer_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef,current_no_old_grant_ref_proof_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionNoOldGrantProof>,summary_key}`; only then may it retire request/grant evidence after its checkpoint floor. `AuthorityAppliedRef = Local{command_ref:StrongRef<ControlCommand>,logical_command_seq}|Meta{command_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlCommand>,global_logical_command_seq}|Shard{command_ref:StrongRef<ShardControlCommand>,shard_raft_index}` is used only inside its owning group and prevents role ambiguity. A crash at any point leaves an authority target root, permanent release proof, or replayable pending transition; no imported leaf contains an ordinary strong edge into its source group.

W12 history wrappers are distinct rather than overloading the local `LogicalCommandRecord` tag: `StrongGlobalCommandRef{record_oid,global_logical_command_seq}`, `ConditionalGlobalCommandRef{record_oid,global_logical_command_seq,axis=GlobalLogical}`, and `WeakGlobalCommandIdentity{record_oid,global_logical_command_seq}` target `GlobalTxnRecord|GlobalControlRecord`; `ConditionalGlobalTxnInputRef{command_oid,assigned_global_logical_command_seq,axis=GlobalLogical}` targets the already-built `GlobalTxnCommand` and is valid only when the record at that sequence names the same input; `StrongShardCommandRef{record_oid,shard_id,shard_raft_index}`, `ConditionalShardCommandRef{record_oid,shard_id,shard_raft_index,axis=ShardRaft}`, and `WeakShardCommandIdentity{record_oid,shard_id,shard_raft_index}` target `ShardCommandRecord`. Strong variants retain, conditional variants stop only at a verified matching meta/shard checkpoint cut, and weak variants compare only. Cross-group carriage of any target still requires `CertifiedRemoteStrongRef`; these wrappers are only within the owning consensus group.

Canonical result objects that can be produced in either posture use closed role tags rather than pretending every input is local: `AppliedControlRef = Local{command_ref:StrongRef<ControlCommand>,logical_command_seq} | Meta{command_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlCommand>,global_logical_command_seq}`; `AppliedAbortRef = LocalControl{command_ref:StrongRef<ControlCommand>,logical_command_seq} | MetaControl{command_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlCommand>,global_logical_command_seq} | MetaTxn{command_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnCommand>,global_logical_command_seq}`; and `AuditCandidateRef = Local{blocked_after_logical_command_seq,candidate_state_root_ref:StrongRef<LogicalStateRoot>} | Meta{blocked_after_global_logical_command_seq,candidate_state_root_ref:StrongRef<GlobalStateRoot>}`. The group-role validator accepts only the matching tag. These tags are part of the v1 durable schema and the generated spec/result compatibility matrix; no decoder infers posture from ambient configuration.

Key-envelope openers use the separate retaining physical edge `StrongCiphertextRef { logical_oid, ciphertext_id, dek_id, ciphertext_digest, protected_length, key_opener_ref:StrongRef, recoverability_profile, selected_realizations[{encoding_id,placement_id,failure_domain_set}],payload_availability_certificate_ref:StrongRef }`. Its target ciphertext, complete authenticated realization inventory, and certificate exist before the referring envelope object, and the certificate must prove that the selected set satisfies the named profile under the exact configuration. It pins that `CiphertextId` and the selected recoverable `EncodingId`/`PlacementId` set; recoding or movement first creates a successor envelope/grant edge with a newly certified set before the old set can retire, while re-encryption cannot substitute a new ciphertext under a live reference. This is intentionally stronger than ordinary logical reachability and is included in GC, reconfiguration, backup, and key-destruction floors.

The schemas below use a flattened prose rendering, but **names and suffixes never imply reference strength**. Every field's exact type, cardinality, identity class, target, role/posture predicate, retention/cut behavior, and `PriorObject` construction annotation come from §5.1's generated `durable_fields.toml`; the rendering checker rejects any brace field that lacks or disagrees with its row. A compact phrase such as “typed mandatory inventory” is a named closed sub-schema, never an open bag or slash-separated set of ambient refs. Bootstrap-slot root identity is an external GC root and is followed as strong. Pending/prepared traversal treats a registered `ConditionalCoordinateRef` as strong because no committed-marker cut context exists. Archive and prior-incarnation identities are separate nonlocal classes and can never enter the current local ObjectId mark set. Every concrete target of a strong or currently followed conditional edge must exist before the parent encoder runs. Recursive persistent nodes are legal only in that child-before-parent direction. Generated schema/reference/DAG checkers compare the field table, Appendix rendering, Rust encoders, and registry rows; they reject unresolved, untyped, role-invalid, self, mutual, or future-result cycles and fail G0 on drift. Unknown tags or context fail closed.

**RootSlot + RootBootstrap.** Each slot is exactly 4096 bytes at offsets 0 and 4096:

```text
RootSlot {
  magic="FGRT", format_major:u16, format_minor:u16, slot_generation:u64,
  local_writer_fence_epoch:u64, database_id:[u8;16],
  database_security_namespace_id:[u8;32], cluster_incarnation:u64,
  incarnation_continuity_profile_id:u16,
  cluster_incarnation_continuity_digest:[u8;32], continuity_cas_version:u64,
  service_visibility_epoch:u64,
  root_manifest_oid:[u8;32],
  bootstrap: RootBootstrap, reserved_zeroes, tear_checksum:[u8;32]
}
RootBootstrap {
  root_encoding_id:[u8;32], root_placement_id:[u8;32],
  root_placement_epoch:u64, failure_domain_policy_id:[u8;32],
  root_failure_domain_id:[u8;32], segment_id:[u8;16], offset:u64,
  encoded_len:u64, root_symbol_inventory_digest:[u8;32],
  object_kind:u16, canonical_plaintext_len:u64, codec_profile:u32,
  compressed_len:u64, data_crypto_profile:u32, dek_id:[u8;32],
  nonce_len:u8, nonce_or_siv:[u8;32], object_tag_len:u8,
  fec_profile:u32, transfer_length:u64, oti_common:u64, oti_scheme:u32,
  symbol_size:u32, source_block_count:u32, symbol_auth_profile:u16,
  ciphertext_id:[u8;32], ciphertext_digest:[u8;32], opener_kind:u16,
  oid_key_id:[u8;32], opener_payload_len:u16, opener_payload:[u8;1024],
  opener_digest:[u8;32]
}
```

Unused nonce/opener bytes are zero. Profile registries fix bounds and tag lengths. Together with `root_manifest_oid`, these fields reproduce the root's exact `CipherDescriptorWithoutDigest`, complete `EncodingDescriptorWithoutId`, and specialized `PlacementDescriptorWithoutId { encoding_id, root_placement_epoch, failure_domain_policy_id, ContiguousSpan { root_failure_domain_id, segment_id, offset, encoded_len, root_symbol_inventory_digest } }` byte-for-byte. Recovery scans the declared span, authenticates canonical SymbolRecords, verifies the sorted inventory commitment, and recomputes `root_placement_id` before decode. `opener_payload` is a versioned bundle of inline wraps or authenticated KMS/HSM locators sufficient to recover both the named root DEK and immutable `K_oid` without consulting the object index; its digest covers kind, key IDs, locators/wraps, and namespace/incarnation. The authenticated root repeats the exact database/security-namespace/incarnation tuple, and recovery rejects disagreement before following its closure. A structurally valid highest-generation slot is never silently rolled back after authentication/closure failure (§5.1).

**Filesystem durability and writer takeover.** `FilesystemDurabilityProfile` is a signed/checked-in artifact `{ profile_id, profile_version, os/kernel_range, allowed_filesystems_and_mount_predicates, forbidden_layers/options, required_lock_primitive, owner_death_rule, stable_inode_rule, slot_write_rule, file_sync_rule, directory_sync_rule, rename_no_replace_rule, cache_flush_assumption, probe_suite_oid }`. `FGFS-LINUX-LOCAL-V1` has exactly §5.1's ext4/XFS allowlist; a profile/mount not matching every predicate is not writable. A local `FilesystemInstanceRecord { profile_id, probe_suite_oid, mount_id, filesystem_type, canonical_mount_options, device_chain_digest, directory_device_inode, manifest_device_inode, checked_at, result_digest }` is diagnostic evidence, never a transferable proof or semantic root.

The takeover checker accepts only `NoGuard -> LeaseHeld(identity) -> ClosureRecovered(old_epoch) -> PendingFenceGuard(old_epoch+1) -> FenceRootDurableAndReread(old_epoch+1) -> WriterEnabled(FenceToken)`. Creation is `NoGuard -> StagingInodeLease -> PendingCreationGuard(epoch=1) -> CompleteStagingRootVerified -> RenameNoReplaceAndDirectorySync -> CanonicalRootReread -> WriterEnabled`. `PendingFenceGuard` is linear and can encode/seal exactly one fence-only `RootManifest` preserving the recovered state plus its inactive `RootSlot`; `PendingCreationGuard` can encode/seal only the registered Genesis closure and epoch-1 slot. Neither type implements user-segment, prepared-owner, receipt, Raft, canonical-transition, or general-root traits. `FenceToken` is nonserializable and nonconstructible outside the VFS/commit boundary; it binds the live lease handle, stable directory/root identity, profile, slot generation, and epoch. The fence-only root/slot must retain the exact prior canonical logical root, Raft/audit candidate, prepared root, and durable/applied/visible positions. Every immutable segment trailer records `{ database_security_namespace_id, cluster_incarnation, local_writer_fence_epoch, segment_id, sealed_len, inventory_digest, trailer_checksum }`; after promotion the local VFS refuses a seal, prepared-root update, receipt signature, Raft append acknowledgement/proposal, or root publication without the matching live token. Already receipted/ordered records from an older epoch remain strong obligations but cannot authorize new old-epoch publication. The crash matrix cuts after every lease/identity/recovery/object-sync/slot-write/slot-sync/staging-rename/directory-sync/reread step and includes owner death, path replacement, mount drift, stale descriptors, epoch overflow, competing creators, orphan staging, and a lying-sync profile that must be rejected.

**Cipher/encoding/placement records and SymbolRecord.** `CipherDescriptorWithoutDigest` is `{ logical_oid, object_kind, canonical_plaintext_len, codec_profile, compressed_len, data_crypto_profile, dek_id, object_nonce_or_siv, object_tag_len }`. Object AAD is the domain string plus logical OID and this canonical descriptor. `CiphertextRecord` is `{ descriptor, ciphertext_id, ciphertext_digest, object_tag_digest, protected_length }`; `CiphertextId` hashes descriptor+ciphertext+object tag. Immutable `EncodingDescriptorWithoutId` is `{ ciphertext_id, fec_profile, transfer_length, oti_common, oti_scheme, symbol_size, source_block_count, symbol_auth_profile }`, and `EncodingId` hashes the domain/version plus its **complete canonical bytes**. Separately, `PlacementDescriptorWithoutId` is `{ encoding_id, placement_epoch, failure_domain_policy, location_form }`, where `location_form = ContiguousSpan{failure_domain_id,segment_id,offset,encoded_len,symbol_inventory_digest} | Explicit{sorted_symbol_inventory_and_locators,failure_domains}`. `PlacementId` hashes the placement domain/version plus exactly that descriptor; immutable `PlacementRecord { placement_id, descriptor }` merely stores and cross-checks it. Moving/adding symbols creates a new placement record without changing encoding identity. KEK/wrap epoch is absent from both ciphertext and encoding identity. The authenticated local physical-realization index maps `CiphertextId`, `EncodingId`, and `PlacementId` to these records with nonretaining locators. An ordinary decoder obtains the complete descriptor/OTI/auth profile from an authenticated `EncodingDescriptorWithoutId` (or FGP's authenticated encoding prelude) before accepting any symbol; a bare `SymbolRecord` is never self-authorizing.

```text
SymbolRecord {
  magic="FGEC", format_version:u16, header_len:u16, record_len:u32,
  logical_oid:[u8;32], ciphertext_id:[u8;32], encoding_id:[u8;32],
  object_kind:u16, source_block:u32, esi:u32, symbol_len:u32,
  transfer_length:u64, oti_common:u64, oti_scheme:u32, flags:u32,
  symbol_mac_profile:u16, symbol_mac_len:u16,
  payload:[u8;symbol_len], symbol_mac:[u8;symbol_mac_len]
}
```

The symbol MAC key/transcript are exactly §5.1's domain-separated construction. All framing/OTI/length fields and payload are MACed. Truncated/noncanonical tails are ignored only in proved-unreferenced staging; a reachable sealed tail triggers authenticated repair or fail-closed recovery.

**LogicalStatePayload / LogicalStateRoot.** `LogicalStatePayload` is `{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,bootstrap_phase:Genesis|CheckpointInstalled|Operational|RecoveryReconciling|RecoveryAbandoned|OperationalPendingIndependentReopen,applied_logical_command_seq,applied_commit_seq,global_transaction_marker_head:StrongMarkerRef?,branch_head_map_root(entries carry StrongMarkerRef),branch_manifest_root,branch_key_epoch_registry_root,key_envelope/grant_registry_root,branch_merge_ledger_root,graph_partition_state_roots,catalog_root,schema_roots,id_allocator_root,identity_continuity_record_ref,constraint_state_roots,resource_ledger_root,privacy_ledger_root,privacy_continuity_record_ref,dp_request_index_root,txn_outcome_index_root:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeIndex>,local_begin_idempotency_index_root:StrongRef<LocalBeginIdempotencyIndex>,local_statement_index_root:StrongRef<LocalStatementIndex>,local_result_delivery_index_root:StrongRef<LocalResultDeliveryIndex>,local_txn_outcome_summary_root:StrongRef<LocalTxnOutcomeSummaryRoot>,local_delta_batch_index_root:StrongRef<LocalDeltaBatchIndex>,local_delta_frontier,terminal_certification_reservation_root:StrongRef<TerminalCertificationReservationRoot<Local>>,recovery_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<RecoveryCheckpoint>?,retained_stream_floor,retention_map_root:StrongRef<RetentionMap>,derived_generation_registry_root:StrongRef<DerivedGenerationRegistry>,delivery_lease_registry_root,replay_registry_root,logical_hlc_state,topology_epoch,policy_epoch,revocation_index,replicated_key_wrap/signing/capability-verifier roots,audit_ticket_index_root,audit_root,audit_continuity_record_ref,transparency_root,backup_registry_root,restore_state_ref:StrongRef<RestoreState>?,restore_promotion_root_seal_ref:StrongRef<RestorePromotionRootSeal<Local>>?,gc_decision_root,remote_retention_authority_root:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionObligationRoot>,remote_retention_consumer_root:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionConsumerRoot>,remote_configuration_trust_root:StrongRef<RemoteConfigurationTrustRoot>,sharding_migration_state_ref:StrongRef<ShardingMigrationState>?,config_payload_floor_ref:StrongRef<ConfigPayloadFloor>?}`. The exact bounded `LocalDeltaBatchIndex` and cut lifecycle are defined with `LogicalDeltaBatch` below; genesis is empty/frontier zero, transaction apply inserts exactly the next commit sequence, and only its role-specific activated cut removes a prefix. `ShardingMigrationState` is `FreezePendingAudit{freeze_ref:StrongRef<ShardingFreezeRecord>}|FrozenVisible{freeze_ref,mirror_applied_ref:AppliedControlRef}|RoleTransitionLocked{begin_ref:StrongRef<BeginRoleTransitionRecord>}|Resolved{terminal_identity}`; no variant names a future command record. Remote roots are empty reserved values before W12 preparation. Fresh bootstrap permits Genesis -> CheckpointInstalled -> Operational. RecoveryReconciling is restore-only and requires the matching `RestoreState`; reconciliation and `LocalRestoreActivationSpec` advance only to hidden `VisibilityCommitted`. The exact `LocalRestoreServicePromotionSpec`, after continuity CAS, current visibility-epoch validation, and required catalog-promotion inputs, selects `OperationalPendingIndependentReopen::Unsealed` and clears `restore_state_ref`; the separate seal-install command selects the Sealed substate, it does not yet admit ordinary work or non-reopen root mutation. Only `LocalRestoreServiceCompletionSpec` with a proof over that pinned seal selects Operational and schedules seal/pin release with source-lease finalization. `LocalRestoreAbandonFinalizeSpec` alone clears the state into `RecoveryAbandoned`, which has no restore-state ref and a registry `AwaitingSourceRelease::Abandoned`; only source-lease renewal/release/finalize and registered tombstone compaction are legal there under `RecoveryCommitCx`. No ordinary work occurs outside Operational, and no request is admitted without the matching service-visibility epoch and receipt. `LogicalStateRoot` is `{payload_ref:StrongRef<LogicalStatePayload>,logical_command_head:StrongCommandRef?}`; fresh genesis alone has no head.

The generated common header of every Local/Meta/Shard payload also contains `{incarnation_continuity_profile_id,cluster_incarnation_continuity_record_ref:StrongRef<ClusterIncarnationContinuityRecord>?,cluster_incarnation_continuity_digest,continuity_cas_version,service_visibility_epoch,time_authority_binding:LocalOrMeta{registry_ref:StrongRef<TimeAuthorityRegistry>}|Shard{active_projection_ref:StrongRef<ActiveMetaProjectionRoot>},restore_registry_root:StrongRef<RestoreRegistry>,terminal_audit_freeze_index_root:StrongRef<AuditTerminalFreezeIndex>}`. `DirectoryBound` uses no external record ref and a fixed local continuity digest; `ExternalCas` requires `Some` and exact byte equality with the live authority. `restore_state_ref` is present only during a live restore, while `restore_registry_root` retains terminal projection/promotion/tombstone evidence. The audit-freeze index is active only in Local/Meta and is the canonical empty reserved value in Shard. Shards may validate only the exact active/accepted time-authority projection certified in their active Meta projection; they cannot originate profile changes. RootManifest and RootSlot repeat and cross-check the same continuity/profile/digest/version/visibility tuple.

**Local 1.0 durable transaction formats.** Local and W12 deliberately share only embedded value schemas (`TxnCompletionState`, posture-tagged `SemanticTerminalDescriptor`, and `TerminalPublicOutcome`) plus public protocol semantics. They do not share durable registration, workspace, statement, result-owner, outcome, audit-owner, claim, or command objects. A Local decoder rejects every `Global*`, Meta, shard, certified-remote, or global-prefix identity in this family, and a W12 decoder rejects every Local identity. `LocalAuditTicketOwner` is `Operation{txn_token,registration_binding_digest}|Statement{registration_ref:StrongRef<LocalAttemptRegistration>,statement_seq,statement_idempotency_key}|Control{control_operation_tag,request_idempotency_key,request_basis_commitment}`. `LocalAuditTicketClaimRecord` is `{ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,owner:LocalAuditTicketOwner,claiming_control_ref:StrongRef<ControlCommand>,claim_applied_ref:AppliedControlRef,request_basis_commitment}` and is constructed during the registration/claim apply before its owning Local record. `LocalOperationAuditAdmission` is `NotRequired{evidence:NonRequiredAuditEvidence}|PendingUnclaimed{ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,ticket_admission_record_ref:StrongCommandRef,operation_request_basis_commitment}|Claimed{ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,claim_record_ref:StrongRef<LocalAuditTicketClaimRecord>,owner:LocalAuditTicketOwner::Operation,operation_request_basis_commitment}`. `LocalStatementAuditAdmission` has the analogous NotRequired/PendingUnclaimed/Claimed forms with `LocalAuditTicketOwner::Statement`; protected Local controls use the Control arm through their exact audit admission. No Local field can encode a global transaction ID, registration generation, GlobalControlRecord, or GlobalControlCommand.

The generated Local payload schema corrects the compact navigation list above by requiring `local_conflict_index_ref:StrongRef<LocalConflictIndex>` immediately after the statement/outcome roots. Genesis installs the canonical empty index. Its checkpoint vector, `ConfigPayloadFloor`, mandatory inventory, backup closure, restore transform/reconciliation, GC root inventory, key-destruction scan, and role-transition projection each have a generated required row; omission disables SERIALIZABLE operation and is a G0 failure, not a recoverable cache miss.

`LocalConflictAttemptKey` is `{txn_token_digest,registration_identity}`. `LocalConflictEdge` is `{kind:wr|ww|rw,from:LocalConflictAttemptKey,to:LocalConflictAttemptKey,coordinate_or_predicate_domain,proof_ref:LocalConflictProofRef,first_observed_statement_seq,edge_digest}` where `LocalConflictProofRef` is a generated closed union over version, absence/range, path, constraint, and final-write proof objects. `LocalConflictEntry` is `{registration_ref:StrongRef<LocalAttemptRegistration>,registered_snapshot,start_logical_command_seq,terminal_logical_command_seq?,state:Active|PrepareAdmitted{admission_generation}|Committed|Aborted|ReadClosed,statement_frontier,workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<LocalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>,cumulative_read_witness_root_ref:StrongRef<LocalCumulativeReadWitnessRoot>,cumulative_write_summary_ref:StrongRef<LocalWriteSummary>?,incoming_edges[LocalConflictEdge],outgoing_edges[LocalConflictEdge],overlap_interval:{start_prefix,closed_prefix?},detail_state:Detailed|Compacted{summary_ref:StrongRef<LocalConflictSummaryLeaf>}}`. Arrays/maps use canonical key/digest order and exact deduplication; an edge must appear byte-identically in both endpoint projections.

`LocalConflictIndex` is `{generation,basis_logical_command_seq,entries[LocalConflictAttemptKey->LocalConflictEntry],safe_snapshot_frontier,overlap_close_floor_ref:StrongRef<LocalConflictOverlapFloor>,root_digest:BodyDigest<LocalConflictIndex>}`. `LocalConflictIndexBasis` is the nonretaining typed `{basis_state:WeakStateIdentity,index_generation,index_root_digest,basis_logical_command_seq,safe_snapshot_frontier,overlap_close_floor_digest}` used by serialization/final-certification inputs; a bare `WeakStateIdentity` is insufficient. Registration atomically inserts Active with workspace zero. Every successful statement publication atomically replaces that exact entry with its successor statement/workspace/witness/write summary and all newly proved bidirectional edges. Prepare admission replays `may_affect` in both directions against every overlapping entry, reruns the registered SCC algorithm, and atomically selects PrepareAdmitted; commit, admitted abort, active cancel, or read close installs the terminal prefix and state in the same command as outcome/attempt changes. Terminal completion changes no serialization decision but retains the entry through its postcondition lifetime.
