`LocalConflictOverlapFloor` is `{closed_through_start_prefix,safe_snapshot_frontier,oldest_live_overlapping_start,retained_detailed_attempt_key_commitment,retained_edge_proof_commitment,checker_version}`. `LocalConflictCompactionSpec {expected_index_basis:LocalConflictIndexBasis,sorted_selected_terminal_keys,sorted_summary_leaf_refs[StrongRef<LocalConflictSummaryLeaf>],no_future_overlap_edge_proof_ref:StrongRef<LocalNoFutureConflictEdgeProof>,expected_oldest_live_overlapping_start,expected_attempt_outcome_statement_workspace_retention_discharge,terminal_audit_gate}` may replace detail only when every possible future transaction has a start/snapshot beyond the selected entry's closed overlap interval and no live witness can add an edge; it never deletes the authenticated summary or changes public outcomes. Every follower reconstructs `may_affect`, verifies symmetric edges/proofs and workspace transport, and reruns SCC before signing `LocalSerializationCertificate`, whose `snapshot_and_conflict_index_basis` field is exactly `LocalConflictIndexBasis`. Missing/stale/asymmetric evidence, unsupported exact witness semantics, or resource exhaustion conservatively aborts/waits. Write-skew, multi-edge rw cycles, same-I/O-batch writers, read-only dangerous structures, statement-workspace transport, restart, checkpoint, compaction, and detail-retirement races are permanent oracle/model tests.

`LocalBeginIdempotencyIndex` maps `(database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,tenant,principal,scoped_begin_idempotency_key)` to exactly `Reserved{reservation_ref:StrongRef<LocalBeginReservationRecord>,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>}|BoundDetailed{registration_ref:StrongRef<LocalAttemptRegistration>,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>}|BoundCompacted{summary_root_ref:StrongRef<LocalTxnOutcomeSummaryRoot>,leaf_key_digest,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>}|NeverRegisteredDetailed{terminal_ref:StrongRef<LocalNeverRegisteredRecord>,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>}|NeverRegisteredCompacted{summary_root_ref:StrongRef<LocalTxnOutcomeSummaryRoot>,leaf_key_digest,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>}|ExpiredTombstone{scoped_key_digest,txn_token_digest,capability_commitment,expiry_evidence_digest}`. `LocalBeginReservationSpec` is `{canonical_begin_request_digest,tenant,principal,authority_ceiling_digest,operation_class:ReadOnly|ReadWrite,isolation_profile,transaction_error_policy,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,service_visibility_epoch,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>,scoped_begin_idempotency_key,expected_index_absence:WeakAbsenceProof,staging_resource_reservation_ref:StrongRef<ResourceLedgerTransition>,operation_audit_admission:LocalOperationAuditAdmission::PendingUnclaimed|NotRequired,terminal_audit_gate:LifecycleScaffoldingNotRequired}`. Apply constructs `LocalBeginReservationRecord {source_spec_ref:StrongRef<LocalBeginReservationSpec>,applied_control_ref:AppliedControlRef,canonical_begin_request_digest,txn_token,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>,capability_commitment,reserved_at_logical_command_seq,staging_generation}`, installs Reserved with the replay ref, and constructs `TxnOutcomeRecord::BeginStaging`; only that visible state permits BEGIN_ACCEPTED. Byte-identical retry returns the same identities. `LocalBeginTerminalSpec` alone consumes Reserved and creates `LocalNeverRegisteredRecord {reservation_ref,reason_class,no_registration_or_effect_proof_ref,terminal_audit_gate,applied_control_ref}` plus NeverRegisteredDetailed; a required ticket resolves directly from PendingUnclaimed with `AuditResolutionOrigin::Unclaimed`. Timeout, disconnect, or memory loss alone is not terminal evidence, and a terminal begin key can never later bind. The spec/record decode the replay object, require request_kind ExplicitBegin and exact request/domain/authority/profile/window equality, and derive txn_token/capability commitment from it; no duplicate inline capability encoding is trusted.

`LocalAttemptRegistrationSpec` has the closed binding `ExplicitBegin{reservation_ref:StrongRef<LocalBeginReservationRecord>,expected_index_value:Reserved,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>}|Autocommit{autocommit_idempotency_key,canonical_request_digest,expected_absence_proof:WeakAbsenceProof,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>}` plus `{authority_permit_ref:AuthorityPermitRef,requested_snapshot_bounds,operation_class,transaction_error_policy,initial_workspace_recipe,policy_epoch,revocation_index,operation_audit_admission:LocalOperationAuditAdmission::PendingUnclaimed|NotRequired,terminal_audit_gate:LifecycleScaffoldingNotRequired}`. Apply atomically claims the operation ticket when required, changes explicit Reserved -> BoundDetailed or creates the autocommit BoundDetailed lineage under the scoped client key, and constructs `LocalAttemptRegistration {source_spec_ref,applied_control_ref,reservation_ref?,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>,request_kind:ExplicitBegin|AutocommitExecute,txn_token,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,service_visibility_epoch,operation_class,registered_snapshot,tenant,principal,authority_ceiling_digest,authority_permit_ref,transaction_error_policy,operation_audit_admission:LocalOperationAuditAdmission::Claimed|NotRequired,policy_epoch,revocation_index,registered_at_logical_command_seq}` followed by workspace generation zero and the succeeding `TxnOutcomeRecord::Registered`. A Local token has exactly one attempt; there is no Local attempt-family generation. No statement/storage observation may precede visible registration, and autocommit differs only in its binding tag and absence of BEGIN frames. Both arms decode and byte-match the replay record; ExplicitBegin must match the reservation's same ref, while Autocommit requires request_kind AutocommitExecute and stores the scoped client key before work. Exact lost EXECUTE retry returns the same registration/outcome capability; body drift fails.

`LocalTxnWorkspaceGeneration` is `{registration_ref:StrongRef<LocalAttemptRegistration>,workspace_generation,predecessor_ref:StrongRef<LocalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>?,through_statement_seq,statement_registration_ref:StrongRef<LocalStatementRegistration>?,overlay_root_ref:StrongRef<LocalWorkspaceOverlayRoot>,cumulative_effect_root_ref:StrongRef<LocalCumulativeEffectRoot>,cumulative_read_witness_root_ref:StrongRef<LocalCumulativeReadWitnessRoot>,policy_epoch,revocation_index,branch_key_epoch_commitment}`. Generation zero contains the canonical empty overlay. `LocalStatementIndex` maps `(registration_identity,statement_seq)` and its scoped idempotency key to the same unique entry `Open{registration_ref:StrongRef<LocalStatementRegistration>}|Published{publication_applied_ref:AppliedControlRef,workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<LocalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>,output:LocalStatementPublishedOutput}|Failed{abort_applied_ref:AppliedControlRef,stable_failure_class}|Abandoned{abort_applied_ref:AppliedControlRef,typed_reason}`. `LocalStatementRegistrationSpec` binds `{registration_ref,exact_next_statement_seq,statement_idempotency_key,statement_class:ReadOnly|WriteReturning|WriteNoResult,canonical_statement_digest,parameter_digest,requested_result_answer_contract,expected_prior_statement_frontier,expected_workspace_generation_ref,transaction_error_policy,statement_audit_admission:LocalStatementAuditAdmission::PendingUnclaimed|NotRequired,terminal_audit_gate:LifecycleScaffoldingNotRequired}`. Apply requires no Open statement in the serialized v1 profile, claims the distinct Local statement owner when required, constructs `LocalStatementRegistration {source_spec_ref,applied_control_ref,registration_ref,statement_seq,statement_idempotency_key,statement_class,canonical_statement_digest,parameter_digest,result_answer_contract,workspace_generation_ref,transaction_error_policy,statement_audit_admission:LocalStatementAuditAdmission::Claimed|NotRequired,registered_snapshot}`, and inserts Open. Exact retry joins; any sequence/key/body/workspace/policy/audit drift fails.

`LocalSerializationCertificate` is a same-group certificate `{SameGroupCertificateHeader,registration_ref:StrongRef<LocalAttemptRegistration>,lifecycle_basis:Statement{statement_registration_ref:StrongRef<LocalStatementRegistration>,prior_workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<LocalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>,successor_workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<LocalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>}|Prepare{terminal_admission_basis_digest}|ReadClose{read_close_basis_digest},snapshot_and_conflict_index_basis,complete_read_witness_refs[LocalReadWitnessRef],complete_write_summary_refs[LocalWriteSummaryRef],candidate_edges[],retained_overlap_projection_digest,scc_verifier_version,acyclic_result,conservative_fallbacks[],certificate_attempt_plan_ref,quorum_signatures}`. `LocalReadWitnessRef` and `LocalWriteSummaryRef` are generated closed unions over the registered Local witness/summary targets; raw StrongRef bags are forbidden. Every follower reconstructs the Local SSI graph and fixed snapshot/workspace inputs. `LocalStatementPublicationSpec` is `{statement_registration_ref:StrongRef<LocalStatementRegistration>,registration_ref:StrongRef<LocalAttemptRegistration>,expected_index_value:Open,statement_audit_admission:LocalStatementAuditAdmission::Claimed|NotRequired,read_access_admission_ref:StrongRef<ReadAccessAdmissionRecord>,read_result_release_decision_ref:StrongRef<ReadResultReleaseDecisionRecord>,local_serialization_certificate_ref:StrongRef<LocalSerializationCertificate>,expected_prior_workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<LocalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>,successor_workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<LocalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>,successor_cumulative_read_witness_root_ref:StrongRef<LocalCumulativeReadWitnessRoot>,successor_cumulative_effect_root_ref:StrongRef<LocalCumulativeEffectRoot>,published_output:LocalStatementPublishedOutput,expected_statement_and_outcome_frontiers,terminal_audit_gate}`. `LocalStatementPublishedOutput` is `NoResult{no_result_proof_ref:StrongRef<NoResultProof>,terminal_delivery_frontier_digest}|Buffered{manifest_ref:StrongRef<LocalBufferedResultManifest>,canonical_result_digest,delivery_lease_recipe:LocalResultDeliveryLeaseRecipe}`; tag, statement class, result owner, schema/answer contract/digest, prior/successor workspace, witness/effect roots, and ticket owner must byte-match. Apply creates the role-valid applied publication reference and lease when Buffered, changes Open to Published, advances the statement/workspace/delivery frontiers, and constructs the immediately succeeding `TxnOutcomeRecord::Registered`. The candidate remains invisible until the exact statement audit mirror. `LocalStatementAbortSpec` alone changes Open to `Failed|Abandoned`, resolves that statement ticket, proves no result/workspace effect, releases named resources, advances its no-result terminal frontier, and applies the registration-pinned `ContinueAttempt|AbortAttempt` policy.

`LocalBufferedResultOwner` is `TerminalRead{registration_ref:StrongRef<LocalAttemptRegistration>}|AutocommitWriteTerminal{registration_ref:StrongRef<LocalAttemptRegistration>,prepare_admission_ref:StrongRef<LocalPrepareAdmissionSpec>}|Statement{registration_ref:StrongRef<LocalAttemptRegistration>,statement_registration_ref:StrongRef<LocalStatementRegistration>}`. `LocalBufferedResultManifest` is `{owner:LocalBufferedResultOwner,canonical_schema_ref:StrongRef<ResultSchema>,public_schema_digest,canonical_encoding_version,result_answer_contract,row_count,byte_count,ordered_chunks[CanonicalResultChunkDescriptor],canonical_result_digest,resource_charge_ref:StrongRef<ResourceLedgerTransition>}` and obeys the exact public schema/chunk/result transcripts defined for `BufferedResultManifest`; only the owner type differs. `ResultDeliveryLeaseOwnerBasis` is the closed pre-apply union `LocalTerminalRead{registration_ref,read_close_spec_body_digest}|LocalAutocommitWriteTerminal{registration_ref,prepare_admission_and_terminal_outcome_basis_digest}|LocalStatement{registration_ref,statement_registration_ref,publication_spec_body_digest}|ShardedTerminalRead{registration_ref,read_close_spec_body_digest}|ShardedAutocommitWriteTerminal{registration_ref,prepare_admission_and_terminal_outcome_basis_digest}|ShardedStatement{registration_ref,statement_registration_ref,publication_spec_body_digest}`. `ResultDeliveryServiceAuthority` is `DirectOrdinary{continuity_digest,service_catalog_version}|PromotionReceiptRequired{promotion_manifest_digest,expected_catalog_predecessor_version,promotion_receipt_digest}`. `ResultDeliveryLeaseTimeBasis` is the complete unsigned semantic lease recipe `{posture:Local|Sharded,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,service_visibility_epoch,tenant,principal,non_widenable_authority_digest,owner_basis:ResultDeliveryLeaseOwnerBasis,manifest_ref:ResultManifestRef,canonical_result_digest,release_subject_digest,pre_minted_delivery_id,lease_generation,service_authority:ResultDeliveryServiceAuthority,time_authority_profile_oid,not_before,expires_at,chunk_replay_profile,maximum_replay_count,successor_capability_generation,successor_capability_nonce,capability_verifier_key_ref:StrongRef<DurableCapabilityVerifierKey>,body_digest:BodyDigest<ResultDeliveryLeaseTimeBasis>}` whose registered body transcript excludes only `body_digest`. `LocalResultDeliveryLeaseRecipe` is `{time_basis_ref:StrongRef<ResultDeliveryLeaseTimeBasis>,required_posture:Local,issuance_time_validation_evidence_ref:StrongRef<TimeValidationEvidence>}`; evidence subject is the basis digest and publish-lease use, so no object hashes itself. Apply constructs `LocalResultDeliveryLease {owner:LocalResultDeliveryOwner,manifest_ref,time_basis_ref,delivery_id,lease_generation,canonical_result_digest,service_visibility_epoch,service_authority:ResultDeliveryServiceAuthority,time_authority_profile_oid,not_before,expires_at,issuance_time_validation_evidence_ref,chunk_replay_profile,maximum_replay_count,successor_capability_fields,created_at_logical_command_seq}` only after the owning command has an AppliedControlRef. `LocalResultDeliveryOwner` is `TerminalRead{registration_ref,read_close_applied_ref:AppliedControlRef}|AutocommitWriteTerminal{registration_ref,terminal_completion_applied_ref:AppliedControlRef,terminal_ready_outcome_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeRecord>}|Statement{registration_ref,statement_registration_ref,publication_applied_ref:AppliedControlRef}`. `LocalResultDeliveryIndex` maps each delivery ID to exactly one latest `StrongRef<ResultIndependentRetentionRecord<Local>>`; there is no attempt-owned AwaitingClientAck leaf. `DeliveryLeaseExpiryEvidence` is the pre-order `{lease:Local{lease_ref:StrongRef<LocalResultDeliveryLease>}|Sharded{lease_ref:StrongRef<ResultDeliveryLease>},expected_active_retention_state_digest,deadline,time_validation_evidence_ref:StrongRef<TimeValidationEvidence>,stable_expiry_reason,validator_version}`; evidence must be Expired for this exact lease/deadline/release action. `LocalResultReleaseEvidence` is exactly `ClientCancel{cancel_receipt_ref:StrongRef<AuthenticatedClientCancelReceipt>}|LeaseExpired{expiry_evidence_ref:StrongRef<DeliveryLeaseExpiryEvidence>}`. Session/region death only closes transport obligations, and attempt terminalization never releases or detaches promised result bytes. `LocalResultDeliveryTransitionSpec` is the closed `Acknowledge|ReleaseUnacked` union with exact owner/manifest/lease/active-retention/digest/prior-state/resource/audit fields. Apply creates one ACK/release record, constructs the terminal retention successor, and atomically advances the semantic owner's delivery frontier only if it was not already detached. No separate expiry-transition record exists and no protected bytes appear before mirror. The basis transcript includes every field above except `body_digest`; it excludes only future AppliedControlRef, issuance evidence, and applied sequence. Issuance evidence names the basis digest, and the applied lease is an exact projection plus those three later fields, so evidence cannot be transplanted across database, authority, owner, manifest, result, or service posture. The write-terminal arm is uninhabited before `LocalTerminalCompletionSpec` has selected TerminalReady and all commit/delta/durability/audit postconditions; that completion apply, not the commit command and never a client ACK, constructs the lease and atomically transfers it into independent retention.

`AuthenticatedClientCancelReceipt` is the immutable pre-release proof `{database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,service_visibility_epoch,auth_context_generation,session_binding,tenant,principal,effective_authority_digest,policy_epoch,revocation_index,posture:Local|Sharded,result_owner_identity,result_delivery_id,expected_active_retention_state_digest,request_id,stream_id,strictly_monotone_child_request_nonce,cancel_frame_transcript_digest,server_process_incarnation,accepted_child_state_version,server_signing_key_epoch,signature}`. It is created only after an authenticated, current-epoch cancel frame passes nonreplay and exact owner/delivery/state checks, and before the release spec; duplicate frame bytes reproduce the same receipt while nonce/body drift fails. `SessionRegionCloseReceipt` is the distinct structured-concurrency proof `{database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,service_visibility_epoch,session_binding,server_process_incarnation,region_id,region_generation,posture:Local|Sharded,result_owner_identity,result_delivery_id,close_cause_class,region_close_transition_digest,child_obligation_inventory_digest,zero_live_transport_sender_and_chunk_obligation_proof,close_receipt_nonce,server_signing_key_epoch,signature}`. It discharges only the in-process sender/chunk obligations after the owning region has irreversibly closed; it is not `ResultReleaseEvidence`, does not change the durable retention record, and conveys no authority to discard resumable bytes. Process death, socket EOF, timeout, or an unsigned region observation proves neither transport quiescence nor durable release.

Published results use an explicit capability-owned transfer, so transaction completion and compaction never wait for a client ACK. `ResultManifestRef` is the exact role union `Local{manifest_ref:StrongRef<LocalBufferedResultManifest>}|Sharded{manifest_ref:StrongRef<BufferedResultManifest>}`; `ResultLeaseRef` and `ResultSemanticOwner` are corresponding closed role unions. `ResultResumeCapabilityCommitment` binds the pre-minted opaque capability's domain, namespace, incarnation, service epoch, tenant/principal, non-widenable authority ceiling, delivery ID/generation, manifest/result digest, expiry profile/window, verifier-key epoch, and successor nonce without storing capability plaintext. `ResultRetentionState` is `ActivePendingVisibility{release_subject_commitment}|ActiveDeliverable{audit_release_evidence:AuditReleaseEvidence}|Acknowledged{ack_ref:StrongRef<ResultAckRecord>}|ReleasedUnacked{release_ref:StrongRef<ResultReleaseRecord>}`. `ResultIndependentRetentionRecord<Role>` is the immutable successor object `{role,semantic_owner:ResultSemanticOwner,manifest_ref:ResultManifestRef,lease_ref:ResultLeaseRef,canonical_result_digest,result_answer_contract,resume_capability_commitment:ResultResumeCapabilityCommitment,resource_ownership_transfer_ref:StrongRef<ResourceLedgerTransition>,predecessor_ref:StrongRef<ResultIndependentRetentionRecord<Role>>?,state:ResultRetentionState,created_or_transition_applied_ref:AppliedControlRef,created_or_transition_logical_command_seq,retention_floor,body_digest}`. An Active record strongly owns the manifest, chunks through it, lease, verifier key/time basis through it, and transferred resource charge. Terminal successors retain only the exact ACK/release evidence and compact disposition needed by the configured replay/lookup floor; an activated retention cut may then drop bulk bytes.

The result-producing Local/Meta command creates the Active record and atomically changes its semantic delivery frontier to `DetachedToIndependentRetention{retention_ref}`. A NotRequired gate creates `ActiveDeliverable`; a Required gate creates `ActivePendingVisibility`, and only that exact audit-mirror apply constructs its `ActiveDeliverable` successor. No public frame guard can select PendingVisibility. `LocalResultDeliveryIndex` and `GlobalResultDeliveryIndex` are authenticated maps `delivery_id -> latest StrongRef<ResultIndependentRetentionRecord<Local|Meta>>` plus generation, active/terminal counts, compacted-disposition floor, and root digest; they are part of the respective logical payload, checkpoint vector, backup closure, restore reconstruction, GC inventory, service-epoch transition, and configuration transfer. Semantic attempt/statement indexes retain only the detached reference until their own compaction; the independent index remains authoritative thereafter. Acknowledgement or release CASes exactly one ActiveDeliverable predecessor, updates this index, and transfers/releases its charge in the same ordered command. Matching retry returns the identical terminal successor; competing ACK/cancel/expiry produces exactly one winner and a stable already-terminal response.

`ResultDeliveryDispositionProof` is `{role,semantic_owner,delivery_id,canonical_result_digest,disposition:ActiveIndependent{retention_ref:StrongRef<ResultIndependentRetentionRecord<Role>>}|Acknowledged{retention_ref,ack_ref}|ReleasedUnacked{retention_ref,release_ref},semantic_frontier_detachment_proof,independent_index_membership_proof,resource_owner_consistency_proof,checkpoint_and_retention_floor}`. `ResultDispositionRef` is the compact typed projection of those three arms. Terminal publication, explicit close/cancel, attempt compaction, workspace release, and outcome compaction require one exact proof for every result owner, but `ActiveIndependent` is already terminal for the **attempt's** delivery frontier. It is not terminal for the independent delivery obligation. An attempt outcome, socket/session loss, region cancellation, process crash, service restart, compaction, backup/restore, or Local-to-Sharded activation cannot release an Active record. Only authenticated client cancellation or profiled lease-expiry evidence may select ReleasedUnacked; complete end-to-end ACK may select Acknowledged. Crash/DPOR tests cover publication before/after audit mirror, terminalization before ACK, session death, lost RESULT_END/ACK/cancel responses, ACK-versus-expiry, attempt compaction, service-epoch change, restore, verifier-key rotation, charge-transfer failure, and GC, requiring byte-identical resume or one explicit terminal disposition with no leaked or prematurely reclaimed byte.

`TxnOutcomeRecord` is the Local predecessor-linked lifecycle object `{database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,service_visibility_epoch,txn_token,tenant,principal,authority_ceiling_digest,predecessor_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeRecord>?,state:BeginStaging{reservation_ref:StrongRef<LocalBeginReservationRecord>}|NeverRegistered{terminal_ref:StrongRef<LocalNeverRegisteredRecord>}|Registered{registration_ref:StrongRef<LocalAttemptRegistration>,statement_terminal_frontier,open_statement_ref:StrongRef<LocalStatementRegistration>?,delivery_terminal_frontier,latest_workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<LocalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>,statement_index_digest}|PrepareAdmitted{admission_spec_ref:StrongRef<LocalPrepareAdmissionSpec>,terminal_admission_fence_ref:StrongRef<LocalTerminalAdmissionFence>,admission_generation,workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<LocalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>,statement_frontier,delivery_frontier,finalization_basis_digest}|CommittedPendingPostconditions{marker_ref:StrongMarkerRef,final_effect_digest,commit_command_ref:StrongRef<CommitCommand>,applied_logical_seq,applied_commit_seq}|Committed{marker_ref:StrongMarkerRef,final_effect_digest,applied_logical_seq,applied_commit_seq,local_delta_frontier,public_outcome:TerminalPublicOutcome::Local}|Aborted{reason_class,applied_abort_ref:AppliedAbortRef,public_outcome:TerminalPublicOutcome::Local}|ReadClosed{read_close_spec_ref:StrongRef<LocalReadCloseSpec>,applied_control_ref:AppliedControlRef,publication_chain_digest,final_result_digest?,public_outcome:TerminalPublicOutcome::Local},audit_state:NotRequired{evidence:NonRequiredAuditEvidence}|ClaimedPending{ticket_digest,claim_identity}|Terminal{audit_outcome_ref:StrongRef<AuditOutcomeRecord>},completion_state:TxnCompletionState,time_authority_profile_oid,issued_at,expires_at,minimum_lookup_retention_floor}`. Each terminal state's inner kind must equal its Local public-outcome kind; no Sharded arm is encodable. `TxnOutcomeIndex` has the three Detailed/Compacted/ExpiredTombstone arms defined in §5.2. `LocalTxnOutcomeSummaryRoot` contains authenticated capability-safe `NeverRegistered` and `TerminalReady` leaves with exact namespace/incarnation/service epoch, tenant/principal, authority-ceiling commitment, scoped token/begin-key digest, public outcome, time-authority profile/window, audit/result disposition, expiry, and lookup floor; it cannot answer an in-progress state.

`TerminalWriteResultPreparation` is the closed posture union `Local{registration_ref:StrongRef<LocalAttemptRegistration>,prepare_admission_ref:StrongRef<LocalPrepareAdmissionSpec>,final_effect_directory_ref:StrongRef<EffectDirectoryRoot>,final_effect_digest,returning_evaluation_plan_ref:StrongRef<DeterministicReturningPlan>,returning_evaluation_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ReturningEvaluationCertificate>,manifest_ref:StrongRef<LocalBufferedResultManifest>,canonical_result_digest,result_answer_contract,time_basis_ref:StrongRef<ResultDeliveryLeaseTimeBasis>,issuance_time_validation_evidence_ref:StrongRef<TimeValidationEvidence>,prepared_owner_identity:PreparedOwnershipId,prepared_closure_inventory_digest}|Sharded{registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,prepare_admission_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,global_final_effect_directory_ref:StrongRef<GlobalEffectDirectoryRoot>,global_final_effect_digest,returning_evaluation_plan_ref:StrongRef<DeterministicReturningPlan>,returning_evaluation_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ReturningEvaluationCertificate>,manifest_ref:StrongRef<BufferedResultManifest>,canonical_result_digest,result_answer_contract,time_basis_ref:StrongRef<ResultDeliveryLeaseTimeBasis>,issuance_time_validation_evidence_ref:StrongRef<TimeValidationEvidence>,meta_prepared_owner_identity:PreparedOwnershipId,prepared_closure_inventory_digest}`. It exists only for autocommit ReadWrite WriteReturning. The registered evaluator reruns after final deterministic rebase against the final effect directory, and its certificate proves the manifest bytes/contract are exactly the RETURNING projection of that effect set. Prepared ownership's typed closure inventory retains preparation, manifest, chunks, time basis/evidence, and verifier/profile before command order. The object names no future command, outcome, applied record, lease, payload, or root; terminal completion consumes it and creates the lease only after TerminalReady.

`LocalPrepareAdmissionSpec` is `{registration_ref:StrongRef<LocalAttemptRegistration>,expected_registered_outcome_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeRecord>,admission_generation,expected_statement_frontier,expected_delivery_frontier,expected_statement_index_digest,expected_workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<LocalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>,expected_cumulative_read_witness_root_ref:StrongRef<LocalCumulativeReadWitnessRoot>,expected_cumulative_effect_root_ref:StrongRef<LocalCumulativeEffectRoot>,local_serialization_certificate_ref:StrongRef<LocalSerializationCertificate>,global_authorization_decision_ref:StrongRef<AuthorizationDecisionRecord>,resource_transition_refs[StrongRef<ResourceLedgerTransition>],operation_audit_admission:LocalOperationAuditAdmission::Claimed|NotRequired,transaction_audit_basis_commitment,finalization_basis_digest,expected_branch_heads[WeakMarkerIdentity],expected_branch_key_epochs,expected_policy_epoch,expected_revocation_index,expected_conflict_index_basis:WeakStateIdentity,terminal_audit_gate:LifecycleScaffoldingNotRequired}`. Apply requires ReadWrite, no Open statement, contiguous terminal statement/delivery frontiers, exact workspace/witness/effect/SSI/security bases, and no prior admission. It constructs immutable `LocalTerminalAdmissionFence::Armed {registration_ref,admission_generation,admission_applied_ref:AppliedControlRef,frozen_statement_delivery_workspace_witness_effect_commitment,frozen_branch_heads,frozen_branch_key_epochs,frozen_resource_and_constraint_commitment,frozen_policy_epoch,frozen_revocation_index,frozen_conflict_basis,operation_audit_claim_commitment,transaction_audit_basis_commitment}` (with no future sequence/HLC), makes the succeeding `TxnOutcomeRecord::PrepareAdmitted` the unique canonical selector of that fence, and atomically replaces the token's Detailed entry.

Only then are the final rebased effect directory, optional `TerminalWriteResultPreparation`, and `TxnOutcomePreparationRecord` constructed. `TxnOutcomePreparationRecord` is `{txn_token,expected_prior_state:PrepareAdmitted{outcome_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeRecord>,terminal_admission_fence_ref:StrongRef<LocalTerminalAdmissionFence>,admission_generation,state_digest},proposed_terminal_kind,final_effect_digest,terminal_write_result:None|Prepared{preparation_ref:StrongRef<TerminalWriteResultPreparation>,required_posture:Local},authorization_decision_ref,resource_transition_refs,terminal_audit_gate}`. Before any terminal audit lock, `LocalFinalCertificationReserveSpec` revalidates the final rebased selection and installs the Active reservation/holds. The audit plan binds that reservation; the stable `CommittedEffectCapsule`, `LogicalDeltaTemplate`, and semantic D1 availability closure include the reservation but no HLC/order observation. After the audit triple is ready, each proposal builds a fresh D1-certified `LocalOrderAttemptInput`; the ordinary `CommitCommand` names both closures. Commit apply requires the exact selected Armed fence and Active LocalCommit reservation, atomically consumes the reservation, constructs `LocalTerminalAdmissionFence::TerminalOrdered {predecessor_ref:StrongRef<LocalTerminalAdmissionFence>,final_certification_reservation_ref:StrongRef<LocalFinalCertificationReservation>,commit_command_ref:StrongRef<CommitCommand>,assigned_logical_command_seq,assigned_commit_seq}`, and makes the succeeding pending outcome select the terminal version. Admitted abort analogously requires an Active LocalAbort reservation and fresh order supplement, consumes it, constructs `LocalTerminalAdmissionFence::Released {predecessor_ref,final_certification_reservation_ref,abort_applied_ref}`, and selects it through the succeeding aborted outcome. These are new immutable objects, never mutation of the Armed or reservation bytes; the outcome/reservation index CAS forbids a second successor.

`LocalTerminalCompletionSpec` is `{pending_outcome_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeRecord>,semantic_outcome:SemanticTerminalDescriptor::Local,expected_required_postcondition_bitmap,observed_satisfied_postcondition_bitmap,configured_durability_evidence_ref,local_delta_frontier_evidence_ref,result_disposition:NoTerminalResult|ReadTerminalResult{delivery_disposition_proof_ref:StrongRef<ResultDeliveryDispositionProof>}|AutocommitWriteReturning{preparation_ref:StrongRef<TerminalWriteResultPreparation>,required_posture:Local},resource_release_refs[],audit_visibility_evidence_ref,expected_conflict_overlap_floor,terminal_audit_gate}`. It monotonically adds verified bits and creates `TerminalReady` only when the required bitmap is exactly satisfied; it cannot alter the semantic outcome. The autocommit-write arm atomically creates the owner, lease, resource transfer, Active retention record/index leaf, and detached semantic frontier; Active retention satisfies the attempt result bit. `LocalReadCloseSpec` is `{registration_ref,operation_audit_admission,mode:AutocommitResult{read_access_admission_ref,read_result_release_decision_ref,buffered_result_manifest_ref,canonical_result_digest,result_answer_contract,delivery_lease_recipe}|ExplicitClose{expected_statement_frontier,expected_delivery_detachment_frontier,result_disposition_proof_refs[StrongRef<ResultDeliveryDispositionProof>],complete_publication_chain_digest,workspace_generation_ref,cumulative_read_witness_root_ref,zero_cumulative_write_effect_proof_ref,no_open_statement_proof_ref},local_serialization_certificate_ref,expected_conflict_index_basis,terminal_audit_gate}`. Apply advances LogicalCommandSeq/HLC but not CommitSeq, creates ReadClosed and, for autocommit, atomically creates and detaches the terminal result into independent retention; it releases success only after mirror and required completion bits, never after client ACK. Strengthened `TxnAbortSpec` is `{registration_ref,expected_prior:Registered{outcome_ref,state_digest}|PrepareAdmittedUnordered{outcome_ref,fence_ref,consensus_nonorder_proof_ref},all_open_statement_abort_refs[],result_disposition_proof_refs[StrongRef<ResultDeliveryDispositionProof>],workspace_release_evidence_refs[],conflict_close_evidence_ref,stable_reason,authorization_decision_ref,resource_release_refs[],operation_audit_admission,terminal_audit_gate}`; it can never race an ordered terminal command, requires every result already detached, and discharges only attempt-owned workspace/resource/conflict/audit obligations. The write-result preparation must equal the one retained by `TxnOutcomePreparationRecord`; completion projects its manifest/time basis/evidence into the lease and cannot reevaluate or substitute RETURNING bytes.

`LocalOutcomeCompactionSpec` is `NeverRegistered{detailed_outcome_ref,terminal_begin_ref,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>,expected_outcome_index_entry:Detailed,expected_begin_index_entry:NeverRegisteredDetailed,summary_leaf_body,all_retention_and_audit_discharge_evidence}|TerminalReady{detailed_outcome_ref,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>,expected_terminal_public_outcome,expected_outcome_index_entry:Detailed,expected_begin_index_entry:BoundDetailed,summary_leaf_body,result_workspace_conflict_replay_retention_discharge_evidence}`. Apply writes the authenticated leaf and atomically changes `TxnOutcomeIndex Detailed -> Compacted` together with `LocalBeginIdempotencyIndex NeverRegisteredDetailed -> NeverRegisteredCompacted` or `BoundDetailed -> BoundCompacted`; both compact arms retain the same replay record, and status/acceptance retry bytes remain identical. `LocalOutcomeExpirySpec` is the distinct ordered transition `{capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>,summary_root_ref:StrongRef<LocalTxnOutcomeSummaryRoot>,leaf_key_digest,expected_outcome_index_entry:Compacted,expected_begin_index_entry:BoundCompacted|NeverRegisteredCompacted,time_validation_evidence_ref:StrongRef<TimeValidationEvidence>,expected_verifier_key_and_profile_floors,expected_begin_retry_and_lookup_floors,permanent_tombstone_body,terminal_audit_freeze:AuditFreezeField::Required<LocalControl>,terminal_audit_gate}`. Evidence must classify the replay record's exact window Expired for this action and every advertised retry/lookup floor must be closed. Apply atomically changes both indexes to authenticated `ExpiredTombstone` values containing token/key/capability commitments and evidence digest, drops the replay edge only there, and permanently prevents key/token reuse; valid old bytes return TokenExpired while invalid/unauthorized input remains NotVisibleOrUnknown. The construction DAG is fixed: registration -> workspace zero -> outcome; statement successor workspace and manifest -> publication spec/command -> applied publication/lease/outcome -> payload/record/root; prepare-admission outcome/fence -> final effect directory and optional terminal write-result preparation -> outcome preparation/capsule/prepared ownership -> unchanged `CommitCommand` -> marker/delta/pending outcome -> audit mirror -> completion transitions. No input names its future applied record, payload, command record, root, lease, marker, or summary leaf.

`GenerationRootRef` is the posture-closed union `Local{generation_root:StrongRef}` or `Distributed{manifest_ref:StrongRef<DistributedDerivedGenerationManifest>}`. `DerivedGenerationRegistry` maps a full `DerivedIdentity` strong reference to `{generation_root:GenerationRootRef,global_frontier?,answer_contract:AnswerContract,retention_class,status:Building|Active|Retiring}` and never reconstructs a singular graph/head/schema key. `ShardDerivedComponent` binds `{derived_identity_ref,shard_id,topology_epoch,input_global_batch_interval,resulting_global_frontier,partition_and_authority_coverage,answer_contract,component_root:StrongRef}`; `ShardDerivedComponentCertificate` adds `SameGroupCertificateHeader`, availability/retention floors, and quorum signatures. A meta-local `DistributedDerivedGenerationManifest` is `{derived_identity_ref,topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,exact_global_frontier,sorted_component_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardDerivedComponentCertificate>],complete_partition_and_authority_commitment,answer_contract,build_policy_epoch}`. Shard build/advance controls root components in `shard_derived_component_registry_root`; a meta activation control changes `Active` only after every required certified component at one topology/frontier exists. Partial, stale-topology, or mixed-frontier generations remain nonqueryable, and reads use the exact fallback path when the active manifest is missing. Checkpoint/configuration floors, remote grants, topology transfer, backup/replay, and GC retain every Building/Active/Retiring generation through its terminal transition.

**Replica-local RootManifest** is a closed four-posture, role-tagged union. Its common header is `{generation,database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,incarnation_continuity_profile_id,cluster_incarnation_continuity_digest,continuity_cas_version,service_visibility_epoch,replica_id,group_role:Local|Meta|Shard{shard_id}|RetiredLocal,group_id,filesystem_profile_id,filesystem_instance_digest,local_writer_fence_epoch,metadata_tree_bootstraps[Location|Encoding|KeyOpener],object_location_index_root,local_encoding_root,local_key_opener_root,raft_state_root:StrongRef<RaftStateRoot>?,nonretaining_predecessor_root_digest}` and it contains exactly one matching payload: `Local{logical_state_root_oid:StrongRef<LogicalStateRoot>,prepared_payload_root:StrongRef<LocalPreparedPayloadRoot>,local_applied_logical_command_seq,local_visible_logical_command_seq,local_applied_index,local_durable_index,active_audit_visibility_fence_ref:AuditVisibilityFenceRef?}`; `Meta{global_state_root_oid:StrongRef<GlobalStateRoot>,meta_prepared_payload_root:StrongRef<MetaPreparedPayloadRoot>,global_applied_logical_command_seq,global_visible_logical_command_seq,meta_applied_index,meta_durable_index,active_audit_visibility_fence_ref:AuditVisibilityFenceRef?}`; `Shard{shard_state_root_oid:StrongRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,shard_prepared_payload_root:StrongRef<ShardPreparedPayloadRoot>,shard_applied_index,shard_durable_index,global_applied_logical_command_seq,audit_visible_global_prefix}`; or `RetiredLocal{source_local_domain,transition_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRoleTransitionRef>,retirement_certificate_leaf_ref:StrongRef<ExportLeaf<LegacyLocalRetirementCertificate>>,catalog_receipt_ref:StrongRef<LegacyLocalRetirementCatalogReceipt>,terminal_source_manifest_identity:WeakDigest,terminal_source_root_identity:WeakDigest,terminal_source_logical_and_commit_prefix,terminal_role_transition_seal_digest,compact_physical_inventory_digest,retirement_audit_evidence_ref:StrongRef<LegacyLocalRetirementAuditEvidence>,no_semantic_prepared_raft_fence_or_service_roots,retired:true}`. `raft_state_root` is `Some` and must match the role payload for Local, Meta, and Shard; it is `None` for RetiredLocal, whose encoder also rejects every semantic-state, prepared-owner, Raft-log/configuration, audit-visibility-fence, and service-endpoint root. The active-role tuple `{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,role,group_id,continuity profile/digest/CAS,service_visibility_epoch}` must byte-match the rooted `RaftHardState`, snapshot, configuration, prepared-root records, audit fence, restore state, and canonical state; the retired tuple must instead byte-match the certified transition and retirement evidence. Cross-role, cross-group, cross-incarnation, cross-continuity, and cross-visibility substitution is invalid. A RetiredLocal manifest is authenticated and recoverable only as a compact terminal proof posture: ordinary/read-write open, role resurrection, Raft participation, receipt issuance, and service advertisement all fail before any logical object is exposed. A `MetadataTreeBootstrap` embeds `{tree_kind,tree_generation,tree_key_id,root_oid,cipher_descriptor,ciphertext_id,encoding_descriptor,placement_records,tree_key_opener,closure_digest}`. Each authenticated internal edge carries `{edge_key_or_range,child_oid,child_cipher_descriptor,child_ciphertext_id,child_encoding_descriptor,child_placement_descriptor,wrapped_child_dek_under_tree_key,child_wrap_profile,child_wrap_aad_bytes?,child_wrap_aad_digest,child_wrap_digest}`. If AAD bytes are omitted, they are reconstructed exactly as `canonical("fgdb:metadata-child-wrap:v1",database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,tree_kind,tree_generation,edge_key_or_range,child_oid,child_ciphertext_id,child_encoding_id,child_placement_id,child_wrap_profile,tree_key_id)`; supplied bytes must equal that transcript. Parent ObjectId is absent because it is not known before parent encoding. The digest cross-checks these usable AAD bytes and is never treated as the AAD itself. This is the exact key-opener path for each independently random child DEK; an opened parent/tree key alone is insufficient. Tree-root bootstrap edges are strong, but ordinary location/encoding/placement/key-opener **entries** are `WeakLocator`/`PhysicalRealizationRef` and do not determine liveness. Semantic/prepared/terminal-proof marking first decides which identities live, then resolves their containing realizations. RetiredLocal metadata trees may locate only the compact transition/retirement/audit closure and its physical realizations. The predecessor is `WeakDigest`, not a retention edge. The opened location index supports authenticated nonretaining subobject locators `{container_encoding_id,placement_id,offset,length}` for independently hashed markers.

`MetadataTreeBootstrap.closure_digest` commits only the already-built metadata-tree closure. That same generation MUST NOT contain any entry—strong, weak, or physical-locator—for its current `RootManifest`, `RootSlot`, or bootstrap bytes; the slot bootstrap is the current manifest's sole opener. This is a construction rule in the generated DAG checker, not merely a GC classification.

**ConfigurationState and Raft persistence.** `ConfigurationState` is `{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,group_role:Local|Meta|Shard{shard_id},group_id,configuration_epoch,form:Stable{voters[],storage_members[]}|Joint{old_voters[],new_voters[],old_storage_members[],new_storage_members[]},sorted_member_descriptors[{member_id,replica_namespace,consensus_signing_key_epoch,payload_receipt_key_epoch,roles,failure_domains[]}],raft_quorum_rule,payload_recoverability_predicate,failure_domain_map,gc_ack_policy,predecessor:WeakConfigurationIdentity?,transition_nonce}`; the ObjectId of these bytes is its identity and is not stored inside itself. Stable/joint quorum validation and the one-member specialization are exactly §14.2. Every same-group receipt/certificate carries `configuration_state_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>` plus `payload_predicate_digest`, and its database/security-namespace/incarnation/role/group must match the enclosing log, hard state, snapshot, prepared root, manifest, and command. Another group imports it only through `RemoteConfigurationRef`, whose signed adoption evidence and retention floor are the explicit nonrecursive trust base; identical member lists, epochs, or a bare config OID never authorize cross-group replay.

Every durable posture has the Raft layer; single node is a one-member configuration. `RaftLogSegment` carries `{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,group_role:Local|Meta|Shard{shard_id},group_id,first_index,last_index,entries[]}`, where every entry signature/digest domain repeats that tuple and an entry is `{index,term,entry_type,command,command_digest}` with the closed tagged command union `LocalTxn{StrongRef<CommitCommand>} | LocalControl{StrongRef<ControlCommand>} | MetaTxn{StrongRef<GlobalTxnCommand>} | MetaControl{StrongRef<GlobalControlCommand>} | ShardPrepare{StrongRef<ShardPrepareCommand>} | ShardDecisionApply{StrongRef<ShardDecisionApplyCommand>} | ShardControl{StrongRef<ShardControlCommand>} | Maintenance{StrongRef<RaftMaintenanceCommand>}`. The database/incarnation/group-role validator rejects every wrong-domain or wrong-role tag; a shard-local maintenance command has no global semantic sequence and cannot mutate meta-owned state. `RaftHardState` is `{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,group_role,group_id,current_term,voted_for?,log_first/log_last,commit_index,applied_index,visible_index,config_state_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,snapshot_ref?,maintenance_applied_index,certificate_attempt_ledger_root_ref:StrongRef<CertificateAttemptLedger>,prepared_order_attempt_root_ref:StrongRef<PreparedOrderAttemptRoot>,audit_signer_journal_root_ref:StrongRef<AuditSignerJournalRoot>}`.

`RaftMaintenanceCommand` is the closed nonsemantic union `CertificatePlanInstall{plan_ref:StrongRef<CertificateAttemptPlan>}|CertificateAttemptAbandon{spec_ref:StrongRef<CertificateAttemptAbandonSpec>}|CertificatePublish{certificate_ref:RegisteredStrongRef<AuthorityLocalCertificate>}|OrderAttemptInstall{input_ref:StrongRef<RoleOrderAttemptInput>,availability_certificate_ref:StrongRef<RoleOrderAttemptAvailabilityCertificate>}|OrderAttemptRetireStale{retirement_ref:StrongRef<OrderAttemptRetirementEvidence>}|AuditAttemptStagePublish{attempt_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalAttemptRecord>}|AuditSigningAttemptSupersede{spec_ref:StrongRef<AuditSigningAttemptSupersedeSpec>}` with an exact role-validity matrix. Maintenance entries advance Raft index, maintenance-applied index, and the named maintenance roots only; they never advance LogicalCommandSeq, CommitSeq, HLC, branch heads, audit-visible semantic prefix, or user state. They require the same live writer/incarnation/configuration guards and quorum durability as semantic entries and are included in snapshots, prepared/configuration floors, backup/restore, and GC. Consequently installing or abandoning a certificate plan and installing/retiring an order supplement cannot stale that supplement's expected next semantic sequence. A semantic command atomically consumes the selected ordered supplement in its apply result; a self-staleness fixture fails any implementation whose maintenance entry changes semantic order.

`RaftSnapshot` is a role-tagged union with common `{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,group_role,group_id,last_included_index,term,configuration_at_cut_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,retained_suffix_endpoints,prepared_ownership_floor,certificate_ledger_floor,log_prefix_digest,log_to_state_proof_digest,body_digest:BodyDigest<RaftSnapshot>}` and exactly one payload: `Local{last_included_logical_command_seq,last_included_commit_seq,logical_state_root_ref:StrongRef<LogicalStateRoot>,config_payload_floor_ref:StrongRef<ConfigPayloadFloor>,recovery_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<RecoveryCheckpoint>,checkpoint_state_vector_digest}`; `Meta{last_included_global_logical_command_seq,last_included_global_commit_seq,global_logical_hlc,global_state_root_ref:StrongRef<GlobalStateRoot>,meta_config_payload_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaConfigPayloadFloor>,global_recovery_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<GlobalRecoveryCheckpoint>,global_checkpoint_state_vector_digest}`; or `Shard{shard_id,through_global_logical_command_seq,through_global_commit_seq,topology_epoch,shard_state_root_ref:StrongRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,shard_config_payload_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardConfigPayloadFloor>,shard_recovery_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<ShardRecoveryCheckpoint>,shard_checkpoint_state_vector_digest}`. Its registered body transcript includes the common header and selected role payload and excludes only the `body_digest` field. These values equal application through the exact cut; `last_included_index <= visible_index`, no active audit fence is crossed, and later commands/certificates/remote obligations remain retained. `AuditVisibilityFence` is the one exact durable role-tagged schema `{header:AuditFenceHeader,body:Local{ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,candidate_state_root_ref:StrongRef<LogicalStateRoot>,terminal_resolution_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicketResolution>}|Meta{ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,candidate_state_root_ref:StrongRef<GlobalStateRoot>,terminal_resolution_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicketResolution>}}`; `AuditVisibilityFenceRef` is exactly `StrongRef<AuditVisibilityFence>`. `AuditFenceHeader` is `{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,group_role:Local|Meta,group_id,proposal_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,post_apply_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,origin_local_writer_fence_epoch,blocked_after_order,blocked_after_raft_index}`. Body tag and candidate role must match header. Non-configuration work requires equal configs. A configuration transition binds its old/joint/new phase; current Raft config equals `post_apply_configuration_ref`, old+new floors/quorums retain the proposal basis, and the mirror orders under post-apply config. Shard is uninhabited. Takeover may preserve an origin-E fence under E+1 only through the exact chain; database/incarnation/role/group and both config refs remain exact, with `origin_epoch <= current_epoch`. `RaftStateRoot` repeats the full database/incarnation/role/group domain and owns hard state, logs, configs, matching snapshot, prepared/certificate ledgers, remote obligations, transition seals/locks, and any fence/candidate. Every protocol reply follows durable publication.

`AuthorityLocalCertificateHeader` is the mandatory prefix of every authority-local quorum-signed receipt, certificate, proof, checkpoint/ack/floor, topology/GC/reconfiguration/activation barrier, and certificate-ledger entry: `{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,authority_group_role,authority_group_id,configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,payload_predicate_digest,signer_epoch}`. Object-specific schemas below abbreviate it as `SameGroupCertificateHeader`; that alias is valid only inside the owning group. An imported export leaf instead begins `ImportedCertificateDomain {database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,authority_group_role,authority_group_id,authority_configuration_evidence_ref:RemoteConfigurationRef,payload_predicate_digest,signer_epoch}` and contains no raw `StrongRef<ConfigurationState>` across groups. The generated certificate-domain checker requires the authority-local transcript, imported embedded canonical configuration, `RemoteAuthorityConfigurationEvidence`, and outer `CertifiedRemoteStrongRef` to agree exactly; old-incarnation, old-configuration, wrong-role, or wrong-predicate substitution fails before object-specific validation.

Every authority-local quorum artifact also obeys one universal signing protocol. `CertificateUnsignedBodyDigest<T>` is the registered domain-separated transcript recipe over every semantic field of certificate schema `T`, including its full authority/configuration/predicate header and pre-minted scalar `certificate_attempt_id`, but excluding exactly `certificate_attempt_plan_ref`, the canonical lock/share arrays, and aggregate/signature fields. A certificate schema contains no future certificate-ledger publication ObjectId or applied identity: the later ledger entry points to the completed certificate. It excludes no subject, topology, sequence, closure, result, policy, epoch, or verifier field. Before the first signature, a nonsemantic Raft maintenance entry quorum-roots `CertificateAttemptPlan {certificate_attempt_id,certificate_kind,subject_identity,authority_domain,configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,payload_predicate_digest,certificate_schema_id,certificate_schema_version,canonical_unsigned_body_digest:CertificateUnsignedBodyDigest<T>,canonical_signer_subset[{signer_id,signing_key_id,signer_epoch}],threshold,signature_algorithm_and_encoding}` in `CertificateAttemptLedger`; this changes no semantic sequence or HLC. Each selected signer durably installs its distinct `CertificateSignerLock {plan_ref:StrongRef<CertificateAttemptPlan>,certificate_attempt_id,subject_identity,certificate_schema_id,canonical_unsigned_body_digest,signer_id,signing_key_id,signer_epoch,state:Locked}` in its fenced signer journal before emitting `CertificateSignatureShare {lock_ref:StrongRef<CertificateSignerLock>,signer_id,signing_key_id,canonical_signature_bytes}`. Signer identity/key/epoch make lock bytes and ObjectIds distinct. The completed certificate carries `certificate_attempt_plan_ref`, the sorted exact lock/share bijection, signer-subset bitmap, and canonical aggregate or canonical signature-set encoding outside its unsigned-body transcript; its validator recomputes `CertificateUnsignedBodyDigest<T>`, verifies every share, exact planned subset/threshold, and the aggregate/ordered-set bytes. A `CertificatePublish` maintenance entry records `CertificateAttemptRecord::Published` after the bytes exist. Thus plan -> per-signer locks -> shares -> certificate -> ledger publication is acyclic while semantic-field substitution still changes the signed digest. Signer order, signature encoding, and exact quorum subset are fixed by the plan, so crash/retry/leader change reproduces one certificate byte string and ObjectId. A signer refuses any other digest for that plan/subject.

An unavailable planned subset may be replaced only through the nonsemantic maintenance command `CertificateAttemptAbandonSpec {plan_ref:StrongRef<CertificateAttemptPlan>,expected_ledger_state:Planned|Collecting,sorted_signer_journal_closure_refs,complete_share_bitmap,quorum_impossibility_proof_ref:StrongRef<CertificateQuorumImpossibilityProof>,no_certificate_or_export_publication_proof_ref:StrongRef<CertificateNonpublicationProof>,successor_signer_epoch_or_configuration,terminal_audit_gate:LifecycleScaffoldingNotRequired}`. Apply creates `CertificateAttemptAbandonment` only when the observed shares cannot meet threshold, every signer capable of completing the planned quorum has durably closed that plan at the named journal generation, and no certificate/export was published; otherwise it rejects. The ledger moves `Absent -> Planned -> Collecting -> Published` or `Planned|Collecting -> AbandonPending -> Abandoned`, never between terminal arms. A successor uses a new `certificate_attempt_id`, the same registered subject and unsigned-body digest unless the semantic owner itself legally changed, and a legal subset under the then-current configuration; it retains old plans, locks, shares, closures, and abandonment proof through the retirement floor. The role-local `CertificateAttemptLedger` recovers partial collections and permits at most one Published certificate identity per `(certificate kind,subject identity,unsigned-body digest)`; conflicting published digests are fatal evidence. The generated field table injects `certificate_attempt_id`, `certificate_attempt_plan_ref`, and the exact lock/share set into every routing, read, prepare, constraint, decision, checkpoint, projection, GC, derived, key, topology, backup/restore, acknowledgement, and `ExportLeaf` certificate even when a compact prose schema omits it. G0 generates include/exclude, signer-substitution, duplicate/missing-share, threshold, aggregate-mutation, abandonment, successor-subset, and maintenance-self-staleness fixtures for every registered certificate schema; only the named construction/signature fields may be excluded. Crash tests stop before/after each plan/lock/share/publication/abandon stage and across leader/configuration change.

**W12 global/shard formats (reserved now, activated only by the W12 feature epoch).** There is one meta consensus group and one consensus group per data shard. A raw `StrongRef` never crosses those group boundaries: every registration, basis, routing proof, prepare/decision/checkpoint certificate, fragment batch, apply acknowledgement, or topology proof used by another group is carried as `CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<T>` and therefore has the two-sided retention/GC obligation in the reference contract. All groups remain inside the declared trusted database-process boundary; object-scoped `ShardCryptoCx` unwrap permits reduce accidental key exposure but are not a TEE or shard-compromise-isolation claim. Meta alone owns semantic time and global authority.

`RemoteGrantTargetRef` is the generated closed tagged union over every role-valid registered grant target, with one stable wire tag and exact role/posture matrix per target; raw `StrongRef` plus a kind sidecar is forbidden. `RemoteRetentionObligationRoot` is the authority-group authenticated map `(authority_domain,grant_id) -> Active{grant_record_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantRecord>,target_ref:RemoteGrantTargetRef,consumer_domain,minimum_floor}|TransferredOut{transfer_record_ref:StrongRef<LegacyRetentionAuthorityTransferRecord>,new_authority_domain,target_identity,migration_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardingMigrationRetentionFloor>}|TransferredInPending{transition_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRoleTransitionRef>,source_transfer_record_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,new_meta_grant_record_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantRecord>,legacy_target_ref:RemoteGrantTargetRef,consumer_domain,minimum_floor}|TransferredIn{transfer_evidence_ref:StrongRef<LegacyRetentionAuthorityTransferEvidence>,legacy_target_ref:RemoteGrantTargetRef,consumer_domain,minimum_floor}|ReleaseApplied{tombstone_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionReleaseTombstone>}|AckPublished{tombstone_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionReleaseTombstone>,ack_leaf_ref:StrongRef<ExportLeaf<RemoteRetentionReleaseAckCertificate>>,release_summary_key,retain_ack_through}`. Transfer variants exist only for the one certified Local-to-Meta transition; ordinary reconfiguration uses the successor-grant handshake. Pending retains the already-built new grant and certified legacy target without naming future grant evidence. Release terminal states have no strong path to active target state, while transfer states retain exactly the migration floor/wrapper until adoption.

`RemoteRetentionConsumerRoot` is the consumer-group authenticated map `(authority_domain,grant_id) -> Acquired{grant_evidence_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantEvidence>,local_consumer_set_commitment}|AuthorityTransferPending{transfer_evidence_ref:LegacyTransferEvidenceRef,old_authority_domain,new_authority_domain,local_consumer_set_commitment}|AuthorityTransferAdopted{adoption_record_ref:StrongRef<RetentionAuthorityTransferAdoptionRecord>,new_authority_grant_evidence_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantEvidence>}|ReleaseRequested{request_record_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionReleaseRequestRecord>,frozen_consumer_set_commitment}|ReleaseCertified{request_record_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionReleaseRequestRecord>,request_leaf_ref:StrongRef<ExportLeaf<RemoteRetentionReleaseRequestCertificate>>,frozen_consumer_set_commitment}|Acknowledged{ack_leaf_ref:StrongRef<ExportLeaf<RemoteRetentionReleaseAckCertificate>>,release_summary_key,retire_after_floor}`. `ReleaseRequested|ReleaseCertified` encoders reject any added consumer under the old grant. The release-state identity is an already published weak root/record identity strictly before the request spec, never the request's future result.

`RemoteRetentionControlSpec` is the closed role-valid union `AcquireGrant{grant_spec_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantSpec>}|RegisterConsumerGrant{grant_evidence_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantEvidence>,expected_consumer_root_digest}|RequestConsumerRelease{request_spec_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionReleaseRequestSpec>}|PublishConsumerReleaseEvidence{request_certificate_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionReleaseRequestCertificate>,request_export_leaf_ref:StrongRef<ExportLeaf<RemoteRetentionReleaseRequestCertificate>>}|ApplyAuthorityRelease{apply_spec_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionReleaseApplySpec>}|PublishAuthorityReleaseAck{ack_certificate_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionReleaseAckCertificate>,ack_export_leaf_ref:StrongRef<ExportLeaf<RemoteRetentionReleaseAckCertificate>>}|ConsumeReleaseAck{ack_export_leaf_ref:StrongRef<ExportLeaf<RemoteRetentionReleaseAckCertificate>>,expected_frozen_consumer_set_commitment}|AdoptLegacyAuthorityTransfer{adoption_spec_ref:StrongRef<RetentionAuthorityTransferAdoptionSpec>}`. There is no generic transfer arm: old-Local transfer records are created only by `BeginRoleTransitionSpec`, Meta transfer evidence only by the certified activation projection, and a consumer uses only the exact adoption arm above. The generated role matrix fixes each arm to authority, consumer, or transition-consumer posture and rejects a record/evidence type in the wrong arm. This union is included in Local/Meta/Shard control registries. Checkpoint/configuration floors classify every authority/consumer/transfer entry plus unpublished certificate-ledger evidence. Crash tests cut before/after all six release transitions and every transfer/adoption/publication transition.

Trust-chain compaction also has an input/result split. `RemoteConfigurationTrustRoot` is the consumer-local authenticated map `authority_domain:ConsensusDomain -> CurrentEvidence{evidence_ref:StrongRef<RemoteAuthorityConfigurationEvidence>,trust_generation,minimum_consumer_floor}|ValidatedAnchor{anchor_ref:StrongRef<ValidatedRemoteConfigurationAnchor>,trust_generation,minimum_consumer_floor}`; it is strongly rooted in every Local/Meta/Shard payload, covered by every checkpoint/vector/configuration floor, and is the sole selector of current imported trust. `AdvanceRemoteConfigurationEvidenceSpec` is the ordinary role-valid CAS `{authority_domain,expected_trust_generation,expected_selected_evidence_or_anchor,successor_evidence_ref:StrongRef<RemoteAuthorityConfigurationEvidence>,direct_joint_transition_proof,minimum_consumer_floor}`; apply verifies the exact predecessor/anchor and atomically selects `CurrentEvidence(successor,generation+1)`. Meta shard adoption and every shard application of a Meta configuration projection that changes authority must embed the same expected selector/generation and successor evidence and perform this CAS atomically; topology/configuration can never advance while trust remains behind.

Anchor compaction is legal only after reissuing/advancing every live wrapper, grant, backup, replay manifest, prepared owner, and certificate-ledger entry to the selected current evidence. `RemoteTrustCompactionPrecondition` is the generated exhaustive `{consumer state/checkpoint/floor basis,current evidence ref,scanned typed root classes,zero_live_reference_commitment_to_every_predecessor_evidence,current-wrapper inventory commitment}`. `ValidateRemoteConfigurationAnchorSpec` is `{authority_domain,current_configuration_evidence_ref,ordered_predecessor_evidence_refs,precondition_ref:StrongRef<RemoteTrustCompactionPrecondition>,expected_consumer_state,expected_trust_root_generation,expected_current_anchor_digest?,validation_policy_oid,transition_chain_digest}`. Apply verifies every transition while predecessors remain rooted and the precondition proves no surviving object still binds one. It constructs `ValidatedRemoteConfigurationAnchor {authority_domain,through_configuration_oid,through_epoch,current_configuration_canonical_bytes,current_configuration_bytes_digest,current_member_verification_key_set,current_payload_predicate_digest,validated_transition_chain_digest,zero_old_evidence_commitment,validation_policy_oid,input_spec_digest:WeakDigest,consumer_applied_identity:WeakAuthorityAppliedIdentity}` and atomically selects its strong anchor at generation+1. Those retained verification keys and the full domain/predicate authorize validation of a `ValidatedCheckpointSuccessor`; a digest alone cannot. `WeakAuthorityAppliedIdentity = Local{command_oid,logical_command_seq}|Meta{command_oid,global_logical_command_seq}|Shard{command_oid,shard_raft_index}` is nonretaining. A later checkpoint successor or ordinary advance replaces the anchor atomically; no trust gap is legal. Only after the anchor command is checkpoint-cut and the zero-live-old proof remains valid may predecessor evidence retire. Both specs are explicit Local/Meta/Shard control variants; no result is prebuilt with its future command.

`TopologyState` is the meta-owned routing authority `{topology_epoch,form:Stable|Joint{old_epoch,new_epoch},partition_scheme:SourceRange{partition_function_oid}|HubVertexCut{vertex_owner_function_oid,edge_owner_function_oid,replicated_hub_profile},meta_group_id,meta_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,sorted_shards[{shard_id,group_id,configuration_ref:RemoteConfigurationRef,state:Active|Joining|Draining,failure_domains,key_access_profile}],sorted_range_or_hub_assignments,constraint_owner_function_oid,id_allocation_owner_map,copy_basis_global_prefix?,cutover_global_prefix?,predecessor_topology_identity:WeakDigest?,applied_control_ref:AppliedControlRef?}`. Assignments are total and nonoverlapping, identify one canonical data/edge owner plus explicit read-only replicas, and use imported configuration evidence rooted in `RemoteConfigurationTrustRoot`. `Joint` retains both maps/configurations until its typed retirement floor. A meta configuration transition constructs a same-routing successor with the phase-appropriate meta config; shard adoption constructs a successor replacing exactly one imported shard config. A scalar epoch cannot authorize routing, prepare, ID allocation, constraints, or GC.

**Fresh W12 genesis and one-way Local-to-W12 activation.** `ShardedGenesisCertificate` is the first object in the construction order: `{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,genesis_nonce,meta_group_id,meta_configuration_canonical_bytes_digest_and_payload_predicate,sorted_shards[{shard_id,group_id,configuration_canonical_bytes_digest_and_payload_predicate,failure_domains,key_access_profile}],topology_and_partition_recipe,generated_initial_meta_projection_slot_recipes[one_per_MetaProjectionSlot],initial_global_prefix,root_authority_policy_and_key_epoch,configured_root_authority_signatures}`. It commits no future evidence, payload, topology, projection, checkpoint, or root ObjectId/digest. Construction is certificate → per-group `RootAuthorityTrustArtifact` and Genesis configuration evidence → consumer-local `GenesisMetaProjectionPayload` objects → Topology/ActiveMetaProjection roots → checkpoint/floor/state roots. `GenesisMetaProjectionPayload` is `{genesis_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ShardedGenesisCertificate>,consumer_domain:ConsensusDomain,ordered_slot_values[{slot_tag,typed_canonical_value,source_recipe_digest}],exhaustive_slot_bitmap,configuration_evidence_refs[StrongRef<RemoteAuthorityConfigurationEvidence>],availability_floor}`. Its bitmap equals the complete generated `MetaProjectionSlot` registry—not a five-slot subset—and it has no raw remote-group edge. Every Genesis evidence byte-matches the root-authority-signed role/group entry, and every shard initial floor verifies the reconstructed payload/projection before emitting its barrier. A self-selected member signature or bare digest is not a trust anchor.

Existing Local databases activate W12 only through one offline, audited, one-way role transition. Before freeze, the coordinator obtains `ServiceVisibilityEpochReservation {reservation_id,database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,migration_nonce,source_posture:Local,target_posture:Sharded,source_service_visibility_epoch,target_service_visibility_epoch,complete_target_group_topology_and_endpoint_commitment,expected_continuity_digest_and_cas_version,expected_catalog_version,time_authority_profile_oid,issued_at,expires_at,authority_epoch,signature}`, with target epoch strictly above the external floor; use requires Usable time evidence and abandonment permanently burns it. The coordinator then pre-mints `ShardingRoleTransitionPlan {database/security namespace/incarnation,migration_nonce,service_epoch_reservation_ref:StrongRef<ServiceVisibilityEpochReservation>,source/target service visibility epochs,source Local group/configuration and expected basis prefix,new Meta and sorted shard group/configuration canonical bytes+payload predicates,fresh per-group log-origin nonces,topology/partition body,projection checker/version,local_to_global_projection_ref:StrongRef<LocalToGlobalProjection>,sorted_local_to_shard_projection_refs[StrongRef<LocalToShardProjection>],activation checkpoint/vector/floor body recipes,expected hidden shard barrier predicates,legacy_artifact disposition table,legacy_retention_authority_transfer_plan_ref:StrongRef<LegacyRetentionAuthorityTransferPlan>,cursor transition policy,external continuity/catalog predecessors,rollback_cutoff,completeness_digest}`. Reservation fields byte-match the plan and refer to no future plan identity. Projection objects are pre-order recipes over the existing Local basis plus deterministic freeze result and contain no result/root identity. Every payload field and mandatory inventory class has exactly one disposition `ReencodeForMeta|PartitionAndReencodeForShard{exact shard set}|CertifiedLegacyCarry{promise class,terminal transition}|ArchiveBeforeBegin{archive requirement}|RejectWithBlocker{reason}`. They cover graph/version/constraint/identity/allocator/branch/key/history/derived/replay/backup/cursor/outcome/capability/DP/resource/audit/transparency/prepared/certificate/remote-trust/retention state. Freeze is invalid while any blocker remains.

`ShardingFreezeSpec {plan_ref:StrongRef<ShardingRoleTransitionPlan>,expected_operational_state,expected Local state/head/logical/commit/HLC prefix,drain inventory,terminal_audit_gate}` rejects new work and drains every active transaction; unadmitted work is explicitly cancelled, every receipted/ordered owner is terminal or covered by the plan's exact transfer, and no earlier audit fence is active. Apply constructs `ShardingFreezeRecord {spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardingFreezeSpec>,applied_control_ref,source_basis_identity:WeakStateIdentity,assigned frozen prefix,branch/schema/policy/revocation/key/audit/continuity commitments,terminal txn/outcome/prepared proof,live promise inventory,plan_digest,deterministic_frozen_result_commitment,state:FreezePendingAudit}`. It does **not** name its future payload/root. The subsequently built `AuditVisibilityFence` alone owns the candidate root. External audit CAS plus the exact mirror makes that candidate visible and changes migration state to `FrozenVisible`; only then may any transition artifact be consumed. `ShardingUnfreezeSpec` is legal only from that visible state before Begin, invalidates this plan generation, and requires a newly audited plan/freeze.

Before Begin can be proposed, every new replica directory is prepared under a linear `PendingRoleTransitionCreationGuard`. It may create only uniquely named, unreachable transition staging bytes for this plan/configuration/log-origin, exact first-entry authorization closure, and `RoleTransitionSignatureLock`; it cannot publish `manifest.root`, serve traffic, issue ordinary receipts, or accept another migration nonce. New-group members sign `RoleTransitionJoinAcceptance` only after rereading that staging closure. `RoleTransitionReadyCertificate {root-authority domain,plan_ref,service_epoch_reservation_identity,source/target service epochs,sorted new-group acceptances,complete configuration/log-origin/staging availability commitment,old-Local freeze mirror identity,expiry policy,threshold signatures}` is pre-order evidence that every group can complete. After the dual transition certificate and external continuity reservation receipt exist, the guard may order/apply only the registered first entry under a RoleTransitionOnly lease; only after that entry has constructed its command record and hidden canonical root may it publish the first complete Meta/shard manifest. It never publishes a headless destination manifest or becomes an ordinary writer token. Creation and takeover guards cannot substitute for it.

The final old-Local entry is `BeginRoleTransitionSpec {plan_ref,freeze_record_ref:StrongRef<ShardingFreezeRecord>,freeze_mirror_record_ref:StrongRef<LogicalCommandRecord>,role_transition_ready_certificate_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionReadyCertificate>,expected_frozen_visible root/head/prefix,legacy authority-transfer set,migration retention floor recipe,terminal_audit_gate=StructurallyInapplicable{ShardingRoleTransitionAuthority}}`. Acceptance is a terminal Raft seal, not merely an apply-time flag: before any voter acknowledges the Begin `AppendEntries` at index `I`, it durably installs `RaftRoleTransitionSeal {plan_digest,begin_command_digest,terminal_local_raft_index=I,log_origin commitments}` in its `RaftStateRoot` and thereafter rejects every entry or snapshot extending beyond `I`. Once a quorum has accepted Begin, Local recovery may only finish this transition or enter an explicitly fenced restore/clone; it can never unseal and resume Local writes. Apply constructs `BeginRoleTransitionRecord`, advances to `(Lf,Cf,Hf)`, installs the canonical `RoleTransitionLocked` state, and applies the precommitted old-Local side of every authority transfer. The certificate requires both quorum-durable seals and quorum apply through Begin, eliminating the committed-but-unapplied append window.

Every old-Local and new-Meta signer first persists `RoleTransitionSignatureLock {migration_nonce,plan_digest,dual_transcript_digest,state=Locked}` in its staging/certificate ledger; quorum intersection plus the one-digest rule prevents two certificates. `RaftRoleTransitionCertificate` is the unique dual-domain transcript `{database/security namespace/incarnation,plan_ref and digest,migration_nonce,service_epoch_reservation_identity,source/target service visibility epochs,frozen-visible source commitment,Begin input/record weak identities plus Local command/marker/MMR/checkpoint chain digests,Lf,Cf,Hf,projection identities/digests,old Local/new Meta domains/configurations/predicates,all pre-minted log origins,sorted shard domains/configurations and expected hidden-ready barrier predicates,topology,external continuity/catalog predecessors,legacy-retention transfer commitment,migration-floor recipe,rollback cutoff,old-Local quorum seal+apply signatures,new-Meta join+signature-lock quorum signatures}`. It names no future state root, barrier, activation record, or result.

Portable `RoleTransitionContinuityReservationManifest` commits that certificate, epoch reservation, exact prior continuity head, terminal Local seal, destination groups/endpoints, and target epoch. External CAS changes `Operational{posture=Local,epoch=E}` to `RoleTransitionReserved{migration_nonce,transition_certificate_digest,source_posture:Local,target_posture:Sharded,source_service_visibility_epoch:E,target_service_visibility_epoch:E2,service_epoch_reservation_id,source_local_group_and_terminal_seal_commitment,target_group_topology_and_endpoint_commitment,transition_writer_authority_digest,lease_policy:RoleTransitionOnly}` and returns `RoleTransitionContinuityReservationReceipt`. No destination manifest publication is legal before this receipt. Once it exists, sealed Local cannot serve or obtain OrdinaryWrite authority, and destination groups may use RoleTransitionOnly solely for hidden bootstrap/projection/service preparation. A crash here is unavailable but roll-forward-only; it never creates overlapping Local and Sharded service.

No consumer directly references an old-group object. `CertifiedRoleTransitionRef` is the **bootstrap** consumer-local imported leaf `{certificate_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,embedded_dual_transcript_and_digest,old_local_configuration_evidence_ref:RemoteConfigurationRef,new_meta_configuration_evidence_ref:RemoteConfigurationRef,old_and_new_signature_sets,consumer_group_role,consumer_group_id,certificate_availability_evidence,source_transition_retention_grant_evidence}`. Its sole retention evidence is the already-existing source/root-authority migration grant established before Begin; it contains no new-Meta grant, activation record, hidden root, or evidence that activation will create. This bootstrap ref is therefore legal in destination first-entry specs. After hidden Meta activation and its audit mirror, `CertifiedRoleTransitionSuccessorRef` is constructed as `{bootstrap_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRoleTransitionRef>,activation_record_and_hidden_root_evidence,new_meta_grant_evidence_bijection,legacy_transfer_finalize_record_and_mirror_evidence,meta_successor_floor_body_commitment,consumer_group_role,consumer_group_id,successor_availability_evidence}`; every field already exists, and it cannot be built by the activation it names. `CertifiedTransitionArtifactRef<T>` adds `{transition_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRoleTransitionRef>,artifact_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,artifact_digest,artifact_kind,source Local configuration evidence,consumer role/group,artifact availability evidence,source migration retention grant evidence}` for bootstrap. `CertifiedLegacyLocalArtifactRef<T>` is the closed stage union `Bootstrap{artifact_ref:CertifiedTransitionArtifactRef<T>,legacy_promise_class,source_local_prefix,transition_or_expiry_or_archive_condition}|Successor{transition_successor_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRoleTransitionSuccessorRef>,artifact_identity,artifact_digest,legacy_promise_class,source_local_prefix,terminal_condition,successor_owner_acknowledgement}`. Long-lived floors, consumers, service preparation, and retirement must upgrade to Successor before the source migration grant can release. These are the only legal references to Local projections, outcomes, cursors, delivered bytes, replay/backup manifests, verifier keys, or other still-live Local artifacts from Meta or a shard. They never reinterpret a Local `StrongRef` as consumer-local.
