`LegacyRetentionAuthorityTransferPlan` is the pre-order Local object `{migration_nonce,old_local_domain:ConsensusDomain,new_meta_domain:ConsensusDomain,old_local_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,new_meta_configuration_canonical_digest,sorted_entries[{old_grant_id,old_grant_record_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantRecord>,target_ref:RemoteGrantTargetRef,target_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,target_closure_inventory_digest,consumer_domain:ConsensusDomain,new_meta_grant_id,new_meta_grant_body_recipe,transfer_nonce,required_consumer_adoption_predicate}],complete_old_authority_root_digest,complete_transfer_commitment}`. `BeginRoleTransition` creates one `LegacyRetentionAuthorityTransferRecord {migration_nonce,plan_entry_index,old_grant_id,new_meta_grant_id,old_local_domain,new_meta_domain,consumer_domain,target_ref:RemoteGrantTargetRef,target_identity,target_closure_inventory_digest,transfer_nonce,state:TransferredOut,assigned_local_logical_command_seq}` per entry and replaces every matching old authority-map entry atomically. No record names future Meta evidence or adoption.

Activation constructs the already-planned new Meta grant records and installs `TransferredInPending` entries; it cannot construct grant evidence or a transfer certificate for the root it is still building. After the hidden activation root and its audit mirror exist, Meta constructs `RemoteRetentionGrantEvidence` for each new grant, then `LegacyRetentionAuthorityTransferEvidence {transition_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRoleTransitionRef>,source_transfer_record_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,plan_entry_projection,old/new authority domains,consumer_domain,target_identity,target_closure_inventory_digest,old_local_export_leaf_ref:StrongRef<ExportLeaf<LegacyRetentionAuthorityTransferRecord>>,migration_retention_grant_evidence_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantEvidence>,new_meta_grant_evidence_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantEvidence>}`. `RetentionAuthorityTransferFinalizeSpec` names the exact pending-entry/evidence bijection and current MetaPending floor; apply changes every TransferredInPending to TransferredIn and constructs/selects the MetaSuccessor floor. Only then does the Meta quorum create `LegacyRetentionAuthorityTransferCertificate {SameGroupCertificateHeader,evidence_ref:StrongRef<LegacyRetentionAuthorityTransferEvidence>,transition_identity,old/new grant identities,old/new authority domains,consumer_domain,target_identity,target_closure_inventory_digest,transfer_nonce,activation_finalize_and_audit_mirror_identities,one_digest_signer_lock_ref:StrongRef<CertificateSignerLock>,quorum_signatures}` and export it under the ordinary floor. `LegacyTransferEvidenceRef` is `MetaLocal{evidence_ref:StrongRef<LegacyRetentionAuthorityTransferEvidence>}|ImportedMeta{certificate_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<LegacyRetentionAuthorityTransferCertificate>}`. A consumer orders `RetentionAuthorityTransferAdoptionSpec {transfer_evidence_ref:LegacyTransferEvidenceRef,expected_old_authority_domain,expected_old_consumer_entry_digest,new_meta_grant_evidence_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantEvidence>,expected_new_authority_domain,complete_local_consumer_set_commitment}` and apply creates `RetentionAuthorityTransferAdoptionRecord`; only then may it treat Meta as release authority.

`ShardingMigrationRetentionFloor` is the closed role tag `SourceLocked{plan_ref:StrongRef<ShardingRoleTransitionPlan>,source_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<RecoveryCheckpoint>,source_config_floor_ref:StrongRef<ConfigPayloadFloor>,source_root_inventory_ref:StrongRef<MigrationSourceInventory>,transfer_record_refs[StrongRef<LegacyRetentionAuthorityTransferRecord>],legacy_promise_inventory_ref:StrongRef<LegacyPromiseInventory>,rollback_cutoff}|MetaPending{bootstrap_transition_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRoleTransitionRef>,legacy_artifact_registry_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedLegacyArtifactRegistry>,pending_transfer_entry_refs[StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantRecord>],source_retention_evidence,continuity_reservation_receipt_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionContinuityReservationReceipt>,target_service_visibility_epoch,required_finalize_bitmap}|MetaSuccessor{transition_successor_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRoleTransitionSuccessorRef>,legacy_artifact_registry_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedLegacyArtifactRegistry>,transfer_evidence_refs[StrongRef<LegacyRetentionAuthorityTransferEvidence>],consumer_adoption_commitment,new_meta_and_shard_operational_checkpoint_cut_requirements,archive_expiry_cursor_outcome_replay_backup_terminal_conditions,retirement_predicate}`. `MetaPendingMigrationFloorRecipe` contains every MetaPending field as a pre-order body recipe but no future new-Meta grant/evidence ObjectId; `ShardingActivationSpec` consumes that recipe plus certified source retention projection, and apply constructs grants -> pending entries -> MetaPending floor. Finalize later constructs new grant evidence -> transfer evidence -> `CertifiedRoleTransitionSuccessorRef` -> MetaSuccessor. No arm points to a predecessor floor; any spec referencing a floor uses `StrongRef<ShardingMigrationRetentionFloor>` plus an exact required-arm predicate, never `StrongRef<Enum::Variant>`. Service preparation and every long-lived consumer require the MetaSuccessor arm/successor wrapper. Discharge requires every transfer adopted, every new group on a superseding Operational checkpoint/cut, and every legacy promise terminally disposed; only then may the source/bootstrap migration grant enter the six-stage release handshake.

The terminal old-Local `manifest.root` is retired explicitly rather than ignored. `RetirementReadinessRef` is the closed union `MetaLocal{checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<GlobalRecoveryCheckpoint>,activated_cut_ref:StrongRef<ActivatedRetentionCutSet>}|ShardRemote{checkpoint_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardCheckpointCertificate>,activated_cut_ack_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardActivatedCutAck>}`; `ShardActivatedCutAck`, `LegacyPromiseTerminalRecord`, and `LegacyPromiseTerminalAck` are registered role-specific checkpoint/cut and legacy-disposition schemas with exact authority/configuration/availability fields, not aliases. `LegacyDispositionRef` is `TransferAdoption{record_ref:StrongRef<RetentionAuthorityTransferAdoptionRecord>}|MetaTerminal{record_ref:StrongRef<LegacyPromiseTerminalRecord>}|ShardTerminal{ack_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<LegacyPromiseTerminalAck>}|Archived{grant_ref:StrongRef<ArchiveRetentionGrant>}`.

`RetiredLocalManifestRecipe` is the sequence-neutral `{replica_id,terminal_source_manifest_identity,terminal_source_root_identity,terminal_source_logical_and_commit_prefix,filesystem_instance_digest,terminal_role_transition_seal_digest,compact_physical_inventory_digest,stable_retired_header_and_body_fields,late_bindings:[BindThisRetirementCertificateLeaf,BindThisCatalogReceipt,BindThisRetirementAuditEvidence],basis_digest:RetiredLocalManifestBasisDigest}`. The registered basis transcript covers every stable field/late-binding tag but no future ObjectId. `LegacyLocalRetirementAuthorizeSpec {transition_successor_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRoleTransitionSuccessorRef>,meta_migration_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardingMigrationRetentionFloor>,required_floor_arm:MetaSuccessor,complete_floor_discharge_proof_ref:StrongRef<MigrationFloorDischargeProof>,sorted_new_group_readiness_refs[RetirementReadinessRef],all_transfer_adoption_and_legacy_disposition_refs[LegacyDispositionRef],expected_meta_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,expected_old_replica_set_digest,expected_external_posture_catalog_version,sorted_replica_retirement_recipes[RetiredLocalManifestRecipe],terminal_audit_gate}`. After its mirror, `LegacyLocalRetirementAuditEvidence` is the portable certified projection of the exact Meta ticket/event/resolution/external-CAS/mirror and authorization result, including Meta configuration/trust/availability but no raw Meta StrongRef. The Meta quorum creates `LegacyLocalRetirementCertificate {SameGroupCertificateHeader,authorization_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,authorization_audit_evidence_commitment,transition_identity,discharge_commitment,expected_old_replica_set_digest,sorted_replica_recipe_basis_digests,external_posture_cas_basis,one_digest_signer_lock_ref,quorum_signatures}`. `LegacyLocalRetirementCatalogReceipt` binds that certificate, recipe-basis set, prior/result catalog versions, transition, replica set, AuthorizedPendingReplicas, CAS receipt, and signatures. Order is authorize -> mirror/evidence -> certificate -> catalog CAS receipt -> per-replica retirement; no future identity is prehashed.

`LegacyLocalRetirementGuard` is a linear, nonexportable guard acquired separately per old replica. It authenticates inode, terminal Local root/seal, exact recipe basis, certificate/export leaf, catalog receipt, and imported audit evidence, then binds the three late slots and constructs the final RetiredLocal body. The durable field is uniformly `terminal_role_transition_seal_digest`. It first overwrites the alternate slot with RetiredLocal and syncs/rereads it, then overwrites the former active slot with the byte-identical recipe/body and syncs/rereads it; no acknowledgement is legal while either valid slot is Local. The guard cannot append Raft, revive state, issue receipts, reclaim bytes, or publish another root. Recovery rejects ordinary open and exposes only compact proof closure.

Each replica emits `LegacyLocalRetirementAck {database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,transition_identity,retirement_certificate_identity,catalog_authorization_receipt_digest,replica_id,replica_recipe_basis_digest,prior_active_and_alternate_slot_generations,written_retired_slot_generations,retired_slot_manifest_identities_and_body_digests,no_active_local_slot_proof,filesystem_instance_digest,compact_physical_inventory_digest,terminal_role_transition_seal_digest,two_slot_reread_and_durability_proof_digest,replica_signing_key_epoch,replica_signature}`. After the exact ack set, catalog completion moves to RetiredAll. `LegacyLocalRetirementFinalizeSpec` names authorization/certificate/both catalog receipts, exact ack bijection, Meta configuration, `expected_migration_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardingMigrationRetentionFloor>` with required MetaSuccessor arm, discharge proof, and terminal gate. Its mirror yields exact `LegacyLocalRetirementFinalizationCertificate {SameGroupCertificateHeader,finalize_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,finalize_audit_mirror_identity,transition_identity,retirement_certificate_identity,catalog_completion_receipt_digest,sorted_replica_ack_commitment,expected_replica_set_digest,reclaimability_predicate_commitment,one_digest_signer_lock_ref,quorum_signatures}` rooted by the certificate ledger.

Physical cleanup is separately narrow and durable-before-delete. `RetiredLocalReclamationPlan` is `{transition_identity,replica_id,both_retired_slot_identities,finalization_certificate_identity,catalog_completion_digest,sorted_targets[{target_identity,expected_physical_realization_digest,operation_id,method}],preserved_proof_inventory_digest,archive_legal_hold_backup_predicate_commitment,plan_digest}`. Before each irreversible action the offline tool durably records `RetiredLocalReclamationProgress {plan_digest,target_ordinal,operation_id,state:Requested|Completed{pre_and_post_physical_root_digests,receipt_digest}}` in the external retirement ledger; retry is idempotent by operation ID. `RetiredLocalReclamationGuard` verifies both retired slots, ack, final certificate, catalog, cut, predicates, plan, and current realization, and may touch only the selected target while preserving both compact slots/proof closure. Completion emits `LegacyLocalReclamationCompletionReceipt {transition_identity,replica_id,both_retired_manifest_identities,plan_digest,complete_target_receipt_bijection,reclaimed_inventory_digest,preserved_proof_inventory_digest,method,completed_at,time_authority_evidence_digest,authority_signature}`. It cannot create any database writer token or mutate semantics. Crash/partial/hold/proof-preservation tests cover each target boundary.

`LocalToGlobalProjection` is the pre-order recipe `{migration_nonce,source_local_basis:WeakStateIdentity,deterministic_freeze_result_commitment,Lf,Cf,Hf,ordered_global_payload_field_recipes[one per generated field],legacy_artifact_registry_recipe,attempt_summary_genesis_recipe,authority_transfer_recipe,complete_source_field_and_object_coverage_digest,semantic_equivalence_digest}`. `LocalToShardProjection` is `{migration_nonce,target_shard_domain:ConsensusDomain,source_local_basis:WeakStateIdentity,deterministic_freeze_result_commitment,partition_assignment,ordered_shard_payload_field_recipes[one per generated field],ordered_meta_projection_slot_recipes[one per MetaProjectionSlot],history_key_derived_prepared_retention_recipes,complete_source_range_and_field_coverage_digest,semantic_equivalence_digest}`. They contain no future freeze result, transition certificate, target object, checkpoint, or root identity. `ActivationMetaProjectionPayload` is built only after the certificate as `{transition_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRoleTransitionRef>,projection_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedTransitionArtifactRef<LocalToShardProjection>>,consumer_domain:ConsensusDomain,ordered_slot_values[{slot_tag,typed_canonical_value,source_recipe_digest}],exhaustive_slot_bitmap,remote_configuration_evidence_refs[StrongRef<RemoteAuthorityConfigurationEvidence>],availability_floor}`; its bitmap equals every generated `MetaProjectionSlot`.

Activation checkpoints use `CheckpointBasis = Genesis|Global{WeakGlobalCommandIdentity}|LocalActivation{transition/projection commitment,frozen Local weak head,Lf,Cf,Hf}`; shard projection checkpoints use the analogous LocalActivationProjection basis. Vectors/floors are generated complete body recipes with no future command/root OID. Fresh W12 genesis and activation use different barriers: `ShardInitialFloorInstallSpec` constructs `ShardGenesisOperationalBootstrapBarrier` only after fresh Genesis reaches Operational, while `ShardProjectionInstallSpec {transition_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRoleTransitionRef>,projection_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedTransitionArtifactRef<LocalToShardProjection>>,activation_meta_projection_payload_ref:StrongRef<ActivationMetaProjectionPayload>,continuity_reservation_receipt_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionContinuityReservationReceipt>,expected_role_transition_first_entry_authorization,installed_checkpoint_vector_floor_body_recipes,target_service_visibility_epoch,expected_first_shard_index_and_global_prefix}` is the first activation entry and constructs only `RoleTransitionPreparedHidden`. It then emits `ShardRoleTransitionReadyBarrier {SameGroupCertificateHeader,migration_nonce,transition_ref,projection_ref,continuity_reservation_receipt_ref,shard_id,target_service_visibility_epoch,hidden_state_root_ref:StrongRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,checkpoint_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ShardCheckpointCertificate>,config_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardConfigPayloadFloor>,history_inventory_ref:StrongRef<ShardHistoryInventory>,active_meta_projection_root_ref:StrongRef<ActiveMetaProjectionRoot>,remote_trust_generation,typed_retention_closure_inventory_ref:StrongRef<ShardRoleTransitionRetentionInventory>,payload_availability_certificate_ref:StrongRef<PayloadAvailabilityCertificate>,installed_global_prefix,queryable_history_interval,service_gate:Hidden,root_slot_durability_digest,one_digest_signer_lock_ref,quorum_signatures}`. Generated producer/origin rows reject fresh/activation substitution.

The first Meta entry is `ShardingActivationSpec {transition_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRoleTransitionRef>,projection_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedTransitionArtifactRef<LocalToGlobalProjection>>,continuity_reservation_receipt_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionContinuityReservationReceipt>,sorted_shard_barrier_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardRoleTransitionReadyBarrier>],topology_and_activation_checkpoint_vector_floor_body_recipes,meta_pending_migration_floor_recipe:MetaPendingMigrationFloorRecipe,certified_source_retention_projection,legacy_authority_transfer_plan_projection,expected_sequence=Lf+1,expected_commit_seq=Cf,target_service_visibility_epoch,terminal_audit_gate=StructurallyInapplicable{ShardingRoleTransitionAuthority}}`. Apply advances HLC once, creates new Meta grant records and TransferredInPending entries, then the MetaPending floor, topology/trust/key/derived roots, canonical empty attempt roots, and `GlobalControlRecord(origin=LocalActivationBridge)` with `bootstrap_phase=RoleTransitionPreparedHidden`; there is no separate `ShardingActivationRecord` type. It does not consume or construct future transfer evidence. Preserved Local outcomes/delivery/replay/backup/capabilities use CertifiedLegacyLocalArtifactRef. After this hidden root and mirror, `RetentionAuthorityTransferFinalizeSpec` constructs/selects MetaSuccessor.

Service preparation is an ordered state transition, not a certificate that appears inside its own source root. `ShardingServicePrepareSpec {transition_successor_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRoleTransitionSuccessorRef>,expected_hidden_meta_state:WeakStateIdentity,meta_successor_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardingMigrationRetentionFloor>,required_floor_arm:MetaSuccessor,continuity_reservation_receipt_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionContinuityReservationReceipt>,exact_sorted_shard_ready_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardRoleTransitionReadyBarrier>],complete_topology_configuration_endpoint_and_shard_ready_commitment,target_service_visibility_epoch,terminal_audit_gate:StructurallyInapplicable{ShardingRoleTransitionAuthority}}` moves only `RoleTransitionActivationState::Meta::ProjectionPreparedHidden -> ServicePrepareApplied{prepare_applied_ref}` and remains `RoleTransitionPreparedHidden`. Only after that applied root and its mirror exist may the quorum create `RoleTransitionMetaServicePrepareCertificate {SameGroupCertificateHeader,transition_successor_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRoleTransitionSuccessorRef>,prepare_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,hidden_meta_state_root_ref:StrongRef<GlobalStateRoot>,meta_successor_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardingMigrationRetentionFloor>,continuity_reservation_receipt_ref,target_service_visibility_epoch,complete_topology_configuration_endpoint_and_shard_ready_commitment,prepare_audit_mirror_identity,certificate_attempt_ref:StrongRef<CertificateAttemptRecord>,canonical_signature_set}`. The certificate ledger owns it until finalize; the prepare source state names only its applied record, never the future certificate.

Portable `RoleTransitionServicePromotionManifest` is `{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,migration_nonce,transition_certificate_evidence,continuity_reservation_receipt_evidence,source_posture:Local,target_posture:Sharded,source_service_visibility_epoch,target_service_visibility_epoch,meta_prepare_evidence:PortableCertificateProjection<RoleTransitionMetaServicePrepareCertificate>,sorted_shard_ready_evidence[PortableCertificateProjection<ShardRoleTransitionReadyBarrier>],complete_group_topology_configuration_and_endpoint_commitment,complete_legacy_transfer_finalize_commitment,continuity_transition_body_digest,expected_catalog_predecessor_version,signer_set_epoch,threshold_signatures}` and contains no local ref/CRSR/future receipt. External publication first CASes RoleTransitionReserved to `Operational{posture=Sharded,service_visibility_epoch=E2,writer_authority_digest,lease_policy=PromotionReceiptRequired}`, then CAS-replaces the exact Local/E catalog entry with the Sharded/E2 endpoints conditioned on the returned continuity digest. `RoleTransitionServicePromotionReceipt` repeats transition/manifest/group commitments, E/E2, all prior/reserved/operational continuity digests/versions, both CAS receipts, catalog versions, and signatures. A crash between CASes leaves all destinations hidden and rolls forward only.

`ShardingServiceFinalizeSpec {transition_successor_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRoleTransitionSuccessorRef>,meta_prepare_certificate_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionMetaServicePrepareCertificate>,manifest_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionServicePromotionManifest>,promotion_receipt_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionServicePromotionReceipt>,exact_sorted_shard_ready_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardRoleTransitionReadyBarrier>],expected_hidden_meta_state:RoleTransitionActivationState::Meta::ServicePrepareApplied,expected_meta_successor_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardingMigrationRetentionFloor>,required_floor_arm:MetaSuccessor,expected_operational_continuity_and_catalog_versions,target_service_visibility_epoch,terminal_audit_gate:StructurallyInapplicable{ShardingRoleTransitionAuthority}}` consumes the already issued receipt but selects only `OperationalPendingIndependentReopen::Unsealed` and `RoleTransitionActivationState::Meta::FinalizedPendingIndependentReopen{finalize_applied_ref,seal_state:Unsealed}`. Admission and routing remain disabled. After its root and mirror, `RoleTransitionServiceFinalCertificate` binds the final record/root, receipt, ready set, topology/configurations, epoch, reopen requirement, certificate attempt, and canonical signature set.

`ShardRoleTransitionServiceOpenSpec {final_certificate_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<RoleTransitionServiceFinalCertificate>,own_ready_barrier_ref:StrongRef<ShardRoleTransitionReadyBarrier>,locally_verified_promotion_receipt_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionServicePromotionReceipt>,expected_hidden_shard_state,target_service_visibility_epoch}` selects only `OperationalPendingIndependentReopen::Unsealed` and `RoleTransitionActivationState::Shard::OpenedPendingIndependentReopen{open_applied_ref,seal_state:Unsealed}`. It does not admit direct service or emit an operational ack.

`RoleTransitionPromotionRootSeal<Role>` is the exact role-tagged `{migration_nonce,role_and_group,finalize_or_open_applied_identity,sealed_role_state_root_ref:StrongRef<RoleStateRoot>,sealed_root_manifest_ref:StrongRef<RootManifest>,winning_root_slot_generation_and_digest,promotion_receipt_digest,target_service_visibility_epoch,typed_physical_inventory_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionPromotionPhysicalInventory<Role>>,physical_pin_id,pin_durability_receipt_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionPromotionPinDurabilityReceipt>,allowed_pending_reopen_successor_classes,seal_digest}`. It is built only after the finalize/open root and mirror are slot-visible. `MetaRoleTransitionPromotionSealInstallSpec` and `ShardRoleTransitionPromotionSealInstallSpec` install the matching seal and move only `Unsealed -> Sealed`; every allowed successor preserves it, and ordinary mutation/maintenance remains forbidden. A fresh process creates `RoleTransitionIndependentReopenProof<Role>` by opening the sealed slot/manifest, every pinned realization/key, receipt/continuity/catalog basis, and an allowed-successor-chain proof. Slot churn alone cannot change its subject.

`MetaRoleTransitionReopenConfirmSpec {migration_nonce,final_certificate_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionServiceFinalCertificate>,seal_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionPromotionRootSeal<Meta>>,independent_reopen_proof_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionIndependentReopenProof<Meta>>,expected_pending_state:Sealed,target_service_visibility_epoch}` alone moves Meta to `Operational` with activation phase `MetaReopenedAwaitingShardAcks`; it still rejects user admission and routing. `ShardRoleTransitionReopenConfirmSpec {migration_nonce,final_certificate_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<RoleTransitionServiceFinalCertificate>,seal_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionPromotionRootSeal<Shard>>,independent_reopen_proof_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionIndependentReopenProof<Shard>>,expected_pending_state:Sealed,target_service_visibility_epoch}` alone moves a shard to `Operational` with phase `ShardOperationalAwaitingMetaCompletion`. Only its applied-and-durable root may yield `RoleTransitionShardOperationalAck {SameGroupCertificateHeader,migration_nonce,final_certificate_identity,shard_id,reopen_confirm_applied_identity,post_reopen_state_root_ref:StrongRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,seal_identity,independent_reopen_proof_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionIndependentReopenProof<Shard>>,root_slot_durability_digest,certificate_attempt_ref:StrongRef<CertificateAttemptRecord>,canonical_signature_set}`.

`ShardingServiceCompletionSpec {migration_nonce,meta_reopen_confirm_applied_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,meta_seal_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionPromotionRootSeal<Meta>>,meta_independent_reopen_proof_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionIndependentReopenProof<Meta>>,exact_sorted_shard_operational_ack_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<RoleTransitionShardOperationalAck>],promotion_receipt_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionServicePromotionReceipt>,successor_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardingMigrationRetentionFloor>,required_floor_arm:MetaSuccessor,exact_required_shard_bijection_proof_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionOperationalBijectionProof>,terminal_audit_gate:StructurallyInapplicable{ShardingRoleTransitionAuthority}}` terminalizes Meta activation as `Complete` only after every and only configured shard ack. Its mirror yields a portable completion certificate. Each shard orders `ShardRoleTransitionCompletionApplySpec` under that certificate, changes its phase to `Complete`, and only then may direct shard service or Meta routing target it. Meta admits/routs only after its own completion mirror. Separate ordered pin-release commands retain every seal/inventory/proof until Meta completion and all shard completion acknowledgements. Completion does not by itself authorize old-Local reclamation. Crash/DPOR tests cut and race prepare, certificate creation, receipt, finalize/open, seal/pin publication, fresh reopen, confirmations, all acknowledgements, completion, projection, and pin release; no hidden or awaiting phase serves traffic.

Old-E sessions, frames, permits, authorization/result leases, and durable capabilities fail before routing or disclosure once RoleTransitionReserved is published. A cursor/outcome promise is either terminally closed before Begin or carries a pre-minted E2 successor gated by the promotion receipt. `RESUME_MIGRATE` under fresh E2 authentication may use an E capability only as proof for the exact `PostActivationCursorTransition`; it grants no E read/existence authority and returns only the E2 successor plus mandatory baseline. Every active cursor must replay/ACK its Local lease before transition; only baseline ACK permits Global deltas. No range changes source role.

Arbitrary online activation is prohibited. Operators run this exact epoch-reservation/freeze/mirror/readiness/seal/certificate/continuity-reservation/hidden-bootstrap/transfer-finalize/service-receipt/open protocol or clone. Rolling upgrades begin only afterward. Crash/model tests stop at every reservation, staging write, readiness signature, freeze/mirror, seal acknowledgement, Begin commit/apply, signature lock, continuity-reserved CAS, shard hidden root/barrier, Meta hidden root, transfer finalize, service manifest, continuity/catalog split, Meta finalize/reopen, shard open/reopen/ack, completion, legacy transition, and floor release. They prove one certificate, E-to-E2 exclusivity, one-way rollback, old-writer/old-credential rejection, exact legacy status/replay/cursor behavior, and no mixed-role visibility.

`GlobalStatePayload` is the generated Meta role schema; the following is its checked navigation projection, while `durable_fields.toml` supplies the exact type/reference row for every field: `{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,bootstrap_phase:Genesis|CheckpointInstalled|Operational|OperationalPendingIndependentReopen|RecoveryReconciling|RecoveryAbandoned|RoleTransitionPreparedHidden,role_transition_activation_state_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionActivationState>?,applied_global_logical_command_seq,applied_global_commit_seq,global_logical_hlc_state,global_transaction_marker_head:StrongMarkerRef?,branch_head_map_root,branch_manifest_root,branch_key_epoch_registry_root,key_envelope_registry_root,key_grant_registry_root,global_key_envelope_manifest_root:StrongRef<GlobalKeyEnvelopeManifest>?,branch_merge_ledger_root,catalog_root,schema_roots,topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,id_allocator_root,identity_continuity_record_ref:StrongRef<IdentityContinuityRecord>,global_constraint_state_root,global_constraint_reservation_index_root,global_conflict_index_ref:StrongRef<GlobalConflictIndex>,global_begin_idempotency_index_root:StrongRef<GlobalBeginIdempotencyIndex>,global_attempt_index_root,global_statement_index_root:StrongRef<GlobalStatementIndex>,global_outcome_directory_root,terminal_certification_reservation_root:StrongRef<TerminalCertificationReservationRoot<Meta>>,resource_ledger_root,privacy_ledger_root,privacy_continuity_record_ref:StrongRef<PrivacyContinuityRecord>,dp_request_index_root,policy_root,policy_epoch,revocation_root,revocation_index,replicated_key_wrap_root,signing_key_root,capability_verifier_root,audit_ticket_index_root,audit_root,audit_continuity_record_ref:StrongRef<AuditContinuityRecord>,transparency_root,global_retained_stream_floor,retention_map_root:StrongRef<RetentionMap>,derived_generation_registry_root:StrongRef<DerivedGenerationRegistry>,delivery_lease_registry_root,replay_registry_root,backup_registry_root,restore_state_ref:StrongRef<RestoreState>?,restore_promotion_root_seal_ref:StrongRef<RestorePromotionRootSeal<Meta>>?,gc_decision_root,remote_retention_authority_root:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionObl `RoleTransitionActivationState` is the role union `Meta{migration_nonce,transition_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRoleTransitionRef>,continuity_reservation_receipt_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionContinuityReservationReceipt>,target_service_visibility_epoch,phase:ProjectionPreparedHidden{activation_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef}|ServicePreparedHidden{prepare_certificate_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionMetaServicePrepareCertificate>}}|Shard{migration_nonce,transition_ref,shard_id,continuity_reservation_receipt_ref,target_service_visibility_epoch,phase:ProjectionPreparedHidden{install_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef}|OpenedAwaitingReopen{open_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef}}`. Fresh bootstrap permits `(Genesis,None,None) -> (CheckpointInstalled,Some,None) -> (Operational,Some,Some)`. Restore uses RecoveryReconciling through hidden preparation and then OperationalPendingIndependentReopen through seal installation and fresh reopen; only GlobalRestoreServiceCompletionSpec selects Operational, while explicit abandonment selects RecoveryAbandoned. `GlobalRestoreAbandonFinalizeSpec` alone selects RecoveryAbandoned with no restore-state ref and an `AwaitingSourceRelease::Abandoned` Meta registry; only source-lease renewal/release/finalize and registered tombstone compaction remain legal under `RecoveryCommitCx`. Local activation uses RoleTransitionPreparedHidden, which rejects ordinary work/service until the exact promotion receipt/finalize/open path clears it. Endpoint exposure and Meta routing reject OperationalPendingIndependentReopen; after completion they require the current receipt, Meta reopen evidence, and every destination shard operational ack.

`TerminalPublicOutcome` is the compact, capability-safe, byte-stable posture union `Local{outcome:WriteCommitted{marker_identity:WeakMarkerIdentity,applied_logical_command_seq,applied_commit_seq,final_effect_digest,published_local_delta_frontier,audit_visible_logical_prefix,service_visibility_epoch,original_response_commitment}|Aborted{reason_class,terminal_logical_prefix,release_completion_commitment,audit_visible_logical_prefix,service_visibility_epoch,original_response_commitment}|ReadClosed{applied_logical_command_seq,publication_chain_digest,final_result_digest?,audit_visible_logical_prefix,service_visibility_epoch,original_response_commitment}}|Sharded{outcome:WriteCommitted{marker_identity:WeakMarkerIdentity,applied_global_logical_seq,applied_global_commit_seq,final_effect_digest,published_global_delta_frontier,audit_visible_global_prefix,service_visibility_epoch,original_response_commitment}|Aborted{reason_class,terminal_global_prefix,release_completion_commitment,audit_visible_global_prefix,service_visibility_epoch,original_response_commitment}|ReadClosed{applied_global_logical_seq,publication_chain_digest,final_result_digest?,audit_visible_global_prefix,service_visibility_epoch,original_response_commitment}}`. It contains exactly the fields needed to reproduce the original terminal response and no tenant, principal, hidden participant, topology, or graph-existence fact. `GlobalOutcomeDirectoryValue` is the closed tag `BeginStaging{reservation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalBeginReservationRecord>,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>,staging_generation}|NeverRegisteredDetailed{terminal_record_ref:StrongRef<NeverRegisteredTerminalRecord>,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>,minimum_lookup_retention_floor}|NeverRegisteredCompacted{capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>,summary_root_ref:StrongRef<TerminalAttemptSummaryRoot>,summary_leaf_key_digest,public_response_commitment,minimum_lookup_retention_floor}|CompactedTerminal{capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>,outcome_capability_key:AttemptLookupKey::ByOutcomeCapability,attempt_key:AttemptLookupKey::ByAttempt,summary_root_ref:StrongRef<TerminalAttemptSummaryRoot>,summary_leaf_key_digest,public_outcome:TerminalPublicOutcome::Sharded,minimum_lookup_retention_floor}|ExpiredTombstone{scoped_key_digest,txn_token_digest,capability_commitment,expiry_evidence_digest,expired_at_global_prefix}|LegacyLocal{outcome_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedLegacyLocalArtifactRef<TxnOutcomeRecord>>,source_local_prefix,capability_domain_commitment}|W12{latest_outcome_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnOutcomeRecord>}`. `BeginStaging` is visible only to the validated same-principal outcome capability and reports `BeginStaging`; `NeverRegisteredDetailed -> NeverRegisteredCompacted` preserves identical reason and response bytes. Every nonexpired W12 lineage retains the compact replay object needed to reproduce the originally issued capability; `ExpiredTombstone` is the sole arm that drops that edge. `CompactedTerminal` is the only legal replacement for a selected detailed W12 outcome; its public outcome must byte-match the authenticated summary leaf, so lookup before build, while compaction is pending, and after publication returns the same bytes and visibility epoch. The legacy tag preserves Local-tagged preactivation outcomes without fabricating Global transaction records or cross-group strong edges. Cross-posture outcome decoding is a hard error.

`GlobalTxnRecord` is `{predecessor:ConditionalGlobalCommandRef,command_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnCommand>,decision:Committed|Aborted,assigned_global_logical_command_seq,assigned_global_commit_seq?,global_logical_hlc,marker_ref:StrongMarkerRef?,final_effect_digest,resulting_global_state_payload_digest:WeakDigest}`. `GlobalControlOrigin` is the closed union `Prior{predecessor:ConditionalGlobalCommandRef}|LocalActivationBridge{transition_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRoleTransitionRef>,frozen_local_head:WeakCommandIdentity,Lf,Cf,Hf,local_chain_mmr_checkpoint_projection_digests}|RecoveryBridge{bridge_spec_ref:StrongRef<RecoveryBridgeSpec>,source_manifest_identity:WeakDigest,transform_and_projection_digest}`. `GlobalControlRecord` is `{origin:GlobalControlOrigin,command_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlCommand>,kind,assigned_global_logical_command_seq,global_logical_hlc,result_refs[StrongRef],resulting_global_state_payload_digest:WeakDigest}`. Only the first activation record may use `LocalActivationBridge`; only the first guarded restore record may use `RecoveryBridge`. Their migration/restore floors and certified/archive evidence, not the weak source identities, own required bytes. Fresh Meta genesis has no head, and every later record uses `Prior`. `GlobalStateRoot` is `{payload_ref:StrongRef<GlobalStatePayload>,global_command_head:StrongGlobalCommandRef?}`. Thus every registration, statement registration/publication, admission/cancel/read close, policy/key/topology/GC/remote-retention transition, directory publication, decision-certificate/global-delta publication, activation, and restore bridge enters one contiguous Meta command-record chain.

Shard canonical state is parallel but deliberately nonsemantic: `ShardLogicalStatePayload` is `{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,bootstrap_phase:Genesis|CheckpointInstalled|Operational|OperationalPendingIndependentReopen|RecoveryReconciling|RecoveryAbandoned|RoleTransitionPreparedHidden,role_transition_activation_state_ref:StrongRef<RoleTransitionActivationState>?,shard_id,topology_epoch,partition_state_roots,shard_constraint_state_root,constraint_reservation_index_root,prepared_attempt_root,applied_decision_index_root,terminal_abort_tombstone_root,fragment_delta_batch_index_root:StrongRef<ShardFragmentDeltaBatchIndex>,shard_derived_component_registry_root,shard_key_material_registry_root,active_meta_projection_root:StrongRef<ActiveMetaProjectionRoot>,global_applied_logical_command_seq,global_applied_commit_seq,meta_policy_epoch,meta_revocation_index,meta_key_epoch_commitment,audit_visible_global_prefix,retention_map_root:StrongRef<RetentionMap>,backup_registry_root,restore_state_ref:StrongRef<RestoreState>?,restore_promotion_root_seal_ref:StrongRef<RestorePromotionRootSeal<Shard>>?,remote_retention_authority_root:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionObligationRoot>,remote_retention_consumer_root:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionConsumerRoot>,remote_configuration_trust_root:StrongRef<RemoteConfigurationTrustRoot>,shard_recovery_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<ShardRecoveryCheckpoint>?,shard_config_payload_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardConfigPayloadFloor>?}`; it has fresh three-state bootstrap, hidden role-transition preparation, and restore reconciliation/abandonment. During restore it remains `RecoveryReconciling` through activation, visibility apply, and `ShardRestoreServicePrepareSpec`; those produce hidden `ActivationAppliedHidden`, `VisibilityApplied`, and `ServicePreparedHidden`. `ShardRestoreAbandonApplySpec` alone selects RecoveryAbandoned with no restore-state ref and a registry `AbandonedParticipantComplete`; that phase admits only certified Meta abandonment/source-release/tombstone controls and can never serve. The exact `ShardRestoreServiceOpenSpec` for the same restore, final Meta certificate, and already-issued promotion receipt clears restore state only into `OperationalPendingIndependentReopen::Unsealed`; seal installation and `ShardRestoreReopenConfirmSpec` with a fresh independent proof alone reach Operational, and request admission rejects every pending phase. `ActiveMetaProjectionRoot` is keyed by the generated exhaustive `MetaProjectionSlot` registry, not a five-slot hand list. Every slot value has exactly one source: `Genesis{certificate_ref:StrongRef<ShardedGenesisCertificate>,payload_ref:StrongRef<GenesisMetaProjectionPayload>,projection_digest}|Activation{transition_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRoleTransitionRef>,projection_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedTransitionArtifactRef<LocalToShardProjection>>,payload_ref:StrongRef<ActivationMetaProjectionPayload>,projection_digest}|Control{source_global_control_identity,source_global_prefix,payload:TypedCertifiedMetaProjectionPayload,projection_digest}`. The registry includes every shard-relevant topology, catalog/schema, constraint/owner, branch/head/key/grant, ID-allocation, policy/revocation/audit, retention/trust, derived-generation, backup/restore, GC/reconfiguration, and delivery/frontier effect; each Global control kind has exactly one generated `NoShardEffect{proof rule}` or typed targeted slot-update row. Genesis/activation payloads are typed consumer-local closures constructed after their certificate and contain no raw remote edge. Aggregate scalars byte-match rooted values and are cross-checks only. `ShardConstraintStateRoot` contains aggregate contributions and prepare-keyed reservation refs; prepare installs and decision consumes/releases them. `ShardCommandOrigin` is the closed union `Prior{predecessor:ConditionalShardCommandRef}|RecoveryBridge{bridge_spec_ref:StrongRef<RecoveryBridgeSpec>,source_manifest_identity:WeakDigest,transform_and_projection_digest}`. `ShardCommandRecord` is `{origin:ShardCommandOrigin,shard_raft_index,command:StrongRef<ShardPrepareCommand|ShardDecisionApplyCommand|ShardControlCommand>,result_refs[StrongRef],resulting_shard_payload_digest:WeakDigest}`; only the first guarded restore record uses `RecoveryBridge`, while fresh Genesis has no head and all later records use `Prior`. `ShardLogicalStateRoot` is `{payload_ref:StrongRef<ShardLogicalStatePayload>,shard_command_head:StrongShardCommandRef?}`. Shard order cannot move branch heads or semantic time. Generated checkpoint/floor/backup/GC coverage includes every root above.

Key authority is Meta-owned but ciphertext/envelope material follows its data shard, using an acyclic four-phase protocol. First, `GlobalBranchKeyDistributionPlan {plan_id,operation:Fork|Grant|Rotate,topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,expected_prior_branch_head_and_key_registry_digests,new_branch_and_epoch_record_refs[StrongRef],sorted_per_shard_recipes[{shard_domain:ConsensusDomain,assigned_partition_ranges,expected_envelope_write_key_epochs,material_commitment,recipient_and_wrap_policy,required_remote_grant_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantEvidence>}],complete_shard_range_and_material_commitment,activation_cas,policy_epoch}` is prebuilt without any shard certificate. `GlobalBranchKeyDistributionPlanSpec` orders it and changes only the plan registry to `Distributing`; the new epoch is nonqueryable.

Second, each shard imports a certified-remote plan/typed recipe and orders `ShardKeyMaterialStageSpec {plan_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalBranchKeyDistributionPlan>,own_recipe_index,expected_topology_epoch,expected_shard_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,expected_prior_key_registry_entry,local_envelope_wrap_opener_root_refs[StrongRef],complete_local_material_inventory_ref:StrongRef<KeyMaterialInventory>,payload_availability_certificate_ref:StrongRef<PayloadAvailabilityCertificate>}`. Apply installs `ShardKeyMaterialProjection {plan_identity,graph,branch,envelope_epoch,write_key_epoch,assigned_partition_ranges,local_envelope_wrap_opener_root_refs,availability_floor,status:Staged}`. Staged material cannot satisfy a read, effect basis, prepare, backup-as-active, or current key lookup. The shard then creates purpose-specific `ShardKeyMaterialAvailabilityCertificate {SameGroupCertificateHeader,purpose:StagedAvailability,plan_identity,shard_id,topology_epoch,configuration_identity,staged_projection_ref:StrongRef<ShardKeyMaterialProjection>,exact_partition_and_material_commitment,inventory_root_ref:StrongRef<KeyMaterialInventory>,payload_availability_certificate_ref:StrongRef<PayloadAvailabilityCertificate>,one_digest_signer_lock_ref,quorum_signatures}`.

Third, Meta builds `GlobalKeyEnvelopeManifest {plan_ref:StrongRef<GlobalBranchKeyDistributionPlan>,topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,branch_epoch_registry_candidate_ref:StrongRef,sorted_shard_availability_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardKeyMaterialAvailabilityCertificate>],complete_shard_range_and_material_commitment,meta_grant_root_ref:StrongRef,body_digest:BodyDigest<GlobalKeyEnvelopeManifest>}` and orders `GlobalBranchKeyManifestActivationSpec {plan_ref,manifest_ref:StrongRef<GlobalKeyEnvelopeManifest>,expected_plan_state:Distributing,expected_prior_branch_head_and_key_registry_digests,activation_cas,terminal_audit_gate}`. The registered body transcript excludes only `body_digest`. Apply verifies one matching certificate for every and only planned shard/range, atomically activates the branch/key epoch, and moves the replaced epoch to `Retiring`; it never creates material. Fourth, each shard consumes the generated typed Meta projection through `ShardKeyMaterialActivateSpec`, byte-matches plan/manifest/material commitment, and changes only its matching `Staged -> Active` entry. Reads/effects/prepares require both the Active local entry and an active-Meta-projection prefix at or beyond activation. Old material remains Active/Retiring and retained until every dependent operation and replacement acknowledgement closes.

Zero-reference is a different certificate kind, never an availability flag. `GlobalKeyDestroyAckRef` is the closed union `Backup{ack_ref:StrongRef<BackupKeyReleaseAck>}|LegalHold{ack_ref:StrongRef<LegalHoldReleaseAck>}|RemoteConsumer{ack_ref:StrongRef<RemoteKeyConsumerReleaseAck>}`. `GlobalKeyDestructionAuthorizationSpec` is `{destruction_id,key_epoch_and_material_set,expected_global_state:WeakStateIdentity,meta_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,expected_branch_key_envelope_and_grant_registry_digests,exact_target_plan:{meta_local:None|Some{material_set,generated_root_inventory_ref:StrongRef<KeyReferenceInventory>,zero_reference_proof_ref:StrongRef<ZeroReferenceProof>,external_operation_plan},sorted_shards[{shard_id,authority_domain,assigned_ranges,material_set,expected_active_or_retiring_projection_digest,external_operation_plan}],complete_meta_shard_range_and_material_coverage_digest},backup_legal_hold_remote_consumer_ack_refs[GlobalKeyDestroyAckRef],expected_state_conditions,terminal_audit_gate}`. Apply atomically changes the global lifecycle `Retiring -> DestroyAuthorized`, installs a global no-new-reference quarantine, and, for Meta-local material, durably creates `MetaExternalKeyDestructionOperationRecord::Requested` before any physical call. After its audit mirror, Meta creates `GlobalKeyDestructionAuthorizationCertificate {SameGroupCertificateHeader,destruction_id,authorization_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,key_epoch_and_material_set,topology_and_configuration_identity,exact_target_commitment,global_quarantine_generation,meta_zero_reference_commitment,one_digest_signer_lock_ref,quorum_signatures}`.

Each planned shard orders `ShardKeyZeroReferenceSpec {authorization_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalKeyDestructionAuthorizationCertificate>,expected_shard_state:WeakStateIdentity,expected_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,expected_topology_epoch,expected_local_key_registry_state:Active|Retiring,exact_material_and_range_set,current_complete_generated_root_inventory_ref:StrongRef<KeyReferenceInventory>,current_zero_reference_proof_ref:StrongRef<ZeroReferenceProof>,quarantine_body_recipe}`. Apply byte-matches the plan, atomically installs the local no-new-reference quarantine and `DestroyAuthorized`, and creates a local record. Only afterward may its quorum create `ShardKeyZeroReferenceCertificate {SameGroupCertificateHeader,purpose:ZeroReference,destruction_authorization_identity,key_epoch_and_material_set,not_before_global_prefix,basis_shard_state_root_ref:StrongRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,basis_checkpoint_floor_and_history_digests,basis_prepared_certificate_backup_replay_cursor_grant_topology_gc_root_digests,complete_scanned_root_set_commitment,zero_reference_proof_ref:StrongRef<ZeroReferenceProof>,quarantine_generation,one_digest_signer_lock_ref,quorum_signatures}`. The certificate is valid only while every named current root, configuration, prefix, and quarantine generation remains byte-identical.

`ShardKeyDestroyApplySpec` is `{authorization_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalKeyDestructionAuthorizationCertificate>,zero_reference_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ShardKeyZeroReferenceCertificate>,expected_current_shard_state:WeakStateIdentity,expected_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,expected_topology_epoch,expected_quarantine_generation,current_inventory_equality_and_no_new_reference_proof_ref:StrongRef<NoNewKeyReferenceProof>,sorted_external_operation_plans[{operation_id,idempotency_token_digest,target_storage_member_or_kms,canonical_request_transcript_digest}],post_apply_registry_body_recipe}`. Apply rechecks the complete current inventory and changes only the authorized set `DestroyAuthorized -> Destroying`, durably creating one `ShardExternalKeyDestructionOperationRecord::Requested` per planned target before calls. `ShardKeyPhysicalDestructionCompletionSpec` is `{authorization_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalKeyDestructionAuthorizationCertificate>,destroy_apply_record_ref:StrongRef<ShardCommandRecord>,expected_destroying_state:WeakStateIdentity,expected_quarantine_generation,operation_record_refs[StrongRef<ShardExternalKeyDestructionOperationRecord>],authenticated_member_and_kms_receipt_refs[StrongRef<AuthenticatedKeyDestructionReceipt>],current_inventory_equality_and_no_new_reference_proof_ref:StrongRef<NoNewKeyReferenceProof>,replicated_wrap_key_inventory_erasure_verification_ref:StrongRef<KeyErasureVerification>,storage_member_completion_quorum_ref:StrongRef<StorageMemberPhysicalCompletionQuorum>,post_destroy_registry_body_recipe}`. Apply verifies exact operation/receipt bijection and changes `Destroying -> Destroyed`; then the quorum creates `ShardKeyPhysicalDestructionCompletionCertificate {SameGroupCertificateHeader,destruction_id,authorization_identity,shard_id,material_and_range_set,quarantine_generation,destroy_apply_identity,operation_and_receipt_commitment,erasure_verification_digest,post_destruction_state_root_ref:StrongRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,one_digest_signer_lock_ref,quorum_signatures}`.

`GlobalKeyDestructionCompletionSpec` is `{authorization_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,authorization_certificate_ref:StrongRef<GlobalKeyDestructionAuthorizationCertificate>,expected_global_destroy_authorized_state:WeakStateIdentity,current_meta_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,current_topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,current_global_inventory_and_no_new_reference_proof_ref:StrongRef<NoNewKeyReferenceProof>,meta_operation_record_and_receipt_refs[MetaKeyPhysicalCompletionEvidence],exact_sorted_shard_completion_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardKeyPhysicalDestructionCompletionCertificate>],complete_planned_target_bijection_proof_ref:StrongRef<TargetCompletionBijectionProof>,terminal_audit_gate}`. `MetaKeyPhysicalCompletionEvidence` is the closed pair `{operation_record_ref:StrongRef<MetaExternalKeyDestructionOperationRecord>,receipt_ref:StrongRef<AuthenticatedKeyDestructionReceipt>,erasure_verification_ref:StrongRef<KeyErasureVerification>}`. Apply reaches global Destroyed only when every and only planned Meta target and shard/range has physical completion evidence under the current topology/configuration and the global quarantine still forbids references. Any new prepared owner, backup, replay, cursor, grant, topology/configuration proposal, checkpoint, or root invalidates equality and forces a new authorized generation. Floors retain every Staged, Active, Retiring, DestroyAuthorized, Destroying, operation, receipt, and certificate state. Crash tests stop at every quarantine, operation-record, call, receipt, apply, signature, and completion boundary, including partial KMS/member failure.

`CheckpointStateVector` is one top-level content-addressed role-tagged object `{schema_version,payload_schema_oid,role:Local{entries[LocalPayloadFieldTag->CheckpointFieldRecipe]}|Meta{entries[GlobalPayloadFieldTag->CheckpointFieldRecipe]}|Shard{shard_id,entries[ShardPayloadFieldTag->CheckpointFieldRecipe]},coverage_bitmap,projection_digest}`; field tags come from the generated payload schema and cannot cross roles. `CheckpointFieldRecipe` is the closed union `CopiedStrong|ProjectedSnapshot|ResetByCheckpointInstall|SelfExcluded|InstallProvisionalCut|ApplyActivationProjection` with the exact per-tag literals defined below. `GlobalRecoveryCheckpoint` is `{basis:Genesis|Global{basis_global_logical_command_seq,basis_global_commit_seq,covered_global_command:WeakGlobalCommandIdentity?,covered_global_marker:StrongMarkerRef?}|LocalActivation{transition_commitment,frozen_local_head:WeakCommandIdentity,Lf,Cf,Hf,local_projection_digest},basis_payload_digest:WeakDigest,basis_projection_digest,global_logical_hlc_state,topology_epoch,global_checkpoint_state_vector_ref:StrongRef<CheckpointStateVector>,nonretaining_predecessor_checkpoint_digest}`. `ShardRecoveryCheckpoint` is `{shard_id,basis:Genesis|Shard{basis_shard_raft_index,basis_global_logical_command_seq,basis_global_commit_seq,covered_shard_command:WeakShardCommandIdentity?}|LocalActivationProjection{transition_commitment,local_to_shard_projection_digest,Lf,Cf,Hf},topology_epoch,basis_shard_payload_digest,basis_projection_digest,shard_checkpoint_state_vector_ref:StrongRef<CheckpointStateVector>,nonretaining_predecessor_checkpoint_digest}`. Each vector has exactly one entry per field of its matching payload schema. The provisional tag is required exactly for operational replacement retention maps; `ApplyActivationProjection` is legal only under the matching activation basis and classifies every destination field from the pre-certified body recipe without a future result OID. Fresh Genesis forbids both. Checkpoint/floor fields use exact literals. Generated coverage and DAG checkers reject any role mismatch, mixed basis, omitted field, future ref, or result recipe mismatch.

Recovery treats every checkpoint as the **post-install** payload. Ordinary Local/Meta basis `(L0,C0)` reconstructs sequence `L0+1`, commit `C0`, deterministic install HLC, literals/resets/provisional cut, verifies the unique retained install input/record, then replays `L0+2..head`; ordinary Shard basis `R0` analogously reconstructs `R0+1`. LocalActivation reconstructs the first Meta activation at `Lf+1/Cf`; LocalActivationProjection reconstructs the first shard projection-install result at its declared shard index and `Lf/Cf`. In each case the transition certificate/projection recipe and retained input/record are the unique witness; recovery never reapplies it. Double apply, missing/duplicate install, mixed basis, scalar/reset/projection mismatch, or pairing with another root fails closed.

`MetaConfigPayloadFloor` is the exact schema `{schema_version,payload_schema_oid,protocol_registry_epoch,basis_global_state:WeakStateIdentity,basis_global_logical_command_seq,basis_global_commit_seq,basis_meta_raft_index,closed_through_meta_raft_index,closed_through_global_logical_command_seq,current_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,prospective_joint_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>?,prospective_final_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,failure_domain_policy_ref:StrongRef,current_checkpoint:WeakCheckpointIdentity,checkpoint_state_vector_digest:WeakDigest,retained_global_command_suffix_endpoints,retained_global_marker_suffix_endpoints,mandatory_inventory_root:StrongRef<MandatoryInventory>,begin_status_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaBeginStatusFloor>,attempt_family_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaAttemptFamilyFloor>,statement_result_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaStatementResultFloor>,conflict_overlap_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaConflictOverlapFloor>,attempt_compaction_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaAttemptCompactionProtocolFloor>,audit_claim_signer_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaAuditClaimSignerFloor>,prepared_owner_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaPreparedOwnerFloor>,certificate_ledger_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaCertificateFloor>,decision_publication_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaDecisionPublicationFloor>,delta_publication_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaDeltaPublicationFloor>,retention_cut_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaRetentionCutFloor>,remote_trust_release_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaRemoteTrustReleaseFloor>,key_lifecycle_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaKeyLifecycleFloor>,derived_generation_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaDerivedGenerationFloor>,gc_protocol_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaGcProtocolFloor>,backup_protocol_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaBackupProtocolFloor>,restore_protocol_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaRestoreProtocolFloor>,activation_retirement_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaActivationRetirementFloor>,continuity_service_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaContinuityServiceFloor>,reconfiguration_topology_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaReconfigurationTopologyFloor>,shard_checkpoint_directory_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaShardCheckpointDirectoryFloor>,shard_apply_ack_directory_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaShardApplyAckDirectoryFloor>,coverage_bitmap,nonretaining_predecessor_floor_digest:WeakDigest}`.

The Meta protocol floors are closed projections, not category bags. `MetaBeginStatusFloor` covers every Reserved/Bound/Detailed/Compacted begin-key entry, outcome-capability directory value, staging resource, terminal-pending postcondition set, and public-status proof through its advertised lookup floor. `MetaAttemptFamilyFloor` covers the family/generation/token/attempt/outcome directory and every Active or PrepareAdmitted attempt. `MetaStatementResultFloor` covers the statement index, cumulative witness roots, buffered spill manifests, delivery leases, publication chain, and statement summaries. `MetaConflictOverlapFloor` covers every live dependency edge and overlap-close proof. `MetaAttemptCompactionProtocolFloor` covers the terminal summary, `PendingAttemptCompactionRoot`, authoritative floor, build closure, signer lock, attestation, publication, audit mirror, and independent obligations. `MetaAuditClaimSignerFloor` covers pending/claimed tickets, owners, terminal-attempt records, signer locks, candidate fences, external-CAS receipts, and mirrors. `MetaDecisionPublicationFloor` covers decision construction, signer lock, certificate, publication, shard audit projection, and post-mirror ack directory; `MetaDeltaPublicationFloor` covers each committed `GlobalLogicalDeltaBatch`, its index, publication record, and contiguous frontier. The remaining exact floors respectively cover provisional plus activated cuts; remote trust/grants/all six release stages; key plan/staged-certificate imports/active manifest/zero-reference/durable destruction/physical completion; distributed derived generations; GC preflights/authorization/quarantine/member receipts/Meta and shard physical completion/`PartialBlocking`; backup intent/pins/shard closures/manifest publication/release authorization/acks/finalize; `RestoreSourceLease`, reconciliation, activation/visibility acks, service promotion and catalog receipt; fresh-sharded Genesis or LocalActivation, migration authority transfer, retirement authorization/certificate/acks/finalize; incarnation continuity and service-visibility state; and configuration/prepared transfer/topology movement. Imported entries are consumer-local CRSR/evidence only.

`ShardConfigPayloadFloor` is the exact schema `{schema_version,payload_schema_oid,protocol_registry_epoch,shard_id,topology_epoch,basis_shard_state:WeakStateIdentity,basis_shard_raft_index,basis_global_logical_command_seq,basis_global_commit_seq,closed_through_shard_raft_index,closed_through_global_logical_command_seq,current_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,prospective_joint_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>?,prospective_final_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,failure_domain_policy_ref:StrongRef,current_checkpoint:WeakCheckpointIdentity,checkpoint_state_vector_digest:WeakDigest,retained_shard_command_suffix_endpoints,mandatory_inventory_root:StrongRef<MandatoryInventory>,prepared_attempt_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardPreparedAttemptFloor>,imported_read_statement_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardImportedReadStatementFloor>,fragment_decision_ack_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardFragmentDecisionAckFloor>,active_meta_projection_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardActiveMetaProjectionFloor>,retention_cut_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardRetentionCutFloor>,key_lifecycle_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardKeyLifecycleFloor>,derived_component_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardDerivedComponentFloor>,gc_protocol_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardGcProtocolFloor>,backup_protocol_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardBackupProtocolFloor>,restore_protocol_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardRestoreProtocolFloor>,remote_trust_release_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardRemoteTrustReleaseFloor>,topology_reconfiguration_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardTopologyReconfigurationFloor>,queryable_history_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardQueryableHistoryFloor>,continuity_service_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardContinuityServiceFloor>,certificate_ledger_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardCertificateFloor>,coverage_bitmap,nonretaining_predecessor_floor_digest:WeakDigest}`. Those floors respectively retain prepared attempts/reservations/ownership transfers; imported registration/statement/read bases and cumulative-witness obligations through publication/close; fragment batches, decision-publication input, audit projection and post-mirror ack; the exhaustive active Meta projection; provisional/activated cuts; every `Staged|Active|Retiring|DestroyAuthorized|Destroying` key object plus zero/physical receipts; derived components; GC preflight/quarantine/member physical receipts/completion; backup pin/closure/release; restore hidden activation/visibility/service promotion/operational ack; remote trust/grants/release; topology copy/configuration/prepared transfer; complete history needed by the advertised interval; and incarnation/service epoch. Every floor field and subfloor field has one `durable_fields.toml` row. Missing, duplicate, wrong-role, raw-cross-group, unactivated, or predecessor-retaining coverage fails G0.

`MetaCheckpointCertificate` is a meta-group object `{SameGroupCertificateHeader,global_recovery_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<GlobalRecoveryCheckpoint>,basis_global_prefix:{logical,commit},install_global_prefix:{logical=basis.logical+1,commit=basis.commit},install_meta_raft_index,checkpoint_install_record_ref:StrongGlobalCommandRef,installed_global_state_root_ref:StrongRef<GlobalStateRoot>,meta_config_payload_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaConfigPayloadFloor>?,log_to_state_proof_digest,certificate_ledger_floor,quorum_signatures}`. Header configuration/predicate are the sole configuration fields. `ShardHistoryInventory` is `{shard_id,topology_epoch,queryable_global_prefix_interval,partition_version_roots[StrongRef],key_epoch_roots[StrongRef],tombstone_and_hole_roots[StrongRef],retention_lease_roots[StrongRef],body_digest:BodyDigest<ShardHistoryInventory>}`; its registered transcript excludes only `body_digest`. `ShardCheckpointCertificate` is `{SameGroupCertificateHeader,shard_id,topology_epoch,basis_shard_raft_index,install_shard_raft_index=basis+1,basis_global_prefix,install_global_prefix,checkpoint_install_record_ref:StrongShardCommandRef,queryable_global_prefix_interval,installed_shard_state_root_ref:StrongRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,shard_recovery_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<ShardRecoveryCheckpoint>,shard_config_payload_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardConfigPayloadFloor>?,retained_history_inventory_ref:StrongRef<ShardHistoryInventory>,payload_availability_certificate_ref:StrongRef<PayloadAvailabilityCertificate>,log_to_state_proof_digest,certificate_ledger_floor,quorum_signatures}`. Genesis certificates require the optional floor `None`; Operational certificates require `Some`. The interval is valid only when the inventory proves every MVCC version/key needed for each included prefix. A database snapshot at `P` requires the meta root at `P` and, for every routed shard, a certified checkpoint whose queryable interval contains `P`; “checkpoint at or beyond P” alone is insufficient.

`MetaRelevanceRangeProof` is `{SameGroupCertificateHeader,target_shard_id,prior_global_prefix:{logical,commit},resulting_global_prefix:{logical,commit},sorted_command_entries[{global_logical_seq,command_kind,terminal_kind:Control|CommittedTxn|AbortedTxn,assigned_global_commit_seq?,routing_or_scope_commitment,generated_meta_effect_class,affected_projection_slots,topology_epoch,policy_epoch,revocation_index,key_epoch_commitment,audit_fence_effect}],irrelevance_checker_version,result:Irrelevant,quorum_signatures}`. Entries are contiguous and exhaustive from `prior.logical+1` through `resulting.logical`; commit sequence increments exactly on `CommittedTxn` and is unchanged on controls/aborts. The generated `MetaControlEffect` registry must classify every entry, and Irrelevant is legal only when every row is `NoShardEffect` for this target and no transaction data, topology/catalog/schema/constraint/branch/key/ID/security/audit/retention/trust/derived/backup/restore/GC/reconfiguration/delivery effect applies. Any targeted slot or data effect requires its typed apply command.

`MetaCertificateLedger` and `ShardCertificateLedger` are replica-local immutable maps rooted by the role's `RaftStateRoot`. Each entry is `{certificate_kind,certificate_ref:StrongRef,authority_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,subject_identity,base_closure_inventory_digest,first_required_index,release_condition,successor_or_publication_status}`; a successor may strengthen but never shorten its closure or release condition. Meta ledgers retain un-published global decisions and remote-reference availability promises; shard ledgers retain prepare/checkpoint/applied-ack certificates. A certificate may leave the ledger only after its canonical publication/replacement is rooted and every named consumer/configuration/GC floor has acknowledged that transfer. The matching config floor and Raft snapshot carry the ledger floor, so log truncation cannot orphan a certificate between creation and publication.

Prepared roots are three distinct top-level kinds sharing a generated header but no cross-role entry union. `PreparedRootHeader<Role> = {database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,group_role:Role,group_id,configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,payload_predicate_digest,published_under_fence_epoch,root_generation,nonretaining_predecessor_digest}`. `LocalPreparedRootEntry = Owned{ownership_id,record_ref:StrongRef<PreparedCommitRecord>}|Transferring{transfer_record_ref:StrongRef<LocalPreparedOwnershipTransferRecord>}|Transferred{new_ownership_id,new_record_ref:StrongRef<PreparedCommitRecord>,transfer_identity:WeakDigest}`; Meta and Shard specialize every record/transfer ref to `MetaPreparedCommandRecord`/`MetaPreparedOwnershipTransferRecord` and `ShardPreparedPayloadRecord`/`ShardPreparedOwnershipTransferRecord`. `LocalPreparedPayloadRoot {header:PreparedRootHeader<Local>,entries[stable_command_identity->LocalPreparedRootEntry]}`, `MetaPreparedPayloadRoot {header:PreparedRootHeader<Meta>,entries[attempt_or_control_identity->MetaPreparedRootEntry]}`, and `ShardPreparedPayloadRoot {header:PreparedRootHeader<Shard{shard_id}>,entries[ShardCommandIdentity->ShardPreparedRootEntry]}` are separate object kinds; a cross-role key, record, or transfer tag is unencodable.

Each role-specific `PreparedOwnershipTransferRecord<Role>` is `{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,group_role,group_id,old_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,new_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,payload_predicate_digest,old_ownership_id,new_ownership_id,old_record_ref:StrongRef<RoleRecord>,new_record_ref:StrongRef<RoleRecord>,identical_base_closure_inventory_digest,old_current_closure_inventory_digest,new_superset_closure_inventory_digest,old/new availability_certificate_refs[StrongRef],command_status:Preparing|Receipted|Ordered{raft_index}|CommittedUnapplied|AuditFenced,transition_phase:Joint|New|RetirementAcknowledged,transition_floor_ref:StrongRef,raft_snapshot_acknowledgement,transfer_digest}`. Reconfiguration atomically changes `Owned(old)` to `Transferring` only after the new owner exists and has the same base plus superset closure, then to `Transferred/Owned(new)` after the exact transition floor and Raft/snapshot acknowledgement. Old ownership releases only after canonical applied/certificate state or completed transfer owns everything; abandonment requires fenced proof of non-order. Ordinarily the root fence epoch equals the manifest. The sole takeover exception preserves the exact epoch-E root OID/entries under E+1 via the takeover proof, then the first ordinary successor reheaders unchanged entries at E+1 before mutation. New records/receipts require E+1; old records remain obligations. Crash tests cover every role and transfer phase for Preparing/Receipted/Ordered/committed-unapplied/audit-fenced states.

Replica-local `MetaPreparedCommandRecord` is `{prepared_ownership_id,record_generation,predecessor_ref:StrongRef<MetaPreparedCommandRecord>?,database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,group_role:Meta,group_id,configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,payload_predicate_digest,local_writer_fence_epoch,attempt_or_control_identity,base_closure_inventory_digest,current_closure_inventory_digest,strong_local_refs[StrongRef],certified_remote_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef],exact_realizations[],command_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnCommand|GlobalControlCommand>?,status:Preparing|Receipted|Ordered{raft_index}|Applied{global_logical_command_seq}|Abandoned{fence_and_nonorder_proof}}`; ownership IDs, receipts, and successors bind the full domain/config/predicate header, preserve the base, and strengthen current closure. `MetaPreCommandBaseAvailabilityCertificate` begins `SameGroupCertificateHeader` and carries `{prepared_ownership_id,attempt_or_control_identity,base_closure_inventory_digest,sorted_payload_receipts,covered_object_kinds,exclusion_rule:Exactly{ThisCertificate,FutureMetaCommand,OrderAttemptSupplement}}`. It covers only already-built stable semantic evidence/base closure and excludes itself, the future command, and repeatable order/HLC supplements. Each proposal separately builds `MetaOrderAttemptInput` plus `MetaOrderAttemptAvailabilityCertificate`; voters revalidate its source signatures/set epoch, quorum, age, uncertainty, normalization, expected next sequence, and forward-jump policy against current state. Stale or sequence-losing evidence retires only that provably unordered supplement and may be replaced without changing semantic prepared ownership or audit bytes. After command construction, every proposer root-publishes the stable-owner successor that adds it.

Replica-local `ShardPreparedPayloadRecord` is `{prepared_ownership_id,record_generation,predecessor_ref:StrongRef<ShardPreparedPayloadRecord>?,database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,group_role:Shard{shard_id},group_id,configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,payload_predicate_digest,local_writer_fence_epoch,shard_command_identity:ShardCommandIdentity,base_closure_inventory_digest,current_closure_inventory_digest,strong_local_refs[StrongRef],certified_remote_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef],exact_realizations[],command_ref:StrongRef<ShardPrepareCommand|ShardDecisionApplyCommand|ShardControlCommand>?,status:Preparing|Receipted|Ordered{raft_index}|Applied{shard_raft_index}|Abandoned{fence_and_nonorder_proof}}`. Ownership IDs and receipts bind the entire domain/config/predicate header. `ShardPreCommandBaseAvailabilityCertificate` begins `SameGroupCertificateHeader` and carries `{prepared_ownership_id,shard_command_identity,base_closure_inventory_digest,sorted_payload_receipts,covered_object_kinds,exclusion_rule:Exactly{ThisCertificate,FutureShardCommand}}`. For prepare, generated coverage includes exact basis/fragment/admission closure formerly called `ShardPayloadAvailabilityCertificate`; that name is an alias, not a second certificate. Decision-apply and every payload-bearing shard control use the same exact-configuration D1 barrier. A stable-owner successor adds the completed command before proposal. Replica fence epochs never enter canonical semantic objects.

`AuthorityPermitRef` is the closed durable tag `ReadOnly{permit_ref:StrongRef<ReadPermitRecord>}|ReadWrite{permit_ref:StrongRef<MutationPermitRecord>}`. Its read projection is the exact `ReadCapablePermitRef = DedicatedRead{permit_ref:StrongRef<ReadPermitRecord>}|MutationReadProjection{permit_ref:StrongRef<MutationPermitRecord>,projected_read_scope_digest}`. The second arm is legal only when the digest is generated from the mutation permit's exact read bindings, snapshot, query/operator/disclosure scope, result-contract ceiling, policy epoch, revocation index, and service visibility epoch; it is never an empty-effect mutation authorization. Cross-group export uses `ImportedReadCapablePermitEvidence = DedicatedRead{permit_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,registration_field_tag}|MutationReadProjection{permit_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,registration_field_tag,projected_read_scope_digest}` and must match the permit field exported from the certified registration. `AuditTicketOwner` is the closed tag `Operation{global_txn_id,registration_generation,operation_request_basis_commitment}|Statement{global_txn_id,registration_generation,statement_seq,statement_idempotency_key,statement_request_basis_commitment}|Control{control_request_identity}`. `AuditResolutionOrigin` is `Unclaimed{admission_record_ref:AppliedControlRef,request_basis_commitment,terminal_class:DeniedBeforeClaim|AbandonedBeforeClaim}|Claimed{claim_record_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicketClaimRecord>,owner:AuditTicketOwner,request_basis_commitment}`. `AuditTicketIndexValue` is the monotone state machine `PendingUnclaimed{ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,admission_record_ref:AppliedControlRef,request_basis_commitment}|Claimed{ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,claim_record_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicketClaimRecord>,owner:AuditTicketOwner,request_basis_commitment}|Resolved{ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,origin:AuditResolutionOrigin,event_ref:StrongRef<AuditEventRecord>,resolution_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicketResolution>,external_cas_receipt_ref:StrongRef<AuditExternalCasReceipt>}`. Only `PendingUnclaimed -> Claimed -> Resolved(origin=Claimed)` or the no-effect pre-claim `PendingUnclaimed -> Resolved(origin=Unclaimed)` is legal. Byte-identical retry returns the same value; mismatched admission/claim/owner/origin fails, and a ticket can never be claimed by two attempts/statements or resolved for another owner.

`OperationAuditAdmission` is `NotRequired{evidence:NonRequiredAuditEvidence}|PendingUnclaimed{ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,ticket_admission_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,operation_request_basis_commitment}|Claimed{ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,claim_record_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicketClaimRecord>,owner:{global_txn_id,registration_generation},operation_request_basis_commitment}`. `GlobalAttemptRegistrationSpec` accepts only `NotRequired` or `PendingUnclaimed`; registration apply atomically transforms the latter into `Claimed` and creates `AuditTicketClaimRecord {ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,owner:AuditTicketOwner::Operation,request_basis_commitment,claiming_control_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlCommand>,claimed_at_global_logical_command_seq}` before constructing the registration/payload. Every later read, statement publication, admission, cancel, commit, abort, or read-close must carry or derive the exact Claimed value from that registration. The claim remains unresolved until the one terminal attempt read-close/commit/abort event. A pre-registration denial or abandoned BEGIN is one semantic mutation—creation of the capability-visible NeverRegistered outcome—so only `GlobalBeginTerminalSpec` may resolve its exact `PendingUnclaimed` ticket and publish that candidate; `AuditTerminalSpec` remains reserved for terminal paths that create no other durable semantic mutation.

Registration and prepare admission are distinct lifecycle-scaffolding rows. A `GlobalBeginReservationSpec`, `GlobalAttemptRegistrationSpec`, or `AuditTerminalFreezeSpec::Arm` exists before the operation claim it may atomically create, so its wrapper is exactly `NotRequired{evidence:LifecycleScaffolding{decision_ref,registered_scaffolding_spec_tag,scaffolding_body_digest,parent_operation_claim_commitment?,compatibility_row_id}}`; the decision is prebuilt against the pending-ticket/request basis and the registered atomic-claim recipe and never points to the future claim. After registration has produced a claim, `GlobalPrepareAdmissionSpec` may use `NotRequired{evidence:CoveredByParentClaim{claim_ref,coverage_rule_id=LifecycleScaffoldingCoveredByOperationTicket,covered_body_digest}}`. Neither form resolves the operation ticket. The typed evidence byte-matches operation tag, pending admission or claim owner, request/body basis, audit epoch, policy, and revocation state. Arm/claim substitution and any pre-order reference to a future claim are G0-invalid and have negative DAG fixtures. Nonterminal statement results use distinct statement tickets below, never the operation ticket. A completeness profile that requires separate registration/admission events supplies distinct tickets and registered lifecycle tags; negotiation fails rather than overloading a claimed ticket.

BEGIN has its own durable, idempotent lineage before an attempt exists. `TxnOutcomeCapabilityFields` is the shared exact inline value `{header:DurableCapabilityHeader{capability_kind=TxnOutcome},body:{request_kind:ExplicitBegin|AutocommitExecute,scoped_request_idempotency_key_digest,txn_token,outcome_capability_key},mac}`; the body key is pre-minted, every header/body field and MAC byte exists before ordering, and `capability_commitment` is the domain-separated digest of those canonical bytes. `GlobalBeginIdempotencyIndex` maps `(database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,tenant,principal,scoped_begin_idempotency_key)` to exactly `Reserved{reservation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalBeginReservationRecord>,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>}|BoundDetailed{registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,reservation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalBeginReservationRecord>,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>}|BoundCompacted{summary_root_ref:StrongRef<TerminalAttemptSummaryRoot>,leaf_key_digest,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>}|NeverRegisteredDetailed{terminal_record_ref:StrongRef<NeverRegisteredTerminalRecord>,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>,audit_terminal_commitment}|NeverRegisteredCompacted{summary_root_ref:StrongRef<TerminalAttemptSummaryRoot>,summary_leaf_key_digest,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>}|ExpiredTombstone{scoped_key_digest,txn_token_digest,capability_commitment,expiry_evidence_digest}`. `GlobalBeginReservationSpec` is the sequence-neutral pre-order body `{scoped_begin_idempotency_key,canonical_begin_request_digest,operation_class,isolation,transaction_error_policy,tenant,principal,non_widenable_authority_digest,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,service_visibility_epoch,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>,operation_audit_admission:OperationAuditAdmission::PendingUnclaimed|NotRequired,expected_begin_index_absence_proof,staging_resource_reservation_ref:StrongRef<ResourceLedgerTransition>,terminal_audit_gate:LifecycleScaffoldingNotRequired}`. The replay object's capability header/body/request kind/key/domain/authority/policy/revocation/profile/window byte-match the request and admission; no command trusts a duplicate inline encoding. Apply creates `GlobalBeginReservationRecord {source_spec_ref:StrongRef<GlobalBeginReservationSpec>,applied_control_ref:AppliedControlRef,canonical_begin_request_digest,txn_token,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>,capability_commitment,operation_audit_admission:OperationAuditAdmission::PendingUnclaimed|NotRequired,reserved_at_global_prefix,staging_generation}` and atomically installs `Reserved` plus `GlobalOutcomeDirectoryValue::BeginStaging` with that same replay ref; only then may Fabric emit `BEGIN_ACCEPTED`. A byte-identical retry returns the replay object's identical canonical capability bytes even after key rotation, while a same key with any request, admission, authority, epoch, profile/window, or policy drift fails. Verifier key and accepted time profile remain rooted through the capability lookup/expiry floor.
