Registration must consume the exact reservation and atomically change `Reserved -> BoundDetailed`; no later command may return it to staging. `BeginRegionClosedReceipt` is the authenticated runtime record `{database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,service_visibility_epoch,session_binding,session_region_id,reservation_identity,canonical_request_digest,observed_region_close_generation,no_registration_worker_or_acceptance_response_obligation_proof_digest,issuer_id,key_epoch,signature}` and is distinct from result-delivery `SessionRegionCloseReceipt`. `BeginTerminalEvidence` is the role-checked closed union `Denied{authorization_decision_ref:StrongRef<AuthorizationDecisionRecord>,stable_denial_class}|AuthenticatedAbandon{request_ref:StrongRef<AuthenticatedBeginAbandonRequest>,request_idempotency_key}|RegionClosed{receipt_ref:StrongRef<BeginRegionClosedReceipt>}|Superseded{request_ref:StrongRef<AuthenticatedBeginSupersedeRequest>,request_idempotency_key,new_request_commitment}`. Its generated compatibility table maps exactly Denied->DeniedBeforeRegistration, RegionClosed->BeginDisconnected, AuthenticatedAbandon->AbandonedStaging, and Superseded->SupersededRetry; every arm binds the same session/principal/authority/reservation/request and includes a typed no-registration/effect/response proof. Time passage, socket suspicion, process death, or a result-delivery receipt inhabits no arm.

`LocalBeginTerminalSpec` is `{reservation_ref:StrongRef<LocalBeginReservationRecord>,expected_index_value:Reserved,evidence:BeginTerminalEvidence::Local,reason_class,operation_audit_admission:LocalOperationAuditAdmission::PendingUnclaimed|NotRequired,staging_resource_release_refs[StrongRef<ResourceLedgerTransition>],terminal_audit_freeze:AuditFreezeField::Required<LocalBeginTerminal>,terminal_audit_gate}`. `GlobalBeginTerminalSpec` is `{reservation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalBeginReservationRecord>,expected_index_value:Reserved,evidence:BeginTerminalEvidence::Meta,reason_class,operation_audit_admission:OperationAuditAdmission::PendingUnclaimed|NotRequired,staging_resource_release_refs[StrongRef<ResourceLedgerTransition>],terminal_audit_freeze:AuditFreezeField::Required<MetaBeginTerminal>,terminal_audit_gate}`. Admission, evidence, reason, and freeze must byte-match the reservation exactly. Apply resolves that exact ticket when present and creates the role's compactable NeverRegistered record; Meta creates `NeverRegisteredTerminalRecord {reservation_identity:WeakDigest,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>,capability_commitment,reason_class,terminal_global_prefix,audit_terminal_commitment,original_response_commitment}` plus detailed index/directory entries. Neither role creates an attempt, attempt family/key, conflict, prepared, statement, or shard entry. `NeverRegisteredFloorSpec` later rewrites Meta Detailed to Compacted after proving that this reservation never bound or escaped; `GlobalOutcomeExpirySpec` then atomically rewrites both outcome-directory and begin-index leaves to permanent capability/key `ExpiredTombstone` only with matching `TimeValidationEvidence::Expired`, verifier/profile floors, terminal proof, and retention cut. Neither step requires the index being rewritten to be absent, and neither fabricates an attempt identity.

`AttemptFamilyState` is the authenticated Meta map value `{global_txn_id,latest_generation,latest_state:Active{registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>}|PrepareAdmitted{outcome_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnOutcomeRecord>}|Terminal{outcome_or_summary_ref:StrongRef},active_generation:None|Some{generation},latest_token_digest,successor_eligibility_floor}`. NeverRegistered is exclusively a terminal begin-key/outcome-directory state and never creates or advances an attempt family. `TransactionErrorPolicy` is the closed v1 union `AbortTransactionOnStatementError|ContinueOnDeclaredRecoverable{recoverable_error_class_table_oid}`; unsupported savepoint/partial-rollback semantics are rejected at BEGIN. `GlobalAttemptRegistrationSpec` is sequence-neutral `{global_txn_id,begin_idempotency_key,begin_binding:BindReserved{reservation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalBeginReservationRecord>,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>,expected_index_value:Reserved}|IdempotentBound{reservation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalBeginReservationRecord>,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>,existing_registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,expected_index_value:BoundDetailed},txn_token,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,service_visibility_epoch,operation_class:ReadOnly|ReadWrite,requested_snapshot_selector,minimum_acceptable_snapshot,authority_permit_ref:AuthorityPermitRef,non_widenable_authority_ceiling_digest,transaction_error_policy:TransactionErrorPolicy,initial_workspace_body_recipe,operation_audit_admission:OperationAuditAdmission::NotRequired|PendingUnclaimed,policy_epoch,revocation_index,topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,registration_generation,expected_attempt_family_state:First{authenticated_absence_proof}|Successor{prior_generation,prior_terminal_outcome_proof_ref:StrongRef<TerminalAttemptOutcomeProof>,prior_release_and_overlap_floor_ref:StrongRef<AttemptReleaseAndOverlapFloor>}|IdempotentRetry{existing_registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,existing_registration_body_digest},expected_outcome_capability_state:ReservedForThisBegin|IdempotentSameRegistration,terminal_audit_gate:LifecycleScaffoldingNotRequired}`; tag/class, begin-key, permit, policy, replay identity, or recipe mismatch is invalid. Apply decodes the replay object, byte-matches it to the reservation and request, atomically installs `BoundDetailed` with that same replay ref, and stores the ref in the first registered outcome lineage. `BoundCompacted` is terminal lookup state, never an idempotent-registration input.

It is applied only through `GlobalControlCommand(kind=RegisterAttempt)`. `First` requires an absent family and generation zero; `Successor` requires `registration_generation=prior_generation+1` with checked overflow, no active generation, an exact terminal predecessor, every required release/overlap floor, and a fresh `txn_token` never bound to an earlier generation. A terminal NeverRegistered begin key cannot later bind or create a family; a new begin key may use `First` only while the family is truly absent. `IdempotentRetry` must byte-match the complete already-applied registration and returns that original record without a second mutation. In every case a scoped token is either absent or bound to that exact generation; two nonterminal generations for one `global_txn_id`, parallel successor generations, generation gaps, token rebinding, or reuse of an aborted/closed token fail closed. `BindReserved` first byte-matches the reserved request and replay object and atomically changes its begin-index entry `Reserved -> BoundDetailed`; `IdempotentBound` must byte-match the existing `BoundDetailed` entry and returns the same registration/outcome without mutation. Only the binding path claims the operation ticket when required, rejects a selected snapshot below `GlobalConflictIndex.safe_snapshot_frontier`, assigns a snapshot no later than the resulting registration prefix, inserts the `Active` family/attempt/conflict entries, changes the outcome directory from `BeginStaging` to `W12`, and constructs `GlobalAttemptRegistration {command_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlCommand>,global_txn_id,begin_idempotency_key,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>,request_kind:ExplicitBegin|AutocommitExecute,txn_token,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,service_visibility_epoch,operation_class,registered_snapshot,registered_at_global_logical_command_seq,topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,tenant,principal,authority_ceiling_digest,authority_permit_ref:AuthorityPermitRef,permit_scope_digest,transaction_error_policy:TransactionErrorPolicy,operation_audit_admission:OperationAuditAdmission::NotRequired|Claimed,policy_epoch,revocation_index,registration_generation}`. Tag, target identity, replay bytes, current cluster/service epoch and promotion receipt, scope, policy/revocation, tenant/principal, and ceiling of the retained permit byte-match the spec. Apply then constructs canonical `GlobalTxnWorkspaceGeneration` zero from the registered body recipe and the `Registered` outcome before payload→control-record→root. Every SERIALIZABLE transaction, including read-only work, finishes ticket admission/mirror and exclusive claim (when required) plus registration before its first participant read; no late-registration or ambient safe-snapshot exception exists. A denial before registration uses only `GlobalBeginTerminalSpec`; registration never fabricates or overwrites a never-registered outcome.

`ShardStatementWorkspaceDelta` is the shard-local immutable `{execution_scope:ShardStatement,shard_id,workspace_generation,prior_local_workspace_root_ref:StrongRef<ShardTxnWorkspaceRoot>,statement_class:ReadOnly|WriteReturning|WriteNoResult,base_snapshot_read_state_ref:StrongRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,ordered_prior_overlay_commitment,statement_read_witness_refs[StrongRef],statement_effect:Write{delta_ref:StrongRef<LogicalDeltaTemplate>}|ReadOnly{no_write_effect_proof_ref:StrongRef<NoWriteEffectProof>},result_fragment_digest,successor_local_workspace_root_ref:StrongRef<ShardTxnWorkspaceRoot>,topology_epoch,configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,active_meta_projection_root_ref:StrongRef<ActiveMetaProjectionRoot>,policy_epoch,revocation_index,key_epoch_commitment,deterministic_recompute_digest}`. The tag must match `statement_class`; a true read-only statement uses the proof arm, not a fabricated mutation. `ShardStatementWorkspaceCertificate` begins `SameGroupCertificateHeader` and strongly names the delta, exact prior/successor overlay roots, statement/workspace generation, partition/effect/read commitments, active projection, and signer lock. `GlobalTxnWorkspaceGeneration` is the Meta object `{registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,workspace_generation,predecessor_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>?,through_statement_seq,statement_registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalStatementRegistration>?,sorted_shard_workspace_certificate_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardStatementWorkspaceCertificate>],complete_partition_and_effect_commitment,cumulative_logical_effect_root_ref:StrongRef<CumulativeTxnEffectRoot>,cumulative_read_witness_root_ref:StrongRef<CumulativeReadWitnessRoot>,topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,policy_epoch,revocation_index,key_epoch_commitment}`. Generation zero is the canonical empty overlay created with registration; each published statement increments exactly once with checked overflow and a complete routed shard set. Active-attempt floors retain all local overlays and Meta generations; final prepare consumes the exact latest generation, and cancel/terminal compaction releases them only after every result, audit, delta, backup, and overlap obligation closes.

`ReadExecutionScope` is the closed posture tag `LocalTerminal{registration_ref:StrongRef<LocalAttemptRegistration>,workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<LocalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>}|LocalStatement{registration_ref:StrongRef<LocalAttemptRegistration>,statement_registration_ref:StrongRef<LocalStatementRegistration>,workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<LocalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>}|MetaTerminal{registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>}|MetaStatement{registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,statement_registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalStatementRegistration>,workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>}|ShardTerminal{registration_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,workspace_generation_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>}|ShardStatement{registration_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,statement_registration_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalStatementRegistration>,workspace_generation_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>}`. Role and Terminal/Statement combinations are disjoint. `ShardReadWitnessBasis` is the shard-owned `{execution_scope:ReadExecutionScope::ShardTerminal|ShardStatement,shard_id,shard_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,topology_epoch,registered_snapshot,registration_global_prefix,workspace_generation,local_workspace_overlay_root_ref:StrongRef<ShardTxnWorkspaceRoot>,active_meta_projection_root_ref:StrongRef<ActiveMetaProjectionRoot>,operation_audit_claim_commitment,statement_audit_claim_commitment?,policy_epoch,revocation_index,key_epoch_commitment,audit_visible_prefix,read_state_root_ref:StrongRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,read_state_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<ShardCheckpointCertificate>,read_index_or_applied_prefix_proof,queryable_history_inventory_ref:StrongRef<ShardHistoryInventory>,exact_read_graph_bindings,read_access_admission_ref:StrongRef<ReadAccessAdmissionRecord>,read_witness_refs[ShardReadWitnessRef],final_read_summary,result_answer_contract,canonical_result_fragment_digest,read_result_release_decision_ref:StrongRef<ReadResultReleaseDecisionRecord>,authority_projection_digest,recompute_verifier_version,basis_digest}`. `ShardReadWitnessRef` is the generated closed union of role-valid witness targets. The access admission exists before the first cursor/storage/statistics observation; the release decision exists only after the final witness/result digest and cannot retroactively authorize access. Reads evaluate the registered snapshot plus the exact ordered local workspace overlay certified by the imported global generation; a missing prior-touched-shard delta or false empty-overlay proof fails. Before any shard read, operation and applicable statement tickets are mirrored/claimed through the two certified registrations. The active Meta projection covers their prefix and security slots, and the shard rechecks revocation. No shard decision contains a raw Meta permit, ticket, claim, statement, or workspace reference.

`ReadParticipantRoutingCertificate` is meta-owned `{SameGroupCertificateHeader,execution_scope:ReadExecutionScope::MetaTerminal|MetaStatement,topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>,sorted_read_basis_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardReadWitnessBasis>],sorted_participants,complete_read_footprint,partition_derivation_proof_ref:StrongRef<ParticipantRoutingDerivationProof>,complete_participant_commitment,aggregate_read_state_cut_commitment,aggregate_workspace_overlay_commitment,aggregate_read_witness_commitment,operation_audit_claim_commitment,statement_audit_claim_commitment?,result_answer_contract,canonical_result_digest,one_digest_signer_lock_ref:StrongRef<CertificateSignerLock>,quorum_signatures}`. The proof reaches a fixed point over every routed read/expansion/constraint-disclosure and previously touched workspace shard; it owns the remote state/witness/security/overlay bases through publication and the attempt conflict-retention floor.

Explicit transactions publish each nonterminal statement through Meta order. `StatementAuditAdmission` is `NotRequired{evidence:NonRequiredAuditEvidence}|PendingUnclaimed{ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,ticket_admission_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,statement_request_basis_commitment}|Claimed{ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,claim_record_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicketClaimRecord>,owner:{global_txn_id,registration_generation,statement_seq,statement_idempotency_key},statement_request_basis_commitment}`. `GlobalStatementRegistrationSpec` is `{registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,expected_attempt_state:Active,statement_seq,statement_idempotency_key,statement_class:ReadOnly|WriteReturning|WriteNoResult,canonical_statement_digest,parameter_digest,requested_result_answer_contract,expected_prior_statement_frontier,expected_workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>,transaction_error_policy:TransactionErrorPolicy,statement_audit_admission:NotRequired|PendingUnclaimed,expected_conflict_index_basis:WeakStateIdentity,terminal_audit_gate:LifecycleScaffoldingNotRequired}`. Apply requires `statement_seq=prior+1`, the workspace to be the current generation through the prior statement, and the error policy to byte-match the attempt; it atomically claims the distinct ticket when required, creates `GlobalStatementRegistration {applied_control_ref:AppliedControlRef,registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,statement_seq,statement_idempotency_key,statement_class,canonical_statement_digest,parameter_digest,result_answer_contract,expected_workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>,transaction_error_policy,statement_audit_admission:NotRequired|Claimed,registered_snapshot,registered_at_global_prefix}`, and inserts `Open` into `GlobalStatementIndex`. A byte-identical retry returns the original registration; key, sequence, class, statement, parameter, workspace, policy, or scope drift fails. No shard read/effect for that statement precedes this visible record.

`ResultSchema` is the immutable public schema `{format_version,columns[{ordinal,name,logical_type,nullability,graph_or_value_annotation}],canonical_public_schema_digest}`, where ordinals are contiguous from zero, names and annotations use the canonical public string/value encodings, and `canonical_public_schema_digest = BLAKE3("fgdb:public-result-schema:v1" || canonical(format_version,columns))`. `CanonicalResultChunkDescriptor` is `{ordinal,canonical_offset,canonical_len,public_chunk_digest,ciphertext_ref:StrongCiphertextRef}`; descriptors are contiguous and cover exactly `[0,byte_count)` without overlap or gap, and each public digest is over the exact plaintext canonical byte slice under `"fgdb:public-result-chunk:v1"`. `BufferedResultOwner` is the pre-publication closed union `TerminalRead{registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>}|AutocommitWriteTerminal{registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,prepare_admission_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>}|Statement{registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,statement_registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalStatementRegistration>}`. `BufferedResultManifest` is the immutable spill-backed closure `{owner:BufferedResultOwner,canonical_schema_ref:StrongRef<ResultSchema>,public_schema_digest,canonical_encoding_version,result_answer_contract,row_count,byte_count,ordered_chunks[CanonicalResultChunkDescriptor],canonical_result_digest,resource_charge_ref:StrongRef<ResourceLedgerTransition>}`. The schema ref must reproduce `public_schema_digest`; descriptors must reproduce `byte_count` and their plaintext digests; and `canonical_result_digest = BLAKE3("fgdb:canonical-result:v1" || public_schema_digest || canonical(result_answer_contract) || canonical_encoding_version || row_count || byte_count || exact_concatenated_canonical_result_bytes)`. That public transcript excludes owner identity, keyed object/schema/chunk identities, ciphertext, resource charge, delivery lease, storage placement, and the digest field itself. The manifest deliberately contains no lease, publication record, read-close record, or delivery state. Chunks use bounded canonical framing, encryption, backpressure-safe iteration, and D1 coverage; prepared ownership retains the manifest before publication, but no schema, row, error detail, or replay reference is client-visible. FGP recomputes the schema, chunk, coverage, and final result digests before emission and on replay; golden and mutation tests flip every included and excluded field to prove the transcript boundary.

`ResultDeliveryLeaseRecipe` is the sequence-neutral `{time_basis_ref:StrongRef<ResultDeliveryLeaseTimeBasis>,required_posture:Sharded,issuance_time_validation_evidence_ref:StrongRef<TimeValidationEvidence>}`; evidence subject is the registered basis digest/use. `StatementPublishedOutput` is the closed union `NoResult{no_result_proof_ref:StrongRef<NoResultProof>,terminal_delivery_frontier_digest}|Buffered{manifest_ref:StrongRef<BufferedResultManifest>,delivery_lease_recipe:ResultDeliveryLeaseRecipe}`; WriteNoResult requires NoResult and every result-bearing class requires Buffered. `ResultDeliveryOwner` is the post-apply closed union `TerminalRead{registration_ref,read_close_applied_ref}|AutocommitWriteTerminal{registration_ref,global_terminal_completion_applied_ref,terminal_ready_outcome_ref}|Statement{registration_ref,statement_registration_ref,publication_applied_ref}`. `ResultDeliveryLease` is constructed during owning apply as `{owner,manifest_ref,time_basis_ref,delivery_id,lease_generation,canonical_result_digest,service_visibility_epoch,service_authority:ResultDeliveryServiceAuthority,time_authority_profile_oid,not_before,expires_at,issuance_time_validation_evidence_ref,chunk_replay_profile,maximum_replay_count,successor_capability_fields,created_at_global_logical_command_seq}`. Construction is manifest/owner basis -> complete time basis -> evidence -> current command apply -> lease -> independent-retention record -> payload; applied fields must be the exact basis projection, and none points to a future Global record/root. Semantic `ResultDeliveryState` is `NotApplicableTerminal|DetachedToIndependentRetention{retention_ref:StrongRef<ResultIndependentRetentionRecord<Meta>>}`. ACK/release state belongs only to the independent record/index, uniformly for terminal and statement results. The Sharded write-terminal lease and Active retention record are constructed only by `GlobalTerminalCompletionSpec` after TerminalReady and complete commit/delta/durability/audit postconditions; commit never waits for its ACK.

`GlobalStatementPublicationSpec` is `{statement_registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalStatementRegistration>,registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,statement_audit_admission:StatementAuditAdmission::Claimed|NotRequired,read_routing_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ReadParticipantRoutingCertificate>,global_read_authorization_decision_ref:StrongRef<GlobalReadAuthorizationDecisionRecord>,sorted_workspace_certificate_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardStatementWorkspaceCertificate>],expected_prior_workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>,successor_workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>,final_read_witness_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef],statement_serialization_certificate_ref:StrongRef<DistributedSerializationCertificate>,published_output:StatementPublishedOutput,expected_prior_cumulative_read_witness_root:WeakDigest,successor_cumulative_read_witness_root_ref:StrongRef<CumulativeReadWitnessRoot>,expected_statement_index_value:Open,expected_attempt_state:Active,expected_conflict_index_basis:WeakStateIdentity,terminal_audit_gate}`. Published-output tag/manifest owner, statement class, exact prior/successor workspace, routed shard set, read witnesses, result, lease recipe, and audit owner all byte-match. Its statement event/resolution commits the exact result and workspace/effect transition without resolving the operation ticket. Apply atomically constructs the role-valid `ResultDeliveryOwner`, lease, resource-ownership transfer, and `ResultIndependentRetentionRecord<Meta>` when Buffered; installs `Published{publication_applied_ref:AppliedControlRef,output:NoResult{delivery_state:NotApplicableTerminal}|Buffered{result_manifest_ref,result_digest,delivery_state:DetachedToIndependentRetention{retention_ref}},workspace_generation_ref}`; inserts the record into `GlobalResultDeliveryIndex`; constructs the immediately succeeding `GlobalTxnOutcomeRecord::Registered`; advances the workspace generation, statement/delivery frontiers and cumulative witness/effect roots; and creates an audit-fenced candidate. Required audit begins PendingVisibility, and only the exact statement-ticket external CAS/mirror successor makes it ActiveDeliverable and streamable. The semantic attempt can finish or compact while this independent record remains Active.

`TerminalOutcomeEvidenceRef` is `Detailed{outcome_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnOutcomeRecord>}|Compacted{summary_root_ref:StrongRef<TerminalAttemptSummaryRoot>,leaf_key_digest}` and is status evidence only, never result-release evidence. `ResultReleaseEvidence` is exactly `ClientCancel{cancel_receipt_ref:StrongRef<AuthenticatedClientCancelReceipt>}|LeaseExpired{expiry_evidence_ref:StrongRef<DeliveryLeaseExpiryEvidence>}`; session/region/process death and attempt terminalization cannot inhabit it. `GlobalResultDeliveryTransitionSpec` is `{owner:ResultDeliveryOwner,result_manifest_ref:StrongRef<BufferedResultManifest>,delivery_lease_ref:StrongRef<ResultDeliveryLease>,active_retention_ref:StrongRef<ResultIndependentRetentionRecord<Meta>>,service_visibility_epoch,expected_current_promotion_receipt_digest,expected_active_retention_state_digest,transition:Acknowledge{delivery_id,result_digest,client_ack_nonce,complete_result_end_transcript_digest}|ReleaseUnacked{stable_reason_class,evidence:ResultReleaseEvidence},resource_transition_refs[StrongRef<ResourceLedgerTransition>],terminal_audit_gate}`. Apply byte-matches owner/manifest/lease/active index membership and creates exactly `ResultAckRecord|ResultReleaseRecord {owner,result_manifest_ref,delivery_lease_ref,delivery_id,result_digest,prior_retention_state_digest,ack_nonce_or_release_evidence_digest,assigned_global_logical_command_seq,applied_control_ref:AppliedControlRef,resource_transition_refs}` plus one terminal retention successor. It atomically CASes `GlobalResultDeliveryIndex` and releases/transfers only the independent charge; the semantic owner was already detached. Acknowledge requires a complete `RESULT_END`; release never retracts published result, audit, conflict, workspace, or terminal outcome state. Matching retry returns the same record; mismatched nonce, digest, owner, epoch, publication/close, or prior state fails. Attempt compaction accepts ActiveIndependent, Acknowledged, or ReleasedUnacked through `ResultDeliveryDispositionProof` and never waits for client activity.

`GlobalStatementAbortSpec` is `{registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,statement_registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalStatementRegistration>,expected_statement_index_value:Open,statement_audit_admission:StatementAuditAdmission::Claimed|NotRequired,stable_failure_class,no_result_and_no_workspace_effect_proof_ref:StrongRef,resource_release_refs[StrongRef<ResourceLedgerTransition>],continuation_action:ContinueAttempt|AbortAttempt,transaction_error_policy:TransactionErrorPolicy,expected_conflict_index_basis:WeakStateIdentity,authorization_decision_ref:StrongRef<AuthorizationDecisionRecord>,terminal_audit_gate}`. The pinned policy and error-class table uniquely determine `continuation_action`; ambient policy cannot choose after failure. Apply resolves the statement ticket, marks `Failed|Abandoned`, leaves workspace/cumulative witnesses unchanged, and, when required, makes `GlobalAttemptCancelSpec` the only next user transition.

Read-write prepare names the exact contiguous published-statement frontier, delivery-detachment frontier, latest `GlobalTxnWorkspaceGeneration`, cumulative read-witness root, and cumulative logical-effect root. An Open/unpublished statement, a buffered result not atomically detached into its independent index, a workspace gap, or a mismatched statement/effect frontier makes admission invalid; an Active independently retained result does not. Final `GlobalReadCloseSpec` is the terminal transition for a read-only attempt: autocommit publishes its `BufferedResultOwner::TerminalRead` result directly into independent retention, while an explicit transaction names the complete prior publication/detachment/workspace chain without replaying those bytes. Both rerun serialization over cumulative witnesses, resolve the operation ticket, install `ReadClosed`, and only then permit COMMIT success. Write-then-read executes against the certified workspace overlay, so multi-statement ReadOnly and intermediate ReadWrite results preserve read-your-own-writes without exposing unaudited or SSI-untracked observations; ACK latency is outside transaction correctness.

`GlobalPrepareAdmissionSpec` is `{registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,expected_attempt_state:Active,admission_generation,expected_published_statement_frontier,expected_delivery_terminal_frontier,expected_global_statement_index_digest,expected_workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>,expected_cumulative_read_witness_root_ref:StrongRef<CumulativeReadWitnessRoot>,expected_cumulative_logical_effect_root_ref:StrongRef<CumulativeTxnEffectRoot>,routing_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ParticipantRoutingCertificate>,sorted_participants,sorted_constraint_owners,sorted_basis_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardEffectBasis>],meta_constraint_reservation_requests[],global_authorization_decision_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAuthorizationDecisionRecord>,resource_transition_refs[StrongRef<ResourceLedgerTransition>],global_outcome_preparation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnOutcomePreparationRecord>,operation_audit_admission:OperationAuditAdmission::Claimed|NotRequired,transaction_audit_basis_commitment,global_final_effect_digest,expected_branch_heads[WeakMarkerIdentity],expected_branch_key_epochs,expected_topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,expected_policy_epoch,expected_revocation_index,expected_conflict_index_basis:WeakStateIdentity,terminal_audit_gate:LifecycleScaffoldingNotRequired}`. Its operation-audit value byte-matches registration; a claimed ticket remains unresolved, and the lifecycle-scaffolding proof commits the admission body and transaction decision without consuming it. Apply requires ReadWrite, exact fixed-point/evidence equality, a contiguous statement frontier with every registered statement terminally `Published|Failed|Abandoned`, every Published output either `NoResult/NotApplicableTerminal` or a Buffered result that is delivery-terminal or independently retained, no Open statement, exact workspace/read/effect roots, no prior admission/terminal, and current authorization/resource/outcome/audit state. Every `ShardEffectBasis` must deterministically finalize the corresponding certified workspace overlay rather than re-executing or omitting a prior statement. Apply atomically changes attempt/conflict state to `PrepareAdmitted`, creates Meta reservations, and constructs `MetaTerminalAdmissionFence::Armed {registration_ref,admission_generation,admission_applied_ref:AppliedControlRef,frozen_branch_heads,frozen_branch_key_epochs,frozen_write_coordinate_commitment,frozen_constraint_reservation_set_commitment,frozen_resource_transition_set_commitment,frozen_statement_delivery_workspace_witness_effect_commitment,frozen_topology_state_ref,frozen_policy_epoch,frozen_revocation_index,frozen_conflict_basis,operation_audit_claim_commitment,transaction_audit_basis_commitment}`. The fence deliberately contains no assigned future sequence or HLC. It prevents a second admission and roots the preparatory obligations, but the later final-certification reservation is the object that atomically revalidates and holds the exact terminal basis through signing/order. The succeeding `GlobalTxnOutcomeRecord::PrepareAdmitted`, `GlobalAttemptIndex`, and `GlobalConflictIndex` entries are the one canonical selector of that Armed version.

After every required prepare/constraint/serialization certificate and exact commit-or-abort release basis exists, `GlobalFinalCertificationReserveSpec` selects one terminal and installs its Active reservation before the audit plan. A terminal command requires that exact reservation and constructs `MetaTerminalAdmissionFence::TerminalOrdered {predecessor_ref:StrongRef<MetaTerminalAdmissionFence>,final_certification_reservation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalFinalCertificationReservation>,global_txn_command_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnCommand>,assigned_global_logical_command_seq,assigned_global_commit_seq:None|Some{value}}`; the same atomic lifecycle transition consumes the reservation and selects the fence successor. Admitted abort uses an Active MetaAbort reservation and constructs/selects `Released {predecessor_ref,final_certification_reservation_ref,abort_release_applied_ref}`. Old versions remain immutable and retained through terminal compaction; CAS of outcome/attempt/conflict/reservation forbids two successors. No CRSR/prepare is exportable until admission is durable, applied, and visible. A profile requiring a distinct admission-control audit event supplies a separately claimed lifecycle ticket; it never reuses the operation or statement ticket. Routing, participants, bases, owner requests, ticket/basis, statement/delivery frontier, workspace, generation, or any admitted semantic basis cannot change without an admitted abort/new generation; once final certification is Active, its exact held basis cannot drift or be reclaimed until consumption/cancel-before-signature.

Final terminal certification is a distinct ordered reservation **after** final rebase/authorization/serialization and **before** any terminal audit lock or signature. `FinalCertificationSelection` is the role-checked closed union `LocalCommit{final_effect_directory_ref:StrongRef<EffectDirectoryRoot>,final_effect_digest,serialization_certificate_ref:StrongRef<LocalSerializationCertificate>,authorization_decision_ref:StrongRef<AuthorizationDecisionRecord>,resource_and_constraint_hold_commitment,outcome_preparation_body_digest,terminal_write_result:None|Prepared{preparation_ref:StrongRef<TerminalWriteResultPreparation>,required_posture:Local}}|LocalAbort{stable_reason,no_effect_and_release_basis_digest}|MetaCommit{global_final_effect_directory_ref:StrongRef<GlobalEffectDirectoryRoot>,global_final_effect_digest,distributed_serialization_certificate_ref:StrongRef<DistributedSerializationCertificate>,participant_prepare_and_constraint_certificate_commitment,global_authorization_decision_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAuthorizationDecisionRecord>,resource_and_constraint_hold_commitment,outcome_preparation_body_digest,terminal_write_result:None|Prepared{preparation_ref:StrongRef<TerminalWriteResultPreparation>,required_posture:Sharded}}|MetaAbort{stable_reason,known_prepare_and_reservation_release_basis_digest,no_effect_proof_digest}`.

`LocalFinalCertificationReserveSpec` is `{registration_ref:StrongRef<LocalAttemptRegistration>,terminal_admission_fence_ref:StrongRef<LocalTerminalAdmissionFence>,required_fence_state:Armed,certification_generation,selection:FinalCertificationSelection::LocalCommit|LocalAbort,expected_current_branch_heads,expected_branch_key_epochs,expected_policy_epoch,expected_revocation_index,expected_conflict_index_basis,expected_writer_fence_and_configuration,complete_write_coordinate_set,complete_resource_constraint_and_id_hold_set,authorization_ceiling_digest,expected_reservation_index_absence_or_cancelled_predecessor,terminal_audit_gate:LifecycleScaffoldingNotRequired}`. `GlobalFinalCertificationReserveSpec` is the Meta analogue with `{registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,terminal_admission_fence_ref:StrongRef<MetaTerminalAdmissionFence>,admission_generation,certification_generation,selection:FinalCertificationSelection::MetaCommit|MetaAbort,expected_current_branch_heads,expected_branch_key_epochs,expected_policy_epoch,expected_revocation_index,expected_conflict_index_basis,expected_topology_and_meta_configuration,complete_participant_write_coordinate_set,complete_resource_constraint_remote_grant_and_id_hold_set,authorization_ceiling_digest,expected_reservation_index_absence_or_cancelled_predecessor,terminal_audit_gate:LifecycleScaffoldingNotRequired}`.

`LocalFinalCertificationReservation` is exactly `{source_spec_ref:StrongRef<LocalFinalCertificationReserveSpec>,registration_ref:StrongRef<LocalAttemptRegistration>,terminal_admission_fence_ref:StrongRef<LocalTerminalAdmissionFence>,admission_generation,certification_generation,selection:FinalCertificationSelection::LocalCommit|LocalAbort,validated_branch_head_and_key_epoch_commitment,validated_policy_revocation_and_authority_commitment,validated_conflict_serialization_commitment,validated_local_configuration_commitment,exclusive_coordinate_head_hold_root_ref:StrongRef<LocalTerminalCoordinateHoldRoot>,resource_constraint_id_hold_root_ref:StrongRef<LocalTerminalObligationHoldRoot>,applied_control_ref:AppliedControlRef,state:Active|CancelledBeforeSignature{cancel_applied_ref:AppliedControlRef,release_commitment}|Consumed{terminal_input_identity,assigned_logical_command_seq}}`. `GlobalFinalCertificationReservation` is exactly `{source_spec_ref:StrongRef<GlobalFinalCertificationReserveSpec>,registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,terminal_admission_fence_ref:StrongRef<MetaTerminalAdmissionFence>,admission_generation,certification_generation,selection:FinalCertificationSelection::MetaCommit|MetaAbort,validated_branch_head_and_key_epoch_commitment,validated_policy_revocation_and_authority_commitment,validated_conflict_serialization_commitment,validated_topology_configuration_commitment,exclusive_coordinate_head_hold_root_ref:StrongRef<MetaTerminalCoordinateHoldRoot>,resource_constraint_id_remote_hold_root_ref:StrongRef<MetaTerminalObligationHoldRoot>,applied_control_ref:AppliedControlRef,state:Active|CancelledBeforeSignature{cancel_applied_ref:AppliedControlRef,release_commitment}|Consumed{terminal_input_identity,assigned_global_logical_command_seq}}`. Apply reruns every named validation against current state and atomically installs the Active record in the role's `TerminalCertificationReservationRoot` with the two hold roots. A conflicting commit/head change, key retirement/destruction, policy/revocation reclamation, topology/configuration retirement, resource release, or GC must wait, transfer the reservation exactly, or reject; later revocation still fences new work and unsent output but cannot reinterpret this already authorized terminal.

`TerminalCertificationReservationRoot<Role>` is the authenticated map `(registration identity,admission generation,certification generation) -> latest StrongRef<RoleFinalCertificationReservation>` plus a unique-active selector per registration, hold-root coverage bitmap, nonretaining predecessor digest, and body digest. Reserve CASes absence/cancelled predecessor to Active; terminal apply or cancel replaces exactly that value with an immutable Consumed or Cancelled successor. Checkpoint/configuration/backup/restore/GC inventories include the root, every Active record, both hold roots, and all audit/order maintenance evidence. A state transition that can affect a held predicate is generated with a mandatory reservation-conflict check; deleting any such check is a G0 negative fixture.

`LocalFinalCertificationCancelSpec` and `GlobalFinalCertificationCancelSpec` each name the exact Active reservation, current index value, complete hold-release recipe, and `NoTerminalPlanLockShareOrOrderProof`. They are legal only before any `AuditTerminalSigningPlan`, event/resolution lock/share, terminal command, or candidate root exists; apply moves the reservation to `CancelledBeforeSignature` and releases exactly its holds. The admission fence remains Armed, so recovery may construct a new higher certification generation or an explicitly certified abort. Once a signing plan or any lock exists, cancellation is permanently illegal and the selected terminal must finish. The audit plan and admitted-write `AuditTerminalFreezeRef` bind the exact Active reservation and selection. The final Local `CommitCommand`/admitted abort or `GlobalTxnCommand` no longer revalidates mutable heads/key/policy/revocation/conflict/resource bases; it verifies the Active reservation, semantic prepared closure, and exact selected terminal, then atomically moves the reservation to `Consumed{terminal_input_identity,assigned_role_order}` and the admission fence to `TerminalOrdered|Released`. Unrelated commands may interleave; commands touching a reserved basis cannot. Crash/reconfiguration/checkpoint floors retain and transfer every Active reservation and hold.

`NoTerminalPlanLockShareOrOrderProof` is the pre-cancellation authority-local certificate `{SameGroupCertificateHeader,role:Local|Meta,final_certification_reservation_ref:StrongRef<LocalFinalCertificationReservation|GlobalFinalCertificationReservation>,required_state:Active,selection_digest,terminal_attempt_index_absence_path,audit_event_and_resolution_signer_journal_absence_or_release_fence_vector,prepared_terminal_command_absence_path,prepared_order_attempt_root_digest,all_matching_order_attempt_dispositions:None|RetiredStale[],semantic_raft_log_nonorder_proof:{term,configuration_ref,read_barrier_index,commit_index,applied_index,closed_semantic_order},candidate_root_and_audit_fence_absence_proof,quiescence_barrier_id,checker_version,certificate_attempt_plan_ref,certificate_signer_lock_refs,quorum_signatures}`. It is built from one linearizable barrier, contains no future cancel command/result, and is invalid if any terminal semantic plan, signing attempt, terminal command, Ordered supplement, candidate, or external audit CAS exists. Generic certificate-plan/lock/share bytes used to sign this proof are a distinct certificate kind and do not count as terminal-audit artifacts.

Order/HLC freshness is deliberately **outside** stable semantic prepared ownership and signed audit bytes. `LocalOrderSubject` is `Terminal{final_certification_reservation_ref:StrongRef<LocalFinalCertificationReservation>,required_state:Active,selected_terminal_digest}|Control{typed_payload_ref:StrongRef<SequenceNeutralSpec>,spec_body_digest,expected_state_conditions_digest,terminal_audit_freeze_commitment}`; `MetaOrderSubject` is the corresponding `Terminal{final_certification_reservation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalFinalCertificationReservation>,...}|Control{typed_payload_ref:StrongRef<GlobalSequenceNeutralSpec>,...}`. After the audit triple is prepared when required—or again after any harmless intervening semantic role command—the proposer builds `LocalOrderAttemptInput {order_attempt_id,subject:LocalOrderSubject,semantic_prepared_ownership_id,hlc_proposal_evidence_ref:StrongRef<LocalHlcProposalEvidence>,expected_next_logical_command_seq,expected_next_commit_seq:NotApplicable|Commit{value},configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,writer_fence_epoch,body_digest}` or `MetaOrderAttemptInput {order_attempt_id,subject:MetaOrderSubject,semantic_prepared_ownership_id,hlc_proposal_evidence_ref:StrongRef<MetaHlcProposalEvidence>,expected_next_global_logical_command_seq,expected_next_global_commit_seq:NotApplicable|Commit{value},configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,body_digest}`. Commit applicability is derived from the immutable selected terminal/control kind; abort/read/control cannot smuggle a commit-sequence assignment. `LocalOrderAttemptAvailabilityCertificate` and `MetaOrderAttemptAvailabilityCertificate` use the universal signer protocol, name the exact input/semantic owner/base-closure digest, and cover that already-built supplement closure while excluding themselves/future command. Their plan/lock/share/publication maintenance entries do not change the expected semantic counters. The role-specific `PreparedOrderAttemptRoot<Role>` is `{generation,entries[order_attempt_id -> Available{input_ref,availability_certificate_ref,maintenance_install_index}|Ordered{role_order,commit_order:None|Some,semantic_command_identity,semantic_raft_index}|RetiredStale{retirement_evidence_ref:StrongRef<OrderAttemptRetirementEvidence>,successor_attempt_id}],subject_to_latest_attempt_map,body_digest}`. `OrderAttemptRetirementEvidence` proves at a linearizable read barrier that the attempt was never a semantic log entry/candidate, identifies the semantic counter drift that made it stale, and retains its plan/certificate closure. Only nonsemantic maintenance transitions install or retire entries; semantic apply atomically selects Ordered. Checked counter mismatch, duplicate subject, self-staleness, retirement-after-order, and command/supplement substitution fail closed.

The command strongly names exactly one role-matching order-attempt input and availability certificate. Voters derive the next sequence/HLC only from that input and current persisted HLC and require its subject, semantic owner, spec/reservation, and any audit-freeze commitment to match. If its observation ages out or expected sequence loses a race, the supplement can be retired with a linearizable nonorder proof and a fresh order attempt can be certified without changing semantic ownership or any reservation/audit plan/lock/share/terminal bytes. Every failed supplement remains rooted until the prepared/order-attempt floor proves nonorder. A terminal reservation CAS, or a control spec's exact idempotency/expected-state CAS, admits at most one ordered semantic command across all supplements. Crash tests cover stale evidence before/during signing, intervening commands, leader/configuration change, multiple fresh supplements, and exactly one semantic application.

`ResultDispositionRef` is the exact compact union `ActiveIndependent{retention_ref:StrongRef<ResultIndependentRetentionRecord<Meta>>}|Acknowledged{retention_ref:StrongRef<ResultIndependentRetentionRecord<Meta>>,ack_ref:StrongRef<ResultAckRecord>}|ReleasedUnacked{retention_ref:StrongRef<ResultIndependentRetentionRecord<Meta>>,release_ref:StrongRef<ResultReleaseRecord>}` and must be backed by `ResultDeliveryDispositionProof`. `WorkspaceReleaseEvidenceRef` is `MetaLocal{release_record_ref:StrongRef<WorkspaceOverlayReleaseRecord>}|ShardRemote{release_ack_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardWorkspaceReleaseAck>}`. `GlobalAttemptCancelSpec` is `{registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,expected_attempt_state:Active,expected_absent_admission_generation,expected_statement_frontier,expected_delivery_detachment_frontier,expected_workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>,expected_cumulative_read_witness_root_ref:StrongRef<CumulativeReadWitnessRoot>,expected_cumulative_logical_effect_root_ref:StrongRef<CumulativeTxnEffectRoot>,all_open_statement_abort_refs[StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>],result_disposition_proof_refs[StrongRef<ResultDeliveryDispositionProof>],workspace_release_evidence_refs[WorkspaceReleaseEvidenceRef],stable_reason,no_committed_graph_effect_proof_ref:StrongRef,authorization_decision_ref:StrongRef<AuthorizationDecisionRecord>,resource_release_refs[StrongRef<ResourceLedgerTransition>],operation_audit_admission:OperationAuditAdmission::Claimed|NotRequired,terminal_audit_gate:TerminalAuditGate,expected_conflict_index_basis:WeakStateIdentity}`. Its audit admission byte-matches registration; a Claimed gate is the exact terminal failure/abandonment event and resolution for that operation ticket, while NotRequired carries its validated proof. `GlobalControlCommand(kind=CancelActiveAttempt)` is valid only before admission, after every Open statement has reached `Failed|Abandoned`, and after every published result is detached with one valid disposition proof. It proves there can be no shard prepare under this generation, but does not pretend staged workspace/audit/conflict/resource state never existed and does not release an ActiveIndependent result; exact overlay/grant release acknowledgements discharge only their own obligations. Apply installs terminal `Aborted`, closes its conflict vertex, and releases only the named attempt-owned closures. It is the deterministic recovery path for client death before admission; clock timeout alone is not a transition.

`MetaReadAuditEvidence` is the closed union `TerminalAttempt{operation:OperationAuditAdmission::Claimed|NotRequired}|Statement{operation:OperationAuditAdmission::Claimed|NotRequired,statement:StatementAuditAdmission::Claimed|NotRequired}`. The exact `GlobalReadAuthorizationDecisionRecord` is the Meta result-release schema defined with the authorization records below; its `ReadAccessAdmissionRecord::MetaTerminal|MetaStatement` exists before routing or observation, while the Global release object is created only after the complete certified shard release-decision set, workspace/witness commitment, realized answer contract, and canonical result digest exist. Scope, workspace generation, permit kind/projection, audit-evidence tag, and every shard access/release pair must agree. The release gate names only the terminal operation ticket for MetaTerminal or the distinct statement ticket for MetaStatement, while both claims remain bound; its complete shard commitment cannot reinterpret one shard decision as Meta-local.

`GlobalReadCloseSpec` is `{registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,operation_audit_admission:OperationAuditAdmission::Claimed|NotRequired,mode:AutocommitResult{read_routing_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ReadParticipantRoutingCertificate>,global_read_authorization_decision_ref:StrongRef<GlobalReadAuthorizationDecisionRecord>,buffered_result_manifest_ref:StrongRef<BufferedResultManifest>,result_delivery_lease_recipe:ResultDeliveryLeaseRecipe,canonical_result_digest,result_answer_contract}|ExplicitClose{expected_published_statement_frontier,expected_delivery_detachment_frontier,complete_publication_chain_digest,result_disposition_proof_refs[StrongRef<ResultDeliveryDispositionProof>],workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>,cumulative_read_witness_root_ref:StrongRef<CumulativeReadWitnessRoot>,zero_cumulative_write_effect_proof_ref:StrongRef,no_open_statement_proof_ref:StrongRef},final_read_witness_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef],distributed_serialization_certificate_ref:StrongRef<DistributedSerializationCertificate>,expected_conflict_index_basis:WeakStateIdentity,terminal_audit_gate}`. Autocommit requires `BufferedResultOwner::TerminalRead`; explicit close requires every statement publication mirrored and every result detached into its independent index. Its event/resolution/gate are the exact terminal extension of the claimed operation ticket. `GlobalControlCommand(kind=ReadClose)` requires `operation_class=ReadOnly`, installs `ReadClosed`, and advances GlobalLogicalCommandSeq/HLC but not GlobalCommitSeq. Autocommit apply atomically creates `ResultDeliveryOwner::TerminalRead`, its lease, charge transfer, and `ResultIndependentRetentionRecord<Meta>`, installs `DetachedToIndependentRetention`, and begins PendingVisibility or Deliverable according to the gate; the exact audit mirror makes a pending record deliverable. Explicit mode returns COMMIT success after close without waiting for ACK. The general `GlobalControlCommand` is `{command_version,kind,typed_payload_ref:StrongRef<GlobalSequenceNeutralSpec>,expected_state_conditions[],order_attempt_input_ref:StrongRef<MetaOrderAttemptInput>,order_attempt_availability_certificate_ref:StrongRef<MetaOrderAttemptAvailabilityCertificate>,authorization_decision_ref:StrongRef<AuthorizationDecisionRecord>,meta_pre_command_base_availability_certificate_ref:StrongRef<MetaPreCommandBaseAvailabilityCertificate>}`. Its MetaOrderSubject::Control must byte-match the typed payload, expected conditions, and audit-freeze commitment. The spec wrapper is the sole terminal audit gate; the command has no duplicate field. Every payload-bearing kind has exact stable pre-command closure coverage, while order/HLC evidence lives only in the replaceable supplement.

`GlobalDerivedGenerationActivationSpec` is `{derived_identity_ref,manifest_ref:StrongRef<DistributedDerivedGenerationManifest>,expected_registry_generation,expected_prior_active_generation?,expected_topology_ref,exact_global_frontier,answer_contract,old_generation_transition:KeepActiveUntilSwap|RetireAfterFloor,terminal_audit_gate}`; apply verifies a complete one-frontier component set, atomically selects it Active, and moves the old generation to Retiring without a query-visible gap. W12 `Fork|Grant|Rotate` are the operation tags inside the exact `GlobalBranchKeyDistributionPlanSpec`; `GlobalBranchKeyManifestActivationSpec` is the only activation tag. There is no `GlobalBranchKeyBundleSpec` alias and no path that lets a shard stage against the future manifest. Meta authority changes only after the complete staged-availability certificate set exists; shards become usable only after the later typed activation projection.

`GlobalSequenceNeutralSpec` has no wildcard arm. Its v1 `wire_types.toml` envelope rows are exactly: `RecoveryBridgeSpec`, `GlobalBeginReservationSpec`, `GlobalBeginTerminalSpec`, `GlobalAttemptRegistrationSpec`, `GlobalStatementRegistrationSpec`, `GlobalStatementPublicationSpec`, `GlobalResultDeliveryTransitionSpec`, `GlobalStatementAbortSpec`, `GlobalPrepareAdmissionSpec`, `GlobalAttemptCancelSpec`, `GlobalReadCloseSpec`, `GlobalDecisionCertificatePublishSpec`, `GlobalDeltaPublishSpec`, `PublishShardCheckpointCertificateSpec`, `PublishShardAppliedAckSpec`, `GlobalClosedAttemptFloorInstallSpec`, `GlobalCheckpointInstallSpec`, `MetaInitialFloorInstallSpec`, `GlobalHistoryCutActivationSpec`, `RemoteRetentionControlSpec`, `AdvanceRemoteConfigurationEvidenceSpec`, `ValidateRemoteConfigurationAnchorSpec`, `ShardingActivationSpec`, `LegacyLocalRetirementAuthorizeSpec`, `LegacyLocalRetirementFinalizeSpec`, `MetaConfigurationTransitionSpec`, `ShardReconfigurationAuthorizationSpec`, `ShardConfigurationAdoptionSpec`, `GlobalGcAuthorizationSpec`, `MetaGcPhysicalApplySpec`, `MetaGcPhysicalCompletionSpec`, `GlobalGcCompletionSpec`, `GlobalDerivedGenerationActivationSpec`, `GlobalBranchKeyDistributionPlanSpec`, `GlobalBranchKeyManifestActivationSpec`, `GlobalKeyDestructionAuthorizationSpec`, `GlobalKeyDestructionCompletionSpec`, `TopologyCopyBeginSpec`, `TopologyCutoverSpec`, `TopologyRetireOldSpec`, `CatalogMutationSpec`, `SchemaMutationSpec`, `IndexDefinitionSpec`, `IndexActivationSpec`, `PolicyTransitionSpec`, `RevocationTransitionSpec`, `GlobalIdRangeGrantSpec`, `ResourceLedgerTransitionSpec`, `PrivacyContinuityMirrorSpec`, `GlobalDpTransitionSpec`, `AuditTicketAdmissionSpec`, `AuditTerminalSpec`, `AuditContinuityMirrorSpec`, `AuditRecoverySpec`, `AuditCompletenessTransitionSpec`, `GlobalBackupIntentSpec`, `GlobalBackupSealSpec`, `GlobalBackupPublishCompletionSpec`, `GlobalBackupReleaseAuthorizeSpec`, `GlobalBackupReleaseFinalizeSpec`, `GlobalRestoreActivationSpec`, `RestoreVisibilityCommitSpec`, `GlobalRestoreServicePrepareSpec`, `GlobalRestoreServiceFinalizeSpec`, `GlobalRestoreServiceCompletionSpec`, `MergePrepareSpec`, and `MergeRejectSpec`. The separately registered inner tags are also closed and exact: `GlobalClosedAttemptFloorInstallSpec::{InstallNeverRegistered,BuildClosed,PublishClosed}`; `RemoteRetentionControlSpec::{AcquireGrant,RegisterConsumerGrant,RequestConsumerRelease,PublishConsumerReleaseEvidence,ApplyAuthorityRelease,PublishAuthorityReleaseAck,ConsumeReleaseAck,AdoptLegacyAuthorityTransfer}`; `GlobalResultDeliveryTransitionSpec::{Acknowledge,ReleaseUnacked}`; `RestoreCreationAuthority::{RecoverSameIdentity,CloneNewIdentity}`; `RecoveryBridgeSpec.target_role_payload::{Local,Meta,Shard}`; `LegacyTransferEvidenceRef::{MetaLocal,ImportedMeta}`; `ShardBackupReleaseSpec::{Authorize,Finalize}`; `GlobalBranchKeyDistributionPlanSpec::{Fork,Grant,Rotate}`; `MetaConfigurationTransitionSpec::{ProposeJoint,CommitJoint,CommitNew,CommitRetirementFloor}`; and the exact transition tags defined by `GlobalDpTransitionSpec`. `RecoveryBridgeSpec` is restricted to the pending restore guard. Backup, restore, result delivery, key, and retirement have no generic phase catchall: every phase is one explicitly named envelope or inner row above. Every envelope and inner tag has one generated body/result/posture/authority/audit/availability compatibility row. Undefined, unregistered, duplicate, role-invalid, ambient-evidence, or future-result-bearing tags are G0-invalid.

`PublicTxnStatusProjection` is the sole externally serializable status union and overrides the misleading historical word “public” in the internal `TxnCompletionState` description below. It is exactly `InProgress{posture,privacy_safe_phase,statement_frontier,delivery_frontier,workspace_generation}|FinalizingOpaque{posture,last_audit_visible_phase,required_stage_class_bitmap,satisfied_stage_class_bitmap}|TerminalPendingAuditVisible{posture,semantic_descriptor:SemanticTerminalDescriptor,required_postcondition_bitmap,satisfied_postcondition_bitmap}|TerminalReady{public_outcome:TerminalPublicOutcome,semantic_descriptor:SemanticTerminalDescriptor,proof_source:Detailed|Compacted,result_resume_capability?,read_your_writes:NotRequested|Issued{capability:ReadYourWritesCapability},audit_release:AuditReleaseEvidence}`. Before the exact terminal audit mirror, only `FinalizingOpaque` is legal: generated stage-class bitmaps use outcome-independent labels and cardinality and reveal no Commit/Abort/ReadClose, marker, sequence, effect, reason, participant, or result fact. At or after that mirror the audit-visible pending arm may expose the authorized descriptor while other postconditions finish. Detailed and compacted paths must emit byte-identical projections and the same prebuilt Resume/ReadYourWrites capability bytes.

`GlobalTxnOutcomePreparationRecord` is the sequence-neutral W12 terminal compare contract `{database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,attempt_key:{global_txn_id,registration_generation},txn_token,registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,expected_registered_outcome_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnOutcomeRecord>,admission_generation,terminal_domain:CommitIfCertifiedElseAbort{global_final_effect_digest,allowed_stable_abort_reason_classes},terminal_write_result:None|Prepared{preparation_ref:StrongRef<TerminalWriteResultPreparation>,required_posture:Sharded},authority/resource/audit_basis_commitment}`. It names neither the future admission spec/outcome nor an applied record. Admission verifies the expected `Registered` predecessor and installs `PrepareAdmitted`; the later global transaction command must present the same record and transition only that exact admission generation to one allowed terminal. The Sharded preparation is built only after final effect fixed point/rebase and before this record; admission, fragments, command, and completion all byte-match its final-effect/result/time-basis tuple.

`SemanticTerminalDescriptor` is the nonretaining inline posture union `Local{terminal:Write{marker_identity:WeakMarkerIdentity,applied_logical_command_seq,applied_commit_seq,final_effect_digest}|Abort{reason_class,terminal_logical_prefix}|ReadClose{applied_logical_command_seq,publication_chain_digest,final_result_digest?}}|Sharded{terminal:Write{marker_identity:WeakMarkerIdentity,applied_global_logical_seq,applied_global_commit_seq,final_effect_digest}|Abort{reason_class,terminal_global_prefix}|ReadClose{applied_global_logical_seq,publication_chain_digest,final_result_digest?}}`. `TxnCompletionState` is the public-status state machine `InProgress{phase:BeginStaging|Registered|StatementOpen|PrepareAdmitted}|TerminalPending{semantic_outcome:SemanticTerminalDescriptor,required_postcondition_bitmap,satisfied_postcondition_bitmap}|TerminalReady{public_outcome:TerminalPublicOutcome}`; descriptor and outcome posture must match the owning record. Local writes require durability, terminal audit visibility, contiguous Local delta publication, result disposition, and resource release bits. Sharded writes additionally require decision publication and every admitted shard's post-mirror acknowledgement; abort/read-close use their exact role-specific bitsets. `GlobalTxnOutcomeRecord` is the canonical registered-attempt value `{database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,service_visibility_epoch,global_txn_id,registration_generation,txn_token,tenant,principal,authority_ceiling_digest,predecessor_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnOutcomeRecord>?,state:Registered{registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,applied_control_ref:AppliedControlRef,published_statement_frontier,delivery_terminal_frontier,latest_workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>,cumulative_read_witness_root_ref:StrongRef<CumulativeReadWitnessRoot>,cumulative_logical_effect_root_ref:StrongRef<CumulativeTxnEffectRoot>,statement_index_digest}|PrepareAdmitted{admission_spec_ref:StrongRef<GlobalPrepareAdmissionSpec>,terminal_admission_fence_ref:StrongRef<MetaTerminalAdmissionFence>,admission_generation,published_statement_frontier,delivery_terminal_frontier,workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>,cumulative_read_witness_root_ref:StrongRef<CumulativeReadWitnessRoot>,cumulative_logical_effect_root_ref:StrongRef<CumulativeTxnEffectRoot>,operation_audit_admission:OperationAuditAdmission::Claimed|NotRequired,audit_basis_commitment,applied_control_ref:AppliedControlRef}|CommittedPendingPostconditions{marker_ref:StrongMarkerRef,final_effect_digest,global_txn_command_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnCommand>,applied_global_logical_seq,applied_global_commit_seq}|Committed{marker_ref:StrongMarkerRef,final_effect_digest,applied_global_logical_seq,applied_global_commit_seq,global_delta_publish_command_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlCommand>,delta_publish_applied_prefix,published_delta_frontier,public_outcome:TerminalPublicOutcome::Sharded}|Aborted{reason_class,applied_abort_ref:AppliedAbortRef,public_outcome:TerminalPublicOutcome::Sharded}|ReadClosed{read_close_spec_ref:StrongRef<GlobalReadCloseSpec>,applied_control_ref:AppliedControlRef,publication_chain_digest,final_result_digest?,public_outcome:TerminalPublicOutcome::Sharded},audit_state:NotRequired{evidence:NonRequiredAuditEvidence}|ClaimedPending{ticket_digest,claim_identity}|Terminal{audit_outcome_ref:StrongRef<AuditOutcomeRecord>},completion_state:TxnCompletionState,minimum_lookup_retention_floor}`. Its predecessor is the immediately prior attempt-lifecycle value; registration creates the first Registered value and thereby roots workspace generation zero, and every statement publication atomically constructs the immediately succeeding Registered value with all frontiers/roots advanced and makes GlobalOutcomeDirectoryValue::W12 point to it. No state names its future Global record. A committed write is semantically decided at CommittedPendingPostconditions but ordinary success and ReadYourWritesCapability are unavailable until all typed postconditions yield TerminalReady; only the matching terminal transition resolves the operation claim.

`GlobalAttemptIndex` maps only an actually registered `(global_txn_id,registration_generation)` to `Active|PrepareAdmitted|Terminalizing{semantic_terminal_kind,missing_postcondition_bitmap}|Terminal`; `AttemptFamilyState` enforces one active registered generation and exact successor rules. A pre-registration `NeverRegistered` outcome has no attempt identity and therefore exists only in the begin-key/outcome-capability directories and their permanent tombstones; no attempt-index row or fabricated attempt burn is legal. `GlobalStatementIndex` maps `(global_txn_id,registration_generation,statement_seq)` and the statement idempotency key to `Open|Published|Failed|Abandoned`, including the immutable result manifest, workspace successor, delivery state, and statement-ticket terminal evidence where applicable. `GlobalTxnOutcomeIndex` maps the scoped outcome token to the latest completion state or the separate begin/never-registered directory value. Family, attempt, statement, begin-key, token, audit-ticket, conflict, workspace, and publication/delivery-frontier entries transition atomically in the command that owns them. Matching retries return the original value; conflicting bodies or owners fail. Capability-safe status resolves the role-tagged directory/summary proof rather than a local-only outcome and reports `TerminalPending` instead of fabricating success while any required postcondition remains incomplete.

`GlobalCheckpointInstallSpec` is `{basis_global_state:WeakStateIdentity,basis_global_logical_command_seq,basis_global_commit_seq,basis_payload_digest:WeakDigest,basis_projection_digest,checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<GlobalRecoveryCheckpoint>,checkpoint_state_vector_digest,paired_meta_config_payload_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaConfigPayloadFloor>?,retention_cut_body_ref:StrongRef<RetentionCutBody>?,reset_field_tags[],terminal_audit_gate}`. Genesis alone uses no cut body and produces `CheckpointInstalled`; an operational replacement requires the body and paired floor, atomically installs the matching provisional cut, and preserves `Operational`. The single exact `ShardOperationalBootstrapBarrier` schema is the origin-tagged, strongly retaining definition in the activation/genesis contract above; no digest-only alternate encoding exists. `MetaInitialFloorInstallSpec` is `{checkpoint_installed_global_state:WeakStateIdentity,checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<GlobalRecoveryCheckpoint>,checkpoint_state_vector_digest,initial_meta_config_payload_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaConfigPayloadFloor>,initial_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,sorted_active_shard_barrier_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardOperationalBootstrapBarrier>],expected_global_logical_command_seq,terminal_audit_gate}` and is the sole fresh `CheckpointInstalled -> Operational` transition. The barrier set equals every and only `Active` topology entry, all at one global prefix; `Joining` shards are unroutable. `GlobalHistoryCutActivationSpec` is `{provisional_cut_ref:StrongRef<ProvisionalRetentionCutSet>,checkpoint_install_record_ref:StrongGlobalCommandRef,expected_retention_map_basis:WeakStateIdentity,verified_contiguous_suffix_start,terminal_audit_gate}` and only strengthens that exact provisional set to `ActivatedRetentionCutSet`.

Meta-owned directories change only through typed CAS controls. `PublishShardCheckpointCertificateSpec` is `{checkpoint_certificate_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardCheckpointCertificate>,expected_topology_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,expected_shard_configuration_ref:RemoteConfigurationRef,expected_prior_directory_value:WeakDigest?,required_remote_grant_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantEvidence>,terminal_audit_gate}`; apply byte-matches shard/config/topology/prefix/history interval and installs the exact CRSR. `PublishShardAppliedAckSpec` similarly binds `{ack_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardAppliedAck>,prepare_key,decision_record_identity,decision_publish_record_identity,expected_topology_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,expected_shard_configuration_ref:RemoteConfigurationRef,expected_prior_directory_value:WeakDigest?,required_remote_grant_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantEvidence>,terminal_audit_gate}` and is required for commit and abort acknowledgements.

`GlobalTerminalCompletionSpec` is the sole W12 postcondition transition `{pending_outcome_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnOutcomeRecord>,semantic_outcome:SemanticTerminalDescriptor::Sharded,expected_required_postcondition_bitmap,observed_satisfied_postcondition_bitmap,decision_publication_evidence:Committed{decision_publish_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>}|NoDecisionApplicable{terminal_kind:ReadClosed},exact_sorted_post_mirror_shard_ack_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardAppliedAck>],shard_ack_coverage_commitment,delta_completion:Committed{global_delta_batch_ref:StrongRef<GlobalLogicalDeltaBatch>,global_delta_publish_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,published_frontier_proof_ref:StrongRef<GlobalDeltaFrontierProof>}|NoDeltaApplicable{terminal_kind:Aborted|ReadClosed,proof_ref:StrongRef<NoDeltaProof>},configured_durability_evidence_ref:StrongRef<GlobalDurabilityEvidence>,result_disposition:NoTerminalResult|ReadTerminalResult{delivery_disposition_proof_ref:StrongRef<ResultDeliveryDispositionProof>}|AutocommitWriteReturning{preparation_ref:StrongRef<TerminalWriteResultPreparation>,required_posture:Sharded},resource_release_refs[StrongRef<ResourceLedgerTransition>],audit_visibility_evidence_ref:StrongRef<AuditOutcomeRecord>,expected_conflict_overlap_floor_ref:StrongRef<ConflictOverlapCloseProof>,terminal_audit_freeze:AuditFreezeField::Required<MetaControl>,terminal_audit_gate}`. Every evidence arm and required bit is generated from terminal kind, participants, result class, and durability policy; arrays are canonical bijections. Apply CASes the exact pending predecessor, monotonically adds only verified bits, constructs the succeeding outcome, and selects `TerminalReady` only when required equals satisfied. The autocommit-write arm byte-matches the preparation retained by `GlobalTxnOutcomePreparationRecord` and is legal only for committed WriteReturning; in the same completion apply it creates `ResultDeliveryOwner::AutocommitWriteTerminal`, its exact lease, charge transfer, Active retention record, index leaf, and detached semantic frontier. Independent retention—not client ACK—is the result postcondition. Matching retry returns the same applied record/lease/retention record; a different bitmap, participant set, frontier, result arm, or predecessor fails. ReadYourWritesCapability and ordinary terminal success remain unavailable until the TerminalReady root and required mirror are visible.

Attempt-history compaction is cumulative and has three separately ordered phases; deterministic apply never manufactures a quorum signature. `AttemptLookupKey` is the closed tag `ByAttempt{database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,global_txn_id,registration_generation}|ByOutcomeCapability{capability_domain_commitment,scoped_token_digest}`. `TerminalAttemptSummaryLeaf` is `NeverRegistered{outcome_capability_key:AttemptLookupKey::ByOutcomeCapability,reason_class:DeniedBeforeRegistration|BeginDisconnected|AbandonedStaging|SupersededRetry,audit_terminal_commitment,original_response_commitment,staging_generation,terminal_global_prefix}|Terminal{attempt_key:AttemptLookupKey::ByAttempt,outcome_capability_key:AttemptLookupKey::ByOutcomeCapability,operation_class,terminal_global_prefix,public_outcome:TerminalPublicOutcome,authority_ceiling_digest,audit_terminal_commitment}`. A NeverRegistered leaf has no optional or synthetic attempt identity: absence of registration is part of the tag's meaning. The public outcome is copied byte-for-byte from the last detailed terminal value and includes its original response commitment; neither leaf has a retaining edge to audit detail. The leaf reveals no tenant, principal, hidden participant, topology, or graph fact. `TerminalAttemptSummaryRoot` is a canonical authenticated persistent map from keyed lookup hashes to leaves plus `{summary_generation,covered_closed_prefix,leaf_count,root_digest}`. Its capability-safe membership/nonmembership proof discloses only the requested leaf and blinded path; status lookup first validates the exact outcome capability. A successor root must equal the prior root plus the command's sorted insertions, proven by `PersistentMapExtensionProof`; it may structurally share map nodes but contains no `StrongRef` to a predecessor summary root, audit detail, or heavy attempt evidence, and an existing key can only be an identical idempotent leaf.

`NeverRegisteredEvidence` is `{begin_reservation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalBeginReservationRecord>,terminal_record_ref:StrongRef<NeverRegisteredTerminalRecord>,capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>,outcome_capability_key:AttemptLookupKey::ByOutcomeCapability,staging_generation,authenticated_detailed_value_proofs:{global_begin_idempotency_index:NeverRegisteredDetailed,global_outcome_directory:NeverRegisteredDetailed},no_reservation_binding_proof_ref:StrongRef<NoReservationBindingProof>,audit_terminal_commitment,absence_of_exported_registration_or_shard_import_commitment}`. `NoReservationBindingProof` is generated from the current begin-index terminal leaf, the reservation-key uniqueness proof, the Meta prepared/certificate/export roots, and the registered inverse-reference index for reservation identities; it proves that this reservation was never consumed by registration or exported, without inventing an attempt/family key. `NeverRegisteredFloorSpec` is `{basis_global_state:WeakStateIdentity,basis_global_prefix,basis_begin_index_digest,basis_outcome_directory_digest,basis_prepared_root_digest,basis_certificate_ledger_digest,basis_reservation_inverse_index_digest,sorted_evidence_refs[StrongRef<NeverRegisteredEvidence>],expected_prior_summary_root_ref:StrongRef<TerminalAttemptSummaryRoot>,candidate_summary_root_ref:StrongRef<TerminalAttemptSummaryRoot>,extension_proof_ref:StrongRef<PersistentMapExtensionProof>,exact_detailed_to_compacted_begin_and_directory_rewrite_commitment,terminal_audit_gate}`. Apply revalidates every detailed value and nonbinding proof against current roots, inserts the exact never-registered summary leaves, atomically changes begin-index and outcome-directory entries from Detailed to Compacted while preserving their same replay ref, and creates compact `NeverRegisteredFloorRecord {assigned_global_logical_command_seq,source_command_digest:WeakDigest,rewritten_lookup_key_commitment,summary_root_ref:StrongRef<TerminalAttemptSummaryRoot>,applied_global_prefix}` with no retaining edge to its command/spec/evidence. It creates, burns, or rewrites no attempt/family/conflict entry and can never change the previously returned reason or response bytes.

`GlobalOutcomeExpirySpec` is a separate ordered control `{capability_replay_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeCapabilityReplayRecord>,summary_root_ref:StrongRef<TerminalAttemptSummaryRoot>,leaf_key_digest,expected_begin_index_entry:BoundCompacted|NeverRegisteredCompacted,expected_outcome_directory_entry:CompactedTerminal|NeverRegisteredCompacted,time_validation_evidence_ref:StrongRef<TimeValidationEvidence>,expected_verifier_key_and_profile_floors,expected_begin_retry_and_lookup_floors,expected_retention_cut_ref:StrongRef<ActivatedHistoryCut>,permanent_begin_tombstone_body,permanent_outcome_tombstone_body,terminal_audit_freeze:AuditFreezeField::Required<MetaControl>,terminal_audit_gate}`. The evidence must classify the replay object's exact window `Expired` for this action, the two compact leaves and replay identity must agree, and every promised retry/lookup floor must be closed. Apply atomically changes both leaves to `ExpiredTombstone` values containing the same scoped-key/token/capability commitments and expiry-evidence digest, drops the replay edge only in that transition, and permanently prevents key/token reuse. A valid old capability thereafter returns `TokenExpired`; an invalid or unauthorized input remains `NotVisibleOrUnknown`. Expiry does not remove the internal terminal summary leaf or fabricate an attempt identity.

`AttemptDeltaCompletionEvidence` is `Committed{global_delta_batch_ref:StrongRef<GlobalLogicalDeltaBatch>,global_delta_publish_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,published_frontier_at_or_beyond_commit_proof_ref:StrongRef<GlobalDeltaFrontierProof>}|NoDeltaApplicable{terminal_kind:Aborted|ReadClosed,proof_digest}`. `AttemptCompactionEvidenceRef` is the exact closed union `MetaDecision{record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>}|MetaConstraintRelease{record_ref:StrongRef<ConstraintReleaseRecord>}|MetaAuditTerminal{record_ref:StrongRef<AuditOutcomeRecord>}|MetaResultDisposition{disposition:ResultDispositionRef}|MetaWorkspaceRelease{evidence:WorkspaceReleaseEvidenceRef}|MetaBackupRelease{record_ref:StrongRef<BackupReleaseRecord>}|MetaReplayRetention{record_ref:StrongRef<ReplayRetentionRecord>}|MetaRemoteRelease{record_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionReleaseTombstone>}|ShardPostMirror{ack_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardAppliedAck>}|ShardConstraintRelease{ack_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardConstraintReleaseAck>}|ShardWorkspaceRelease{ack_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardWorkspaceReleaseAck>}`. `IndependentAttemptObligationRef` is `Result{retention_ref:StrongRef<ResultIndependentRetentionRecord>}|Backup{retention_ref:StrongRef<BackupIndependentRetentionRecord>}|Replay{retention_ref:StrongRef<ReplayRetentionRecord>}|RemoteGrant{grant_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantEvidence>}|CapabilityFloor{floor_ref:StrongRef<CapabilityLookupFloor>}`. `ClosedAttemptEvidenceBundle` is the heavy pre-order closure `{sorted_terminal_ready_outcome_refs[StrongRef<GlobalTxnOutcomeRecord>],begin_idempotency_and_public_status_proof_refs[StrongRef<BeginPublicStatusProof>],sorted_evidence_refs[AttemptCompactionEvidenceRef],sorted_delta_completion_evidence[AttemptDeltaCompletionEvidence],statement_terminal_summary_proof_refs[StrongRef<StatementTerminalSummaryProof>],result_delivery_disposition_proof_refs[StrongRef<ResultDeliveryDispositionProof>],workspace_generation_and_local_overlay_release_proof_refs[StrongRef<WorkspaceReleaseProof>],workspace_remote_grant_release_ack_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardWorkspaceReleaseAck>],overlap_close_proof_refs[StrongRef<ConflictOverlapCloseProof>],complete_selected_attempt_and_public_outcome_commitment}`. `ClosedAttemptCompactionSpec` is `{compaction_id,basis_global_state:WeakStateIdentity,basis_global_prefix,basis_attempt_index_digest,basis_begin_index_digest,basis_outcome_directory_digest,basis_conflict_index_digest,basis_authoritative_floor_digest,basis_pending_root_digest,selected_terminal_attempt_keys[],evidence_bundle_ref:StrongRef<ClosedAttemptEvidenceBundle>,expected_prior_summary_root_ref:StrongRef<TerminalAttemptSummaryRoot>,candidate_summary_root_ref:StrongRef<TerminalAttemptSummaryRoot>,extension_proof_ref:StrongRef<PersistentMapExtensionProof>,retained_active_attempt_commitment,still_live_independent_obligation_refs[IndependentAttemptObligationRef],terminal_audit_gate}`. Apply verifies every selected attempt is `TerminalReady` and audit-mirrored and that its candidate leaf exactly reproduces the detailed `TerminalPublicOutcome`; decision/certificate publication, every admitted shard post-mirror acknowledgement, committed Global-delta publication/frontier, and applicable abort/read-close no-delta proof must be complete. Every statement is `Published|Failed|Abandoned`; every statement output is NoResult/NotApplicableTerminal or, together with every terminal/autocommit result, Acknowledged, ReleasedUnacked, or independently retained; every workspace overlay and remote grant has exact release evidence or a listed independent owner; overlap is closed; and no untransferred backup/replay/retention/capability obligation remains. Apply creates unsigned compact `ClosedAttemptCompactionFloorRecord {compaction_id,assigned_global_logical_command_seq,source_command_digest:WeakDigest,through_global_prefix,terminal_summary_root_ref:StrongRef<TerminalAttemptSummaryRoot>,selected_attempt_commitment,selected_public_outcome_commitment,retained_active_attempt_commitment,still_live_independent_obligation_commitment,meta_checkpoint_identity:WeakDigest}` with no retaining edge to the command/spec/evidence and inserts it into `PendingAttemptCompactionRoot {generation,entries[compaction_id->StrongRef<ClosedAttemptCompactionFloorRecord>],nonretaining_predecessor_digest}`. Build does **not** advance the authoritative floor, rewrite detailed indexes, or release heavy evidence.

Only after the compact record and its audit mirror are durable does the Meta quorum create `AttemptCompactionAttestation {SameGroupCertificateHeader,compaction_id,floor_record_identity:WeakDigest,build_control_identity:WeakGlobalCommandIdentity,build_resulting_root_identity:WeakDigest,audit_mirror_identity:WeakGlobalCommandIdentity,summary_root_ref:StrongRef<TerminalAttemptSummaryRoot>,selected_attempt_commitment,selected_public_outcome_commitment,through_global_prefix,retained_active_attempt_commitment,still_live_independent_obligation_commitment,one_digest_signer_lock_ref:StrongRef<CertificateSignerLock>,quorum_signatures}`.
