It has no strong edge to the record, build command/root/mirror, prior floor, spec, or heavy evidence. The certificate ledger temporarily retains the build closure until publication. `GlobalClosedAttemptFloorPublishSpec` is `{floor_record_ref:StrongRef<ClosedAttemptCompactionFloorRecord>,attestation_ref:StrongRef<AttemptCompactionAttestation>,expected_pending_entry_digest,expected_prior_authoritative_floor:WeakDigest,expected_summary_root_ref:StrongRef<TerminalAttemptSummaryRoot>,exact_selected_attempt_index_rewrite_commitment,exact_selected_outcome_directory_rewrite_commitment,exact_overlap_closed_conflict_rewrite_commitment,exact_begin_status_result_workspace_remote_grant_and_statement_closure_commitment,terminal_audit_gate}`. Apply revalidates monotonic extension, removes exactly that pending entry, replaces selected detailed family/attempt/outcome entries with `CompactedTerminal{capability_replay_ref,summary_root_ref,leaf_key_digest,public_outcome,lookup_floor}`, removes only proved overlap-closed conflict detail, and leaves every independently retained result/workspace grant/backup/replay/capability object rooted by its own typed lease or floor. The installed public outcome must byte-match the authenticated leaf and the pre-compaction detailed response. It installs `GlobalAttemptCompactionFloor {summary_root_ref:StrongRef<TerminalAttemptSummaryRoot>,closed_through_global_prefix,retained_active_attempt_commitment,still_live_independent_obligation_commitment,last_update:Genesis|NeverRegistered{applied_prefix,record_identity:WeakDigest}|Closed{attestation_ref:StrongRef<AttemptCompactionAttestation>}}`. This floor has no strong/CRSR path to the previous floor, the build record, spec, or heavy evidence. Fresh Meta Genesis and Local activation both create the canonical empty `TerminalAttemptSummaryRoot`, empty `PendingAttemptCompactionRoot`, and `GlobalAttemptCompactionFloor{closed_through=0,last_update=Genesis}`; therefore the first extension has a real prior root. `GlobalClosedAttemptFloorInstallSpec` is the closed tag `InstallNeverRegistered{spec_ref:StrongRef<NeverRegisteredFloorSpec>}|BuildClosed{spec_ref:StrongRef<ClosedAttemptCompactionSpec>}|PublishClosed{spec_ref:StrongRef<GlobalClosedAttemptFloorPublishSpec>}`. Heavy evidence becomes reclaimable only after `PublishClosed`, its audit mirror, and an activated checkpoint cut covering the publish/build command and certificate-ledger transfer, subject to every independent live floor. Neither phase decides, aborts, or times out prepared work. Status tests race build, audit mirror, attestation, publish, expiry, and post-cut detail reclamation and require identical validated-capability response bytes, service epoch, and privacy shape before expiry and the exact privacy-collapsed expiry response afterward.

`MetaConfigurationTransitionSpec` is `{phase:ProposeJoint|CommitJoint|CommitNew|CommitRetirementFloor,basis_global_state:WeakStateIdentity,current_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,prospective_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,candidate_closure_proof_ref:StrongRef,expected_global_prefix,expected_topology_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,resulting_topology_body_digest,paired_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<GlobalRecoveryCheckpoint>?,paired_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaConfigPayloadFloor>,required_certificate_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaCertificateFloor>,required_remote_obligation_floor_ref:StrongRef<RemoteObligationFloor>,prepared_ownership_transfer_refs[StrongRef<MetaPreparedOwnershipTransferRecord>],terminal_audit_gate}`. Deterministic apply constructs a `TopologyState` successor with identical epoch, form, shard assignments, and routing but the phase-appropriate current/joint/new `meta_configuration_ref` plus this applied control; no topology object may retain the retired Meta configuration as current. Every phase is separate, and `CommitRetirementFloor` proves the new set owns all Meta prepared, certificate, and certified-remote obligations. The sole transfer format is the role-specialized `PreparedOwnershipTransferRecord<Meta>` defined above; no later generic or cross-role encoding exists. A current Meta prepared root may carry a prior-configuration entry only in that exact transfer state, and old ownership releases only after new ownership plus Raft/snapshot/apply/GC acknowledgement.

Shard membership is Meta-authorized and later Meta-adopted. `ShardReconfigurationAuthorizationSpec` is `{shard_id,topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,old_configuration_ref:RemoteConfigurationRef,expected_meta_remote_trust_generation,expected_meta_selected_old_evidence_ref:RemoteConfigurationRef,joint_and_final_canonical_configuration_bytes_and_digests,transition_nonce,payload_predicates,required_checkpoint_floor_remote_prepared_certificate_obligations,successor_evidence_recipe,terminal_audit_gate}`; its applied `ShardReconfigurationAuthorizationRecord` fixes the one permitted transition and current trust selector. Each `ShardConfigurationTransitionSpec` consumes the certified record and transfers every old-configuration owner. After `CommitRetirementFloor`, old and new quorums create `ShardConfigurationAdoptionEvidence {SameGroupCertificateHeader,authorization_identity,old/joint/new configuration identities,final_floor,through_shard_index/global_prefix,remote_obligation_commitment,predecessor_remote_configuration_evidence_identity,old_and_new_quorum_signatures,one_digest_signer_lock_ref}`. The successor `RemoteAuthorityConfigurationEvidence::Successor` is authenticated from the currently trusted predecessor and both quorums; new members alone cannot bootstrap it.

`RemoteGrantRetirementPlan` is the Meta-local pre-order object `{plan_id,basis_topology_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,basis_remote_trust_generation,retired_authority_domain,retired_configuration_ref:RemoteConfigurationRef,successor_configuration_ref:StrongRef<RemoteAuthorityConfigurationEvidence>,sorted_entries[{old_grant_id,old_grant_evidence_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantEvidence>,target_identity,consumer_domain,target_closure_commitment,disposition:ReplaceWithSuccessorGrant{successor_grant_body_recipe,required_consumer_adoption_predicate}|Release{release_request_body_recipe},required_six_stage_transition:RequestConsumerRelease->PublishConsumerReleaseEvidence->ApplyAuthorityRelease->PublishAuthorityReleaseAck->ConsumeReleaseAck->Acknowledged,completion_predicate}],complete_old_grant_set_and_target_coverage_digest,expected_consumer_root_digest,completion_floor_body_recipe}`. It names no future request, tombstone, ack, applied record, or result; adoption verifies the exhaustive old-grant set before selecting it. `ShardConfigurationAdoptionSpec` is Meta input `{authorization_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,adoption_evidence_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardConfigurationAdoptionEvidence>,expected_topology_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,expected_old_shard_configuration_ref:RemoteConfigurationRef,expected_remote_trust_generation,expected_selected_old_evidence_ref:RemoteConfigurationRef,successor_configuration_evidence_ref:StrongRef<RemoteAuthorityConfigurationEvidence>,expected_successor_evidence_digest,old_grant_retirement_plan_ref:StrongRef<RemoteGrantRetirementPlan>,terminal_audit_gate}`. Apply verifies the direct trust transition and atomically CASes both the topology shard entry and `RemoteConfigurationTrustRoot` selector/generation; neither may advance alone. Only then may the six-stage handshake release old-configuration grants and membership. Stale trust generation, anchor, topology, old/new signature domain, or successor bytes reject with no partial adoption.

Distributed GC separates preflight, semantic authorization/quarantine, physical completion, and aggregate completion. A stage-4 certificate is not release completion. `PortableRemoteReleaseAckEvidence` is consumer-local `{authority_domain,consumer_domain,grant_id,target_identity,release_nonce,ack_leaf_bytes_and_identity,authority_configuration_evidence:RemoteConfigurationRef,summary_entry_key,summary_inclusion_proof,permanent_release_proof_floor,authority_signatures}` and contains no CRSR, new retention grant, or cross-group strong edge. `GcRemoteReleaseCompletionRef` is the closed role-checked union `AuthorityPublished{publish_record_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionAckPublishRecord>,summary_entry_ref:StrongRef<RemoteReleaseSummaryEntry>,ack_leaf_ref:StrongRef<ExportLeaf<RemoteRetentionReleaseAckCertificate>>}|ConsumerAcknowledged{consume_record_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionConsumeAckRecord>,ack_leaf_ref:StrongRef<ExportLeaf<RemoteRetentionReleaseAckCertificate>>,current_no_old_grant_ref_proof_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionNoOldGrantProof>}|ImportedPermanent{evidence_ref:StrongRef<PortableRemoteReleaseAckEvidence>}`. The candidate's ownership/consumer role selects the one legal arm; every arm proves stage 5 or stage 6 plus the permanent summary floor. A request, stage-4 certificate, tombstone, plan, unsigned identity, or a newly granted CRSR cannot inhabit it. A shard first orders `ShardGcPreflightSpec {basis_shard_state:WeakStateIdentity,basis_shard_raft_index,basis_global_prefix,configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,topology_epoch,complete_typed_root_inventory_ref:StrongRef<GcRootInventory>,candidate_derivation_profile,excluded_obligation_commitment}`. Apply creates `ShardGcPreflightRecord {source_spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardGcPreflightSpec>,basis identities,generated current/cut/prepared/certificate/lease/key/derived/backup/replay/restore/remote inventories,exact_candidate_local_reclaim_set,excluded_obligations,candidate_set_digest}`; only afterward does the quorum create `ShardGcPreflightEvidence {SameGroupCertificateHeader,preflight_record_ref:StrongRef<ShardGcPreflightRecord>,candidate_set_digest,root_inventory_digest,one_digest_signer_lock_ref,quorum_signatures}`. Meta likewise builds `MetaGcPreflightRecord` for its local physical universe before ordering `GlobalGcAuthorizationSpec {basis_global_state:WeakStateIdentity,basis_global_prefix,meta_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,meta_preflight_record_ref:StrongRef<MetaGcPreflightRecord>,exact_meta_candidate_set,sorted_shard_preflight_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardGcPreflightEvidence>],exact_per_shard_candidate_commitments,excluded_global_obligation_commitment,completed_remote_release_proof_refs[GcRemoteReleaseCompletionRef],terminal_audit_gate}`. Apply creates `GlobalGcAuthorizationRecord` authorizing only those bounded sets; a planned remote release is not completion, and an active/ReleaseRequested grant target is never a reclaim candidate.

Each participant next orders a role-specific quarantine command. `ShardGcApplySpec` is `{authorization_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalGcAuthorizationRecord>,preflight_record_ref:StrongRef<ShardGcPreflightRecord>,expected_current_shard_state:WeakStateIdentity,expected_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,expected_topology_epoch,expected_root_inventory_digest,exact_authorized_local_reclaim_set,completed_remote_release_ack_refs[GcRemoteReleaseCompletionRef],current_reachability_recomputation_ref:StrongRef<GcReachabilityProof>,newly_reachable_disjoint_proof_ref:StrongRef<GcDisjointnessProof>}`. Followers recompute from the **current** role payload, both root slots, prepared/certificate/Raft state, every new protocol root, and the candidate command result. They require `reclaim_set ⊆ authorized_set ∩ preflight_set` and disjointness from the current reachable set; “unchanged or stronger” is not a relation. Apply creates `ShardGcReclaimAuthorizationRecord` and atomically installs `GcReclaimQuarantineRoot {authorization_identity,object_and_realization_set,quarantine_generation,state:AuthorizedNotStarted}`. Every object encoder, dedupe lookup, prepared receipt, command validator, and root publisher rejects a new retaining edge or realization selection to a quarantined identity. Cancellation may remove quarantine only before any physical-member start receipt; afterward resurrection is impossible.

Physical workers act only under that published quarantine and the same per-member Requested/Started/Completed idempotency machine defined for Local GC. Every Shard/Meta quarantine apply creates one `GcPhysicalOperationRecord::Requested` for every and only required member/target before dispatch. `GcPhysicalMemberReceipt {gc_id,authorization_identity,quarantine_generation,operation_id,idempotency_token_digest,storage_member_id,storage_profile_oid,target_inventory_digest,canonical_request_transcript_digest,exact_deleted_or_crypto_erased_inventory,pre_operation_physical_root_digest,post_operation_physical_root_digest,post_operation_probe_digest,durability_evidence,member_monotonic_start_and_completion_counters,started_at_observation,completed_at_observation,time_authority_profile_oid,signer_key_and_epoch,signature}` byte-matches its operation and cannot cover another member or target. After all members required by the storage profile finish, the shard orders `ShardGcPhysicalCompletionSpec {reclaim_authorization_record_ref:StrongRef<ShardGcReclaimAuthorizationRecord>,expected_quarantine_root_ref:StrongRef<GcReclaimQuarantineRoot>,sorted_member_receipt_refs[StrongRef<GcPhysicalMemberReceipt>],complete_member_and_target_bijection_proof_ref:StrongRef<GcPhysicalCompletionBijectionProof>,post_reclaim_inventory_ref:StrongRef<PhysicalInventory>,current_root_recheck_ref:StrongRef<GcReachabilityProof>,completed_two_sided_release_commitment}`. Apply verifies exact set equality and unchanged quarantine, moves it to `PhysicallyCompleted`, and creates `ShardGcPhysicalCompletionRecord`. Only then may the quorum export `ShardGcAppliedAck {SameGroupCertificateHeader,authorization_identity,completion_record_ref:StrongRef<ShardGcPhysicalCompletionRecord>,post_completion_state_root_ref:StrongRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,post_completion_shard_index/global_prefix,reclaimed_inventory_digest,retained_exclusion_digest,completed_two_sided_release_commitment,one_digest_signer_lock_ref,quorum_signatures}`.

Meta performs the symmetric `MetaGcPhysicalApplySpec -> MetaGcReclaimAuthorizationRecord/quarantine -> member operations/receipts -> MetaGcPhysicalCompletionSpec -> MetaGcPhysicalCompletionRecord`; authorization alone never counts as Meta-local reclaim. `GlobalGcProgressSpec {authorization_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalGcAuthorizationRecord>,expected_progress_generation,meta_status:Pending|Completed{completion_record_ref:StrongRef<MetaGcPhysicalCompletionRecord>},sorted_shard_statuses[{shard_id,status:Pending|Completed{ack_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardGcAppliedAck>}|FailedRetryable{evidence_digest}}],exact_required_participant_commitment,terminal_audit_gate}` may monotonically publish `PartialBlocking{missing_or_failed_participants}` and retains every unfinished quarantine/retry state; it never releases global authorization or claims completion. `GlobalGcCompletionSpec {authorization_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalGcAuthorizationRecord>,meta_completion_record_ref:StrongRef<MetaGcPhysicalCompletionRecord>,exact_sorted_shard_completion_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardGcAppliedAck>],complete_required_participant_and_reclaim_set_bijection_proof_ref:StrongRef<GlobalGcCompletionBijectionProof>,expected_latest_progress_generation,terminal_audit_gate}` requires the exact Meta completion plus one matching certified physical-completion ack from every and only required shard. Any missing/failed/duplicate/substituted participant makes the command invalid; successful apply can select only `Completed`. Checkpoints, configuration transitions, backup/restore, key destruction, and topology retirement root every in-flight stage. Tests cover stale preflights, newly reachable objects, attempted resurrection/dedupe, configuration/topology change, cancellation races, missing/duplicate member receipts, progress/completion races, crash at each quarantine/deletion/completion publication, Meta-local partial failure, and all six-stage remote-release interleavings.

Effects use a two-stage acyclic construction. A shard first builds `ShardEffectBasis {global_txn_id,registration_generation,shard_id,registered_snapshot,topology_epoch,active_meta_projection_root_ref:StrongRef<ActiveMetaProjectionRoot>,operation_audit_admission_commitment,sorted_coordinate_bindings,write_key_material_projection_refs[StrongRef<ShardKeyMaterialProjection>],final_effect_refs[ConditionalCoordinateRef],logical_delta_fragment_template_ref:StrongRef<LogicalDeltaTemplate>,read_witness_refs[StrongRef],final_write_summary,constraint_requests_and_deltas,resource_charge_basis,authority_projection_digest,intent_semantics_oid,basis_effect_digest}`. Prepared traversal follows the conditional effect refs strongly; after the global marker assigns the commit coordinate, only matching activated/provisional effect cuts may stop them, while partition versions, delta leases, backup, and replay roots independently retain what remains promised. `basis_effect_digest` hashes the effect-only projection through `intent_semantics_oid`; it excludes every authorization decision, audit object, outcome preparation, resource transition object, fragment wrapper, prepare record, and certificate. `ParticipantRoutingDerivationProof` is `{topology_state_ref:StrongRef,initial_footprint_commitment,ordered_fixed_point_rounds[{round,prior_participant_set,discovered_cross_partition_effects,discovered_cascades,discovered_constraint_owners,resulting_participant_set}],final_read_write_cascade_constraint_footprint,partition_function_oid,proof_checker_version}`. Meta reaches that deterministic fixed point and builds `ParticipantRoutingCertificate {SameGroupCertificateHeader,registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,topology_state_ref:StrongRef,sorted_basis_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardEffectBasis>],sorted_participants,sorted_constraint_owners,complete_read_write_cascade_constraint_footprint,partition_derivation_proof_ref:StrongRef<ParticipantRoutingDerivationProof>,complete_participant_commitment,operation_audit_admission_commitment,aggregate_template_digest,global_final_effect_digest,quorum_signatures}`, where `global_final_effect_digest = H("fgdb:global-effect:v1", sorted(shard_id,basis_effect_digest))`. Missing or extra bases/owners, a non-fixed-point cascade, or an unsupported routing proof fails closed.

The operation ticket, when required, has already passed external issuance, Meta `AuditTicketAdmissionSpec` mirror, and exclusive registration claim. After the participant fixed point exists, Meta builds exactly one standalone `GlobalAuthorizationDecisionRecord {registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,operation_audit_admission:OperationAuditAdmission::Claimed|NotRequired,mutation_permit_ref:StrongRef<MutationPermitRecord>,authority_ceiling_digest,routing_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ParticipantRoutingCertificate>,sorted_basis_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardEffectBasis>],global_final_effect_digest,expected_branch_heads,expected_branch_key_epochs,constraint_and_resource_basis_commitment,policy_epoch,revocation_index,decision,authorization_audit_gate:AuthorizationAuditGate}`. A Required authorization gate names that already-claimed operation ticket; this object never points to a future ticket. The global validator replays the permit across the union, including hidden cascades and disclosure contracts; per-shard approvals cannot substitute. Meta next creates resource transitions, `GlobalTxnOutcomePreparationRecord`, and the immutable transaction audit-basis commitment—but no outcome event, resolution, or terminal gate yet. Admission orders and publishes that exact still-pending bundle.

Only then may a participant build `ShardEffectFragment {basis_ref:StrongRef<ShardEffectBasis>,prepare_admission_record_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,admission_generation,routing_certificate_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ParticipantRoutingCertificate>,global_authorization_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalAuthorizationDecisionRecord>,global_resource_transition_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ResourceLedgerTransition>],global_outcome_preparation_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalTxnOutcomePreparationRecord>,operation_audit_claim_commitment,transaction_audit_basis_commitment,fragment_envelope_digest}`. Every Meta object is an exact certified-remote wrapper bound to the Meta authority domain/configuration, this shard consumer domain, payload availability, and two-sided grant; only `basis_ref` is shard-local. The admission ExportLeaf closure owns the ticket claim without exposing a raw cross-group ticket ref. Wrong role/group/incarnation/configuration/grant or a locally encoded Meta `StrongRef` is unrepresentable and covered by substitution tests. The admission identifies all exact objects/commitments and includes this shard; the envelope digest is excluded from `global_final_effect_digest`. Prepare certificates bind the claimed-pending operation-audit and transaction-basis commitments.

Every protected terminal—not only an admitted W12 write—first freezes exactly the state that its signed event will terminalize. `TerminalAuditOwner` is the closed union `Local{owner:LocalAuditTicketOwner}|LocalPendingBegin{reservation_identity,txn_token,request_basis_commitment}|Meta{owner:AuditTicketOwner}|MetaPendingBegin{reservation_identity,scoped_begin_key_digest,request_basis_commitment}`; pending-begin owner arms are legal only before registration for their exact role's BeginTerminal scope and resolve `AuditResolutionOrigin::Unclaimed`, while Local/Meta owner arms require the registered claim domain. Every tag must match group, ticket admission, request basis, and freeze scope. `ControlTerminalBasisHoldRoot {domain,freeze_scope,typed_held_predicates[ControlTerminalHeldPredicate],strong_dependency_refs[RegisteredStrongRef],coordinate_index_config_key_policy_resource_continuity_coverage_bitmap,conflict_matrix_version,body_digest}` is generated from the exact control spec/expected conditions. Every possibly conflicting mutation, checkpoint cut, GC, key/config/policy retirement, and restore/backup transition consults the active hold root and must wait, transfer it exactly, or reject.

`AuditTerminalFreezeRecord` is an immutable predecessor-linked Local-or-Meta object `{domain:{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,group_role:Local|Meta,group_id},predecessor_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalFreezeRecord>?,state:Armed{freeze_scope,owner:TerminalAuditOwner,ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,expected_state_conditions_digest,terminal_semantic_basis_commitment,control_terminal_basis_hold_root_ref:StrongRef<ControlTerminalBasisHoldRoot>,scaffolding_applied_ref:AppliedControlRef}|Consumed{terminal_input_identity,assigned_role_order,hold_disposition:ConsumedByTerminal}|ReleasePending{release_admission_closed_at_role_order,control_terminal_basis_hold_root_ref:StrongRef<ControlTerminalBasisHoldRoot>,closed_terminal_attempt_index_generation,closed_signer_release_fence_vector[{signer_id,event_journal_generation,resolution_journal_generation,release_fence_receipt_ref}],blocking_set_proof_ref:StrongRef<AuditSignerBlockingSetProof>,begin_release_applied_ref:AppliedControlRef}|Released{typed_no_terminal_proof_ref:StrongRef<NoTerminalSignatureOrOrderProof>,hold_release_commitment,release_applied_ref:AppliedControlRef}}`; `AuditTerminalFreezeIndex` maps `(domain,owner,ticket)` to the unique latest version and forbids two successors. Prepared/configuration floors, backup/restore, and GC retain each live hold. The terminal apply or FinalizeRelease is the only operation that releases it.

`AuditTerminalFreezeSpec` is the closed lifecycle-scaffolding transition `Arm{group_role,freeze_scope,owner:TerminalAuditOwner,ticket_ref,expected_state_conditions_digest,terminal_semantic_basis_commitment,control_terminal_basis_hold_root_ref:StrongRef<ControlTerminalBasisHoldRoot>,expected_index_absence_or_matching_retry,terminal_audit_gate:LifecycleScaffoldingNotRequired}|BeginRelease{group_role,armed_freeze_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalFreezeRecord>,expected_index_value:Armed,expected_terminal_attempt_index_generation,sorted_signer_release_fence_receipts,blocking_set_proof_ref:StrongRef<AuditSignerBlockingSetProof>,expected_state_conditions_digest,terminal_audit_gate:LifecycleScaffoldingNotRequired}|FinalizeRelease{group_role,release_pending_freeze_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalFreezeRecord>,no_terminal_signature_or_order_proof_ref:StrongRef<NoTerminalSignatureOrOrderProof>,expected_index_value:ReleasePending,expected_closed_attempt_and_signer_journal_vector,exact_hold_release_recipe,terminal_audit_gate:LifecycleScaffoldingNotRequired}`. Arm scopes are `LocalControl`, `LocalBeginTerminal`, `MetaControl{registered_global_control_tag,spec_body_digest,expected_state_conditions_digest}`, `MetaBeginTerminal`, `MetaStatementPublishOrAbort`, `MetaActiveCancel`, and `MetaReadClose`; Arm apply atomically validates the complete basis, installs its hold, and freezes it before any terminal signature. BeginRelease first makes every signer in the complete eligible universe—or a registered blocking set proved to intersect every legal event and resolution threshold subset—durably reject new attempts/locks/shares for this freeze at the named journal generations, then selects ReleasePending without dropping the hold. FinalizeRelease byte-matches proof/freeze/ticket/domain/basis, unchanged generations, and exact hold release and alone produces Released; `Consumed` remains an atomic terminal output. Admitted Local mutation and W12 write use their ordered final-certification reservation holds instead.

`AuditTerminalFreezeRef` is the closed union `LocalMutation{fence_ref:StrongRef<LocalTerminalAdmissionFence>,required_fence_state:Armed,final_certification_reservation_ref:StrongRef<LocalFinalCertificationReservation>,required_reservation_state:Active}|LocalControl{freeze_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalFreezeRecord>,required_scope:LocalControl}|LocalBeginTerminal{freeze_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalFreezeRecord>,reservation_identity,txn_token,request_basis_commitment,required_scope:LocalBeginTerminal}|MetaControl{freeze_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalFreezeRecord>,required_scope:MetaControl{registered_global_control_tag,spec_body_digest,expected_state_conditions_digest}}|MetaBeginTerminal{freeze_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalFreezeRecord>,reservation_identity,scoped_begin_key_digest,request_basis_commitment,required_scope:MetaBeginTerminal}|MetaStatementPublishOrAbort{freeze_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalFreezeRecord>,required_scope:MetaStatementPublishOrAbort}|MetaActiveCancel{freeze_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalFreezeRecord>,required_scope:MetaActiveCancel}|MetaReadClose{freeze_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalFreezeRecord>,required_scope:MetaReadClose}|MetaAdmittedWrite{fence_ref:StrongRef<MetaTerminalAdmissionFence>,required_fence_state:Armed,final_certification_reservation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalFinalCertificationReservation>,required_reservation_state:Active}`. The exact SequenceNeutralSpec envelope field matrix makes this ref required on every final protected terminal tag and forbidden elsewhere; it is never silently injected into a body. An admitted-write plan byte-matches the reservation's one selected terminal. Final protected apply atomically consumes its unique reservation/freeze or constructs the terminal successor while Armed; release is legal only after ReleasePending with the typed proof that no signature share, quorum object, final command, or candidate root exists.

`NoTerminalSignatureOrOrderProof` is an authority-local quorum certificate `{SameGroupCertificateHeader,freeze_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalFreezeRecord>,required_freeze_state:ReleasePending,ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,owner:TerminalAuditOwner,terminal_semantic_basis_commitment,plan_disposition:NeverCreated{terminal_attempt_index_absence_path,signer_release_fence_and_attempt_absence_proofs_by_signer}|SemanticPlanAbandoned{terminal_plan_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalSigningPlan>,abandonment_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalPlanAbandonment>,all_event_attempt_disposition_refs[],no_event_or_resolution_object_proof,retired_attempt_epoch_floor},audit_terminal_attempt_index_root_digest,sorted_event_signer_journal_closures,sorted_resolution_signer_journal_closures,certificate_ledger_root_digest,complete_signer_set_and_key_epoch,raft_nonorder_evidence:{term,configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,read_barrier_index,commit_index,applied_index,closed_role_order,terminal_command_index_absence_path},candidate_root_and_audit_fence_absence_proof,external_audit_continuity_digest_and_cas_version,quiescence_barrier_id,checker_version,certificate_attempt_plan_ref,certificate_signer_lock_refs,quorum_signatures}`. All paths, release fences, attempt dispositions, signer-journal closures, and authority roots are observed at one linearizable quiescence barrier after BeginRelease selected ReleasePending; generations equal the closed vector in that state. A release fence covers every current eligible event/resolution signer or a proved blocking set intersecting every legal subset. NeverCreated is invalid if any matching semantic plan/signing attempt/lock/share existed. SemanticPlanAbandoned requires every concrete event attempt terminally superseded/abandoned with no event; a partial-share attempt needs quorum-impossibility and signer-closure evidence. The certificate is built after BeginRelease and before FinalizeRelease, names no future release command/result/root, and remains through freeze/audit retirement floors. Any missing signer/blocking proof, later-orderable command, candidate, stale Raft/configuration basis, or latent completable attempt makes release ineligible.

`AuditTerminalPlanAbandonSpec` is the exact freeze-backed Local-or-Meta maintenance input `{group_role,release_pending_freeze_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalFreezeRecord>,terminal_plan_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalSigningPlan>,expected_attempt_index_entry:PlanSelected|EventAttemptSelected|AttemptSuperseded,expected_per_signer_release_fence_vector,event_attempt_disposition_refs[],no_event_or_resolution_object_proof_ref:StrongRef<AuditStageNonpublicationProof>,complete_eligible_signer_universe,attempt_epoch_retirement_recipe,terminal_audit_gate:LifecycleScaffoldingNotRequired}`. It is legal only while the freeze is ReleasePending, every concrete event attempt is either share-free or quorum-impossible and durably closed, no event/resolution/terminal order/candidate exists, and every otherwise eligible signer is release-fenced. Apply creates `AuditTerminalPlanAbandonment {freeze_identity,terminal_plan_identity,closed_attempt_index_generation,closed_signer_journal_vector,event_attempt_disposition_commitment,retired_attempt_epoch_floor,maintenance_applied_index}` and marks the semantic plan AbandonedForFreezeRelease. It erases nothing and authorizes no replacement terminal. Any event, resolution attempt, prepared terminal, order, or candidate makes true plan abandonment permanently illegal. Admitted-write reservations cannot use this spec; they keep the selected terminal and use signing-attempt supersession until completion. All abandoned plan/attempt/lock/share evidence remains rooted through FinalizeRelease and the audit-retirement floor.

After the freeze/reservation, matching mutation/read/control/no-effect audit bytes use one acyclic, crash-recoverable signing pipeline; only the completed ticket/event/resolution triple becomes the final `TerminalAuditGate`. `SequenceNeutralAuditEventBody` is the pre-order immutable `{ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,owner:TerminalAuditOwner,chosen_terminal_kind,semantic_input_commitment,authorization_decision_digest,outcome:TransactionMutation|ControlMutation|ReadResult|Denied|Failed|Abandoned,event_attested_at,stable_ticket_domain_profile_epoch_and_unresolved_membership_commitment,body_digest}`. Its registered digest excludes only `body_digest` and contains no plan/attempt/lock/share/aggregate, mutable audit-continuity head/CAS version/append position, future role order/HLC/marker/candidate, or result root. `SequenceNeutralAuditResolutionBody` is `{ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,owner,terminal_class,expected_event_body_digest,stable_ticket_domain_profile_epoch_and_unresolved_membership_commitment,resolution_attested_at,body_digest}` with the same exclusions. `AuditTerminalSigningPlan` is the immutable semantic plan `{plan_id,plan_generation,predecessor_plan_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalSigningPlan>?,terminal_freeze_ref:AuditTerminalFreezeRef,ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,owner:TerminalAuditOwner,chosen_terminal_kind,semantic_input_commitment,event_body_ref:StrongRef<SequenceNeutralAuditEventBody>,event_body_digest,resolution_body_ref:StrongRef<SequenceNeutralAuditResolutionBody>,resolution_body_digest,event_signer_policy_ref,resolution_signer_policy_ref,event_threshold_rule,resolution_threshold_rule,signature_algorithm_and_encoding}`. It selects no concrete signer subset and binds only stable ticket/domain/profile/epoch/unresolved-membership facts; unrelated ticket issue/resolve and the mutable external audit head may advance without invalidating it.

Concrete subsets are replaceable attempts. `AuditEventSigningAttemptPlan {attempt_id,terminal_plan_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalSigningPlan>,event_body_digest,configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,canonical_signer_subset[{signer_id,signing_key_id,signer_set_epoch,key_epoch}],threshold,signature_algorithm_and_encoding}` is installed through nonsemantic maintenance before any event lock. For each selected signer, `AuditEventSignerLock {attempt_plan_ref:StrongRef<AuditEventSigningAttemptPlan>,terminal_plan_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalSigningPlan>,event_body_digest,signer_id,signing_key_id,signer_set_epoch,key_epoch,canonical_signing_transcript_digest,one_digest_only=true}` is signer-journal-published before `AuditEventSignatureShare`. `AuditEventRecord` deterministically adds `{terminal_plan_ref,event_attempt_plan_ref,event_body_ref,event_lock_refs,event_signature_share_refs,signer_subset_bitmap,threshold,canonical_aggregate_or_signature_set}` to the exact pre-order body; its signing transcript is `H(domain,terminal_plan_oid,event_attempt_oid,event_body_digest,signer identity/key/epochs)` and thereby binds the plan without a plan↔event cycle.

Only after the event exists may maintenance install `AuditResolutionSigningAttemptPlan {attempt_id,terminal_plan_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalSigningPlan>,event_ref:StrongRef<AuditEventRecord>,resolution_body_digest,configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,canonical_signer_subset[{signer_id,signing_key_id,signer_set_epoch,key_epoch}],threshold,signature_algorithm_and_encoding}`. Each selected signer publishes `AuditResolutionSignerLock {attempt_plan_ref:StrongRef<AuditResolutionSigningAttemptPlan>,terminal_plan_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalSigningPlan>,event_ref:StrongRef<AuditEventRecord>,resolution_body_digest,signer_id,signing_key_id,signer_set_epoch,key_epoch,canonical_signing_transcript_digest,one_digest_only=true}` before its share. `AuditTicketResolution` deterministically adds the terminal plan, resolution attempt, event ref, exact resolution lock/share bijection, signer bitmap, threshold, and canonical aggregate/signature set to the pre-order resolution body. Signer identity/key/epoch are part of every lock/share transcript, so selected signers cannot share a lock ObjectId. Missing, duplicate, unplanned, wrong-key, wrong-epoch, reordered, or aggregate-mismatched shares fail closed.

`AuditSigningAttemptSupersedeSpec` is the nonsemantic maintenance input `{stage:Event|Resolution,terminal_plan_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalSigningPlan>,old_attempt_plan_ref:StrongRef<AuditEventSigningAttemptPlan|AuditResolutionSigningAttemptPlan>,new_attempt_plan_ref:StrongRef<AuditEventSigningAttemptPlan|AuditResolutionSigningAttemptPlan>,required_identical_body_and_event_commitment,old_signer_release_fence_vector,old_share_state:ZeroShares|PartialShares{complete_share_bitmap,quorum_impossibility_proof_ref:StrongRef<AuditSignerQuorumImpossibilityProof>},no_completed_stage_object_or_terminal_order_candidate_proof_ref:StrongRef<AuditStageNonpublicationProof>,terminal_freeze_or_final_certification_reservation_ref,terminal_audit_gate:LifecycleScaffoldingNotRequired}`. Every old signer capable of completing the subset must close that attempt; the new attempt uses a higher ID, the identical terminal/event/resolution body, and a currently legal subset. Event supersession is illegal after an event exists; resolution supersession preserves the exact event. It never changes/release the terminal freeze, final-certification selection, ticket, semantic body, or result. Old attempts/locks/shares/closures remain rooted. Thus signer loss before or after partial shares cannot strand an admitted terminal, while two attempts can never both complete. True freeze release/terminal-plan abandonment remains the separate preterminal path below.

`AuditTerminalAttemptRecord` is a predecessor-linked durable stage chain `{predecessor_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalAttemptRecord>?,terminal_plan_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalSigningPlan>,state:PlanSelected|EventAttemptSelected{attempt_plan_ref:StrongRef<AuditEventSigningAttemptPlan>}|EventLocksPublished{attempt_plan_ref,event_lock_refs[StrongRef<AuditEventSignerLock>],complete_planned_lock_bijection}|EventSharesCollected{attempt_plan_ref,event_lock_refs,event_share_refs[StrongRef<AuditEventSignatureShare>],event_ref:StrongRef<AuditEventRecord>}|ResolutionAttemptSelected{event_ref,resolution_attempt_plan_ref:StrongRef<AuditResolutionSigningAttemptPlan>}|ResolutionLocksPublished{event_ref,resolution_attempt_plan_ref,resolution_lock_refs[StrongRef<AuditResolutionSignerLock>],complete_planned_lock_bijection}|Prepared{event_ref,resolution_attempt_plan_ref,resolution_lock_refs,resolution_share_refs[StrongRef<AuditResolutionSignatureShare>],resolution_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicketResolution>,terminal_gate_digest}|Ordered{terminal_input_identity,role_order}|CandidateApplied{candidate_root_identity}|ExternalCasCommitted{receipt_ref:StrongRef<AuditExternalCasReceipt>}|Mirrored{record_ref:AppliedControlRef}|AttemptSuperseded{stage,old_attempt_identity,new_attempt_identity,supersede_evidence_ref:StrongRef<AuditSigningAttemptSupersession>}}`. Each successor retains its predecessor and needed artifacts. The matching prepared root plus generated `AuditTerminalAttemptIndex` maps `(domain,freeze_or_reservation_identity,terminal_plan_identity)` to the latest record and separately maps each concrete signing-attempt ID to Active|Superseded|Completed; exact absence/membership proofs are therefore available even at PlanSelected.

Before event locks, validation checks the Armed freeze/Active final-certification reservation rather than reserving semantic order. Immediately before ordering, the final transaction/control input consumes that hold, takes the then-next role order/HLC through the order supplement, and records Ordered. External audit resolution then CASes from the **then-current** continuity head, removes exactly this ticket, assigns chain position, and commits the exact event/resolution/candidate receipt; the mirror verifies it is the direct successor returned by that CAS. The signed bodies never bind a stale expected head. A crash resumes the selected or legally superseded attempt, locked digests, collected shares, durable stage, and exact external CAS. A definitive external conflicting result triggers fail-closed recovery/permanent-gap handling and retains the attempt; it never exposes the candidate. Decision/shard apply verify the mirrored terminal against the original claim and hold. Crash/DPOR suites race two unrelated ticket issue/resolve operations, every scope/lock/share/supersede stage, alternate terminal, leader loss, reproposal, external CAS, and mirror recovery.

`ShardPrepareCommand` is fence-free canonical input `{command_version,registration_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,prepare_admission_record_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,admission_generation,admission_global_logical_command_seq,admission_global_commit_seq,expected_prior_global_applied_prefix,routing_certificate_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ParticipantRoutingCertificate>,basis_ref:StrongRef<ShardEffectBasis>,fragment_ref:StrongRef<ShardEffectFragment>,active_meta_projection_root_ref:StrongRef<ActiveMetaProjectionRoot>,shard_pre_command_base_availability_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ShardPreCommandBaseAvailabilityCertificate>,expected_shard_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,expected_topology_epoch,expected_policy_epoch,expected_revocation_index,expected_branch_heads,expected_branch_key_epochs,prepare_key:{global_txn_id,registration_generation,admission_generation},local_prepare_generation}`. Before ordering, the shard first advances through every global command up to and including the unique admission—typed projection for every relevant control and exhaustive irrelevance proof otherwise—then verifies the active meta projection, topology/policy/revocation/key/audit state, configuration, admission, basis, fragment, and exact D1 base certificate byte-for-byte. Prepare does not advance that prefix a second time. A stale projection or matching abort tombstone rejects. Apply builds `ShardPrepareRecord {command_ref:StrongRef<ShardPrepareCommand|ShardDecisionApplyCommand>,prepare_key,shard_id,shard_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,topology_epoch,admission_global_prefix,local_prepare_generation,predecessor_ref:StrongRef<ShardPrepareRecord>?,basis_ref:StrongRef<ShardEffectBasis>,fragment_ref:StrongRef<ShardEffectFragment>,reservation_refs[StrongRef<ConstraintReservationRecord>],base/current_closure_inventory,state:Prepared|GloballyCommitted{global_logical_command_seq,global_commit_seq,decision_identity}|GloballyAborted{global_logical_command_seq,decision_identity}|Applied{global_logical_command_seq,global_commit_seq?,decision_identity,fragment_batch_ref:StrongRef<LogicalDeltaBatch>?}|GcEligible{terminal_floor_ref:StrongRef}}` and atomically installs the canonical constraint reservations plus a `ShardCommandRecord`; no local fence appears in either. Successors preserve the base inventory and strengthen the current closure. The shard-group `ShardPrepareCertificate` then quorum-signs its `SameGroupCertificateHeader` plus `{prepare_record_ref,admission/registration/routing remote identities,prepare_key,admission_generation/admission global prefix,shard/topology/active-projection identities,registered snapshot,expected heads/key epochs,basis/fragment/global-effect/witness/write/constraint/resource/authorization/audit commitments,pre_command_base_availability_certificate_ref,verifier_version,quorum_signatures}`. Followers recompute all fields. A late prepare after an abort tombstone, a second admission generation under one registration, or any mismatched/stale admission/routing/fragment/security projection is rejected; the later decision adds its assigned global sequence.

`ConstraintReservationRecord` is an owner-shard object `{reservation_id,constraint_id,canonical_domain_key_or_range,owner_shard,topology_epoch,prepare_key,registration_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,prepare_admission_record_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,routing_certificate_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ParticipantRoutingCertificate>,exact_global_basis_digest,before_contribution,after_contribution,predecessor_ref:StrongRef<ConstraintReservationRecord>?,state:Held|Consumed{global_decision_identity}|Released{global_decision_identity}}`. `GlobalConstraintReservationCertificate` is produced by that owner shard after prepare and is `{SameGroupCertificateHeader,reservation_record_ref:StrongRef<ConstraintReservationRecord>,prepare_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ShardPrepareCertificate>,admission_record_remote_identity,constraint/domain/owner/topology identities,prepare_key,exact_global_basis_digest,before/after contribution,registered_snapshot,expiration:None,quorum_signatures}`. Meta receives only its generated `ExportLeaf` through a certified-remote ref.

For a constraint whose topology declares meta ownership, admission apply creates `MetaConstraintReservationRecord {reservation_id,constraint_id,canonical_domain_key_or_range,topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,admission_spec_ref:StrongRef<GlobalPrepareAdmissionSpec>,admission_generation,exact_global_basis_digest,before_aggregate,after_aggregate,predecessor_ref:StrongRef<MetaConstraintReservationRecord>?,state:Held|Consumed{global_txn_command_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnCommand>,global_logical_command_seq}|Released{applied_abort_ref:AppliedAbortRef}}` from the spec's pre-order request. `ConstraintReservationRef` is the closed tag `LocalMeta{reservation_ref:StrongRef<MetaConstraintReservationRecord>} | RemoteShard{reservation_certificate_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalConstraintReservationCertificate>}`. `GlobalTxnCommand::Commit` names the exact complete sorted set; meta apply consumes local reservations atomically and each shard decision consumes its remote reservations. Abort names whatever remote certificates already exist, releases all meta reservations, and sends the published abort to every admitted shard so a present or late reservation cannot survive. Reservations are acquired in canonical order; clock timeout, suspicion, or coordinator loss has no effect.

`DistributedSerializationCertificate` is meta-owned and sequence-neutral and counter-free `{SameGroupCertificateHeader,attempt_key:{global_txn_id,registration_generation},lifecycle_basis:ReadOnly{read_routing_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ReadParticipantRoutingCertificate>}|ReadWrite{prepare_admission_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,admission_generation,routing_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ParticipantRoutingCertificate>},held_final_certification_basis_commitment,conflict_index_basis:WeakStateIdentity,conflict_index_basis_digest:WeakDigest,overlapping_attempt_key_set_commitment,candidate_read_witness_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef],candidate_write_summary_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef],candidate_edges[{kind:wr|ww|rw,from_attempt_key,to_attempt_key,witness_or_version_proof_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef}],retained_graph_projection_digest,scc_verifier_version,acyclic_result,conservative_fallbacks[],quorum_signatures}`. `GlobalConflictIndex` is `{basis_global_logical_command_seq,entries[(global_txn_id,registration_generation) -> {snapshot/start/terminal prefixes,state:Active|PrepareAdmitted|Committed|Aborted|ReadClosed,admission_generation?,participants,read_witness_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef],write_summary_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef],incoming/outgoing_edges,overlap_close_floor}],safe_snapshot_frontier}`. Every meta follower reconstructs both directions of `may_affect`, verifies every routed shard/constraint contribution, and reruns the registered SCC algorithm; stale/missing support rejects. `GlobalAttemptIndex`, `GlobalTxnOutcomeIndex`, and the matching conflict entry must make the same lifecycle transition atomically. A new registration generation never overwrites an older overlapping generation; each entry remains rooted until its own overlap-close rule proves no future registered transaction can add an edge. The certificate names the conflict/head/constraint basis later held by `GlobalFinalCertificationReservation`; assigned next logical/commit counters occur only in `MetaOrderAttemptInput`.

`GlobalTxnCommand` is the closed union with common `{command_version,registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,prepare_admission_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,terminal_admission_fence_ref:StrongRef<MetaTerminalAdmissionFence>,required_terminal_admission_fence_state:Armed,final_certification_reservation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalFinalCertificationReservation>,required_final_certification_state:Active,admission_generation,meta_pre_command_base_availability_certificate_ref:StrongRef<MetaPreCommandBaseAvailabilityCertificate>,order_attempt_input_ref:StrongRef<MetaOrderAttemptInput>,order_attempt_availability_certificate_ref:StrongRef<MetaOrderAttemptAvailabilityCertificate>,topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,policy_epoch,revocation_index}` and exactly one intent. The supplement alone supplies both expected semantic counters when applicable and HLC evidence; neither is signed into the audit event/resolution. A harmless intervening Meta command retires/replaces only the provably unordered supplement against the same still-Active reservation and Armed fence. Dynamic basis fields are integrity projections of the reservation, not fresh CAS gates. `Commit{routing_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ParticipantRoutingCertificate>,participant_prepare_certificate_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardPrepareCertificate>],distributed_serialization_certificate_ref:StrongRef<DistributedSerializationCertificate>,constraint_reservation_refs[ConstraintReservationRef],global_authorization_decision_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAuthorizationDecisionRecord>,resource_transition_refs[StrongRef<ResourceLedgerTransition>],global_outcome_preparation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnOutcomePreparationRecord>,terminal_audit_gate:TerminalAuditGate,expected_branch_heads[WeakMarkerIdentity],expected_branch_key_epochs,global_final_effect_digest}` requires exact admission/fence/reservation/order-subject equality, one valid prepare for every admitted participant, the complete reservation set, and byte-equality across every serialization/auth/resource/outcome/audit field; apply assigns the exact next GlobalLogicalCommandSeq and, only for Commit, the exact next GlobalCommitSeq from the supplement, atomically marks it Ordered, consumes the final-certification reservation, and constructs/selects the unique TerminalOrdered fence successor. `AbortAfterAdmission{stable_reason,no_effect_proof_ref:StrongRef,known_prepare_certificate_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardPrepareCertificate>],known_remote_constraint_reservation_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalConstraintReservationCertificate>],meta_constraint_reservation_refs[StrongRef<MetaConstraintReservationRecord>],abort_authorization_decision_ref:StrongRef<AuthorizationDecisionRecord>,resource_release_refs[StrongRef<ResourceLedgerTransition>],global_outcome_preparation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnOutcomePreparationRecord>,terminal_audit_gate:TerminalAuditGate,expected_conflict_index_basis:WeakStateIdentity}` is constructible only from the matching Active MetaAbort reservation, matching MetaOrderSubject::Terminal supplement, published admission, and pre-order no-effect/authorization/release/audit evidence even if no participant prepared; known certificates are retained only for deterministic release. It adopts no effects, creates no marker/delta, releases every reserved Meta resource named by that selection, consumes the certification reservation, constructs/selects the unique terminal fence successor, and terminalizes conflict/attempt/outcome state. Shard abort acknowledgements necessarily arise only after decision -> certificate publication -> shard apply; they gate client completion, attempt compaction, remote-retention release, and GC, never construction/admission of this abort command. Active-but-unadmitted cancellation is exclusively `GlobalAttemptCancelSpec`, so the two abort paths cannot race.

Meta transaction apply assigns the next global logical sequence/HLC; commit also assigns commit sequence. Commit builds marker/heads/terminal outcome/constraints/payload; abort builds terminal no-effect state; then apply constructs `GlobalTxnRecord` and candidate `GlobalStateRoot`, never shard batches. A required terminal audit gate keeps that candidate fenced until external CAS and the exact next Meta mirror record publish it. Only then is `GlobalDecisionCertificate` built, with `SameGroupCertificateHeader`, and quorum-signs `{global_txn_record_ref,resulting_global_state_root_ref,terminal_audit_mirror_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,prepare_admission_record_ref,admission_generation,exact participants,meta term/index,assigned sequences/HLC,decision,marker/effect digest,topology_epoch,retention_floor}`. Deterministic signer selection/bytes are ledgered before release. `GlobalDecisionCertificatePublishSpec {decision_certificate_ref,expected transaction/root/mirror identities,terminal_audit_gate}` then installs it in the global registry; only this published certificate is exportable. Recovery uses exact ledgered bytes under the retained decision configuration and never substitutes another signer transcript.

`ShardAbortTombstone` is `{prepare_key,prepare_admission_record_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,decision_certificate_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalDecisionCertificate>,decision_publish_record_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,shard_id,topology_epoch,applied_shard_raft_index,global_abort_logical_command_seq,state:TerminalAbort}`. The consumer-local wrappers are rooted in the shard's applied-decision index/configuration floor until compaction; no bare remote identity or local `StrongRef` can replace them. `ShardDecisionApplyCommand` is `{decision_certificate_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalDecisionCertificate>,decision_publish_record_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,prepare_key,expected_prepare_record_ref?,expected_absent_or_matching_abort_tombstone,expected_prior_global_applied_logical_command_seq,exact_decision_global_logical_command_seq,expected_topology_epoch,shard_pre_command_base_availability_certificate_ref}`. Its D1 certificate uses the exact current domain/config/predicate and complete decision/publish plus prior-state closure. Commit requires Prepared; abort accepts Prepared or proven absence and installs the terminal tombstone when absent. At global decision `N`, deterministic apply consumes/releases reservations, materializes hidden fragment effects/batch for commit, and creates `ShardDecisionInstallRecord {command_ref:StrongRef<ShardDecisionApplyCommand>,prepare_key,decision_certificate_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalDecisionCertificate>,decision_publish_record_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,resulting_terminal_prepare_or_tombstone_ref:StrongRef,fragment_batch_ref:StrongRef<LogicalDeltaBatch>?,decision_global_prefix,precomputable_transition_commitment}`. The transition commitment hashes only prior shard-state identity, command identity, assigned shard/global order, and already constructed result identities; it excludes the future payload, command record, and root. Apply advances only `N-1 -> N`; after all results exist, `ShardCommandRecord.resulting_shard_payload_digest` cross-checks the constructed payload. It never jumps through the later Meta audit mirror or certificate-publication control. That record/root is durable but not yet a visibility acknowledgement.

The shard must next apply the exact audit-mirror `MetaControlProjectionCertificate` at `N+1` (and any preceding required control in order). Only that projection can make `audit_visible_global_prefix >= N`. From the post-mirror root, the quorum creates `ShardAppliedAck {SameGroupCertificateHeader,decision_certificate_identity,decision_publish_record_identity,audit_mirror_record_identity,prepare_key,terminal_result:Prepared{terminal_prepare_record_ref}|NoPrepare{abort_tombstone_ref},resulting_post_mirror_shard_state_root_ref:StrongRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,fragment_batch_ref:StrongRef<LogicalDeltaBatch>?,global_applied_logical_command_seq>=N+1,decision_global_logical_command_seq:N,global_applied_commit_seq,local_raft_index,audit_visible_prefix>=N,shard_payload_floor_ref,quorum_signatures}`. No pre-mirror ack is exportable. Meta publishes this typed ack in its directory and requires one from every admitted participant before global delta construction, client completion, attempt compaction, remote release, or GC. Retry reproduces the same terminal commitment; decision install never bypasses the audit mirror.

After every committed participant has produced its batch and acknowledgement, meta constructs `GlobalLogicalDeltaBatch {global_txn_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnRecord>,marker_identity:WeakMarkerIdentity,global_commit_seq,sorted_fragment_batches[{shard_id,fragment_batch_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<LogicalDeltaBatch>,fragment_digest}],sorted_apply_ack_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardAppliedAck>],complete_participant_commitment,resulting_global_frontier,batch_digest}`. The already-known transaction record points to no batch, so the object graph is acyclic. `GlobalDeltaPublishSpec {global_batch_ref:StrongRef<GlobalLogicalDeltaBatch>,expected_prior_global_frontier,expected_transaction_and_marker:WeakDigest,terminal_audit_gate}` is a `GlobalControlCommand`; apply verifies exact prepare-set equality and contiguous frontier, then atomically installs the batch/index/frontier through payload→control-record→root. Ripple and client commit acknowledgement wait for this publication, every touched shard durability/apply quorum, terminal audit visibility, and durable outcome; a crash before them yields capability-scoped `Unknown`, never partial delta visibility.

`ShardCheckpointInstallSpec` is `{basis_shard_state:WeakStateIdentity,basis_shard_raft_index,basis_global_prefix,basis_payload_digest:WeakDigest,basis_projection_digest,checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<ShardRecoveryCheckpoint>,checkpoint_state_vector_digest,paired_shard_config_payload_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardConfigPayloadFloor>?,retention_cut_body_ref:StrongRef<RetentionCutBody>?,reset_field_tags[]}`. Genesis requires no body/floor and produces `CheckpointInstalled`; operational replacement requires both, atomically installs the matching provisional cut, applies only registered reset/equivalence transitions, and preserves `Operational`. `ShardInitialFloorInstallSpec` is `{checkpoint_installed_shard_state:WeakStateIdentity,checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<ShardRecoveryCheckpoint>,checkpoint_state_vector_digest,initial_shard_config_payload_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardConfigPayloadFloor>,initial_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,expected_shard_raft_index}` and is the sole fresh `CheckpointInstalled -> Operational` transition. Local-to-W12 migration uses only the canonical `ShardProjectionInstallSpec` above with consumer-local certified transition/projection refs and the exact role-transition Genesis authorization; its barrier must byte-match the plan predicate and canonical strong-closure schema. It is invalid for an ordinary fresh shard. `ShardHistoryCutActivationSpec` is `{provisional_cut_ref:StrongRef<ProvisionalRetentionCutSet>,checkpoint_install_record_ref:StrongShardCommandRef,expected_retention_basis:WeakStateIdentity,verified_contiguous_suffix_start}` and only strengthens the exact provisional set.

`ShardConfigurationTransitionSpec` is `{phase:ProposeJoint|CommitJoint|CommitNew|CommitRetirementFloor,basis_shard_state:WeakStateIdentity,current_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,prospective_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,candidate_closure_proof_ref:StrongRef,expected_shard_raft_index,expected_global_prefix,paired_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<ShardRecoveryCheckpoint>?,paired_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardConfigPayloadFloor>,meta_authorization_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardReconfigurationAuthorizationRecord>,prepared_ownership_transfer_refs[StrongRef<ShardPreparedOwnershipTransferRecord>]}`; every field byte-matches the Meta authorization, and final apply enables adoption evidence but does not mutate Meta topology. `ShardTopologyCopyApplySpec` is `{copy_record_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<TopologyTransitionRecord>,transfer_plan_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<TopologyTransferPlan>,source_checkpoint_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardCheckpointCertificate>],received_inventory_digest,expected_destination_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,through_global_prefix}`. `ShardDerivedBuildSpec` and `ShardDerivedAdvanceSpec` bind the exact `DerivedIdentity`, input `GlobalLogicalDeltaBatch` CRSR interval, active Meta projection, topology/config, prior component, result component root, answer contract, and availability floor; apply roots the component before a certificate is exported. Key lifecycle uses only `ShardKeyMaterialStageSpec`, `ShardKeyMaterialActivateSpec`, `ShardKeyZeroReferenceSpec`, `ShardKeyDestroyApplySpec`, and `ShardKeyPhysicalDestructionCompletionSpec` with the exact plan/manifest/authorization, current topology/configuration, prior registry entry, full root-set basis, and envelope/wrap/opener or physical-receipt closure described above. These typed controls, not a generic payload import, are the only derived/key installation, activation, proof, or destruction paths.

The same generated registry drives classification, certification, import, and apply. Each `GlobalControlKind` has exactly one `MetaControlEffectRow`: `NoShardEffect{exhaustive_checker_id,proof_rule}` or `Targeted{destination_selector,ordered_slot_tags[MetaProjectionSlot],typed_payload_schema_id,per_slot_cas_rule}`. `TypedCertifiedMetaProjectionPayload` is the closed object `{source_global_control_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,source_global_command_kind,target_shard_id,effect_row_id,before_global_prefix,after_global_prefix,ordered_slot_deltas[{slot_tag,before_value_digest,after_value:InlineRegisteredValue|StrongRef,import_projection[RemoteObjectIdentity],retention_grant_identity,slot_specific_transition_commitment}],exhaustive_slot_bitmap,topology_and_configuration_selector,projection_checker_version}`. The bitmap must equal the row's generated slot set; a missing, duplicate, extra, reordered, or wrong-schema delta is invalid.

`MetaControlProjectionCertificate` is the Meta-quorum-signed `{SameGroupCertificateHeader,source_global_control_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,source_global_command_kind,target_shard_id,before_global_prefix,after_global_prefix,effect_row_id,typed_payload_ref:StrongRef<TypedCertifiedMetaProjectionPayload>,exhaustive_slot_bitmap,payload_closure_inventory_digest,one_digest_signer_lock_ref,quorum_signatures}`. It is valid only for one published relevant control and one target; it cannot summarize transaction effects or a range. `ShardMetaControlApplySpec` is `{projection_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<MetaControlProjectionCertificate>,typed_payload_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<TypedCertifiedMetaProjectionPayload>,expected_shard_state:WeakStateIdentity,expected_active_meta_projection_root_ref:StrongRef<ActiveMetaProjectionRoot>,expected_prior_global_prefix,ordered_slot_cas_expectations[{slot_tag,expected_before_value_digest}],expected_topology_epoch,expected_remote_trust_selectors[],expected_audit_visibility_prefix}`. Its body contains no authority value; the outer tag-specific `ShardControlAuthority<ApplyMetaControl>` must name the same projection CRSR and effect commitment. Apply verifies the exact next Global command, certificate/payload equality, generated destination and slot bitmap, imports only the typed payload's remote identities under their two-sided grants, CAS-updates those slots, and advances exactly one contiguous durable prefix. A `NoShardEffect` row is admissible only inside the contiguous `MetaRelevanceRangeProof` path and cannot be wrapped as an empty projection. Audit visibility may remain fixed behind a fence but never decrease; only the generated audit-mirror row advances it. G0 and negative tests delete, duplicate, swap, or substitute every slot/payload/destination and require rejection.

`ShardControlAuthority<Tag>` is the closed tag `MetaAuthorized{authorization_ref:MetaAuthorizationEvidence<Tag>,authorized_effect_commitment}|ProtocolEvidenceAuthorized{evidence_ref:ProtocolAuthorizationEvidence<Tag>,protocol_kind,effect_commitment}|StructurallyInapplicable{system_authority_class,no_global_semantic_effect_proof}`. The generated associated types `MetaAuthorizationEvidence<Tag>` and `ProtocolAuthorizationEvidence<Tag>` are each either one exact typed `StrongRef<T>` or `CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<T>` schema or `Uninhabited`; no erased reference union exists. Every body tag has exactly one allowed authority arm/evidence target, and the outer evidence must byte-match the body input. Ambient shard-maintainer privilege cannot change trust, retention, keys, GC, backup, restore, topology, or visibility. `ShardControlCommand` is the fence-free envelope `{command_version,kind,body,control_authority:ShardControlAuthority<kind>,expected_shard_raft_index,expected_state_conditions[],shard_pre_command_base_availability_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ShardPreCommandBaseAvailabilityCertificate>}` where the closed v1 body union is exactly `RecoveryBridge{spec_ref:StrongRef<RecoveryBridgeSpec>}|AdvanceIrrelevantRange{proof_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<MetaRelevanceRangeProof>}|ApplyMetaControl{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardMetaControlApplySpec>}|RemoteRetention{spec_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionControlSpec>}|AdvanceRemoteConfigurationEvidence{spec_ref:StrongRef<AdvanceRemoteConfigurationEvidenceSpec>}|ValidateRemoteConfigurationAnchor{spec_ref:StrongRef<ValidateRemoteConfigurationAnchorSpec>}|InstallCheckpoint{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardCheckpointInstallSpec>}|InstallInitialFloor{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardInitialFloorInstallSpec>}|InstallMigrationProjection{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardProjectionInstallSpec>}|ActivateHistoryCut{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardHistoryCutActivationSpec>}|ConfigurationTransition{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardConfigurationTransitionSpec>}|GcPreflight{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardGcPreflightSpec>}|GcApplyQuarantine{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardGcApplySpec>}|GcPhysicalCompletion{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardGcPhysicalCompletionSpec>}|DerivedBuild{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardDerivedBuildSpec>}|DerivedAdvance{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardDerivedAdvanceSpec>}|KeyMaterialStage{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardKeyMaterialStageSpec>}|KeyMaterialActivate{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardKeyMaterialActivateSpec>}|KeyZeroReference{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardKeyZeroReferenceSpec>}|KeyDestroyApply{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardKeyDestroyApplySpec>}|KeyPhysicalDestructionCompletion{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardKeyPhysicalDestructionCompletionSpec>}|TopologyCopyApply{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardTopologyCopyApplySpec>}|BackupPin{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardBackupPinSpec>}|BackupClosurePublish{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardBackupClosurePublishSpec>}|BackupRelease{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardBackupReleaseSpec>}|RestoreActivationApply{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardRestoreActivationApplySpec>}|RestoreVisibilityApply{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardRestoreVisibilityApplySpec>}|RestoreServicePrepare{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardRestoreServicePrepareSpec>}|RestoreServiceOpen{spec_ref:StrongRef<ShardRestoreServiceOpenSpec>}`. `RecoveryBridge` accepts only `StructurallyInapplicable{RecoverySystemAuthority}` under `PendingRestoreCreationGuard`; restore/key/GC/backup tags use their exact Meta or protocol evidence. There is no generic payload or generic authority arm.

The D1 certificate, owner, authority, body, current domain/configuration, and expected conditions must match before proposal. The command cannot change global semantic values. `AdvanceIrrelevantRange` is legal only for an exhaustive `MetaRelevanceRangeProof`; topology, policy, revocation, key, audit-fence, admission/decision, remote-retention, derived activation, backup/restore, GC, or target-data effects require their typed path and can never be skipped. `audit_visible_global_prefix` never decreases: a fence may hold it unchanged while durable apply advances, and only the exact generated mirror projection advances it. Never-registered and closed-attempt compaction powers remain Meta-only; neither a floor nor timeout may terminalize a prepared attempt.

Topology evidence is typed. `TopologyTransferPlan` is `{old_topology_ref,new_joint_topology_ref,new_final_topology_ref,affected_ranges,copy_basis_global_prefix,sorted_source_checkpoint_identities,object_and_suffix_inventory,destination_assignments,copy_crypto_profile,completion_predicate}`. A destination shard produces `TopologyTransferAck {SameGroupCertificateHeader,plan_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<TopologyTransferPlan>,destination_shard,received_inventory_digest,applied_through_global_prefix,destination_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<ShardCheckpointCertificate>,signatures}`. Meta builds `TopologyAttemptClosureProof {SameGroupCertificateHeader,old_topology_epoch,cutover_global_prefix,registration_generation_range,sorted_attempt_evidence[(global_txn_id,registration_generation) -> Terminal{outcome_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnOutcomeRecord>,published_decision_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>?,old_owner_ack_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardAppliedAck>]}|AbortForPostCutoverRetry{abort_outcome_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnOutcomeRecord>,published_abort_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,old_owner_release_ack_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardAppliedAck>],retry_request_nonce,intent_commitment,old_to_future_attempt_mapping_commitment}],exact_old_epoch_active_and_admitted_set_commitment,conflict_index_basis,signatures}`. The sorted evidence is exhaustive against old-epoch attempt indexes. No new-epoch registration can preexist cutover: only a later meta command after ownership switches may create a new generation and link it to the recorded retry intent. A registration racing the cutover basis is either included/terminalized under the old epoch or rejected for later retry. `TopologyRetirementFloor` is `{cutover_record_ref:StrongRef<TopologyTransitionRecord>,through_global_prefix,old_owner_inventory,remaining_certified_remote_obligations,backup_floor,key_floor,retention_floor,prepare_floor,external_backup_and_key_receipt_refs[StrongRef],required_meta_ack_set,required_shard_ack_set}`. `TopologyRetirementAck` carries `SameGroupCertificateHeader` and `{floor_ref:LocalMeta{StrongRef<TopologyRetirementFloor>}|RemoteMeta{CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<TopologyRetirementFloor>},satisfied_floor_digest,signature}`; only meta encodes `LocalMeta`, and every shard encodes `RemoteMeta`.

Movement has three distinct pre-order global-control specs so apply never consumes ambient evidence. `TopologyCopyBeginSpec` is `{move_id,old_topology_ref,new_joint_topology_ref,new_final_topology_ref,affected_ranges,copy_basis_global_prefix,old/new_shard_configuration_refs[RemoteConfigurationRef],source_checkpoint_certificate_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardCheckpointCertificate>],transfer_plan_ref:StrongRef<TopologyTransferPlan>,expected_branch/key/allocation_epochs,terminal_audit_gate}`. `TopologyCutoverSpec` is `{move_id,copy_record_ref:StrongRef<TopologyTransitionRecord>,cutover_global_prefix,sorted_transfer_ack_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<TopologyTransferAck>],new_owner_catchup_certificate_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardCheckpointCertificate>],active_attempt_closure_proof_ref:StrongRef<TopologyAttemptClosureProof>,old/new_shard_configuration_refs[RemoteConfigurationRef],expected_branch/key/allocation_epochs,terminal_audit_gate}` and proves every old-epoch registration has exhaustive Terminal or `AbortForPostCutoverRetry` evidence before ownership switches at the next prefix. `TopologyRetireOldSpec` is `{move_id,cutover_record_ref:StrongRef<TopologyTransitionRecord>,topology_retirement_floor_ref:StrongRef<TopologyRetirementFloor>,sorted_meta_ack_refs[StrongRef<TopologyRetirementAck>],sorted_shard_ack_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<TopologyRetirementAck>],terminal_audit_gate}`. Each apply constructs one `TopologyTransitionRecord {move_id,phase:CopyInProgress|CutoverCommitted|OldOwnersRetired,command_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlCommand>,phase_predecessor:NoneForCopy|Copy{ref:StrongRef<TopologyTransitionRecord>}|Cutover{ref:StrongRef<TopologyTransitionRecord>},copy_basis_global_prefix,cutover_global_prefix?,affected_ranges,evidence_commitment,resulting_topology_ref,assigned_global_logical_command_seq}`. The predecessor is the immediately prior same-move phase; completed moves do not form an unbounded strong chain. Source bytes/keys remain live through final retirement and its two-sided remote floors.

**AdjRunSegment**: `{ graph, branch_projection, source_partition, direction, edge_type, source_ordinal_map_id, destination_map_table[{partition,ordinal_map_id}], source_ordinal_range, edge_count, seq_range, codec_table, offsets_ef, encoded_neighbor_lists, stable_eids, origin_birth_orders, branch_admission_orders?, marker_aware_retire_or_hole_data, property_locators, canonical_stable_id_digest, checksum }`. Each destination carries either stable VId or a destination-map-table slot plus ordinal. Mutable labels do not identify a primary run; per-list codec governs legal rank/select/skip operations.

**IdentityContinuityRecord / IdAllocatorState / IdRangeLease**: `IdentityContinuityRecord` binds `{database_security_namespace_id,allocation_epoch,predecessor_digest,external_registry_id,cas_version,status,issued_at,signer_set_epoch,threshold_signatures}`; its external registry/witness copy is the anti-rollback authority and its Chronicle copy is checked against it. Allocator state binds `{graph_id,element_kind,allocation_epoch,identity_continuity_record_ref,topology_epoch,per_partition_high_water,spent_range_commitments,exhausted_partitions}`. Pre-order `IdRangeGrantSpec` binds the requested range, allocator basis, authority, and issuance profile/window. Its applied lease is `{lease_id,graph,element_kind,allocation_epoch,partition,half_open_range,authority_digest,applied_control_ref:AppliedControlRef,time_authority_profile_oid,issuance_not_before,issuance_not_after,permanent_spent_commitment}`; its authenticated transcript covers the complete profiled window. The applied tag must match the owning local/meta state machine and assigned sequence. Use consumes fresh `TimeValidationEvidence::Usable`; expiry ends issuance authority only through matching `Expired` evidence and every epoch/range pair remains permanently spent and can never overlap or recycle.

An identity becomes externally stable at its **first escape**, not at transaction commit. `AllocationValueKind` is the closed union `VertexId{graph,partition}|EdgeId{graph,partition}|GeneratedKey{graph,generator_id,key_type}`. `TxnAllocationSlotKey` is `{posture:Local|Sharded,attempt_identity,statement_seq_or_terminal,tmp_ref_ordinal,value_kind}` and is never a client value. `EscapingAllocationCause` is `PublishedStatementResult|LaterStatementWorkspace|ProcedureOrUdfBoundary|DurableProvenanceOrAudit|TerminalResultPreparation`; the `TerminalResultPreparation` arm is optional because a terminal-only value may instead be assigned in finalization before publication. `EscapingAllocationBinding` is `{slot_key,permanent_value,lease_ref:Local{lease_ref:StrongRef<IdRangeLease>}|Shard{lease_ref:StrongRef<ShardIdRangeLease>},lease_offset,escape_cause,first_escaping_statement_seq,canonical_binding_digest}`. The permanent value must equal the role/kind/epoch/partition/offset encoded by its lease; generated-key encoders additionally obey the registered generator profile. A binding is immutable, namespace-scoped, and cannot be repurposed for a different temporary reference, attempt, kind, or create.

Local orders `LocalEscapingAllocationReservationSpec {registration_ref:StrongRef<LocalAttemptRegistration>,expected_workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<LocalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>,expected_allocator_root:WeakStateIdentity,sorted_binding_recipes[],sorted_lease_refs[StrongRef<IdRangeLease>],fresh_lease_use_evidence_refs[StrongRef<TimeValidationEvidence>],expected_unconsumed_offsets_and_spent_commitment,resulting_allocation_binding_root_ref:StrongRef<TxnAllocationBindingRoot>,resulting_workspace_generation_recipe,terminal_audit_gate}` before the first escaping manifest/workspace/procedure object is constructed. Apply checks a canonical bijection between recipes and fresh offsets, marks every offset consumed in `IdAllocatorState`, installs `EscapingAllocationReservationRecord {source_spec_ref,applied_control_ref,registration_ref,sorted_bindings,resulting_binding_root_ref,permanent_spent_commitment}`, and advances the workspace generation atomically. The statement publication or later terminal preparation names that record and can encode only its permanent values. A lost response retries the same record and result bytes.

In Sharded posture, the shard owning each disjoint range first orders `ShardEscapingAllocationReserveSpec {registration_projection_ref,workspace_generation,lease_ref:StrongRef<ShardIdRangeLease>,sorted_binding_recipes_for_this_shard,fresh_lease_use_evidence_ref,expected_shard_allocator_root,resulting_shard_binding_root_ref}` and installs both the consumed-offset state and `ShardEscapingAllocationReservationRecord` in one shard command. Its quorum exports `ShardEscapingAllocationEvidence {SameGroupCertificateHeader,reservation_record_ref:StrongRef<ShardEscapingAllocationReservationRecord>,workspace_generation,sorted_bindings,permanent_spent_commitment,one_digest_signer_lock_ref,quorum_signatures}`. Meta then orders `GlobalEscapingAllocationReservationSpec {registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,expected_workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>,sorted_shard_evidence_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardEscapingAllocationEvidence>],complete_tmp_ref_to_permanent_value_bijection,resulting_global_binding_root_ref:StrongRef<TxnAllocationBindingRoot>,successor_workspace_generation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnWorkspaceGeneration>,terminal_audit_gate}`. Apply rejects a missing, duplicate, overlapping, foreign-range, wrong-workspace, or nonparticipant binding and makes the global workspace's mapping authoritative. Shard holds remain independently rooted until Meta publication and the ordinary two-sided retention release; a Meta failure cannot make a certified slot reusable.

`TxnAllocationBindingRoot` maps every escaped `TxnAllocationSlotKey` to exactly one binding and carries `{generation,attempt_identity,through_statement_seq,sorted_spent_commitments,root_digest}`. Rebase and finalization must preserve all existing leaves and may append only new escapes; if the logical create disappears, conflicts with a constraint, or changes kind/partition, the attempt aborts or records `AbandonedAllocationTombstone {binding_digest,attempt_terminal_identity,reason_class,permanent_spent_commitment}`. Abort, no-op, statement failure after reservation, lease expiry, compaction, branch fork/merge, topology movement, backup/restore, and same-identity recovery retain the spend through the allocator's cumulative spent commitment even after detailed binding evidence is cut. `AllocationBindingCompactionSpec` may replace closed-attempt detail only with a checked cumulative spent-range extension and exact tombstone commitment; it never returns capacity. Tests force crash/lost response before and after every Local, shard, and Meta publication; expose an ID to a later statement and force rebase; abort after exposure; retry under a new process; expire a lease; restore an old backup; move a partition; and prove that the visible value is stable and no offset is ever issued twice.
