A role-invalid, untyped, duplicate, missing, or ambient strong edge is unencodable. `BackupInventoryBijectionProof` is `{backup_id,scope:Local|Meta|Shard{shard_id},source_pin_identity:WeakDigest,source_inventory_digest,archive_inventory_root_digest,canonical_sorted_source_to_archive_key_commitment,no_missing_source,no_extra_archive,no_duplicate_target,per_entry_length_and_digest_commitment,checker_version}`. `BackupRecoverabilityProof` is `{backup_id,scope,archive_inventory_root_digest,protection_profile_oid,required_failure_domain_predicate,observed_failure_domain_inventory,deterministic_decode_campaign_commitment,key_escrow_recovery_commitment,all_required_profiles_satisfied,checker_version}`.

Reopen proof is deliberately two-stage. `BackupContentReopenProof`, created before sealing by an independent fresh reader, is `{backup_id,scope,source_pin_identity:WeakDigest,archive_authority_id,archive_inventory_root_digest,authenticated_archive_access_receipt,precommitted_challenge_digest,opened_entry_commitment,decoded_root_and_sample_commitment,recomputed_semantic_digest,reader_software_and_profile_oid,observed_at,signer_epoch,signature}`; it names no future manifest, signature set, publication receipt, transparency inclusion, or retention grant. Copy verification owns the inventory, recoverability, and content-reopen proofs, and closure certificates/manifest body commit their digests.

`BackupArtifactReopenProof` is necessarily post-publication and is `{backup_id,scope,manifest_ref:BackupArchiveRef<BackupManifest>,manifest_body_digest,manifest_signature_set_digest,publication_receipt_ref:StrongRef<BackupPublicationReceipt>,transparency_state:NotRequired{policy_digest}|Included{inclusion_ref:StrongRef<BackupTransparencyInclusion>,checkpoint_digest},archive_retention_grant_ref:StrongRef<ArchiveRetentionGrant>,grant_authority_observation_ref:StrongRef<ArchiveGrantAuthorityObservation>,grant_time_validation_evidence_ref:StrongRef<TimeValidationEvidence>,required_observation_action:ArtifactReopen,archive_inventory_root_digest,authenticated_fresh_archive_access_receipt,precommitted_artifact_challenge_digest,opened_manifest_signature_receipt_grant_head_and_inventory_commitment,verified_key_escrow_and_decoder_profile_commitment,decoded_root_and_required_sample_commitment,recomputed_semantic_digest,reader_software_and_profile_oid,observed_at,time_authority_profile_oid,signer_epoch,signature}`. A different independent fresh reader opens the actually published portable artifact, verifies exact manifest bytes/signatures, publication receipt, required transparency, inventory, key recovery material, and root/sample semantics while consuming an action-bound current-grant use guard. The object cannot be committed by the manifest it validates. Only this artifact proof—not the earlier content proof—may establish content/publication equivalence; pin release additionally requires a new current observation under an Activated source-release hold at the release command. Required transparency remains an explicit nonterminal state until inclusion; optional/not-required policy is signed in the manifest and cannot be inferred from absence. Lost-response retry returns the same proof identity, while any manifest, signature, receipt, grant/head generation, policy, inventory, key, or semantic drift fails closed.

Local backup starts with `LocalBackupBarrierSpec {backup_id,authorized_request_digest,expected_source_root_manifest_ref:StrongRef<RootManifest>,expected_logical_state_root_ref:StrongRef<LogicalStateRoot>,expected_logical_command_seq,expected_commit_seq,expected_raft_index,expected_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<RecoveryCheckpoint>,expected_checkpoint_vector_digest,expected_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,expected_config_payload_floor_ref:StrongRef<ConfigPayloadFloor>,expected_prepared_root_generation,expected_certificate_ledger_digest,expected_retained_history_interval,archive_profile_ref:StrongRef<ArchiveProfile>,recipient_and_key_recovery_profile_ref:StrongRef<KeyRecoveryProfile>,format_matrix_ref:StrongRef<FormatMatrix>,terminal_audit_gate}`. Apply requires `Operational` and exact equality, then creates `LocalBackupPinRecord {backup_id,source_domain:ConsensusDomain,barrier_logical_command_seq,barrier_commit_seq,barrier_raft_index,source_root_manifest_ref:StrongRef<RootManifest>,source_logical_state_root_ref:StrongRef<LogicalStateRoot>,pinned_closure_refs[BackupPinnedClosureRef<Local>],pinned_closure_coverage_bitmap,complete_logical_and_physical_inventory_root_ref:StrongRef<BackupSourceInventory>,pin_generation}`. The generated Local union includes the exact checkpoint/vector, current/joint/prospective configuration and floor, prepared/certificate/Raft, retained stream/history, key/envelope/grant/wrap, identity/privacy/audit/continuity, replay/cursor/delivery/derived, and remote-trust/retention classes previously grouped informally. This ordered record, not the manifest, is the source retention lease.

After copy and an independent content reopen, `LocalBackupCopyVerification {backup_id,pin_identity:WeakDigest,sorted_source_to_archive_entries[{source:BackupSourceIdentity,archive:BackupArchiveRef}],complete_inventory_bijection_proof_ref:StrongRef<BackupInventoryBijectionProof>,per_object_decode_and_digest_results,recoverability_and_failure_domain_proof_ref:StrongRef<BackupRecoverabilityProof>,content_reopen_proof_ref:StrongRef<BackupContentReopenProof>,canonical_semantic_digest}` and `LocalBackupClosureCertificate {SameGroupCertificateHeader,backup_id,barrier_coordinates,source_state:BackupSourceIdentity<LogicalStateRoot>,copy_verification_ref:StrongRef<LocalBackupCopyVerification>,archived_state_ref:BackupArchiveRef<LogicalStateRoot>,complete_archive_inventory_digest,inventory_bijection_proof_digest,recoverability_proof_digest,content_reopen_proof_digest,semantic_digest,certificate_attempt_ref:StrongRef<CertificateAttemptRecord>,canonical_signature_set}` contain no retaining source edge.

The Local registry is exactly `Absent -> Pinned{pin_ref} -> ClosureCertified{certificate_ref} -> Sealed{manifest_ref} -> (PublicationReceiptedPendingTransparency{receipt_ref,required_policy_digest} ->)? Published{receipt_ref,transparency:NotRequired|Included,grant_ref,mirrored_grant_head} -> ArtifactVerified{artifact_proof_ref,verification_observation_ref} -> ReleasedPendingArchiveHoldCompletion{source_release_evidence_ref,activated_hold_ref} -> Released{manifest_identity,archive_grant_identity,artifact_proof_identity,completed_hold_identity,completion_receipt_identity}`. `LocalBackupClosurePublishSpec` and `LocalBackupSealSpec` retain their exact pin/copy/certificate/manifest fields above. If the manifest requires transparency, `LocalBackupTransparencyPendingSpec {manifest_ref,publication_receipt_ref,required_policy_digest,expected_registry_state:Sealed,terminal_audit_gate}` durably records the receipt but no grant and enters the pending state. It is not Published, reopenable, servable, or pin-releasable. NotRequired manifests cannot use this transition.

`LocalBackupPublishCompletionSpec` is `{manifest_ref:StrongRef<BackupManifest>,publication_receipt_ref:StrongRef<BackupPublicationReceipt>,transparency:NotRequired{policy_digest}|Included{inclusion_ref:StrongRef<BackupTransparencyInclusion>,checkpoint_digest},archive_retention_grant_ref:StrongRef<ArchiveRetentionGrant>,current_grant_head_mirror_ref:StrongRef<ArchiveGrantAuthorityMirror>,expected_registry_state:Sealed|PublicationReceiptedPendingTransparency,terminal_audit_gate}`. Sealed is legal only for NotRequired; pending is legal only for Included. The grant subject must byte-match the selected arm and therefore cannot predate required inclusion. `LocalBackupArtifactVerifySpec` consumes the exact current-use guard and installs ArtifactVerified. `LocalBackupReleaseSpec` names the pin, manifest, receipt, grant, artifact proof, Activated hold, fresh release observation/time evidence, and expected ArtifactVerified state; it is the sole pin-removing transition and installs `ReleasedPendingArchiveHoldCompletion`, not final Released. `ArchiveSourceReleaseCompletionMirrorSpec` alone installs final Released after the archive authority's completion CAS.

Closure publication is the only Pinned-to-Certified path; seal cannot skip it, required transparency cannot skip inclusion, and release byte-matches the artifact proof, latest grant head, and Activated hold. Final Released has no path to the pin/source closure. `LocalBackupAbortSpec` is the only failure transition: before external publication it requires a complete no-advertised-artifact proof plus ordered cleanup acknowledgements; after a receipt exists it must preserve every advertised envelope and proceed through transparency when required, grant, artifact verification, hold-backed source release, and hold completion. Disconnect, timeout, grant renewal, or a stale Active generation never drops a pin.

Sharded backup begins with `GlobalBackupIntentSpec {backup_id,barrier_global_prefix:P,expected_global_state_root_ref:StrongRef<GlobalStateRoot>,expected_meta_pinned_closure_refs[BackupPinnedClosureRef<Meta>],expected_meta_pinned_closure_coverage_bitmap,expected_topology_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,exact_sorted_required_shard_domains[ConsensusDomain],exact_partition_and_authority_commitment,expected_global_history_interval,meta_live_closure_inventory_ref:StrongRef<BackupSourceInventory>,archive_profile_ref:StrongRef<ArchiveProfile>,recipient_and_key_recovery_profile_ref:StrongRef<KeyRecoveryProfile>,format_matrix_ref:StrongRef<FormatMatrix>,terminal_audit_gate}`. The generated Meta closure union includes the exact global checkpoint/vector, current/joint/prospective configurations and floor, and every other live mandatory class; no open `StrongRef[]` profile or floor bag exists. Apply creates `GlobalBackupIntentRecord` strongly pinning the exact Meta closure and fixing `P`, topology/configurations/shards/policy; its later `GlobalBackupIntentCertificate` is quorum-signed under the universal signer lock.

Each required shard orders `ShardBackupPinSpec {intent_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalBackupIntentCertificate>,expected_shard_state_ref:StrongRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,barrier_state:ExactCurrentPrefix{global_applied_prefix=P}|ExactHistoricalCut{current_global_applied_prefix,historical_state_ref:StrongRef<ShardHistoricalStateAtPrefix>,checkpoint_and_history_proof_ref:StrongRef<ExactHistoricalPrefixProof>},expected_shard_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,expected_topology_epoch,expected_pinned_closure_refs[BackupPinnedClosureRef<Shard>],expected_pinned_closure_coverage_bitmap,remote_retention_grant_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantEvidence>}`. There is no `LatestAtLeastP` tag. An irrelevance proof is accepted only inside a contiguous authenticated Global-command coverage proof that reconstructs exact state at `P`. Apply creates `ShardBackupPinRecord` strongly owning the generated-complete state/checkpoint/vector/config/floor/history/prepared/certificate/active-projection/key/derived/trust/retention closure at `P` and records `pin_generation`. `ShardBackupCopyVerification` is `{backup_id,pin_identity:WeakDigest,pin_generation,barrier_global_prefix:P,topology_and_configuration_identities,sorted_source_to_archive_entries,complete_inventory_bijection_proof_ref:StrongRef<BackupInventoryBijectionProof>,per_object_decode_results,recoverability_and_failure_domain_proof_ref:StrongRef<BackupRecoverabilityProof>,content_reopen_proof_ref:StrongRef<BackupContentReopenProof>,canonical_shard_semantic_digest}`. `ShardBackupClosureCertificate` is `{SameGroupCertificateHeader,backup_id,barrier_global_prefix:P,shard_id,source_domain,topology_and_configuration_identities,exact_partition_coverage,source_state:BackupSourceIdentity<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,archived_state_ref:BackupArchiveRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,copy_verification_ref:StrongRef<ShardBackupCopyVerification>,pinned_closure_digest,active_meta_projection_digest,key_derived_remote_obligation_digests,complete_archive_inventory_digest,inventory_bijection_proof_digest,recoverability_proof_digest,canonical_shard_semantic_digest,content_reopen_proof_digest,certificate_attempt_ref:StrongRef<CertificateAttemptRecord>,canonical_signature_set}` and contains no retaining source-pin edge. `ShardBackupClosurePublishSpec {pin_record_ref:StrongRef<ShardBackupPinRecord>,copy_verification_ref:StrongRef<ShardBackupCopyVerification>,closure_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ShardBackupClosureCertificate>,expected_registry_state:Pinned,expected_pin_generation,expected_barrier_topology_and_configuration,expected_current_root:WeakStateIdentity}` is the only `Pinned -> Certified` transition and byte-matches every field. Shard pins remain until Meta presents the post-publication artifact proof inside the release authorization; content proof alone never releases them.

`GlobalBackupSealSpec {intent_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalBackupIntentRecord>,exact_sorted_shard_closure_certificate_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardBackupClosureCertificate>],meta_copy_verification_ref:StrongRef<MetaBackupCopyVerification>,backup_manifest_ref:StrongRef<BackupManifest>,expected_topology_and_configurations,exact_complete_group_and_partition_commitment,terminal_audit_gate}` accepts one certificate from every and only required shard, all at exact `P`; `MetaBackupCopyVerification` has the same typed bijection/recoverability/content-reopen fields and Meta scope as its Local/Shard counterparts.

If the manifest requires transparency, `GlobalBackupTransparencyPendingSpec {intent_record_ref,backup_manifest_ref,publication_receipt_ref,required_policy_digest,expected_registry_state:Sealed,terminal_audit_gate}` enters `PublicationReceiptedPendingTransparency` without a grant. It is not Published and cannot authorize reopen or release. `GlobalBackupPublishCompletionSpec` is `{intent_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalBackupIntentRecord>,backup_manifest_ref:StrongRef<BackupManifest>,publication_receipt_ref:StrongRef<BackupPublicationReceipt>,transparency:NotRequired{policy_digest}|Included{inclusion_ref:StrongRef<BackupTransparencyInclusion>,checkpoint_digest},archive_retention_grant_ref:StrongRef<ArchiveRetentionGrant>,current_grant_head_mirror_ref:StrongRef<ArchiveGrantAuthorityMirror>,expected_registry_state:Sealed|PublicationReceiptedPendingTransparency,expected_manifest_body_and_signature_digests,terminal_audit_gate}`. Sealed accepts only NotRequired and pending accepts only Included; the grant subject must byte-match that arm. It alone installs Published and never releases a source pin.

`GlobalBackupArtifactVerifySpec` consumes a current-use guard, verifies the exact post-publication artifact, and installs ArtifactVerified. `GlobalBackupReleaseAuthorizeSpec` names the intent, manifest, receipt, grant, artifact proof, Activated source-release hold, fresh action-bound observation/time evidence, exact shard set, expected ArtifactVerified state, and complete release commitment; apply installs Releasing and yields the portable `GlobalBackupReleaseAuthorizationCertificate`. Every shard verifies that projection plus a new current hold observation. `GlobalBackupAbortSpec` and `ShardBackupAbortSpec` are exact cleanup transitions only before any publication receipt; after a receipt exists they preserve the envelope and ordinary required-inclusion, grant, artifact-verification, hold-backed source release, and hold-completion protocol is mandatory.

`ShardBackupReleaseSpec` is the closed inner union `Authorize{authorization_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalBackupReleaseAuthorizationCertificate>,own_pin_ref:StrongRef<ShardBackupPinRecord>,own_closure_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ShardBackupClosureCertificate>,manifest_ref:BackupArchiveRef<BackupManifest>,publication_receipt_ref:StrongRef<BackupPublicationReceipt>,archive_retention_grant_ref:StrongRef<ArchiveRetentionGrant>,activated_source_release_hold_ref:StrongRef<ArchiveSourceReleaseHold>,fresh_grant_authority_observation_ref:StrongRef<ArchiveGrantAuthorityObservation>,time_validation_evidence_ref:StrongRef<TimeValidationEvidence>,required_observation_action:ShardSourcePinRelease{own_shard_id},expected_registry_state:Certified,expected_barrier_topology_configuration_and_pin_generation}|Finalize{authorization_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalBackupReleaseAuthorizationCertificate>,own_pin_ref:StrongRef<ShardBackupPinRecord>,own_closure_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ShardBackupClosureCertificate>,expected_registry_state:ReleaseAuthorized,current_root_no_other_pin_proof_ref:StrongRef<BackupPinAbsenceProof>,post_release_registry_body_recipe}`. `BackupPinAbsenceProof` binds the exact current role root, backup registry generation, backup ID/pin generation, complete scan commitment, and checker version; it cannot be a generic reachability assertion. `Authorize` verifies the current activated hold but keeps the pin and enters ReleaseAuthorized; `Finalize` alone removes it, installs shard Released, and creates the exact signed `ShardBackupReleaseAck` with authorization/hold/observation, post-release root/no-pin proof, applied index, and certificate-attempt closure.

`GlobalBackupReleaseFinalizeSpec` is `{authorization_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,authorization_certificate_ref:StrongRef<GlobalBackupReleaseAuthorizationCertificate>,exact_sorted_shard_release_ack_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardBackupReleaseAck>],activated_source_release_hold_ref:StrongRef<ArchiveSourceReleaseHold>,fresh_grant_authority_observation_ref:StrongRef<ArchiveGrantAuthorityObservation>,time_validation_evidence_ref:StrongRef<TimeValidationEvidence>,required_observation_action:GlobalSourceReleaseFinalize,expected_registry_state:Releasing,exact_required_shard_commitment,meta_post_release_body_recipe,terminal_audit_gate}`. It drops the Meta pin and enters `ReleasedPendingArchiveHoldCompletion` only after every and only configured shard ack under the still-current Activated hold, and constructs the portable sharded `ArchiveSourceReleaseEvidence`. `ArchiveSourceReleaseCompletionMirrorSpec` alone enters final Released. Meta states are `Absent|Collecting|Sealed|PublicationReceiptedPendingTransparency|Published|ArtifactVerified|Releasing|ReleasedPendingArchiveHoldCompletion|Released`; shard states are `Absent|Pinned|Certified|ReleaseAuthorized|Released`. Reconfiguration, GC, key destruction, topology retirement, checkpoints, and floors retain every nonterminal state and every grant-head/hold/completion observation needed for recovery. Renewal/revocation/expiry is raced before reopen, verification, authorization, every shard authorize/finalize, Meta finalize, archive completion CAS, and completion mirror; stale generations always fail closed.

`BackupState` in the sealed manifest is the closed nonretaining posture tag `Local{barrier_coordinates,source_state:BackupSourceIdentity<LogicalStateRoot>,archived_state_ref:BackupArchiveRef<LogicalStateRoot>,checkpoint_configuration_history_inventory_digests,local_closure_certificate_identity}|Sharded{barrier_global_prefix,source_global_state:BackupSourceIdentity<GlobalStateRoot>,archived_global_state_ref:BackupArchiveRef<GlobalStateRoot>,topology_and_configuration_digests,sorted_shards[{shard_id,source_state:BackupSourceIdentity<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,archived_state_ref:BackupArchiveRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,closure_certificate_identity,partition_commitment}],complete_group_and_partition_commitment}`. Legacy Local manifests remain Local after activation and are never reinterpreted as Sharded. Unknown/mixed posture, group, inventory, trust, barrier, or configuration fields fail closed.

Same-identity write authority comes from one external linearizable chain. `ClusterIncarnationContinuityRecord` is `{continuity_domain_id,database_id,database_security_namespace_id,predecessor_digest,cas_version,retired_incarnation_floor,active_or_reserved_incarnation,state:Operational{posture:Local|Sharded,writer_authority_digest,service_visibility_epoch,lease_policy:DirectOrdinary|PromotionReceiptRequired{promotion_manifest_digest,expected_catalog_predecessor_version}}|RestoreFencePending{restore_id,source_backup_manifest_digest,deny_old_lease_renewal_after,last_possible_old_lease_expiry}|RestoreReserved{restore_id,source_backup_manifest_digest,source_backup_incarnation,retired_through_incarnation,target_incarnation,recovery_writer_authority_digest,service_visibility_epoch,lease_policy:RecoveryOnly}|CloneReserved{restore_id,source_database_and_security_identity,source_backup_manifest_digest,target_incarnation,recovery_writer_authority_digest,service_visibility_epoch,lease_policy:RecoveryOnly,new_identity_allocation_receipt_digest}|RoleTransitionReserved{migration_nonce,transition_certificate_digest,source_posture:Local,target_posture:Sharded,source_service_visibility_epoch,target_service_visibility_epoch,service_epoch_reservation_id,source_local_group_and_terminal_seal_commitment,target_group_topology_and_endpoint_commitment,transition_writer_authority_digest,lease_policy:RoleTransitionOnly}|RestoreAbandoned{restore_id,target_incarnation,service_visibility_epoch,abandonment_manifest_digest,target_tombstone_body_recipe_digest,retired_through_incarnation,no_operational_successor_at_this_incarnation:true},issued_at,signer_set_epoch,threshold_signatures}`. Every state tag and field is inside the threshold-signed transcript; the predecessor digest and CAS version form one direct-successor chain.

Same-identity recovery CASes `Operational{posture}(I_current) -> RestoreFencePending`, denies renewals and proves every old lease expired/revoked, then CASes `RestoreReserved(J)` with `J > max(I_current,I_backup,retired_incarnation_floor)`. Clone recovery CAS-creates exactly one previously absent target database/security namespace into `CloneReserved(J)` under a nonreusable identity-allocation receipt; it never traverses the source continuity chain as target authority. Successful restore promotion changes exactly `RestoreReserved|CloneReserved -> Operational{posture=target,lease_policy=PromotionReceiptRequired{promotion_manifest_digest,expected_catalog_predecessor_version}}` at the reserved incarnation/epoch. That continuity state alone cannot issue an ordinary lease or serve: every such action must validate the completed continuity-plus-catalog promotion receipt and canonical role finalize/open state. DirectOrdinary is reserved for fresh/direct service activation whose catalog and continuity publication are one externally atomic authority operation. Abandonment changes exactly the matching reservation to `RestoreAbandoned`, advances the retired floor through the abandoned incarnation, and permanently forbids an Operational successor at that incarnation. A later same-identity recovery may move `RestoreAbandoned{retired through J} -> RestoreReserved{target K}` only for a new restore ID with `K > J`, a fresh recovery authority, and an exact `LeasesRevokedOrExpiredThrough` proof that the abandoned recovery authority can neither issue nor renew; no state at J is resurrected. Role transition changes exactly `Operational{posture=Local,epoch=E} -> RoleTransitionReserved{target_epoch=E'}` and then, after the receipt-first destination service protocol, to `Operational{posture=Sharded,epoch=E',lease_policy=PromotionReceiptRequired{promotion_manifest_digest,expected_catalog_predecessor_version}}`; no other source or target posture is registered in v1. Checked overflow fails. Only one direct successor can win for a target identity, no recovery/transition write precedes its exact reservation, and continuity, lease/time guards, service-catalog validation, promotion/activation receipts, and open/session admission all byte-match the active state/posture/incarnation/service epoch.

**Rollback-protected authority time.** Canonical logical HLC orders database state; it is never an expiry clock. Process-local monotonic time may enforce a short-lived in-memory use budget and drive advisory timers; ambient wall time is display-only. Any authorization, lease-validity, expiry, release, retirement, key destruction, archive downgrade, restore fencing, or retention-cut decision uses the following rollback-protected authority-time contract or fails closed.

`AuthorityInstant` is `{time_domain_id,authority_epoch,tick:u128}` and compares only within one domain/epoch; windows are closed-open: `not_before <= true_authority_time < expires_at`. `TimeAuthorityProfile` is the immutable threshold-signed `{schema_version,time_domain_id,authority_epoch,tick_scale,external_registry_id,ordered_signers[{signer_id,key_id,verification_key}],threshold,maximum_source_uncertainty_ticks,maximum_challenge_round_trip_ticks,maximum_guard_use_ticks,comparison_semantics:ClosedOpen,unavailable_policy:FailClosed,predecessor_profile_digest:WeakDigest?,signer_set_epoch,signatures}`. `TimeAuthorityObservation` is the fresh challenged `{profile_ref:StrongRef<TimeAuthorityProfile>,challenge_nonce,subject_digest,intended_use_digest,authority_sequence,possible_time_interval:{earliest:AuthorityInstant,latest:AuthorityInstant},external_registry_head_digest,external_registry_cas_version,signer_set_epoch,threshold_signatures}`. Challenge nonce, subject, and use are signed. Replay, wrong profile/domain/epoch, noncurrent registry head, excessive round trip/uncertainty, or signature failure is unusable.

`TimeBoundSubject` is the exhaustive `wire_types.toml` union with separate arms for durable capability bytes, mutation/read permits, authorization leases, Local/Global result-delivery leases, resume cursors, cluster-incarnation leases, restore-source leases, database-identity reservations, replay/archive records, backup/archive grants, verifier-key retirement, and every other registered time-bearing object; it has no raw `StrongRef` or generic-object arm. `TimeValidationEvidence` is the already-built immutable `{profile_ref:StrongRef<TimeAuthorityProfile>,observation_ref:StrongRef<TimeAuthorityObservation>,subject:TimeBoundSubject,intended_use_digest,classification:Usable{not_before,expires_at}|NotYetValid{not_before}|Expired{expires_at},validator_version,validation_digest}`. `Usable` exists only when `observation.earliest >= not_before` and `checked_add(observation.latest.tick,maximum_guard_use_ticks)` succeeds in the same domain/epoch and the resulting instant is `< expires_at`; `NotYetValid` only when `observation.latest < not_before`; `Expired` only when `observation.earliest >= expires_at`. An interval overlapping either boundary yields no evidence and the uniform retryable `TimeAuthorityUnavailable`, before any protected lookup or disclosure. Tick addition, bound normalization, and profile drain arithmetic are checked; overflow, saturation requirement, or domain/epoch mismatch yields `TimeAuthorityUnavailable` and never wraps.

The registered subject arms bind the canonical pre-evidence body, never a future object that embeds the evidence: `CapabilityBytes{header_and_body_digest}`, `MutationPermit{permit_unsigned_body_digest}`, `ReadPermit{permit_unsigned_body_digest}`, `AuthorizationLease{lease_unsigned_body_digest}`, `ResultDeliveryLeaseBasis{basis_digest}`, `ResumeCursorCapability{capability_header_and_body_digest}`, `TxnOutcomeWindow{outcome_token_and_profiled_window_digest}`, `FollowerReadLease{lease_unsigned_body_digest}`, `IdRangeIssuanceLease{lease_unsigned_body_digest}`, `ClusterIncarnationLease{lease_unsigned_body_digest}`, `RestoreSourceLease{lease_unsigned_body_digest}`, `NewDatabaseIdentityReservation{reservation_unsigned_body_digest}`, `ServiceVisibilityEpochReservation{reservation_unsigned_body_digest}`, `AllocationEpochReservation{reservation_unsigned_body_digest}`, `ReplayArchiveLease{record_unsigned_body_digest}`, `BackupArchiveGrant{grant_unsigned_body_digest}`, `KeyEnvelopeGrantWindow{grant_unsigned_body_digest}`, `TransparencyFreshness{cross_log_receipt_unsigned_body_digest}`, and `VerifierKeyWindow{key_record_unsigned_body_digest}`. Each unsigned-body transcript includes its `time_authority_profile_oid`, both bounds when the object has a window, and every authority/domain/generation field, excluding only signatures/MAC and the later `TimeValidationEvidence` reference. `TimeBoundSubject` generation fails if any `durable_fields.toml` time-bearing schema lacks exactly one acyclic arm. A status-only check may consume a runtime guard; an ordered expiry, release, tombstone, retirement, compaction, or reclamation must retain the exact durable evidence in its applied transition.

A successful Usable validation creates a linear, nonserializable `TimeUseGuard` bound to observation, subject, intended action, process incarnation, and remaining monotonic use budget. It is consumed immediately before the protected observation/irreversible step and cannot survive restart, over-budget suspend, clone, serialization, or replay. Local monotonic time measures only challenge/use age; it never establishes absolute time. Expired evidence is durable and monotone for its one bound canonical release/expiry action. Every canonical transition whose legality depends on expiry strongly retains the exact evidence; a scalar deadline or timeout alone never changes canonical state or cuts retention. `TimeAuthorityRegistry` is `{generation,active_profile_ref:StrongRef<TimeAuthorityProfile>,sorted_accepted_profile_refs[StrongRef<TimeAuthorityProfile>],profile_retirement_floor,body_digest:BodyDigest<TimeAuthorityRegistry>}`; accepted refs are unique and canonically sorted, and the registered `"fgdb:time-authority-registry:v1"` body transcript excludes only `body_digest`. Every profile needed by a live window remains rooted. Each encoded security window names `time_authority_profile_oid`. `durable_fields.toml` assigns every time-bearing field a semantics ID, authorized predicate, evidence type, owner floor, and exact transition; G0 rejects ambient comparisons or an expiry transition without evidence. Mutation/golden tests prove that every semantic field changes the body digest.

`TimeAuthorityEpochTransition` is the external CAS-linear dual-authority record `{transition_id,predecessor_profile_ref:StrongRef<TimeAuthorityProfile>,successor_profile_ref:StrongRef<TimeAuthorityProfile>,predecessor_registry_head_digest_and_cas_version,successor_registry_head_digest_and_cas_version,old_final_challenged_interval,new_initial_challenged_interval,dual_signed_handoff_transcript,old_profile_subject_inventory_root,max_old_subject_expiry,old_observation_service_and_verification_key_live_through,successor_activation_tick,retirement_preconditions,old_and_new_signer_set_epochs,old_threshold_signatures,new_threshold_signatures}`. It does not make `AuthorityInstant`s from different epochs directly comparable. Before activating the successor, every old-profile subject must be in the authenticated inventory, have a finite checked expiry no later than the advertised drain bound, and the old authority must durably commit to serve challenged observations and retain verification keys through that bound. Renewable leases/grants are renewed under the successor before their old window ends; immutable capabilities remain on the old profile until they expire. `TimeAuthorityProfileTransitionSpec` installs the successor while retaining both profiles and the transition. `TimeAuthorityProfileRetirementSpec` is legal only after a generated-complete bijection proves every old-profile subject terminal, expired with retained direct old-profile evidence, or reissued with the old identity tombstoned; it then advances the profile-retirement floor. A bridge record alone can never classify an old window, disappearing old signers fail closed, and configurations whose old authority cannot meet the drain commitment cannot rotate profiles.

`ContinuityAuthorityObservation` is the continuity authority's challenged signed `{database_security_namespace_id,continuity_profile_id,current_continuity_record_digest,current_cas_version,cluster_incarnation,member_writer_id,lease_generation,scope,lease_status:Active,authority_tick,time_observation_ref:StrongRef<TimeAuthorityObservation>,intended_irreversible_action_digest,challenge_nonce,signer_set_epoch,signatures}`. `IncarnationLeaseGuard` exists only from the exact current observation plus `TimeValidationEvidence::Usable` for the same member/generation/scope/window/action. Every segment/object/root seal, prepared-root publication, receipt, Raft proposal/ack, certificate, and RootSlot publication consumes a fresh action-bound guard. Cached validity, canonical HLC, OS wall time, or a signature over an older continuity head never authorizes a write.

`ClusterIncarnationLease` is `{continuity_record_digest,cas_version,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,restore_id?,member_writer_id,scope:RecoveryOnly|OrdinaryWrite|RoleTransitionOnly,lease_generation,time_authority_profile_oid,not_before,expires_at,nonce,authority_signature}`. `CommitCx` contains a nonconstructible `IncarnationLeaseGuard`; recovery gets `RecoveryCommitCx` with only RecoveryOnly and role migration gets a guard whose encoders accept only transition objects. Immediately before every irreversible action, code validates the inode lease/fence, exact external continuity head/CAS version, action-bound authority observation/evidence, live member lease, and operation scope. Authority outage, ambiguity, expiry, or rollback poisons publication; cached validity is insufficient. `RootSlot` and every role payload carry the continuity digest/CAS version, service visibility epoch, and time-authority binding.

Prior-incarnation/archive edges use exact nonlocal types. `PriorIncarnationObjectRef<T> {restore_id,source_backup_manifest_digest,source_cluster_incarnation,target_cluster_incarnation,source:BackupArchiveRef<T>}` is legal only in restore plans/results/bridges/evidence/provenance and never enters the current mark set. `RestoreSourceLeaseIdentity` is `{restore_id,database_id,database_security_namespace_id,target_incarnation,archive_authority_id,lease_lineage_id,backup_manifest_digest,archive_inventory_root_digest,permitted_inventory_digest,holder_authority_digest}`. `RestoreSourceLeaseRecord` is the immutable `{identity:RestoreSourceLeaseIdentity,generation,predecessor_record_digest:WeakDigest?,record_kind:Acquire|Renew,time_authority_profile_oid,not_before,expires_at,renewal_nonce,archive_monotonic_counter,archive_authority_signature}`. Generation one has no predecessor; each renewal is prior+1 with checked overflow, names the prior canonical digest, preserves identity/inventory/holder, advances the archive counter, and may only extend validity. `RestoreArchiveRef<T> {source:PriorIncarnationObjectRef<T>,lease_identity:RestoreSourceLeaseIdentity,permitted_inventory_leaf,leaf_proof}` contains no strong lease-generation edge. Resolution requires the latest locally registered live generation, an exact inventory proof, and current Usable time evidence; the role-valid `RestoreRegistry` is the sole canonical strong owner of that record.

**Restore registry, immutable lease release, and abandonment.** `RestoreRegistry` is the closed role union `Local{registry_generation,activity:Idle|OneLive{restore_id},entries[restore_id->LocalRestoreRegistryValue]}|Meta{registry_generation,activity:Idle|OneLive{restore_id},entries[restore_id->MetaRestoreRegistryValue]}|Shard{shard_id,registry_generation,activity:Idle|OneLive{restore_id},entries[restore_id->ShardRestoreRegistryValue]}`; role/group substitution or more than one live restore is unencodable. `RestoreRegistryCommon` is `{restore_id,restore_epoch,mode:RecoverSameIdentity|CloneNewIdentity,source_posture,target_posture,source_manifest_identity,target_database_and_security_identity,target_incarnation,service_visibility_epoch,source_lease_identity:RestoreSourceLeaseIdentity,transform_plan_ref:StrongRef<RecoveryIncarnationTransformPlan>,projection_result_ref:StrongRef<RecoveryIncarnationProjectionResult>,state_generation}`.

Local registry values are exactly `ActiveHidden{common,restore_state_ref:StrongRef<RestoreState>,latest_lease_record_ref:StrongRef<RestoreSourceLeaseRecord>}|AbandonAuthorizedHidden{common,restore_state_ref:StrongRef<RestoreState>,abandon_operation_record_ref:StrongRef<RestoreAbandonOperationRecord>,latest_lease_record_ref}|PromotedAwaitingReopen{common,promotion_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef,manifest_ref:StrongRef<RestoreServicePromotionManifest>,promotion_receipt_ref:StrongRef<RestoreServicePromotionReceipt>,latest_lease_record_ref}|AwaitingSourceRelease{common,terminal:Operational{completion_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef,promotion_receipt_ref:StrongRef<RestoreServicePromotionReceipt>,independent_reopen_proof_ref:StrongRef<LocalRestoreIndependentReopenProof>}|Abandoned{abandon_finalize_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef,abandonment_tombstone_ref:StrongRef<RestoreAbandonmentTombstone>,abandonment_receipt_ref:StrongRef<RestoreAbandonmentReceipt>},latest_lease_record_ref}|ReleaseRequested{common,completion_evidence_ref:StrongRef<RestoreCompletionEvidence>,operation_record_ref:StrongRef<RestoreSourceLeaseReleaseOperationRecord>,latest_lease_record_ref}|Released{terminal_common,completion_evidence_ref:StrongRef<RestoreCompletionEvidence>,operation_record_ref:StrongRef<RestoreSourceLeaseReleaseOperationRecord>,archive_release_receipt_ref:StrongRef<ArchiveLeaseReleaseReceipt>,release_finalize_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef,terminal_tombstone_ref:StrongRef<RestoreTerminalTombstone>}`. Meta has the same authority-owning progression; its promoted/operational arms additionally carry the final certificate, Meta reopen proof, exact required-shard commitment, and complete operational-ack commitment. Shard values are `ActiveHidden{common,restore_state_ref,participant_lease_record_ref}|OpenedAwaitingIndependentReopen{common,open_applied_ref,promotion_receipt_ref,participant_lease_record_ref}|OperationalParticipantComplete{terminal_common,reopen_confirm_applied_ref,independent_reopen_proof_ref,promotion_receipt_ref}|AbandonedParticipantComplete{terminal_common,abandon_apply_ref,abandonment_tombstone_ref,abandonment_receipt_ref}`. Only Local or Meta authority may renew/release the external source lease.

Initial construction is `lease record -> transform plan -> projection result -> reconciliation root -> initial hidden RestoreState -> initial role-valid RestoreRegistry -> RecoveryBridgeSpec`; the bridge therefore carries `initial_restore_registry_ref:StrongRef<RestoreRegistry>`. Neither initial object names the bridge, command record, payload, state root, manifest, or RootSlot. `RestoreSourceLeaseRenewSpec` is `{restore_id,expected_registry_basis:WeakStateIdentity,expected_lineage_identity,expected_generation,successor_lease_record_ref:StrongRef<RestoreSourceLeaseRecord>,expected_live_registry_tag,time_validation_evidence_ref:StrongRef<TimeValidationEvidence>,terminal_audit_gate}`; it performs only the exact immutable-generation replacement and is illegal after ReleaseRequested/Released.

`RestoreCompletionEvidence` is the closed union `LocalOperational{restore_id,completion_applied_ref,audit_mirror_identity,promotion_receipt_ref,independent_reopen_proof_ref}|ShardedOperational{restore_id,completion_applied_ref,audit_mirror_identity,promotion_receipt_ref,meta_independent_reopen_proof_ref,exact_sorted_operational_ack_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<RestoreShardOperationalAck>],complete_required_group_commitment}|LocalAbandoned{restore_id,abandon_finalize_applied_ref,audit_mirror_identity,abandonment_receipt_ref,tombstone_ref,no_target_observation_proof_ref}|ShardedAbandoned{restore_id,abandon_finalize_applied_ref,audit_mirror_identity,abandonment_receipt_ref,meta_tombstone_ref,exact_sorted_shard_abandon_ack_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<RestoreShardAbandonAck>],complete_required_group_commitment}`. It is built only after the named completion/abandon candidate's audit mirror and contains no source-lease strong edge.

`RestoreSourceLeaseReleaseSpec` is `{restore_id,expected_registry_basis:WeakStateIdentity,expected_registry_tag:AwaitingSourceRelease,completion_evidence_ref:StrongRef<RestoreCompletionEvidence>,lease_identity:RestoreSourceLeaseIdentity,expected_latest_generation,operation_recipe:{operation_id,idempotency_key_digest,archive_authority_id,canonical_release_request_digest},minimum_dispatch_validity,time_validation_evidence_ref:StrongRef<TimeValidationEvidence>,terminal_audit_gate}`. Apply constructs `RestoreSourceLeaseReleaseOperationRecord {restore_id,operation_id,idempotency_key_digest,lease_identity,expected_latest_generation,archive_authority_id,canonical_release_request_digest,source_spec_ref:StrongRef<RestoreSourceLeaseReleaseSpec>,state:Requested}` and enters ReleaseRequested. No archive call is legal until this ordered state is audit-visible and yields `RestoreSourceLeaseReleaseDispatchEvidence {operation_record_ref:StrongRef<RestoreSourceLeaseReleaseOperationRecord>,applied_command_identity,audit_mirror_identity,winning_root_slot_generation,root_slot_durability_digest,current_registry_generation,time_use_guard_observation_digest}`. The external call always uses that exact idempotency transcript.

`ArchiveLeaseReleaseReceipt` is portable `{archive_authority_id,lease_identity,released_through_generation,operation_id,idempotency_key_digest,canonical_request_digest,prior_and_result_archive_counters,outcome:Released|AlreadyReleased|AlreadyExpired,released_at,time_authority_evidence_digest,signer_epoch,signature}`. Timeout/local expiry is never a substitute. `RestoreSourceLeaseReleaseFinalizeSpec` is `{restore_id,expected_registry_basis:WeakStateIdentity,expected_registry_tag:ReleaseRequested,operation_record_ref:StrongRef<RestoreSourceLeaseReleaseOperationRecord>,dispatch_evidence_ref:StrongRef<RestoreSourceLeaseReleaseDispatchEvidence>,archive_release_receipt_ref:StrongRef<ArchiveLeaseReleaseReceipt>,expected_lease_identity,expected_latest_generation,expected_completion_evidence_digest,terminal_audit_gate}`. Apply verifies the exact operation/receipt/transcript/generation and constructs Released without a lease edge. The prior visible registry remains the sole strong owner while the candidate is audit-fenced; the edge disappears exactly when the finalize mirror makes the candidate visible. Retry is idempotent; conflicting operation, inventory, holder, authority, generation, or transcript fails closed.

`RestoreNoTargetObservationProof<Role>` is generated from the exact role schema and binds `{restore_id,restore_epoch,target_incarnation,service_visibility_epoch,role_and_group,current_hidden_state_root_identity,current_root_slot_generations,zero_ordinary_writer_lease_proof,zero_READY_handshake_session_query_transaction_result_delivery_and_capability_issuance_proof,no_service_promotion_receipt_proof,external_catalog_absent_or_hidden_version,complete_endpoint_set,service_admission_log_commitment,audit_commitment,checker_version,signatures}`. Sharded abandonment requires a Meta proof and one certified proof from every configured shard. `RestoreAbandonSpec` is the closed `Local{restore_id,expected_hidden_state,no_target_observation_proof_ref:StrongRef<RestoreNoTargetObservationProof<Local>>,expected_continuity_reservation_and_catalog_versions,abandonment_manifest_body_recipe,external_operation_recipe,source_lease_disposition:ReleaseRequired,terminal_audit_gate}|ShardedMeta{restore_id,expected_hidden_meta_state,meta_no_target_observation_proof_ref:StrongRef<RestoreNoTargetObservationProof<Meta>>,exact_sorted_shard_no_observation_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<RestoreNoTargetObservationProof<Shard>>],complete_group_commitment,expected_continuity_reservation_and_catalog_versions,abandonment_manifest_body_recipe,external_operation_recipe,source_lease_disposition:ReleaseRequired,terminal_audit_gate}`. Apply remains hidden, enters AbandonAuthorizedHidden, and durably constructs `RestoreAbandonOperationRecord` before any external CAS.

After its audit mirror, `RestoreAbandonmentManifest` portably commits the exact authorization/no-observation/group evidence, target tombstone recipe, source-lease identity/disposition, and expected continuity/catalog predecessors. External CAS changes the reserved continuity head to `RestoreAbandoned{restore_id,target_incarnation,service_visibility_epoch,abandonment_manifest_digest,target_tombstone_recipe_digest,retired_through_incarnation,no_operational_successor_at_this_incarnation}`, then installs a no-endpoint catalog tombstone; `RestoreAbandonmentReceipt` carries both chains. `LocalRestoreAbandonFinalizeSpec` consumes it, clears `restore_state_ref`, enters `RecoveryAbandoned`, creates `RestoreAbandonmentTombstone`, and moves to AwaitingSourceRelease::Abandoned. Sharded restore applies `ShardRestoreAbandonApplySpec` and collects one `RestoreShardAbandonAck` per configured shard before `GlobalRestoreAbandonFinalizeSpec`. Source release begins only after the finalize audit mirror. RecoveryAbandoned admits only lease renewal/release/finalize and registered tombstone compaction under RecoveryCommitCx; it rejects ordinary open, service, sessions, capabilities, user work, maintenance, reconfiguration, and resurrection. A later same-identity restore must reserve a strictly higher incarnation.

`RecoveryIncarnationTransformPlan` is the pre-order object `{restore_id,mode:RecoverSameIdentity|CloneNewIdentity,source_manifest:BackupArchiveRef<BackupManifest>,restore_source_lease_identity,source_posture:Local|Sharded,source_database_and_security_identity,source_backup_incarnation,externally_retired_incarnation_floor,target_database_and_security_identity,target_incarnation,target_service_visibility_epoch,registry_versions,canonical_topological_source_inventory,sorted_transform_recipes[],expected_posture,expected_semantic_digest,complete_schema_and_field_coverage_digest}`. Each recipe is exactly `ReaddressAndReprotect{source:RestoreArchiveRef<T>,target_kind_and_schema,canonical_body_recipe,references_to_earlier_mapping_entries[],target_physical_profile,target_key_recipient_profile}|ReuseIncarnationNeutral{source,neutrality_registry_row,proof_of_no_incarnation_authority_capability_or_reference_fields,target_availability_recipe}|CarryPriorIncarnationEvidence{source,evidence_class,original_canonical_bytes_and_signature_digest,original_signer_domain_and_verification_chain,target_prior_evidence_registry_slot}|RecreateCurrentAuthority{source_evidence_inputs[],target_configuration_key_or_certificate_recipe,target_signing_ceremony_ref}|InvalidateAndReissueCapability{source_capability_or_verifier_domain,invalidation_tombstone_recipe,reauthentication_policy}|Reject{stable_reason}`. Invalidation creates no replacement capability.

Execution is leaves-first. `ReaddressAndReprotect` opens/verifies source bytes, substitutes only earlier target mappings, canonical-encodes, computes the new ObjectId, encrypts under new AEAD AAD containing that ObjectId, computes CiphertextId, builds complete encoding/placement/opener/wrap records, and verifies recoverability. Changed bodies cannot reuse old ciphertext. Historical external signatures are carried byte-identically and never presented as target authority; current configurations/certificates/keys/trust are recreated. The completed `RecoveryIncarnationProjectionResult {plan_ref:StrongRef<RecoveryIncarnationTransformPlan>,sorted_source_to_target_entries[],target_logical_root_set,target_configuration_checkpoint_floor_and_prepared_roots,target_physical_inventory,target_availability_certificates,carried_prior_evidence_registry_root,invalidated_capability_tombstone_root,recreated_current_authority_root,no_missing_duplicate_or_unclassified_entry_proof,posture_preservation_proof,semantic_equivalence_digest,complete_field_and_object_coverage_digest}` exists before any bridge and names no future root.

`LeasesRevokedOrExpiredThrough` is the external immutable certificate `{database_security_namespace_id,continuity_profile_id,restore_id,prior_incarnation,target_reserved_incarnation,current_restore_reserved_continuity_digest,current_cas_version,maximum_issued_prior_lease_generation,disposition:RevokedThrough{revocation_transition_digest,revocation_receipt_commitment}|ExpiredThrough{last_possible_expiry,time_validation_evidence_ref:StrongRef<TimeValidationEvidence>},no_future_prior_incarnation_lease_issuance_proof,authority_tick,signer_set_epoch,threshold_signatures}`. Its continuity head already forbids issuance/renewal under the prior incarnation; a scalar expiry or unsigned generation range is never retirement proof.

The three allocation-style reservations share one nonreuse protocol but have distinct bodies. `NewDatabaseIdentityReservation` is `{reservation_id,restore_id,mode:CloneNewIdentity,new_database_id,new_database_security_namespace_id,staging_inode_identity,expected_target_incarnation,authority_epoch,time_authority_profile_oid,not_before,expires_at,issuance_nonce,signature}`. `ServiceVisibilityEpochReservation` is `{reservation_id,database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,migration_nonce,source_posture:Local,target_posture:Sharded,source_service_visibility_epoch,target_service_visibility_epoch,external_service_epoch_floor,complete_target_group_topology_and_endpoint_commitment,expected_continuity_digest_and_cas_version,expected_catalog_version,authority_epoch,time_authority_profile_oid,not_before,expires_at,issuance_nonce,signature}`, with target strictly greater than both source and external floor. `AllocationEpochReservation` is `{reservation_id,restore_id,mode:RecoverSameIdentity|CloneNewIdentity,target_database_id,target_database_security_namespace_id,target_incarnation,source_manifest_digest,sorted_allocator_families[{allocator_kind,source_max_epoch,external_retired_floor,target_epoch,possibly_issued_source_ranges_digest,burn_through_range,successor_start}],complete_source_allocator_root_and_range_coverage_digest,external_allocator_floor_digest,authority_epoch,time_authority_profile_oid,not_before,expires_at,issuance_nonce,signature}`; every target epoch/range begins strictly beyond all source, external, restored, and possibly issued values with checked arithmetic.

`ReservationAuthorityHead` is the external CAS-linear `{authority_domain,reservation_kind,reservation_id,cas_version,predecessor_head_digest,monotonic_nonreuse_floor,issuance_body_digest,state:Reserved|ClaimedForUse{claim_id,intended_use_kind,intended_use_commitment,claimant_identity,no_reassignment:true}|Consumed{claim_id,applied_use_identity,consumption_receipt_digest}|BurnedBeforeUse{claim_id?,stable_reason,no_matching_use_proof_digest},authority_tick,signer_set_epoch,threshold_signatures}`. Only `Reserved -> ClaimedForUse -> Consumed`, `Reserved -> BurnedBeforeUse`, or `ClaimedForUse -> BurnedBeforeUse` with an authority-verified no-use proof is legal. Expiry can authorize BurnedBeforeUse but never returns the value to an allocation pool; the nonreuse floor only advances. A claim has no timeout/reassignment path: exact retry joins it, a conflicting commitment fails, and recovery must consume or prove the named use absent before burn. `ReservationAuthorityObservation` is challenged/action-bound and signs the exact current head/CAS/state/claim/intended use plus a `TimeAuthorityObservation`; claiming requires fresh `TimeValidationEvidence::Usable`. `ReservationConsumptionReceipt` signs the direct `ClaimedForUse -> Consumed` successor and exact applied bridge/continuity/catalog identity. Local/Meta `ReservationConsumptionMirror` records the direct successor; rollback/fork/skip is a permanent gap.

The first restore bridge consumes already exclusive claims, not bare Reserved objects. `RestoreCreationAuthority` is the closed mode union `RecoverSameIdentity{restore_reserved_continuity_record_ref:StrongRef<ClusterIncarnationContinuityRecord>,live_recovery_incarnation_lease:ClusterIncarnationLease,old_lease_barrier_ref:StrongRef<LeasesRevokedOrExpiredThrough>}|CloneNewIdentity{creation_authority:DirectoryBound{new_database_and_security_namespace_reservation_ref:StrongRef<NewDatabaseIdentityReservation>,claimed_reservation_head_ref:StrongRef<ReservationAuthorityHead>,claim_observation_ref:StrongRef<ReservationAuthorityObservation>,claim_time_validation_evidence_ref:StrongRef<TimeValidationEvidence>,staging_inode_identity}|ExternalCas{clone_reserved_continuity_record_ref:StrongRef<ClusterIncarnationContinuityRecord>,live_recovery_incarnation_lease:ClusterIncarnationLease},audit_clone_boundary_ref:StrongRef<AuditCloneBoundary>}`. `PendingRestoreCreationGuard` is linear/nonexportable `{restore_id,target_role_and_group,staging_inode_and_filesystem_profile,local_whole_inode_lease,root_publication_sequencer,restore_creation_authority:RestoreCreationAuthority,allocation_epoch_reservation_ref:StrongRef<AllocationEpochReservation>,allocation_claimed_head_ref:StrongRef<ReservationAuthorityHead>,allocation_claim_observation_ref:StrongRef<ReservationAuthorityObservation>,allocation_claim_time_validation_evidence_ref:StrongRef<TimeValidationEvidence>,restore_source_lease_record_ref:StrongRef<RestoreSourceLeaseRecord>,projection_result_ref:StrongRef<RecoveryIncarnationProjectionResult>,exact_allowed_object_inventory,exact_recovery_bridge_body_recipe,exact_first_recovery_payload_root_manifest_and_slot_recipes,service_visibility_epoch,unconsumed}`. The two claims byte-match the same restore/bridge commitment. The bridge atomically installs every reserved allocator epoch, burned range/tombstone, and local consumed-reservation marker with the first hidden payload; after slot durability, recovery finalizes each external head to Consumed with that applied identity and mirrors the receipt. A crash before publication can burn only after proving the unique staging inode/slot and continuity head never published the bridge; a crash after publication can only complete consumption. The encoder permits only projection-result bytes, recreated current authority/configuration/checkpoint/floor, initial `RestoreState` and `RestoreRegistry`, one `RecoveryBridgeSpec` plus its role-valid first control command/log entry/result/command record, the first complete `RecoveryReconciling` payload/root, RootManifest/bootstrap/RootSlot, and their D1 availability closure. It rejects Genesis, Operational, user work, any second/general control, prepared user receipt, ordinary Raft traffic, or service advertisement. It uses an exclusive staging inode, full sync, no-replace rename, directory sync, inode revalidation, and the exact root-publication permit/reread, then becomes `RecoveryWriterLeaseGuard`, never an ordinary token. Double-use, competing restore, expiry, crash before/after bridge, external-finalize loss, clone/same-identity substitution, allocator-coverage omission, and checked-range exhaustion are permanent model/property/crash tests.

`RestoreReconciliationEvidenceRef<Role>` and `RestoreExplicitRetentionOwnerRef<Role>` are generated closed tagged unions over the role-valid `RegisteredStrongRef` targets for identity/allocation, privacy, audit, prepared/decision, cursor/delivery, resource, key, remote retention/trust, history, replay, backup, DP, derived state, and capability invalidation. `RestoreReconciliationRoot` has exactly one generated slot per activated class; each value is `Pending{reason_code}|Resolved{evidence:RestoreReconciliationEvidenceRef<Role>}|ExplicitlyRetained{owner:RestoreExplicitRetentionOwnerRef<Role>,floor,expiry_or_terminal_rule}|Disabled{exact_fail_closed_policy}`. `RestoreReconciliationCompletionProof` is `{restore_id,restore_epoch,role_and_group,reconciliation_root_ref:StrongRef<RestoreReconciliationRoot>,activated_slot_bitmap,resolved_slot_bitmap,explicitly_retained_slot_bitmap,disabled_slot_bitmap,zero_pending_proof,all_explicit_retention_rules_live_proof,complete_transform_projection_coverage_digest,checker_version}`. The four bitmaps are disjoint and exhaustive. `RestoreReconciliationStatus` is `Pending{unresolved_slot_bitmap}|Complete{proof_ref:StrongRef<RestoreReconciliationCompletionProof>}`; no nullable proof or inferred readiness exists. `RestoreStateCommon` is `{restore_id,restore_epoch,source_posture,source_manifest_identity,source_backup_incarnation,externally_retired_incarnation_floor,target_incarnation,service_visibility_epoch,target_role_and_group,continuity_record_digest_and_cas_version,transform_plan_ref:StrongRef<RecoveryIncarnationTransformPlan>,projection_result_ref:StrongRef<RecoveryIncarnationProjectionResult>,restore_source_lease_identity,target_configuration_and_topology_identity,reconciliation_root_ref:StrongRef<RestoreReconciliationRoot>,reconciliation_status:RestoreReconciliationStatus,service_gate:Hidden,state_generation}`.

`RestoreState` is the closed role union `Local{common,phase:Reconciling|VisibilityCommitted{activation_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef}|ServicePreparedHidden{prepare_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef}}|Meta{common,phase:Reconciling|ActivationOrdered{activation_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef}|VisibilityCommitted{visibility_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef}|ServicePreparedHidden{prepare_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef}}|Shard{common,shard_id,phase:Reconciling|ActivationAppliedHidden{activation_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef}|VisibilityApplied{visibility_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef}|ServicePreparedHidden{prepare_applied_ref:AuthorityAppliedRef}}`. The generated role validator accepts only the matching Local, Meta, or Shard `AuthorityAppliedRef` arm. A ready certificate/barrier may be signed only over `Reconciling + Complete`; it is owned outside `RestoreState` by the certificate ledger after the source root exists. Each applied phase stores only its already identified input command plus assigned order—never the future command record, resulting root, post-apply certificate, or acknowledgement. `ServicePreparedHidden` additionally requires exact visibility evidence but does not clear the state or service gate. No ordinary work, session admission, endpoint advertisement, capability issuance, or result delivery is legal while `restore_state_ref` is present.

`RecoveryBridgeDependencyRef<Role>` is the generated closed union of role-valid recreated signing/wrap/verifier authority, identity/privacy/audit reconciliation-plan, and prepared/cursor/delivery/remote-obligation plan objects. `RecoveryBridgeSpec` is the exact special first-control body `{restore_id,restore_epoch,source_manifest:PriorIncarnationObjectRef<BackupManifest>,transform_plan_ref:StrongRef<RecoveryIncarnationTransformPlan>,projection_result_ref:StrongRef<RecoveryIncarnationProjectionResult>,authority:RecoverSameIdentity{restore_reserved_continuity_record_ref:StrongRef<ClusterIncarnationContinuityRecord>,recovery_incarnation_lease_identity}|CloneNewIdentity{target_identity_creation_reservation_ref:StrongRef<NewDatabaseIdentityReservation>,target_continuity_or_directory_creation_identity,audit_clone_boundary_ref:StrongRef<AuditCloneBoundary>,recovery_incarnation_lease_identity?},restore_source_lease_identity,target_role_payload:Local{target_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,assigned_logical_command_origin}|Meta{target_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,target_topology_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,assigned_global_command_origin}|Shard{shard_id,target_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,target_topology_epoch,assigned_shard_raft_origin},initial_restore_state_ref:StrongRef<RestoreState>,initial_restore_registry_ref:StrongRef<RestoreRegistry>,target_checkpoint_floor_and_prepared_root_body_recipes,allocation_epoch_reservation_ref:StrongRef<AllocationEpochReservation>,dependency_refs[RecoveryBridgeDependencyRef<Role>],dependency_coverage_bitmap,complete_posture_field_and_object_coverage_digest,terminal_audit_gate:StructurallyInapplicable{RecoverySystemAuthority}}`. Its mode/role must match the guard, transform plan, initial state, and role-valid registry; source lease identity/generation and every registry common field must byte-match. The bridge D1 closure, guard body recipe, dependency bitmap, and complete-coverage digest include both initial objects. Body recipes name no future command record, payload, state root, manifest, or slot. The initial `RestoreState` and registry are built before the spec, are necessarily hidden `Reconciling`/`ActiveHidden`, and name neither the spec nor any future record. The spec is registered for Local, Meta, and Shard but is legal only as the first staged control entry consumed by `PendingRestoreCreationGuard`. Apply validates and installs both already-built initial objects, then constructs the role payload, a real role-valid command record with `RecoveryBridge` origin, and finally the state root/manifest/slot. Fresh Genesis alone has no command head; restore never validates an old root as current and never creates a headless non-Genesis state.

`RestoreReadyClosureRef<Role>` is a generated closed union over the role-valid checkpoint/vector/floor/history/prepared/certificate/key/derived/remote-obligation/configuration roots, and `RestoreReadyClosureInventory<Role>` is `{role_and_group,sorted_refs[RestoreReadyClosureRef<Role>],exhaustive_coverage_bitmap,inventory_digest}`. No raw `[StrongRef]` bag is legal. For sharded restore, `RestoreShardReadyBarrier {SameGroupCertificateHeader,restore_id,restore_epoch,service_visibility_epoch,shard_id,target_domain,exact_global_barrier,target_topology_and_configuration,local_projection_result_ref:StrongRef<RecoveryIncarnationProjectionResult>,state_root_ref:StrongRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,ready_closure_inventory_ref:StrongRef<RestoreReadyClosureInventory<Shard>>,active_meta_projection_root_ref:StrongRef<ActiveMetaProjectionRoot>,reconciliation_completion_proof_ref:StrongRef<RestoreReconciliationCompletionProof>,local_root_slot_durability_digest,one_digest_signer_lock_ref,quorum_signatures}` strongly owns the exact local closure. Its completion proof allows both Resolved and ExplicitlyRetained slots and rejects any Pending slot.

`GlobalRestoreActivationSpec` is `{restore_id,expected_meta_state:WeakStateIdentity,exact_global_barrier,expected_topology_and_meta_configuration,meta_reconciliation_proof_ref:StrongRef<RestoreReconciliationCompletionProof>,meta_ready_closure_inventory_ref:StrongRef<RestoreReadyClosureInventory<Meta>>,exact_sorted_ready_barrier_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<RestoreShardReadyBarrier>],complete_group_partition_and_authority_commitment,continuity_reservation_digest,recovery_lease_generation,service_visibility_epoch,terminal_audit_gate}`. After apply and the exact audit mirror, Meta creates `GlobalRestoreActivationCertificate {SameGroupCertificateHeader,restore_id,activation_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,exact_global_barrier,topology_and_meta_configuration_identity,sorted_ready_barrier_identities,complete_group_partition_and_authority_commitment,post_apply_global_state_root_ref:StrongRef<GlobalStateRoot>,service_visibility_epoch,audit_mirror_identity:WeakGlobalCommandIdentity,one_digest_signer_lock_ref,quorum_signatures}`. `ShardRestoreActivationApplySpec` is `{activation_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalRestoreActivationCertificate>,own_ready_barrier_ref:StrongRef<RestoreShardReadyBarrier>,expected_local_restore_state:WeakStateIdentity,expected_topology_configuration_and_remote_trust_selector,exact_typed_restore_projection_payload}` and leaves the shard hidden. Its `ShardControlAuthority` compatibility row requires `MetaAuthorized` with that exact activation CRSR; there is no duplicate authority field in the body. It then emits `RestoreShardActivationAck {SameGroupCertificateHeader,restore_id,activation_identity,ready_barrier_identity,post_apply_state_root_ref:StrongRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,applied_shard_raft_index,exact_global_barrier,service_visibility_epoch,service_gate:Hidden,root_slot_durability_digest,audit_mirror_prefix,one_digest_signer_lock_ref,quorum_signatures}`.

`RestoreVisibilityCommitSpec` is `{restore_id,activation_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,activation_certificate_ref:StrongRef<GlobalRestoreActivationCertificate>,exact_sorted_activation_ack_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<RestoreShardActivationAck>],expected_meta_restore_state:WeakStateIdentity,expected_topology_and_configurations,complete_required_shard_commitment,service_visibility_epoch,terminal_audit_gate}`. It makes Meta `VisibilityCommitted` but still service-hidden and, after its audit mirror, yields `RestoreVisibilityCommitCertificate {SameGroupCertificateHeader,restore_id,visibility_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,activation_identity,sorted_activation_ack_identities,topology_and_configuration_commitment,post_apply_global_state_root_ref:StrongRef<GlobalStateRoot>,service_visibility_epoch,audit_mirror_identity:WeakGlobalCommandIdentity,one_digest_signer_lock_ref,quorum_signatures}`. Each shard orders `ShardRestoreVisibilityApplySpec {visibility_commit_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<RestoreVisibilityCommitCertificate>,own_activation_ack_ref:StrongRef<RestoreShardActivationAck>,expected_local_restore_state:WeakStateIdentity,service_visibility_epoch}`; its outer authority row requires `MetaAuthorized` with that visibility CRSR. It becomes `VisibilityApplied` but remains hidden and emits `RestoreShardVisibilityAck {SameGroupCertificateHeader,restore_id,visibility_commit_identity,own_activation_ack_identity,post_apply_state_root_ref:StrongRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,applied_shard_raft_index,service_visibility_epoch,service_gate:Hidden,root_slot_durability_digest,audit_mirror_prefix,one_digest_signer_lock_ref,quorum_signatures}`.

Service opening is acyclic and receipt-first. `GlobalRestoreServicePrepareSpec` is `{restore_id,visibility_commit_ref:StrongRef<RestoreVisibilityCommitCertificate>,exact_sorted_visibility_ack_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<RestoreShardVisibilityAck>],expected_meta_restore_state:WeakStateIdentity,exact_topology_configuration_and_endpoint_set,expected_restore_reserved_or_clone_reserved_continuity_digest_and_cas_version,service_visibility_epoch,expected_catalog_predecessor_version,terminal_audit_gate}`. It remains `RecoveryReconciling`, installs Meta `ServicePreparedHidden`, and after its audit mirror creates `GlobalRestoreServicePrepareCertificate {SameGroupCertificateHeader,restore_id,prepare_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,visibility_commit_identity,sorted_visibility_ack_identities,topology_configuration_endpoint_commitment,reserved_continuity_digest_and_cas_version,service_visibility_epoch,expected_catalog_predecessor_version,audit_mirror_identity:WeakGlobalCommandIdentity,one_digest_signer_lock_ref,quorum_signatures}`.

Each shard orders `ShardRestoreServicePrepareSpec {prepare_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalRestoreServicePrepareCertificate>,own_visibility_ack_ref:StrongRef<RestoreShardVisibilityAck>,expected_local_restore_state:WeakStateIdentity,expected_topology_configuration_and_remote_trust_selector,service_visibility_epoch}` under the outer exact `MetaAuthorized` row, remains hidden, and emits `RestoreShardServiceReadyAck {SameGroupCertificateHeader,restore_id,prepare_identity,own_visibility_ack_identity,post_prepare_state_root_ref:StrongRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,applied_shard_raft_index,service_visibility_epoch,service_gate:Hidden,root_slot_durability_digest,one_digest_signer_lock_ref,quorum_signatures}`. The externally signed `RestoreServicePromotionManifest` is the portable closed posture union with common `{restore_id,database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,target_posture:Local|Sharded,service_visibility_epoch,continuity_transition_body_digest,expected_catalog_predecessor_version,signer_set_epoch,threshold_signatures}` and exactly one body: `Local{local_prepare_evidence:PortableCertificateProjection<LocalRestoreServicePrepareCertificate>,local_configuration_and_endpoint_commitment}` or `Sharded{meta_prepare_evidence:PortableCertificateProjection<GlobalRestoreServicePrepareCertificate>,sorted_shard_ready_evidence[PortableCertificateProjection<RestoreShardServiceReadyAck>],complete_group_topology_configuration_and_endpoint_commitment}`. `PortableCertificateProjection<T>` embeds the target `RemoteObjectIdentity`, complete export projection bytes, canonical configuration/trust evidence bytes, and signatures; it contains no `StrongRef`, `CertifiedRemoteStrongRef`, or consumer-local locator. Nullable cross-posture fields are forbidden.

`RestorePromotionRootSeal<Role>` closes the proof-of-reopen race. It is created only after the role's promotion/finalize/open candidate and audit mirror are RootSlot-visible and is the generated exact union `{restore_id,role_and_group,promotion_or_open_applied_identity,sealed_role_state_root_ref:StrongRef<RoleStateRoot>,sealed_root_manifest_ref:StrongRef<RootManifest>,winning_root_slot_generation_and_digest,continuity_and_catalog_receipt_digest,service_visibility_epoch,typed_physical_inventory_ref:StrongRef<RestorePromotionPhysicalInventory<Role>>,physical_pin_id,pin_durability_receipt_ref:StrongRef<RestorePromotionPinDurabilityReceipt>,allowed_pending_reopen_successor_classes,seal_digest}`. It is built after, and therefore may strongly name, the already-published root; neither that root nor its manifest names the seal. The role-specific ordered `LocalRestorePromotionSealInstallSpec`, `MetaRestorePromotionSealInstallSpec`, or `ShardRestorePromotionSealInstallSpec` installs the seal into the still-hidden `OperationalPendingIndependentReopen::Sealed` payload. Before seal installation the only legal work is exact promotion recovery, source-lease renewal where the role owns it, audit mirroring, shutdown, or seal installation. Afterward only those operations plus reopen confirmation are legal. Every allowed successor preserves the same seal/pin; ordinary admission, maintenance, checkpoint, GC, reconfiguration, key/policy/schema/data mutation, and a second promotion are rejected.

`RestoreIndependentReopenProof<Role>` opens the seal from an independent fresh process/context, not merely the current mutable head. It binds the seal, reopens every typed pinned object/encoding/key, reconstructs the sealed canonical/prepared/Raft closure, revalidates continuity/catalog receipt and service epoch, and supplies an authenticated proof that every successor from the sealed root to the current pending root is one of the allowed nonsemantic/recovery classes. Slot churn or a lease renewal therefore cannot erase the proof basis or legitimize an intervening mutation. The role-specific reopen-confirm command consumes that exact proof and is the only transition to `Operational`. Local/Meta retain the seal and physical pin until `RestoreSourceLeaseReleaseFinalizeSpec`; that finalize atomically removes the local pin owner and emits a portable `RestorePromotionPinReleaseAuthorization`. Each shard retains its seal through its operational ack and removes it only through `ShardRestorePromotionPinReleaseSpec` consuming the matching certified authorization. Release/tombstone floors retain every seal, inventory, proof, and pin receipt until all configured shard release acknowledgements and the source-release terminal are complete. Crash tests cut every seal-build, pin, slot publish, proof open, confirm, source-release, and shard-pin-release step, including arbitrary slot convergence and allowed lease renewals.

Publication first CAS-advances the exact `RestoreReserved|CloneReserved` continuity head to `Operational` at the same incarnation/visibility epoch, then CAS-installs the manifest into the external service catalog conditioned on that returned continuity digest. `RestoreServicePromotionReceipt {restore_id,manifest_digest,prior_and_operational_continuity_digests_and_cas_versions,continuity_cas_receipt,catalog_predecessor_and_result_versions,catalog_cas_receipt,service_visibility_epoch,authority_signatures}` exists only after both succeed; a crash between them is a hidden roll-forward state and cannot admit service. `GlobalRestoreServiceFinalizeSpec {restore_id,prepare_certificate_ref:StrongRef<GlobalRestoreServicePrepareCertificate>,manifest_ref:StrongRef<RestoreServicePromotionManifest>,promotion_receipt_ref:StrongRef<RestoreServicePromotionReceipt>,exact_sorted_ready_ack_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<RestoreShardServiceReadyAck>],expected_meta_restore_state:WeakStateIdentity,expected_operational_continuity_and_catalog_versions,service_visibility_epoch,terminal_audit_gate}` clears Meta restore state only into `OperationalPendingIndependentReopen::Unsealed`; request admission and routing remain disabled. After its audit mirror it yields `GlobalRestoreServiceFinalCertificate {SameGroupCertificateHeader,restore_id,finalize_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,manifest_and_receipt_digests,ready_ack_commitment,post_apply_global_state_root_ref:StrongRef<GlobalStateRoot>,service_visibility_epoch,audit_mirror_identity:WeakGlobalCommandIdentity,certificate_attempt_ref:StrongRef<CertificateAttemptRecord>,canonical_signature_set}`.

A shard leaves `RecoveryReconciling` only through `ShardRestoreServiceOpenSpec {final_certificate_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalRestoreServiceFinalCertificate>,own_ready_ack_ref:StrongRef<RestoreShardServiceReadyAck>,locally_verified_promotion_receipt_ref:StrongRef<RestoreServicePromotionReceipt>,expected_local_restore_state:WeakStateIdentity,service_visibility_epoch}` under its exact outer Meta authority, and that command selects `OperationalPendingIndependentReopen::Unsealed`, not Operational. After the open mirror, it builds/installs the role seal above. A fresh process then creates `ShardRestoreIndependentReopenProof`, and `ShardRestoreReopenConfirmSpec {restore_id,final_certificate_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalRestoreServiceFinalCertificate>,seal_ref:StrongRef<RestorePromotionRootSeal<Shard>>,independent_reopen_proof_ref:StrongRef<ShardRestoreIndependentReopenProof>,expected_pending_state:OperationalPendingIndependentReopen::Sealed,service_visibility_epoch}` alone selects Operational. Only its applied-and-durable root may produce `RestoreShardOperationalAck {SameGroupCertificateHeader,restore_id,final_certificate_identity,own_ready_ack_identity,reopen_confirm_applied_identity,post_open_state_root_ref:StrongRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,seal_identity,independent_reopen_proof_ref:StrongRef<ShardRestoreIndependentReopenProof>,applied_shard_raft_index,service_visibility_epoch,root_slot_durability_digest,certificate_attempt_ref:StrongRef<CertificateAttemptRecord>,canonical_signature_set}`. Meta routing waits for the target shard ack; direct shard endpoints reject every pending-reopen phase and require the current receipt, final Meta certificate, Operational root, and reopen proof.

Meta follows the same pattern after finalize: it installs `RestorePromotionRootSeal<Meta>`, a fresh context produces `MetaRestoreIndependentReopenProof`, and `GlobalRestoreServiceCompletionSpec {restore_id,final_certificate_ref:StrongRef<GlobalRestoreServiceFinalCertificate>,meta_seal_ref:StrongRef<RestorePromotionRootSeal<Meta>>,meta_independent_reopen_proof_ref:StrongRef<MetaRestoreIndependentReopenProof>,exact_sorted_operational_ack_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<RestoreShardOperationalAck>],promotion_receipt_ref:StrongRef<RestoreServicePromotionReceipt>,expected_restore_registry_state:PromotedAwaitingReopen,expected_meta_pending_state:OperationalPendingIndependentReopen::Sealed,expected_source_lease_generation,terminal_audit_gate}` verifies one ack from every required shard and alone selects Meta Operational. Its audit mirror moves the registry to AwaitingSourceRelease. It neither hides an unready group nor releases the source lease/pins directly.

The exact Local path is independent of sharded evidence. `LocalRestoreReadyCertificate` is `{SameGroupCertificateHeader,restore_id,restore_epoch,service_visibility_epoch,current_hidden_state_root_ref:StrongRef<LogicalStateRoot>,reconciliation_completion_proof_ref:StrongRef<RestoreReconciliationCompletionProof>,ready_closure_inventory_ref:StrongRef<RestoreReadyClosureInventory<Local>>,current_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,current_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<RecoveryCheckpoint>,current_config_floor_ref:StrongRef<ConfigPayloadFloor>,root_slot_durability_digest,one_digest_signer_lock_ref,quorum_signatures}`. `LocalRestoreActivationSpec` is `{restore_id,ready_certificate_ref:StrongRef<LocalRestoreReadyCertificate>,expected_local_restore_state:WeakStateIdentity,expected_configuration_checkpoint_and_floor,expected_reserved_continuity_digest_and_cas_version,service_visibility_epoch,terminal_audit_gate}` and moves only Reconciling -> VisibilityCommitted. After its mirror, `LocalRestoreActivationCertificate` owns the hidden root and exact ready evidence. `LocalRestoreServicePrepareSpec` is `{restore_id,activation_certificate_ref:StrongRef<LocalRestoreActivationCertificate>,expected_local_restore_state:WeakStateIdentity,exact_configuration_and_endpoint_set,expected_reserved_continuity_digest_and_cas_version,expected_catalog_predecessor_version,service_visibility_epoch,terminal_audit_gate}` and moves only to ServicePreparedHidden; its mirror yields `LocalRestoreServicePrepareCertificate` over the prepare record, hidden root, endpoint/configuration commitment, continuity/catalog basis, epoch, and signer transcript.

The Local arm of `RestoreServicePromotionManifest` is then continuity/catalog-CAS-published, producing the receipt first. `LocalRestoreServicePromotionSpec {restore_id,prepare_certificate_ref:StrongRef<LocalRestoreServicePrepareCertificate>,manifest_ref:StrongRef<RestoreServicePromotionManifest>,promotion_receipt_ref:StrongRef<RestoreServicePromotionReceipt>,expected_local_restore_state:WeakStateIdentity,expected_operational_continuity_and_catalog_versions,service_visibility_epoch,terminal_audit_gate}` clears restore state only into `OperationalPendingIndependentReopen::Unsealed` after its mirror; its registry becomes PromotedAwaitingReopen and still owns the source lease. It then installs `RestorePromotionRootSeal<Local>`. The exact generated `RestoreIndependentReopenProof<Role>` schema is the seal-bound proof above, including the allowed-successor-chain proof rather than an unpinned observation of whichever slot happens to be current. A fresh process produces `LocalRestoreIndependentReopenProof`; `LocalRestoreServiceCompletionSpec {restore_id,promotion_record_ref:StrongRef<LogicalCommandRecord>,promotion_receipt_ref:StrongRef<RestoreServicePromotionReceipt>,seal_ref:StrongRef<RestorePromotionRootSeal<Local>>,independent_reopen_proof_ref:StrongRef<LocalRestoreIndependentReopenProof>,expected_restore_registry_state:PromotedAwaitingReopen,expected_pending_state:OperationalPendingIndependentReopen::Sealed,expected_source_lease_generation,terminal_audit_gate}` alone selects Operational and moves the registry to AwaitingSourceRelease after its mirror. Source release then uses the ordered operation/dispatch/receipt/finalize protocol above; completion never directly drops the lease or pin.

Every handshake/session/request/forwarded shard request/transaction/query child/delivery cursor/cross-session capability carries `{cluster_incarnation,service_visibility_epoch}`. Mixed or stale epochs fail before authorization or observation. `RestoreSourceLease` remains live through promotion/finalize/open, independent target reopen, operational acknowledgements, and the role-valid post-open completion audit mirror. `CloneNewIdentity` uses the same transform/result/guard/reconciliation/promotion machinery but assigns a new database/security namespace, `K_oid`, continuity domain, current groups/authority, and Audit clone boundary; historical evidence remains carried, old capabilities remain invalid, and source authority is never current target authority. `source_posture == expected_posture` is mandatory for both modes; Local-to-W12 is a later separate role transition.
