**ReplayManifest / executable and archive closure.** `ReplayCompleteness` is `Replayable|StructuralReplay|VerifiableIfArtifactsSupplied|AuditOnly` with explicit class lists. `ArchiveObjectIdentity` is nonlocal and never a local reachability edge. `ReplayObjectRef<T>` is exactly `LocalStrong{ref:StrongRef<T>}|CertifiedRemote{ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<T>}|Archived{identity,expected_logical_object_id,expected_canonical_digest}`. CertifiedRemote requires a live matching authority configuration/trust selector/grant and participates in two-sided retention; Archived resolves only through the active registry and never marks local data. Every slot uses `ReplayEvidenceRef<T> = Present{object:ReplayObjectRef<T>}|Unavailable{class,expected identity/digest?,reason}|Redacted{class,commitment?,policy}`. `ReplayLogicalStateEvidence = Local{state:ReplayEvidenceRef<LogicalStateRoot>}|Sharded{global_state:ReplayEvidenceRef<GlobalStateRoot>,topology:ReplayEvidenceRef<TopologyState>,exact_global_prefix,sorted_shard_states[ReplayEvidenceRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>],complete_partition_commitment}`; a Sharded grade is no stronger than its weakest required group/evidence lease.

`ReplayManifest` binds `{format major/minor,slot schema,database/security namespace/incarnation,logical/commit seq,logical_state:ReplayLogicalStateEvidence,graph bindings,topology/policy/revocation epochs,language/semantic/scalar/numeric profiles,answer requirement/result contract,logical/physical plan IDs,bound/normalized query,typed parameters,replay authority,module/UDF set,external inputs,derived generation snapshots,decision cards/policies/evidence,executable artifacts,structural projection,result encoding/digest,structural completeness,archive requirements,created HLC}`. The generated slot schema derives the maximum grade: Replayable requires every execution-semantic Local or Sharded slot live; structural replay requires its typed projection; supply-later carries all identities/digests; audit/redaction is explicit. Live effective grade may only weaken as any local, certified-remote, or archive trust/lease/authority fails. Legacy Local manifests survive activation unchanged.

`ExecutableArtifactSet` binds `{ exact_binary:ReplayObjectRef | reproducible_build_closure[ReplayObjectRef], source_tree:ReplayObjectRef?, rust_toolchain:ReplayObjectRef,target,cpu_feature_contract,runtime_allocator_config:ReplayObjectRef,vm_jit_compiler_artifacts[ReplayObjectRef],kernel_profile_registry:ReplayObjectRef,platform_abi:ReplayObjectRef,build_recipe:ReplayObjectRef,artifact_digest }`; exactly one executable route must be complete whenever this set is present. `StructuralReplayProjection` binds its reproduced event/data-shape classes, canonical projection schema, required evidence-slot classes, omitted/redacted classes, expected commitments, and output verifier. `ReplayArchiveRecord` is immutable `{ archive_id,generation,predecessor_record_digest:WeakDigest?,security_domain,resolver_profile_oid,authenticated_external_locator,archive_closure_digest:WeakDigest,sorted_object_inventory[{identity:ArchiveObjectIdentity,expected_logical_object_id,expected_canonical_digest,length}],availability_commitment,time_authority_profile_oid,lease_not_before,lease_not_after,status:Active|Revoked|Expired,signer_set_epoch,signatures }`; its signature transcript covers the profile and both bounds. Its inventory/closure explicitly excludes the record itself, `ReplayRegistry`, and the locally rooted manifest, so archive and manifest identities can be constructed in the order `external evidence inventory -> archive record -> manifest -> registry` without a digest cycle. `ReplayRegistry` maps `manifest_id -> {manifest:StrongRef<ReplayManifest>,lease/status}` and `archive_id -> latest_record:StrongRef<ReplayArchiveRecord>`. Renewal creates a logical-command-sequenced successor after re-verifying the entire inventory and validating fresh Usable evidence. Revocation/expiry never asserts deletion; the ordered status successor retains the exact subject-bound time evidence when expiry is its cause, then consensus removes the registry availability edge, after which ordinary GC may release otherwise-unrooted local manifest objects/records. A manifest is advertised `Replayable` only while every required local object opens and every archive requirement resolves through an active, time-validated, trusted record with a matching inventory/closure digest. Resolver credentials and replay contents require scoped `Replay` authority; capability-safe lookup does not disclose whether another authority's manifest/archive exists.

**Authorization, durable capabilities, DP, resources, and audit records.** `MutationPermitRecord` is `{database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,service_visibility_epoch,tenant,principal,issuer,authority_ceiling,authority_digest,policy_semantics_oid,policy_epoch,revocation_index,exact_role_bearing_read_bindings,role_free_write_coordinates,snapshot_scope,operation_scope,nonce,time_authority_profile_oid,not_before,expiry,signer_epoch,signature_or_mac_transcript}`. `ReadPermitRecord` is the distinct no-write format `{database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,service_visibility_epoch,tenant,principal,issuer,authority_ceiling,authority_digest,policy_semantics_oid,policy_epoch,revocation_index,exact_role_bearing_read_bindings,allowed_snapshot_scope,allowed_query/operator/disclosure_scope,result_answer_contract_ceiling,nonce,time_authority_profile_oid,not_before,expiry,signer_epoch,signature_or_mac_transcript}`; it has no write coordinate, mutation capability, or empty-effect convention. Each permit transcript covers every field, especially the time profile and complete closed-open window; use requires a matching fresh `TimeValidationEvidence::Usable` and linear guard. `AuthorizationLease` is the exact profiled signed consensus-domain/service-epoch/snapshot-range/read-binding/query-disclosure/answer-ceiling lease defined in §14.3, not an inferred extension. Rust exposes only verified nonconstructible wrappers.

`AuditCompletenessProfile` is `{profile_oid,schema_version,audit_domain_id,effective_audit_epoch,exact_operation_rules[AuditOperationTag -> Required|NotRequired],redaction_contract_oid,signer_set_epoch,signatures}`. `AuditRequirementDecisionRecord` is the same-group immutable `{profile_ref:StrongRef<AuditCompletenessProfile>,audit_domain_id,effective_audit_epoch,operation_tag,request_basis_commitment,policy_epoch,revocation_index,requirement:Required|NotRequired,evaluator_version}`. `AuditCoverageClaimRef` is the role-aware closed union `Local{claim_ref:StrongRef<LocalAuditTicketClaimRecord>}|Meta{claim_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicketClaimRecord>}` whose arm must match the containing domain. `NonRequiredAuditEvidence` is `ProfileExempt{decision_ref:StrongRef<AuditRequirementDecisionRecord>}|CoveredByParentClaim{claim_ref:AuditCoverageClaimRef,coverage_rule_id,covered_body_digest}|LifecycleScaffolding{decision_ref:StrongRef<AuditRequirementDecisionRecord>,registered_scaffolding_spec_tag,scaffolding_body_digest,parent_operation_claim_commitment?,compatibility_row_id}`. The LifecycleScaffolding arm is constructible only when the profile's exact operation rule says NotRequired for that internal registration/admission/freeze step and the generated row proves it cannot terminalize or expose the protected semantic operation; it cannot excuse a later commit, abort, read release, control mutation, or result publication. `LifecycleScaffoldingNotRequired` is the exact inline value `{evidence:NonRequiredAuditEvidence::LifecycleScaffolding}` rather than a magic enum literal. Every evidence form's decision/claim, operation tag, request/body basis, audit epoch, policy, and revocation state must match the containing object. `StructuralAuditExemption` is a generated inline singleton `{spec_tag,system_authority_class,compatibility_row_id}` constructible only for the exact registered recovery/audit/bootstrap tag; the associated type is uninhabited for every ordinary/user tag.

`AuthorizationAuditGate` is the same-group-only union `StructurallyInapplicable{exemption:StructuralAuditExemption}|NotRequired{evidence:NonRequiredAuditEvidence}|Required{ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>}`; an encoder may place Required only in an object whose consensus domain owns that ticket. `AuthorizationDecisionRecord` is the closed tag `Mutation{permit_ref:StrongRef<MutationPermitRecord>,permit_scope_digest,tenant,principal,final_effect_digest,write_and_hidden_cascade_commitment,policy_epoch,revocation_index,decision,authorization_audit_gate}` | `ReadAccess{access_admission_ref:StrongRef<ReadAccessAdmissionRecord>}` | `ReadRelease{release_decision_ref:StrongRef<ReadResultReleaseDecisionRecord>}` | `Lifecycle{lifecycle_decision_ref:StrongRef<LifecycleAuthorizationDecisionRecord>}` | `GlobalMutation{global_decision_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAuthorizationDecisionRecord>}`. The generated role matrix permits Mutation only in Local, GlobalMutation only in Meta, and ReadAccess/ReadRelease/Lifecycle only in the exact role/scope variant defined below.

`ImportedOperationAuditAdmissionEvidence` is the closed union `NotRequired{source_registration_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,registration_field_tag,evidence_projection:ImportedNonRequiredAuditEvidence}|Claimed{source_registration_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,registration_field_tag,ticket_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,claim_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,owner:AuditTicketOwner::Operation,request_basis_commitment}`. `ImportedStatementAuditAdmissionEvidence` is the distinct union `NotRequired{source_statement_registration_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,statement_field_tag,evidence_projection:ImportedNonRequiredAuditEvidence}|Claimed{source_statement_registration_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,statement_field_tag,ticket_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,claim_identity:RemoteObjectIdentity,owner:AuditTicketOwner::Statement,request_basis_commitment}`. `ImportedNonRequiredAuditEvidence` embeds the exact profile/decision or parent-claim projection, source field tag, audit epoch, policy/revocation, coverage rule, and signatures; it is not an opaque digest. `ImportedReadAuditEvidence` is exactly `TerminalAttempt{operation:ImportedOperationAuditAdmissionEvidence}|Statement{operation:ImportedOperationAuditAdmissionEvidence,statement:ImportedStatementAuditAdmissionEvidence}`. No generic Owner parameter or independent gate commitment exists.

Read authorization is split at the observation boundary. `ReadAccessCommon` is `{database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,service_visibility_epoch,tenant,principal,permit_scope_digest,registered_snapshot_and_workspace_scope,exact_read_graph_bindings,authority_projection_digest,descriptor_visibility_projection_ref:StrongRef<DescriptorVisibilityProjection>,policy_epoch,revocation_index,allowed_query_operator_disclosure_scope,result_answer_contract_ceiling,decision}`. `ReadAccessAdmissionRecord` is the closed posture/scope union `LocalTerminal{common:ReadAccessCommon,execution_scope:ReadExecutionScope::LocalTerminal,permit_ref:ReadCapablePermitRef,operation_audit:LocalOperationAuditAdmission::Claimed|NotRequired,audit_gate:AuthorizationAuditGate}|LocalStatement{common,execution_scope:ReadExecutionScope::LocalStatement,permit_ref:ReadCapablePermitRef,operation_audit:LocalOperationAuditAdmission::Claimed|NotRequired,statement_audit:LocalStatementAuditAdmission::Claimed|NotRequired,audit_gate:AuthorizationAuditGate}|MetaTerminal{common,execution_scope:ReadExecutionScope::MetaTerminal,permit_ref:ReadCapablePermitRef,operation_audit:OperationAuditAdmission::Claimed|NotRequired,audit_gate:AuthorizationAuditGate}|MetaStatement{common,execution_scope:ReadExecutionScope::MetaStatement,permit_ref:ReadCapablePermitRef,operation_audit:OperationAuditAdmission::Claimed|NotRequired,statement_audit:StatementAuditAdmission::Claimed|NotRequired,audit_gate:AuthorizationAuditGate}|ShardTerminal{common,execution_scope:ReadExecutionScope::ShardTerminal,permit:ImportedReadCapablePermitEvidence,operation_audit:ImportedOperationAuditAdmissionEvidence}|ShardStatement{common,execution_scope:ReadExecutionScope::ShardStatement,permit:ImportedReadCapablePermitEvidence,operation_audit:ImportedOperationAuditAdmissionEvidence,statement_audit:ImportedStatementAuditAdmissionEvidence}`. Scope refs and audit owners must byte-match; Local terminal and Local statement are not substitutable. The Shard gate is derived exactly from tagged imported admission and is not locally reissued. Only this admission can create `AuthorizedSnapshot`/secure-view cursors, and it contains no read witness, realized result, or result digest.

`ReadResultReleaseCommon` is `{access_admission_ref:StrongRef<ReadAccessAdmissionRecord>,read_routing_or_local_view_commitment,workspace_generation_and_overlay_commitment,read_witness_commitment,realized_result_answer_contract,disclosure_contract_digest,canonical_result_digest,release_decision}`. `ReadResultReleaseDecisionRecord` is the closed union `LocalTerminal{execution_scope:ReadExecutionScope::LocalTerminal,common:ReadResultReleaseCommon,operation_audit:LocalOperationAuditAdmission::Claimed|NotRequired,release_audit_gate:AuthorizationAuditGate}|LocalStatement{execution_scope:ReadExecutionScope::LocalStatement,common,operation_audit:LocalOperationAuditAdmission::Claimed|NotRequired,statement_audit:LocalStatementAuditAdmission::Claimed|NotRequired,release_audit_gate:AuthorizationAuditGate}|ShardTerminal{common,imported_audit:ImportedReadAuditEvidence::TerminalAttempt}|ShardStatement{common,imported_audit:ImportedReadAuditEvidence::Statement}`. `GlobalReadAuthorizationDecisionRecord` is the Meta release object `{execution_scope:ReadExecutionScope::MetaTerminal|MetaStatement,access_admission_ref:StrongRef<ReadAccessAdmissionRecord>,audit_evidence:MetaReadAuditEvidence,read_routing_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ReadParticipantRoutingCertificate>,sorted_shard_release_decision_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ReadResultReleaseDecisionRecord>],complete_shard_release_decision_commitment,workspace_and_witness_commitment,result_answer_contract,canonical_result_digest,decision,release_audit_gate:AuthorizationAuditGate}`. The exact order is permit/imported projection -> access admission -> authorized traversal into buffered bytes -> result-release decision -> event/resolution/terminal gate -> publication/read close -> external mirror -> output. A wrong Local Terminal/Statement owner, raw Meta permit/ticket/claim/registration/workspace ref in a shard object, wrong domain/configuration/grant/field tag/owner, swapped claim, access-after-result construction, or illegal scope cross-product is unencodable and has a negative golden fixture.

`LifecycleAuthorizationDecisionRecord` is the pre-result/no-effect form `{operation:RegisterAttempt|CancelActiveAttempt|PrepareAdmissionScaffolding|StatusOrMaintenance,authority_permit_ref:AuthorityPermitRef?,tenant,principal,authority_ceiling_digest,sequence_neutral_spec_body_digest,requested_snapshot_or_scope_commitment,no_effect_or_control_effect_class,operation_audit_admission_commitment?,policy_epoch,revocation_index,decision,authorization_audit_gate:AuthorizationAuditGate}`. RegisterAttempt uses Lifecycle bound to its permit/spec. PrepareAdmission uses `Lifecycle(PrepareAdmissionScaffolding)` with exact NotRequired proof, while its spec embeds the one GlobalMutation decision for complete effects. ReadClose uses GlobalRead; each shard basis uses its own Read decision. All registration/routing/workspace/witness/result/audit fields byte-match; a mutation decision or fabricated zero effect cannot substitute.

`TerminalAuditGate` is the same-group-only union `StructurallyInapplicable{exemption:StructuralAuditExemption}|NotRequired{evidence:NonRequiredAuditEvidence}|Required{ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,event_ref:StrongRef<AuditEventRecord>,terminal_resolution_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicketResolution>}`. A required gate is encodable only in the ticket-owning consensus domain and only when all three objects and the earlier authorization gate agree on namespace/domain/profile/principal/request; the resolution owns the event and its typed outcome matches the command/spec. The sole Local `TxnOutcomePreparationRecord` body is the PrepareAdmitted CAS schema in the Local transaction section; `Absent` and `Submitted` tags are unregistered. W12 exclusively uses the separate gate-free `GlobalTxnOutcomePreparationRecord`; no object is reinterpreted or wrapped as the other kind, and only the later `GlobalTxnCommand` carries W12's terminal gate. `DurableCapabilityVerifierKey {issuer_id,key_id,key_epoch,algorithm,public_or_protected_verifier_material,time_authority_profile_oid,not_before,verify_through,format_versions[],rotation_predecessor?,status}` is Chronicle-sequenced and strongly retained until no live capability can require it; retirement requires exact Expired evidence for its registered subject/action. Each capability uses the exact common header/body/MAC format, names this key, and is never reinterpreted across versions or visibility epochs.

`PrivacyContinuityRecord` is the external-and-mirrored `{ privacy_accounting_domain_id,privacy_epoch,cumulative_renyi_state_commitment,request_tombstone_root,predecessor_digest,external_registry_id,cas_version,status,issued_at,signer_set_epoch,threshold_signatures }`. `PrivacyLedgerState` canonically maps identity-level principals/aliases to composition state and debits, records the exact continuity head/receipt chain, and carries policy/mechanism epochs plus retention floor. `DpRequestKey` contains the stable privacy domain and request idempotency identity; cluster incarnation is provenance, not an accounting reset.

`DpRequestRecord` binds that canonical key, predecessor/state-transition digest, and exactly one state payload: `Prepared{no_sensitive_access,applied_control_ref:AppliedControlRef}`; `Abandoned{stable_reason,applied_control_ref:AppliedControlRef}`; `Charged{budget_debit,external_charge_receipt_ref:StrongRef,encrypted_seed_ref:StrongRef,applied_control_ref:AppliedControlRef}`; `Computing{same_charge_receipt_and_seed_refs,attempt_generation,no_output=true,applied_control_ref:AppliedControlRef}`; `ResultCommitted{same_charge_receipt_and_seed_refs,encrypted_result_ref:StrongRef,result_digest,applied_control_ref:AppliedControlRef}`; or `Delivered{budget_debit,external_charge_receipt_ref:StrongRef,encrypted_seed_ref:StrongRef,encrypted_result_ref:StrongRef,result_digest,delivery_receipt_digest,delivery_channel_class,applied_control_ref:AppliedControlRef}`. Each input is a sequence-neutral `DpTransitionSpec`; results cite the already known role-tagged command and sequence through `AppliedControlRef`. `DpRequestIndex` uniqueness-serializes the key and roots the latest record; seed/result/receipt refs and key wraps remain strong through the privacy/retry floor. Only `Prepared` can become `Abandoned`; no transition after external/local charge releases debit or exposes a data-dependent signal before `ResultCommitted`.

`AuditTicket` is `{database_security_namespace_id,audit_domain_id,cluster_incarnation_provenance,tenant,principal_scope,ticket_sequence,event_class,request_digest,completeness_profile_oid,issued_at,sequencer_epoch,signature}`. The sole `SequenceNeutralAuditEventBody`, `SequenceNeutralAuditResolutionBody`, semantic plan, and concrete attempt schemas are those in the audit construction contract above; Appendix A registers those exact body hashes and no duplicate inline body. Final `AuditEventRecord` is `{event_body_ref:StrongRef<SequenceNeutralAuditEventBody>,ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,terminal_plan_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalSigningPlan>,event_attempt_plan_ref:StrongRef<AuditEventSigningAttemptPlan>,canonical_signing_transcript_digest,event_lock_refs[StrongRef<AuditEventSignerLock>],event_signature_share_refs[StrongRef<AuditEventSignatureShare>],signer_subset_bitmap,threshold,canonical_aggregate_or_signature_set}`. The body owns the authorization/outcome/attested-time/stable-ticket facts; every repeated ticket/plan/digest field byte-matches it. Lock/share arrays are sorted by the concrete attempt's `(signer_id,signing_key_id,signer_set_epoch,key_epoch)` order and are an exact bijection. The signing transcript binds terminal plan ID, concrete attempt ID, event body digest, and signer identity/key/epochs. Transaction/control semantic basis excludes capsule/command/certificate identity, terminal gate, assigned sequence/HLC/marker/audit-chain position, and mutable external continuity head while still committing every stable effect/condition/security input. Mutation fixtures change each included field and each forbidden exclusion independently.

`AuditTicketResolution` is `{resolution_body_ref:StrongRef<SequenceNeutralAuditResolutionBody>,terminal_plan_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalSigningPlan>,resolution_attempt_plan_ref:StrongRef<AuditResolutionSigningAttemptPlan>,ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,terminal:Completed{event_ref:StrongRef<AuditEventRecord>}|Denied{event_ref:StrongRef<AuditEventRecord>}|Failed{event_ref:StrongRef<AuditEventRecord>}|Abandoned{event_ref:StrongRef<AuditEventRecord>,typed_no_effect_reason},canonical_signing_transcript_digest,resolution_lock_refs[StrongRef<AuditResolutionSignerLock>],resolution_signature_share_refs[StrongRef<AuditResolutionSignatureShare>],signer_subset_bitmap,threshold,canonical_aggregate_or_signature_set}`. The body/terminal/event/plan/attempt must agree exactly; lock/share arrays form the concrete resolution attempt's exact bijection. Attestation time comes only from the pre-order body and is not canonical logical HLC. Apply verifies the later command/result as the deterministic extension of stable committed bases. No final event/resolution body points back into a plan that already embeds it, so the durable strong graph remains acyclic.

`AuditOutcomeRecord` is constructed only by the exact Local/Meta mirror apply and is `{domain:{database_security_namespace_id,audit_domain_id,cluster_incarnation,group_role:Local|Meta},terminal_attempt_mirrored_ref:StrongRef<AuditTerminalAttemptRecord>,ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,event_ref:StrongRef<AuditEventRecord>,resolution_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicketResolution>,external_cas_receipt_ref:StrongRef<AuditExternalCasReceipt>,mirror_applied_ref:AppliedControlRef,candidate_state_identity:WeakStateIdentity,outcome_commitment}`. The attempt stage must be Mirrored under the same applied ref and own the exact plan/locks/triple/CAS predecessor chain. Construction is current mirror command -> Mirrored attempt stage -> AuditOutcomeRecord -> outcome/index/payload -> command record/root; no field points forward. Local/Global outcome audit state stores only this ref, never duplicate mirror identity/commitment fields.

`AuditContinuityRecord` is the external-and-mirrored `{database_security_namespace_id,audit_domain_id,audit_epoch,highest_ticket_sequence,ticket_index_commitment,unresolved_ticket_commitment,audit_chain_head_digest,predecessor_digest,external_registry_id,cas_version,status:Complete{profile_oid}|PermanentGap{latest_transition_ref:StrongRef<AuditCompletenessTransitionRecord>,current_profile_oid},last_transition:TicketIssued{ticket_digest}|TicketResolved{ticket_digest,resolution_digest,event_digest,candidate_root_digest:WeakDigest}|CompletenessChanged{transition_ref:StrongRef<AuditCompletenessTransitionRecord>},signer_set_epoch,threshold_signatures}`. The registry retains authenticated ticket/event/resolution/transition bytes or authenticated resolver refs. `AuditExternalCasReceipt` is built **after** the returned continuity record and binds `{external_registry_id,prior_head_digest,returned_head_digest,prior_cas_version,returned_cas_version,transition_kind,subject_digest,registry_signature_set}`; the continuity record never points forward to its receipt.

Exact `AuditTicketAdmissionSpec` is `{ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,expected_prior_continuity_ref:StrongRef<AuditContinuityRecord>,expected_prior_cas_version,returned_continuity_ref:StrongRef<AuditContinuityRecord>,external_cas_receipt_ref:StrongRef<AuditExternalCasReceipt>}`. Its validator requires the direct `TicketIssued` successor, exact sequence increment, exact addition to ticket/unresolved commitments, matching receipt subject and CAS versions, and no unrelated field change; recovery of an externally issued but not-yet-mirrored ticket runs this same idempotent validator. The only fence type/reference is the `AuditVisibilityFence`/`AuditVisibilityFenceRef` defined with `AuditFenceHeader` in the Raft contract; shard groups never originate one. Exact `AuditTerminalSpec` is `{ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,expected_pending_ticket_digest:WeakDigest,event_ref:StrongRef<AuditEventRecord>,terminal_resolution_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicketResolution>}`; it is the non-mutating/pre-effect terminal path and apply rejects any ticket/event/resolution scope or outcome mismatch. Transaction preparation and every state-changing control command carry the same exact triple through `TerminalAuditGate::Required`. Exact `AuditContinuityMirrorSpec` is `{active_fence_digest:WeakDigest,ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,candidate:AuditCandidateRef,terminal_resolution_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicketResolution>,expected_prior_continuity_ref:StrongRef<AuditContinuityRecord>,expected_prior_cas_version,returned_continuity_ref:StrongRef<AuditContinuityRecord>,external_cas_receipt_ref:StrongRef<AuditExternalCasReceipt>}`. Its validator requires the candidate role/group/blocked sequence/root to byte-match the active fence and the mirror command's `AppliedControlRef`, then enforces the complete equality/direct-successor relation in §12.8 before removing exactly that fence. `AuditCompletenessTransitionRecord` is created before its external CAS and is `{audit_domain_id,prior_continuity_ref:StrongRef<AuditContinuityRecord>,exact_missing_ticket_or_event_interval,missing_commitment,evidence_or_reason,old_profile_oid,new_profile_oid,permanent_effective_audit_epoch,authorization,signer_set_epoch,threshold_signatures}`. Exact `AuditCompletenessTransitionSpec` is `{transition_ref:StrongRef<AuditCompletenessTransitionRecord>,expected_prior_continuity_ref:StrongRef<AuditContinuityRecord>,expected_prior_cas_version,returned_continuity_ref:StrongRef<AuditContinuityRecord>,external_cas_receipt_ref:StrongRef<AuditExternalCasReceipt>}`; it validates the returned record as the direct `CompletenessChanged` successor for that transition and validates the receipt against both heads and CAS versions. Only that ordered transition may resume at the permanently weakened profile. Ticket admission, mirror, recovery, and completeness transition use `TerminalAuditGate::StructurallyInapplicable` under system-audit authority; terminal consumes the existing ticket.

`AuditCloneBoundary` is `{source_database_security_namespace_id,source_audit_domain_id,source_continuity_head_digest,target_database_security_namespace_id,target_audit_domain_id,clone_manifest_ref,retained_source_evidence_contract,source_signatures,target_signatures}` and never rewrites source tickets into the target domain. `AuditSegment` is a contiguous signed range with previous-chain digest, ticket/resolution ranges, event records, redaction profile, signing epoch, and external-anchor ref. `AuditTicketIndex` makes every issued ticket pending or uniquely resolved and retains its event, external receipt, and mirror status across recovery. `AuditCheckpoint` commits retained ticket/event floors and heads, unresolved-ticket set, continuity/gap heads, signer-rotation chain, and anchor. Missing external evidence disables completeness-gated operations; it never silently weakens the advertised profile.

**WitnessPolicy / TransparencyCheckpoint.** `WitnessPolicy` is `{format_version,log_id,security_domain_id,policy_epoch,claim_class:EquivocationDetection|NonEquivocation,ordered_witnesses[{witness_id,key_id,verification_key,endpoint_identity,optional_cross_log_authority}],n,threshold_t,byzantine_bound_f,signature_profile,consistency_proof_profile,durable_head_state_profile,anti_rollback_profile,authenticated_gossip_profile:None|Required{transport_auth_profile,peer_identity_registry,checkpoint_message_schema,replay_window,evidence_retention_floor,maximum_convergence_delay},activation_log_size,maximum_checkpoint_age,cross_log_policy:None|Required{ordered_authorities,threshold},rotation:Genesis|JointSuccessor{predecessor_policy_ref:StrongRef<WitnessPolicy>}}`. Canonical validation requires exactly `n` unique ordered witnesses, `0 <= f < t <= n`, supported signature/consistency/persistence profiles, and—before `claim_class=NonEquivocation` is usable—`2t > n + f`. A detection claim that relies on gossip requires the complete authenticated profile; an unnamed/best-effort channel proves nothing. Each honest witness durably stores `{log_id,security_domain_id,policy_oid,last_size,last_root,anti_rollback_counter}` before acknowledging a signature; it signs only a verified append-only consistency extension, never two roots at one size or non-extending histories. Rollback or loss of this state disables that witness until an authenticated recovery/rotation procedure; it cannot silently start fresh.

`TransparencyCrossLogReceipt` is `{authority_id,authority_key_id,source_log_id,source_security_domain_id,source_policy_ref:StrongRef<WitnessPolicy>,source_log_size,source_root,target_log_id,target_log_size,target_inclusion_commitment,target_inclusion_proof,observed_at,not_after,signature}`. `TransparencyCheckpoint` is `{format_version,mode:LocalRollbackDetection|WitnessedEquivocationDetection{witness_policy_ref:StrongRef<WitnessPolicy>}|WitnessedNonEquivocation{witness_policy_ref:StrongRef<WitnessPolicy>},log_size,global_mmr_root,branch_head_commitment_root,security_domain_commitment,previous_checkpoint_digest:WeakDigest,consistency_proof_from_previous,issued_at,operator_key_id,operator_signature,sorted_witness_signatures[{witness_id,key_id,signature}],cross_log_receipt_refs[StrongRef<TransparencyCrossLogReceipt>],rotation_proof:None|JointActivation{old_policy_ref:StrongRef<WitnessPolicy>,new_policy_ref:StrongRef<WitnessPolicy>,old_sorted_signatures[],new_sorted_signatures[]}}`. Every signature covers the domain-separated canonical checkpoint body excluding all signature arrays. A witnessed mode requires its policy identity, freshness, threshold of distinct configured keys, and any required cross-log receipts.

Canonical cross-log validation requires `1 <= cross_log_policy.threshold <= count(unique ordered authorities)`; at least that many receipts come from distinct configured authority/key pairs, and every accepted receipt's source policy/log/security domain/size/root equals the current checkpoint's policy/log/domain/`log_size`/global root commitment exactly. Its target inclusion proof must verify under the named target log/size, `observed_at <= issued_at <= not_after`, and age must satisfy both policies; duplicates, foreign source roots, stale inclusions, or self-asserted target sizes fail. `JointActivation` additionally requires: the old policy equals the currently active policy; `new.rotation == JointSuccessor{predecessor=old}`; old/new log and security-domain identities are equal; `new.policy_epoch > old.policy_epoch`; checkpoint mode names the new policy; `log_size >= new.activation_log_size`; and the checkpoint body has valid distinct-key thresholds under both old and new policies. Only after that exact activation checkpoint may successors use the new policy alone.

The branch commitment is domain-separated and reveals no plain branch identity/head; authorized clients receive scoped inclusion/consistency proofs under the metadata-declassification policy, and mutually hidden branch sets use distinct security-domain logs. `LocalRollbackDetection` proves only consistency relative to a client's cached head. `WitnessedEquivocationDetection` promises durable evidence once conflicting heads reach the declared gossip/cross-log path. Only `WitnessedNonEquivocation` with a valid intersection-safe policy, honest durable-head assumption, consistency proofs, joint rotation, and freshness may claim split-view prevention. If any premise fails, verification fails closed or downgrades the advertised claim to detection/local scope; later gossip is never relabeled as prevention. **PolicyEpoch** is `{ policy_id,version,scope,logical_effect_class,pinned_table_oid,fallback_oid,evidence_refs[],previous_epoch_oid }`; statistical evidence may justify promotion but is never encoded as an invariant.

## Appendix B — Graph Intent Log (the semantic vocabulary)

Intents are deterministic commands captured at statement execution; they are **not** committed effects or Ripple deltas. `IntentElementRef` is the closed union `Existing{database_security_namespace_id,graph,vid_or_eid}|EscapedAllocation{binding_ref:StrongRef<EscapingAllocationReservationRecord>,slot_key,permanent_value}|StatementLocal{tmp_ref_ordinal}`. `StatementLocal` can appear only within one `GraphIntentBatch` and cannot enter result bytes, a later statement, procedure/UDF output, provenance/audit, a durable witness, or a committed effect. First escape uses §4.5's ordered reservation and all subsequent intents use the EscapedAllocation arm. `IntentCoordinateRef` is exactly `{binding_role_id,coordinate:CoordinateSchemaBinding,write_basis:WeakMarkerIdentity}`; no raw graph/branch name, run locator, or untyped reference is legal.

`CapturedIntentObservation` is the generated closed union of exact value/CAS, element-version, key absence/range gap, adjacency/degree, valid-time range, constraint, escrow, and procedure-output observations. Every arm names its coordinate role, schema/contract epoch, witness ref, disclosure class, and deterministic recomputation rule. `GraphIntent` is `{intent_ordinal,intent_semantics_oid,read_coordinate_roles[],write_coordinate_refs[],policy_epoch,revocation_index,captured_observation_refs[CapturedIntentObservationRef],structural_effect_class,operation:GraphIntentOperation}`. `GraphIntentBatch` is the independently addressable per-statement object `{registration_identity,statement_seq,canonical_statement_classification_ref:StrongRef<CanonicalStatementClassification>,intent_semantics_ref:StrongRef<IntentSemantics>,prior_workspace_generation_identity,sorted_intents,escaped_allocation_binding_root_ref:StrongRef<TxnAllocationBindingRoot>,statement_observation_commitment,resource_bounds,body_digest}`. Ordinals are contiguous, arrays and maps have registered size/depth/string/value limits, and the batch's semantics/coordinate/policy values must match every child. Registration owns no future batch. `LocalStatementPublicationSpec`/`GlobalStatementPublicationSpec` must name the already-built exact batch, prior/successor workspace and cumulative roots, and the Published successor plus successor workspace/cumulative root strongly own it. A statement abort proves no batch exists or retains one exact failed diagnostic batch under its registered retention policy. Every shard workspace delta/certificate binds its routed batch projection and complete batch digest. Prepare proves a gap-free bijection between published statements, batches, workspace effects, observations, and cumulative roots; DAG and substitution tests reject a registration-to-future-batch edge, missing/extra batch, or reused certificate from another batch.

```
CreateVertex   { new_ref, label_set, props, valid_time_assignment }
DeleteVertex   { target, expected_version, cascade_policy }
AddLabel/RemoveLabel { vid, label }
AddEdge        { new_ref, src, etype, dst, requested_key?, props, valid_time_assignment }
RemoveEdge     { target, expected_version }
SetProp        { elem, name, value, merge_policy_id }
RemoveProp     { elem, name }
EnsureEdge     { src, etype, dst, constraint_id, props }
CompareAndSet  { elem, name, expected, value, mismatch: NoOp|StatementError|TxnAbort }
SetInsert      { elem, name, element, set_epoch }
SetRemove      { elem, name, element, observed_tags_or_remove_policy }
SetValidTime   { elem, contract_id, expected:Any|Exact(ValidTimeAssignment),
                 replacement:ValidTimeAssignment,
                 mismatch:NoOp|StatementError|TxnAbort }
AdjustCounter  { elem, property, delta,
                 algebra:ExactAdd|Escrow{constraint_id,domain_epoch},
                 operation_key, overflow:Reject }
SketchUpdate   { elem_or_relation, sketch_profile_oid, operation_key,
                 canonical_input, exact_delete_token? }
AssertSameAs   { a, b, confidence, source } // canonical sugar for AddEdge(SAME_AS)
BulkLoad       { logical_batch_ref:StrongRef<CanonicalBulkLogicalBatch>,
                 source_digest, row_count,
                 optional_staged_run_refs[ConditionalCoordinateRef] }
SchemaOp       { canonical_schema_operation } // ordinary transactional intent/effect
```

`CanonicalBulkLogicalBatch` contains bounded canonical logical rows with explicit operation tag, coordinate role, element/key/value/valid-time/provenance fields, row ordinal, source-row digest, and batch digest. Staged runs are optional accelerators checked against that batch; no effect is inferred from physical run bytes. `AssertSameAs` creates an ordinary protected `SAME_AS` edge with stable EId, endpoints, properties, valid time, and provenance; there is no second entity-resolution mutation mechanism. Catalog graph/branch aliases and all branchable schema/constraint/index definitions use ordinary `SchemaOp` transaction effects and the same marker/head/authorization/SSI path. Database-global topology, security policy, key, configuration, physical index-build progress, and derived-generation activation remain typed control commands, not `SchemaOp`.

LWW policies use canonical `EffectOrder { commit_seq, intent_ordinal, merge_ordinal, effect_ordinal }`, never element birth or an ambient wall clock. `ExactAdd` is checked integer/fixed-decimal addition identified by a registered algebra profile; raw addition is not idempotent, so ACI merge operates on the set-union of unique operation keys followed by deterministic checked summation. Escrow uses §4.7's custody ledger. Every sketch profile fixes its merge/delete algebra, precision/error contract, canonical state, duplicate-operation behavior, and fallback; a sketch without exact deletion either rejects delete/update workloads or rebuilds, and never becomes authoritative constraint state. Generic SetProp/RemoveProp against counter/escrow/sketch-governed state is invalid unless the binder rewrites it into the registered typed operation with captured-before/CAS semantics. `ConsistencyClass` is derived only after composing intent semantics, captured observations, active constraints, rights/authority, and branch policy. Commutativity tables are caches of proved contextual results.

`StatementObservationCommitment` covers the exact canonical published result bytes or NoResult proof, escaped identities/generated values, error class, workspace successor, and every read/constraint/rights observation visible to later statements. Rebase may freely regenerate an unpublished autocommit terminal result, but it may not alter any prior published statement commitment. If re-evaluation would change one byte, identity, row order, error/no-op choice, valid period, or workspace-visible effect, the explicit transaction fails with a serialization/retry outcome rather than silently committing a history the client did not observe.

Finalization evaluates all commands and emits only canonical effects:

```text
CreateVertexEffect { permanent_vid, allocation_binding_or_finalization_proof,
                     birth_ordinal, labels, canonical_props, valid_time_assignment }
DeleteVertexEffect { vid, complete_before_version, retirement_basis,
                     sorted_retired_incident_edge_before_images[],
                     sorted_constraint/temporal/escrow_contribution_retractions[] }
LabelMembershipEffect { vid, label, before, after }
CreateEdgeEffect { permanent_eid, allocation_binding_or_finalization_proof,
                   birth_ordinal, src, type, dst, canonical_key?, props,
                   valid_time_assignment }
DeleteEdgeEffect { eid, complete_before_version, retirement_basis,
                   sorted_constraint/temporal/escrow_contribution_retractions[] }
PropertyEffect { elem, property, before, after }
ValidTimeEffect { elem, contract_id, before, after, before_version_identity,
                  temporal_constraint_transition_refs[], witness_basis }
CounterEffect { operation_key, elem, property, algebra_profile,
                delta, before, after, overflow:Reject }
EscrowAdjustmentEffect { domain_id, epoch, operation_key, contribution_key?,
                         elem_property_or_cardinality_subject, delta,
                         before_value, after_value, consumed_reservation_refs[],
                         produced_right_kind_and_amount, target_owner,
                         conservation_basis_digest }
SketchEffect { operation_key, sketch_profile_oid, before_state_digest,
               after_state_ref, realized_answer_contract }
SchemaEffect { transition:CoordinateSchemaTransition,
               canonical_catalog_schema_constraint_index_operations[] }
ConstraintStateEffect { apply_basis, before_schema_root, before_schema_epoch,
                        after_schema_root, after_schema_epoch,
                        before_constraint_root, after_constraint_root,
                        exact_removed_and_added_contributions[] }
ResourceChargeEffect { reservation_id, scope, before_charge, after_charge, reason }
```

Every effect carries `EffectProvenance {source_batch_ref:StrongRef<GraphIntentBatch>,source_intent_ordinal,source_statement_seq,source_coordinate_role,source_observation_commitment,merge_or_import_origin?,authorization_decision_digest,canonicalization_profile_oid}`. `CoordinateEffectEnvelope {coordinate:WriteCoordinateBinding,effect_ordinal,effect,provenance}` is the sole coordinate source, so nested effects cannot disagree. `GlobalEffectEnvelope` is the closed union `Resource{transition_ref,effect}|Audit{ticket_and_event_commitment}|AuthorityGlobalEscrow{domain_id,operation_summary_ref,effect}`; a coordinate effect cannot smuggle a global charge and a global effect cannot mutate graph state. Resource reservation/charge/release ownership and audit ticket/event ownership are typed strong refs, never bare IDs or an English “handled elsewhere” promise.

`NetEffectNormalForm` groups by coordinate and logical identity/key, cancels only inverse effects proved unobserved and algebraically cancellable, preserves create/delete before-images and all unique operation keys, sorts cascades/contributions canonically, and rejects two incompatible terminal values. It includes a proof mapping every source intent to its surviving effects or an explicit `NoOp{captured_basis,policy}`; no intent disappears implicitly. `CommittedEffectSet` is `{intent_semantics_ref,ordered_source_batch_refs[],statement_observation_commitments[],net_effect_normal_form_ref,coordinate_effect_envelopes[],global_effect_envelopes[],complete_allocation_binding_commitment,constraint_temporal_escrow_evidence,authorization_decision_ref,resource_transition_refs,audit_ownership_commitment,body_digest}`. It has explicit before/after semantics, permanent IDs/BirthOrdinals, branch-aware retirement bases, full cascade before-images, and no conditional operation.

The sequence-neutral graph/branch/relation/schema/intent-semantics-keyed `LogicalDeltaTemplate` is derived from that normal form and differential-tested against applying the gap-free ordered batches once under the pinned `IntentSemanticsOid` to the recorded basis. Create/delete/property/valid-time/counter/escrow/sketch/schema/constraint deltas are exact typed rows; only the committed `MarkerRef` turns the template into an ordered `LogicalDeltaBatch`. Fuzz/model tests delete or duplicate intents/effects/provenance/observations, reorder bulk rows/cascades, force no-op/CAS drift, replay operation keys, expose IDs then rebase/abort, and compare batch application, workspace state, reference finalization, normal form, committed effects, and integrated deltas byte-for-byte.

## Appendix C — GLA Operator Inventory (executor contracts)

Every physical implementation registers input/output factorization, strict/relaxed determinism, minimum resident set and spill algorithm, maximum work between cancellation checkpoints, incremental derivative or `none`, witness domain, authorization boundary, path preservation, input/output `AnswerContract` transfer or rejection, and legal `ReplanClass`. “Propagate” below means retain the complete upstream approximation provenance and apply a registered sound transformation; it never means relabel approximate data as exact. The initial normative matrix is:

| Family | Memory / spill | Incremental contract | Replan / witness contract | Answer-contract rule |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `ScanVertices/ScanEdges/Values` | bounded cursor; external batch buffers | linear derivative | partition boundary; label/type/range/gap witness | exact base cursor/value input emits `Exact` |
| `IndexProbe{btree,hash,fts,vector,path}` | bounded cursor plus candidate heap; exact tail path may spill | registered per index | before output unless continuation proved; generation/range/gap/watermark witness | emit the pinned generation contract; `Exact` requires exact index+tail completion |
| `HybridSearch` | spillable per-source candidate runs, fusion heap, rerank and expansion frontier | registered only for a complete fusion/expansion derivative; otherwise recompute | before output or a fully materialized candidate/fusion boundary; all source-generation, tail, candidate, fusion, authorization, and expansion witnesses | compose every source/stage; `Exact` only through complete exact sources or pinned exact fallback, otherwise emit fully qualified `Approximate` |
| `Expand/VarLengthExpand` | bounded descriptor cursor; factorized/path history spill | bounded-hop derivative only where registered | descriptor or checkpointed path frontier; adjacency ranges and path cuts | exact adjacency preserves `Exact`; approximate seed/input coverage propagates under a registered law |
| `PathFind` | spillable frontier, history sets, path DAG | registered mode/selector subsets only | no switch after emission without state transfer; full mode-aware witness | `Exact` requires exact graph/input and complete algorithm; approximation needs a selector-specific bound/recall law |
| `FreeJoin/HashJoin` | radix/grace partitions; partitioned COLT | bilinear/custom derivative | build/materialization barrier or verified state transfer; all input predicate witnesses | all-exact inputs yield `Exact`; any approximate input requires a registered join error/completeness transform |
| `LeftOuter/Semi/Anti/Apply/NullExtend` | spillable correlation/match state | custom or recompute | materialization boundary; absence and correlated-domain witnesses mandatory | absence-sensitive forms require exact negative domains for `Exact`; otherwise a registered approximation law or rejection |
| `Select/Project/Unnest/Flatten` | vector-bounded; flatten spillable | linear where expression is registered | batch boundary; preserve or explicitly transform factorization/path/witness laws | deterministic total transforms preserve `Exact`; approximate provenance is transformed, never erased |
| `Aggregate/Distinct` | radix-partitioned retained state | registered algebra with deletion law | completed partition or state transfer; group-domain and multiplicity witness | `Exact` only from exact complete inputs; approximation requires a registered estimator/error algebra |
| `OrderBy/Limit{offset,count}` | top-k heap or external stable merge sort | top-k custom; full sort normally recompute | no switch after emitted prefix; order/tie and early-stop gap witnesses | exact ordered prefix requires exact gap/completeness proof; approximate top-k carries recall/error and population |
| `SetOp{Union,Intersect,Except}` | partition-spillable multiplicity state | registered per ALL/DISTINCT form | materialization boundary; negative/right-side domains where applicable | all-exact inputs yield `Exact`; approximate difference/intersection requires a sound registered law |
| `Fixpoint` | LSM-backed arrangements and iteration spill | validated SCC only | iteration barrier; termination and recursive-domain witness | `Exact` requires exact seed/relations and convergence; approximate recursion is unavailable unless separately registered |
| `TemporalSlice/TemporalJoin` | interval-partition spill | registered interval algebra | interval boundary; system/valid-time ranges and gaps | preserves `Exact` only with complete temporal coverage; otherwise propagates qualified interval approximation |
| `SemiringMxV` | sparse/dense frontier spill | registered annotation algebra | iteration/frontier barrier; projection/capability/path semantics pinned | exact algebra+inputs yield `Exact`; numeric/coverage approximation requires its registered bound |
| `ProcedureCall` | declared per procedure; otherwise reject | none unless explicitly registered | none by default; authorized view only; external nondeterminism badge as required | signature independently declares answer-contract transfer and replay-input capture; external/nondeterministic execution may still be semantically exact but downgrades replay completeness, while an approximate procedure remains approximate even if perfectly replayable |
| `GraphConstruct` | spillable canonical key/value and path/provenance runs; generation-local dense ordinals allowed | registered pure construction derivative with deletion/multiplicity law | batch/materialization boundary; complete source/provenance witnesses and canonical `ViewElementRef` identity | pure deterministic construction preserves/propagates its inputs; it has no proposal or commit side effect |
| `Mutate` | proposal-local buffered intents/effects | emits canonical logical delta only after successful commit | never replanned after side-effect ordering; complete read/write/constraint/authorization witness | consumes `Exact` only; approximate data cannot authorize a mutation target/effect |
| `ViewDelta/CertEmit` | bounded envelope plus spillable forensic detail | stream tap | no semantic replan; watermark/evidence closure must remain exact | preserves and serializes the full input/output contract without upgrading it |

Any operator without a complete row, a total answer-contract rule, and conformance tests is unavailable, not implicitly “bounded.” Strict flatten/factorization, spill/no-spill, compaction, and legal replan variants are metamorphically required to produce identical canonical results **within the same answer contract and pinned approximate generation closure**. A transition that changes approximate candidates/topology is a new semantic generation, not an equivalent physical variant.

## Appendix D — FGP Protocol Contract
Connection state is exactly `TransportEstablished -> VersionNegotiated -> Authenticated{AuthContext} -> Ready{ReadyBinding} -> Draining -> Closed`. `DatabasePosture` is exactly `Local|Sharded`. `HELLO/HELLO_ACK` negotiate protocol mechanics only; they contain no database selector, namespace, incarnation, service epoch, posture, promotion receipt, topology, existence signal, or database-specific limit. `AUTH/AUTH_OK` establish a transport-authenticated principal and immutable session binding. `SELECT_DATABASE/READY` then select one authorized database and independently reread its current Operational role root, continuity state, service-promotion receipt when required, and catalog entry. Nonexistent and unauthorized selectors have the same authenticated failure surface. Changing database, posture, incarnation, service epoch, or promotion receipt drains the Ready binding and requires a fresh selection; it is never an in-band refresh.

The three headers are distinct. `TransportHeader={frame_len,protocol_version,frame_type,flags,request_id,stream_id}` is used through AUTH. `SessionHeader=TransportHeader+{session_binding,auth_context_generation}` is legal after AUTH_OK. `ReadyHeader=SessionHeader+{database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,service_visibility_epoch,database_posture,promotion_receipt_digest_or_direct_authority_commitment}` is mandatory for database work. A stale, mixed, or missing binding fails before allocation, routing, authorization, schema/status/error disclosure, or timing-distinct lookup. `session_binding` is derived from the completed HELLO/HELLO_ACK/AUTH transcript and a server secret before AUTH_OK is encoded; no frame hashes itself.

`AUTH_REFRESH/AUTH_REFRESHED` is a self-transition in Authenticated or Ready. It cannot change the selected database or ReadyBinding and cannot widen beyond the original non-widenable ceiling. New authority applies only to subsequently created children; narrowing or revocation fences every unsent protected byte of existing children while an already admitted semantic decision still completes under its durable rules. A posture or service-epoch change forces Draining and fresh selection/authentication.

Ready owns typed children. A transaction child is `Idle -> BeginStaging -> Begun{StatementIdle} -> Closing{ReadClose|WritePrepare|Rollback} -> Terminal -> Idle`. A statement or terminal-result child is `Accepted -> Bound -> Registering -> Registered -> Executing -> Buffered -> PublicationSubmitted -> Visible{NotRequired} -> Streaming -> AwaitingAck -> Completed` or `... -> PublicationSubmitted -> AuditFenced -> Visible{RequiredMirrored} -> Streaming -> AwaitingAck -> Completed`. Subscriptions, exports, replay retrievals, replay execution results, and protected errors use the same `Buffered -> PublicationSubmitted -> Visible|AuditFenced -> Visible -> Streaming/Terminal` release submachine. Draining creates no child and closes only after required mirrors, result/cursor releases, active cancellation, admitted-decision recovery, and terminal records are durable.

Every role-sensitive public identity is a closed opaque posture union: begin reservation, attempt, statement registration/publication, result owner, snapshot, marker outcome, logical position, delivery position, cancellation lineage, and audit release. A client never receives a Local ObjectId, Meta/shard reference, raw Raft index, or untagged integer from which posture must be inferred.

`AuditReleaseEvidence` is exactly `NotRequired{release_subject_commitment,nonrequired_evidence_projection,visibility:Opaque{visibility_commitment}|Declassified{authorized_position_projection,declassification_decision_digest}}|RequiredMirrored{release_subject_commitment,audit_outcome_commitment,visibility:Opaque{visibility_commitment}|Declassified{authorized_position_projection,declassification_decision_digest}}`. It contains no nullable fields, raw ticket/event/root references, or default logical/commit/audit positions; a raw position is legal only in the explicit authorized declassification arm. `ReadReleaseAuthorizationEvidence` is `{posture,release_subject_commitment,result_or_output_digest,release_decision_commitment,non_widenable_authority_digest,disclosure_contract_digest,policy_epoch,revocation_index}` and is the portable projection of the exact Local/Global release decision.

The socket-write boundary uses two nested linear guards without holding an ordinary lock across `await`. `FrameSubjectVersion` is the closed union `Delivery{delivery_id,state_version}|Cursor{resume_cursor_id,state_version}|TxnOutcome{capability_commitment,outcome_generation}|MergeOutcome{capability_commitment,outcome_generation}|AuditReceipt{audit_subject_handle,state_version}|ProtectedError{error_delivery_id,state_version}|None{registered_frame_class}`; a generated matrix assigns exactly one arm to every protected frame class. `AuthGenerationUseGuard {ready_binding,session_binding,auth_context_generation,effective_non_widenable_authority_digest,policy_epoch,revocation_index,release_subject_commitment,intended_frame_digest_or_range}` is acquired while linearizing against the session authority generation and proves that generation still covers the release subject.

`PublicFrameSendGuard` is the closed union `DataOutput{read_release_authorization_digest,audit_release_digest}|CapabilityTerminalOutcome{validated_capability_commitment,terminal_projection_authorization_digest,audit_release_digest}|PendingOutcomeStatus{validated_outcome_capability_commitment,opaque_status_projection_digest}|AuditReceiptStatus{audit_subject_handle_commitment,current_scoped_audit_authority_digest,receipt_status_projection_digest}|ProtectedError{error_delivery_authorization_digest,audit_release_digest}` plus common `{auth_generation_use_guard,ready_binding,session_binding,stream_id,frame_subject_version:FrameSubjectVersion,exact_frame_class_and_digest_or_byte_range,fresh_time_use_guard}`. `DataOutput` releases result/baseline/delta/export/replay/proof bytes. `CapabilityTerminalOutcome` alone emits `NeverRegistered`, `TerminalPendingAuditVisible`, `TerminalReady`, or `MERGE_STATUS_RESULT::{Committed,Rejected}` after the exact audit-visible terminal authorization. `PendingOutcomeStatus` alone emits `BeginStaging`, `InProgress`, `FinalizingOpaque`, `MERGE_STATUS_RESULT::InFlight`, `TokenNotYetValid`, `TokenExpired`, `TimeAuthorityUnavailable`, or `NotVisibleOrUnknown`; none may encode a semantic terminal kind. `AuditReceiptStatus` emits only its authorized receipt projection, and `ProtectedError` uses its bounded owner lifecycle. The generated public-frame-class matrix assigns every protected frame or byte range to exactly one arm and rejects aliases or wildcard classes. `OutputSendGuard` is the legacy alias for `DataOutput`, not a generic escape hatch.

Guard consumption atomically copies the exact authenticated frame bytes into a bounded `TransportSendObligation {session_binding,auth_context_generation,frame_subject_version,frame_digest,encoded_len,state:Queued|Writing{bytes_written}|Sent|CancelledBeforeWrite|Failed{bytes_written,transport_poisoned:true}}` under the generation transition, then releases the authority latch before socket I/O. `Sent` means the complete authenticated frame was accepted by the transport; any write failure, including a zero-byte failure, selects `Failed`, permanently poisons that connection, and forces close without an `AUTH_REFRESHED` or later application frame. A peer can accept only a complete frame, so a partial prefix is never application-visible; the independently retained delivery/result/proof owner remains resumable on a fresh connection from its canonical boundary. A narrowing/revoking refresh cancels every still-`Queued` old-generation obligation and waits for every `Writing` obligation to become `Sent` or `Failed`; it emits `AUTH_REFRESHED(new_generation)` only if all such obligations reached `Sent` and the transport remains usable, otherwise it closes. Drain/close performs the same join. Backpressure cannot retain unbounded obligations because queue bytes were reserved and capped before guard creation. Refresh/revocation, epoch/receipt drift, subject-version change, ACK/release, audit mismatch, or generation change before queue admission discards the frame. No guard is serialized or retained as durable evidence. DPOR tests block and fail the socket while interleaving refresh/revocation/drain at guard acquisition, byte-copy, queue admission, write start, every partial-write boundary, completion, and reconnect/resume.

`ResumeCapabilityBody` is the closed union `SubscriptionCursor{resume_cursor_id,cursor_state_version,capability_generation,lineage,derived_identity_digest,baseline_id,public_state_commitment}|BufferedResult{posture,owner_commitment,result_delivery_id,lease_generation,retention_state_version,capability_generation,lineage,canonical_result_digest,state_hint:PendingVisibilityOpaque|ActiveDeliverable|Acknowledged{ack_commitment}|ReleasedUnacked{release_commitment}}`. It uses the common profiled `DurableCapabilityHeader`. The independent index, not the hint, is authoritative; PendingVisibility returns no semantic/result disclosure. Current or immediate-predecessor retry returns the same pre-minted successor or consumption proof; older generations fail capability-safely. Neither arm exposes internal commit provenance or retains bytes by itself.

`ExecutionScope` is `Autocommit{autocommit_idempotency_key,operation_class:ReadOnly|ReadWrite,statement_class:ReadOnly|WriteReturning|WriteNoResult,isolation,transaction_error_policy,default_snapshot_selector}|Transaction{txn_handle,statement_seq,statement_idempotency_key,statement_class,expected_prior_statement_frontier,expected_workspace_generation}`. Before autocommit work, Local or Meta orders the exact reservation/registration mapping from scoped client key and canonical request digest to one `TxnOutcomeCapabilityFields`, attempt, and eventual result capability. `EXECUTE_ACCEPTED` is emitted before result/outcome frames. Exact retry joins; any query/template, parameter, authority, posture, epoch, snapshot, or option drift fails.

For `Autocommit{ReadWrite,WriteReturning}`, the buffered manifest owner is the distinct posture-valid `AutocommitWriteTerminal`. Prepared ownership retains it through prepare/commit/audit. No streamable result lease exists until the semantic commit is TerminalReady, the required terminal audit is mirrored, the Local/Global delta and durability postconditions are satisfied, and an exact independently retained delivery lease is installed. Commit completion never waits for client ACK; ACK/release only discharges that independent result promise.

Normative frame families:

```text
HELLO{versions,features,client_nonce,transport_limits,concurrency_profiles}
HELLO_ACK{version,features,server_nonce,transport_limits,concurrency_profile,transcript_binding}
AUTH{token,channel_binding,transcript_binding,requested_authority_ceiling}
AUTH_OK{session_binding,auth_context_generation,principal_binding,
        non_widenable_authority_digest,policy_epoch,revocation_index,
        time_authority_profile_oid,auth_not_before,auth_expiry}
SELECT_DATABASE{database_selector,expected_posture?}
READY{auth_context_generation,database_posture,operational_role_identity,
      cluster_incarnation,service_visibility_epoch,service_authority_commitment,
      ready_binding_digest,database_limits,concurrency_profile}
AUTH_REFRESH{token,channel_binding,expected_auth_context_generation}
AUTH_REFRESHED{auth_context_generation,non_widenable_authority_digest,
               policy_epoch,revocation_index,time_authority_profile_oid,
               auth_not_before,auth_expiry,
               existing_child_effect:NewWorkOnly|NarrowedUnsentOutputFenced}

BEGIN{begin_idempotency_key,operation_class,isolation,transaction_error_policy,
      write_coordinates,default_snapshot_selector,read_your_writes_capability?,resource_request}
BEGIN_ACCEPTED{posture,reservation_identity,txn_outcome_capability,
               begin_request_digest,service_visibility_epoch}
BEGUN{posture,txn_handle,registration_identity,txn_outcome_capability,
      registered_snapshot,workspace_generation,next_statement_seq,transaction_error_policy}
BEGIN_OUTCOME{txn_outcome_capability,state:
    BeginStaging{posture,staging_generation}
  | NeverRegistered{posture,proof_source:Detailed|Compacted,reason_class,
                    original_response_commitment}}

PREPARE{text,language_contract_oid}
PREPARED{stmt_id,param_schema,prepared_template_digest,compatibility_contracts}
EXECUTE{scope:ExecutionScope,stmt_id,params,consistency,read_your_writes_capability?,
        determinism,answer_requirement,fetch,resource_request}
EXECUTE_TEXT{scope:ExecutionScope,text,language_contract_oid,params,consistency,
             read_your_writes_capability?,determinism,answer_requirement,fetch,resource_request}
EXECUTE_ACCEPTED{scope:
    Autocommit{posture,registration_identity,txn_outcome_capability,canonical_request_digest}
  | Transaction{posture,statement_registration_identity,canonical_request_digest}}

RESULT_BEGIN{result_delivery_id,delivery_state_version,owner:PostureResultOwner,
             result_resume_capability,read_release_authorization:ReadReleaseAuthorizationEvidence,
             audit_release:AuditReleaseEvidence,schema,result_answer_contract,
             canonical_encoding_version,canonical_result_digest,total_chunks,total_len,
             replay_manifest_projection?}
RESULT_CHUNK{result_delivery_id,delivery_state_version,canonical_result_digest,
             chunk_ordinal,chunk_count,canonical_offset,chunk_digest,payload}
RESULT_END{result_delivery_id,delivery_state_version,canonical_result_digest,
           effective_snapshot:PostureSnapshotIdentity}
RESULT_RESUME{resume_capability,replay_from:Beginning|AfterCompleteChunk{chunk_ordinal,chunk_digest}}
RESULT_RESUMED{rotated_resume_capability,result_delivery_id,delivery_state_version,
               accepted_replay_from_chunk,canonical_result_digest,total_chunks}
RESULT_ACK{resume_capability,result_delivery_id,expected_delivery_state_version,
           canonical_result_digest,complete_result_end_transcript_digest,client_ack_nonce}
RESULT_ACKED{result_delivery_id,delivery_state_version,
             capability_disposition:Rotated{resume_capability}|Consumed{consumption_proof}}

ROLLBACK{txn_handle,expected_statement_frontier,expected_delivery_terminal_frontier,
         expected_workspace_generation}
COMMIT{txn_handle,expected_statement_frontier,expected_delivery_terminal_frontier,
       expected_workspace_generation}
TXN_OUTCOME{txn_outcome_capability,outcome:TerminalPublicOutcome,
            semantic_descriptor:SemanticTerminalDescriptor,audit_release:AuditReleaseEvidence,
            result_resume:None|Issued{resume_capability},
            read_your_writes:NotRequested|Issued{read_your_writes_capability}}
TXN_STATUS{txn_outcome_capability}
TXN_STATUS_RESULT{status:
    BeginStaging{posture,staging_generation}
  | NeverRegistered{posture,proof_source:Detailed|Compacted,reason_class}
  | InProgress{posture,phase,statement_frontier,delivery_frontier,workspace_generation}
  | FinalizingOpaque{posture,last_audit_visible_phase,required_stage_class_bitmap,
                     satisfied_stage_class_bitmap}
  | TerminalPendingAuditVisible{posture,
                    required_postcondition_bitmap,satisfied_postcondition_bitmap,
                    semantic_descriptor:SemanticTerminalDescriptor}
  | TerminalReady{public_outcome:TerminalPublicOutcome,
                  semantic_descriptor:SemanticTerminalDescriptor,
                  proof_source:Detailed|Compacted,
                  result_resume_capability?,
                  read_your_writes:NotRequested|Issued{read_your_writes_capability},
                  audit_release:AuditReleaseEvidence}
  | TokenNotYetValid | TokenExpired | TimeAuthorityUnavailable | NotVisibleOrUnknown}

READ_YOUR_WRITES_ISSUED{txn_outcome_capability,read_your_writes_capability,
                        posture,minimum_visible_logical_position,
                        committed_branch_head_commitment}
READ_YOUR_WRITES_WAIT{read_your_writes_capability,requested_snapshot_selector}
READ_YOUR_WRITES_READY{rotated_or_same_capability,posture,effective_snapshot,
                       minimum_visible_logical_position,
                       read_release_authorization,audit_release}

MERGE_PREPARE{merge_request_idempotency_key,canonical_request_digest,target,
              source_heads,merge_bases,resolution_policy_oid}
MERGE_PREPARED{merge_prepare_id,merge_outcome_capability,
               canonical_request_digest,service_visibility_epoch}
MERGE_EXECUTE{merge_outcome_capability,expected_target_basis,resource_request}
MERGE_STATUS{merge_outcome_capability}
MERGE_STATUS_RESULT{state:InFlight|Committed{target_marker:PostureMarkerIdentity,
                                           final_effect_digest,
                                           txn_outcome_capability}|
                          Rejected{stable_reason_class}|
                          TokenNotYetValid|TokenExpired|TimeAuthorityUnavailable|
                          NotVisibleOrUnknown}

QUERY_CANCEL{request_id,expected_child_state_version,cancel_nonce}
QUERY_CANCEL_RESULT{BeforePublicationAborted|PublishedDeliveryStopped|TooLate|Unknown}
COMMIT_CANCEL{txn_handle,expected_attempt_state_version,cancel_nonce}
COMMIT_CANCEL_RESULT{CancelledBeforeAdmission|TooLate|Unknown}
CANCEL_EXPLANATION{lineage,exact_drain_state,read_release_authorization,audit_release,
                   statistical_estimate?}

SUBSCRIBE_BEGIN{subscription_idempotency_key,canonical_request_digest,definition,
                snapshot_mode,authority_mode}
SUBSCRIBE_READY{subscription_idempotency_key,canonical_request_digest,derived_identity_digest,
                graph_reference_bindings,authorized_cursor_position,resume_capability,
                baseline_lease_id,baseline_id,baseline_digest,
                read_release_authorization,audit_release}
SNAPSHOT_BEGIN{baseline_lease_id,baseline_id,cursor_state_version,authorized_cursor_position,
               read_release_authorization,audit_release,output_schema,result_answer_contract,
               canonical_encoding_version,total_chunks,total_len,digest}
SNAPSHOT_CHUNK{baseline_lease_id,baseline_id,cursor_state_version,digest,
               chunk_ordinal,chunk_count,canonical_offset,payload}
SNAPSHOT_END{baseline_lease_id,baseline_id,cursor_state_version,digest}
SNAPSHOT_ACK{resume_capability,baseline_lease_id,baseline_id,baseline_digest,
             expected_cursor_state_version,client_ack_nonce}
SNAPSHOT_ACKED{rotated_resume_capability,cursor_state_version,authorized_cursor_position}

AuthorizedDeltaPublicProvenance =
    Opaque{delivery_sequence,authorized_cursor_position}
  | Declassified{delivery_sequence,authorized_cursor_position,
                 source_posture_and_frontiers,atomic_or_coalesced_source_commitment,
                 declassification_authorization,audit_release}
DELTA_BEGIN{delivery_lease_id,delivery_id,public_delivery_digest,cursor_state_version,
            authorized_cursor_position,output_schema,result_answer_contract,
            canonical_encoding_version,canonical_payload_len,output_payload_digest,
            public_provenance:AuthorizedDeltaPublicProvenance,
            read_release_authorization,audit_release,total_chunks}
DELTA_CHUNK{delivery_id,public_delivery_digest,output_payload_digest,cursor_state_version,
            chunk_index,chunk_count,canonical_offset,payload}
DELTA_END{delivery_id,public_delivery_digest,output_payload_digest,cursor_state_version,
          authorized_proof_projection?}
ACK{resume_capability,delivery_lease_id,delivery_id,public_delivery_digest,
    expected_cursor_state_version,client_ack_nonce}
ACKED{rotated_resume_capability,cursor_state_version,authorized_cursor_position}
RESUME{resume_capability}
RESUMED{rotated_resume_capability,cursor_state_version,
        outstanding:Baseline{baseline_lease_id,baseline_id,baseline_digest}|
                    Delta{delivery_lease_id,delivery_id,public_delivery_digest}|None,
        authorized_cursor_position}
SUBSCRIBE_CLOSE{resume_capability,expected_cursor_state_version,request_idempotency_key,
                expected_outstanding_lease:None|Baseline|Delta}
SUBSCRIPTION_ENDED{terminal_digest,capability_disposition,final_cursor_state_version,
                   read_release_authorization,audit_release}
GAP{expected_authorized_cursor_position,available_from_authorized_position,
    new_baseline_contract,read_release_authorization,audit_release}
PROOF{proof_class,authorized_scope,read_release_authorization,audit_release,payload}

RESUME_MIGRATE{legacy_resume_capability,transition_identity,expected_cursor_version,
               request_idempotency_key}
RESUME_MIGRATED{posture:Sharded,rotated_e2_resume_capability,cursor_state_version,
                mandatory_baseline{baseline_lease_id,baseline_id,baseline_digest,
                                   authorized_cursor_position,
                                   read_release_authorization,audit_release}}

EXPORT_BEGIN{export_idempotency_key,graph_reference_bindings,export_projection,
             format_contract_oid,snapshot_selector,consistency,resource_request}
EXPORT_READY{export_request_digest,export_delivery_id,posture,
             read_release_authorization,audit_release,
             canonical_export_digest,total_chunks,total_len}
EXPORT_CHUNK{export_delivery_id,canonical_export_digest,chunk_ordinal,
             canonical_offset,payload}
EXPORT_END{export_delivery_id,canonical_export_digest}
EXPORT_ACK{export_delivery_id,canonical_export_digest,client_ack_nonce}
EXPORT_ACKED{export_delivery_id,delivery_state_version}

REPLAY_GET{replay_request_idempotency_key,manifest_oid,requested_projection}
REPLAY_MANIFEST_BEGIN{manifest_oid,effective_completeness,
                      read_release_authorization,audit_release,total_chunks,total_len,digest}
REPLAY_MANIFEST_CHUNK{manifest_oid,chunk_ordinal,canonical_offset,payload}
REPLAY_MANIFEST_END{manifest_oid,digest}
REPLAY_EXECUTE{replay_request_idempotency_key,manifest_oid,fetch,resource_request}
REPLAY_STATUS{manifest_oid,effective_completeness,authorized_availability_projection,
              read_release_authorization,audit_release}

AuditReceiptSubject = Transaction{txn_outcome_capability}
                    | Result{resume_capability}
                    | Subscription{resume_capability}
                    | Export{export_request_identity}
                    | Replay{replay_request_identity}
                    | ProtectedError{error_delivery_identity}
AUDIT_RECEIPT_REQUEST{subject:AuditReceiptSubject}
AUDIT_RECEIPT{subject,state:NotRequired{evidence_projection}
                           |RequiredPending{ticket_identity_projection}
                           |RequiredMirrored{portable_receipt_projection}
                           |NotReadyOrUnavailable}

FLOW_CREDIT{stream_id,expected_flow_state_version,credit_sequence,
            cumulative_byte_credit,cumulative_row_credit}
DATA_FRAGMENT{envelope_id,chunk_ordinal,row_ordinal,fragment_ordinal,total_fragments,
              canonical_row_len,row_digest,payload}
FEC_BEGIN{authenticated_ciphertext_record,authenticated_encoding_descriptor,
          placement_context,reservation}
FEC_SYMBOL{canonical_symbol_record_bytes}
ERROR{scope,code,retry_class,detail:
    PublicNonDataDependent{redacted_detail?}
  | Protected{error_delivery_identity,read_release_authorization,
              audit_release,redacted_detail}}
GOODBYE{reason}
```

`SubscriptionCreationIndex` durably maps the scoped subscription key and canonical request digest to exactly one cursor, baseline lease, resume capability lineage, and READY response commitment. Exact retry reproduces READY; drift fails. `SUBSCRIBE_CLOSE` first terminally ACKs or releases any outstanding baseline/delta under its typed evidence, then orders `ResetOrExpire`, stores a capability-safe tombstone, and makes lost close-response replay deterministic. Generic `STREAM_END` is not a durable unsubscribe. `FLOW_CREDIT` is a versioned cumulative assignment, not an additive increment: the next `credit_sequence` and expected flow-state version must match; an exact duplicate is idempotent, an older/different duplicate or gap rejects, and each cumulative total is nondecreasing, policy-bounded, and checked for integer overflow before state change. `GAP` and `SUBSCRIPTION_ENDED` are protected data-dependent output and require a fresh `PublicFrameSendGuard::DataOutput` validating their read/audit release evidence immediately before every write.

The complete internal delta provenance remains in `DeltaDeliveryEnvelope` and its `InternalDeliveryDigest`; it is never a wire type. Every `baseline_digest` frame field above means `PublicBaselineDigest`, and every baseline ACK validates that public digest; internal baseline identity/coverage/frontier are likewise server-side only. `AuthorizedDeltaPublicProvenance` and `PublicDeliveryDigest` are separately derived after authorization. The default Opaque arm reveals only delivery sequence and authorized cursor position. Atomic/coalesced source ranges, batch IDs/digests, source count, zero-net cadence, and hidden commits appear only in the explicitly authorized and audited Declassified arm. Hidden-commit differential tests require byte-identical public streams, timings within the declared deterministic envelope, and digests under the Opaque policy.

Local dispatch uses `LocalStatementAbortSpec`, `TxnAbortSpec`, `LocalResultDeliveryTransitionSpec`, Local read-close/prepare/terminal-completion, and Local status/index types. Sharded dispatch uses `GlobalStatementAbortSpec`, `GlobalAttemptCancelSpec`, `GlobalResultDeliveryTransitionSpec`, Global read-close/prepare/terminal-completion, and Meta outcome/directory types. After publication, cancellation can only stop/release delivery; it cannot retract Published. After prepare admission, cancellation returns TooLate or Unknown and recovery completes the admitted terminal. `CANCEL_EXPLANATION` and data-dependent cancellation errors are protected output.

`RESUME_MIGRATE` is legal only under a fresh Sharded E2 Ready binding. The E capability is checked solely as proof for the exact `PostActivationCursorTransition`, with the same principal, no-wider authority, immediately preceding Local epoch, no outstanding Local lease, and a prebuilt E2 baseline. It grants no E read, delivery, lookup, or existence authority. Exact retry returns the same pre-minted E2 successor; ineligible or invalid proof is a uniform nonrevealing failure. No Local-to-Global delta range is emitted.

Frame-order validity never substitutes for value, authorization, decompression, time, or resource validation. Every `*_BEGIN`, chunk, end, proof, replay/status projection, exported byte, protected error, and cancellation explanation consumes the one fresh `PublicFrameSendGuard` arm assigned by the generated frame-class matrix; `DataOutput` is not valid for status, terminal outcomes, audit receipts, or protected errors. Canonical chunking uses deterministic record/row boundaries; oversized legal rows use `DATA_FRAGMENT` after bounded spill reservation, and nothing is exposed until row and envelope verification completes. ACK is legal only after the matching END transcript. Incomplete unacked output replays from its declared canonical boundary or releases through a typed transition; it is never silently acknowledged.

A ReplayManifest ObjectId is only a selector. Replay retrieval/execution requires current scoped Replay authority, release authorization, and audit release; replay execution results use the ordinary result lifecycle. `FEC_SYMBOL` is the exact canonical SymbolRecord and is verified against authenticated metadata before admission. Compression/FEC is negotiated only after authenticated metadata and resource reservation. HTTP/2, gRPC, WebSocket, and Bolt adapters preserve the same idempotency, posture, release, output-guard, cancellation, result-resume, and cutover semantics and add origin/CSRF, listener, trace-baggage, authorization, and decompression limits.

State-model, golden, differential, fuzz, crash, and DPOR suites cover pre-auth database non-disclosure; missing/out-of-order AUTH_OK/READY; Local/Sharded dispatch parity; lost/duplicate/conflicting BEGIN, autocommit, subscription, result resume/ACK, unsubscribe, export, and replay requests; NotRequired versus RequiredMirrored release; revocation/refresh/epoch change between every two chunks; protected-error silence; hidden zero-net provenance noninterference; E-to-E2 migration exclusivity; and adapter parity.
